jaina- vividha sāhitya - śāstramālā ( 4 )
śrīlakṣmaṇagaṇiviracitaṁ
supāsanāhacariyaṁ ।
( tr̥tīyō bhāgaḥ )
gūrjara dēśāntargatarājadhanyapura vāstavyēna śrēṣṭhitrikamacandratanūjēna kalikātā viśvavidyālayē
saṁskr̥ta-prākr̥tādhyāpaka-parīkṣakēṇa nyāya-vyākaraṇatīrthapadavīkēna paṇḍita-
daragōvindadāsēna
saṁśōdhita saṁskr̥tacchāyayā vibhūṣitaṁ ca ।
vīrasaṁvat 2445
Jain Education International
For Private & Personal Use Only
| hr̥dayaṁ rūpyakadvayamā

samarpaṇam ।
yasyānanyasamaṁ madēna rahitaṁ pāṇḍityamatyujjvalaṁ
vāṇī candanaśītalā janamana:- saṁtāpahāriṇī ।
iṣṭē'niṣṭatarē ca vastunicayē cētō vikārōjjhitaṁ
bāhyāḍambaravarjitā parahitādhānē pravr̥ttiḥ śubhā ॥ 1 ॥
anyē cāpi guṇāḥ sudhāṁśuvimalā gāmbhīryadhairyādaya-
stattatpūrvamaharṣicārucaritaṁ satyāpayanti dhruvam ।
1
tasya śrīmunirājarājavijayasyēdaṁ karāmbhōruhē
bhaktyā pustakamarpayāmi kr̥payā tasyaiva saṁpāditam || 2 |
saṁpādaka: ।

sahāyakōṁ kē śubha nāma |
yaha prākr̥tabhāṣākā prācīna aura vistīrṇa grantha kā sānuvāda prakāśanakā pavitra kāryamēṁ
nāta:smaraṇīya muni mahārāja śrī rājavijayajīkē sadupadēśa sē jina sadgr̥hasthōṁnē ullēkhanīya ārthika
sahāyatā karakē apanī dhārmikatā aura śāsanapriyatā kē sātha udāratākā paricaya diyā hai una
hānubhāvōṁ sādhuvādāī nāma aura madadakī rakama isa prakāra hai । jisamēṁ śrīyuta mōhanalālabhāī
buśālacaṁda, jisanē isa kāryakī pahala kī hai; śrīyuta śāmacaṁda kēvaladāsa, jisakī tarphasē sabasē
adhika madada kī gaī hai; aura śrīyuta rāva sāhēba ātmārāma bhāī harakhacaṁda, jō jainadharmāvalambī
hōnē para bhī jaina sāhityakī tarpha kriyātmaka anurāga rakhatē haiṁ, viśēṣataḥ dhanyavāda kē pātra haiṁ ।

prastāvanā |
ayaṁ supārśvanāthacaritanāmā padyātmakō vistīrṇaḥ prākr̥tagranthaḥ । saptamatīrthakarasya bhagavataḥ
supārśvanāthasya caritamatra pratipādya viṣayō granthanāmnēva prakaṭaḥ । bhagavadupadēśamastāva ēvāsya granthasya
mahāntamaṁśamavaruṇaddhi । tatra śrāvakāṇāṁ samyaktvamūlāni dvādaśa vratāni pratyēkaṁ tēṣāṁ pañca pañcāti-
cārān । dūṣaṇāni ) cādhikr̥tya vratapālanē suphalōpalambhaḥ, aticārādhānē ca samucitō daṇḍavi
dhirēkaikakathādvārā samupadiṣṭaḥ । prāyaḥ pratyēkamapi kathāyāḥ kēvalaṁ vratādyupadēśavidhāvēva paryavasānama-
kr̥tvā prasaṅgānusaṁdhānapurassaraṁ kasyāṁcid buddhimāhātmyam, kvacit kalā kauśalyam, kāpi vāsanā -
vaiṣamyam, kvacana prakr̥tiprabhāvam kutrāpi ca tattvarahasyādikaṁ saralēnātha ca sarasēna racanāsaṁdarbhēṇa
vyāvarṇayana granthakāraḥ svasamayavidyamānasya laukikācāra-vyavahārasya, sāmājika prathāyāḥ, rājakīya-
paristhitē:, dhārmikabhāvasya, naitikajīvanasya, anyasyāpi ca tādr̥śasyānuṣaṅgikasya jñātavyavastunaḥ
samullēkhaṁ vihitavān । atō'yaṁ granthō yathā jainadharmāvalamvināṁ dhārmika śikṣāviṣayatvēnōpakārakatā-
mākalayati, anyēṣāmapi kāvyarasāsvādara tikānāṁ rasikānāṁ purātatvānusaṁdhānaikalakṣāṇāṁ dakṣāṇāṁ,
bhāratavarṣīyabhāṣātattva pariśīlanōdyuktānāṁ cābhiyuktānāṁ tathaivōpayōgitāmāvahati, iti saṁpradhārya,
adyāpyamudritasyāsya granthasya saṁpādanakarmaṇi vyāpr̥tō'bhavam ।
"
,
itara prākr̥ta kāvyagranthēṣviva prakr̥tagranthē paricchēdarūpaḥ auśvāsakātmakaḥ, sam̐rgasvarūpaḥ, anyō
vā kaścana tādr̥śaḥ prakaraṇavibhāgō nōpalabdhaḥ atha ca gauvadha iva gāthāṅkānāmakhaṇḍitapravāhō yāva-
dantaṁ granthasyāsya purātanādarśapustakēṣu dr̥ṣṭaḥ kēvalaṁ bhagavataḥ pūrvabhavadyavarṇanaparisamāptāvupāntyagāthāyāṁ
“paḍhamapatthāvō” iti, upasaṁhāravākyē " iya sirisupāsanāhacariē paḍhamō bīōō
surajavō asamattō" iti ca; dīkṣā varṇanāvasānē 'ntyagāthāyāṁ “ḍuśyapatthāvō” iti
kēvalajñānōtpatyupakramāntē " iti śrī supārśvajinacaritrē kēvalajñānaśrī prāptiḥ” iti;
ēvamēva ca tataḥ paraṁ pratyēkakathāvasānē " iti samyaktvapraśaṁsāyāṁ campakamālākathā-
nakaṁ samāptam" ityādyākārāṇi saṁskr̥tabhāṣāyāmēvōpasaṁhāravākyānyupalabdhāni । atō gāthā -
kāṁstēṣvēva granthakārābhimatēṣu sthānēṣu vibhajya tadullēkhānusārī prakaraṇavibhāgō vihitaḥ; granthakārēṇā-
ntarāntarā pramāṇarūpēṇōddhr̥tāḥ saṁskr̥ta ślōkāśca pravāhāgatēna padyāṅkana virahayya ladhvakṣarēṣu mudritā:;
pāṭhakagaṇaḥ saukaryēṇa tadbhēdaṁ vikarōtviti ।
1 yathā surasundaryādau । 2 yathā satuvan । 3 yathā kumārapālacaritē ( prākr̥tadvayāśrayē ) ।

( 2 )
prastutagranthasya prākr̥tabhāṣāvyatvaṁ prāgēvōktam । prākr̥tabhāṣā ca, āsatāmitarē, saṁskr̥taviduṣāmapi
saṁprati duravabōdhā । prākr̥tavyākaraṇātiriktaṁ prākr̥tasāhityagrantha pariśīlanamavaśyamapēkṣatē prākr̥tabhāṣāva-
bōdhaḥ । vinā saṁskr̥tānuvādasāhāyyaṁ tatpariśīlanaṁ ca nēpatkaram । iti saṁskr̥tānuvāda sahakr̥tasyaivāsya
samupakārakatvamavadhārya, vihitē'pi gavēṣaṇē kyāpi prācyācāryavinirmitamasya saṁskr̥tānuvādam, anu-
vādōpayōgi vivaraṇa, viṣamasthānaṭippana kaṁ vā kiñcidapyanāsādya, tatkaraṇē'pi pravr̥ttimakārṣam ।
1
prākr̥tasya saṁskr̥tānuvādaḥ ( na tu ṭīkā ) prācyagranthēṣvapi kramēṇa yāvatsaṁbhavaṁ tatpratirūpakaiḥ
( abhikr̥tikaiḥ ) ēvaṁ saṁskr̥ta śabdairvihitaḥ, viśiṣṭēna 'chāyā' śabdēnābhihitaśca vilōkyatē ।
ēvaṁvidhasya cchāyārūpasyānuvādasya niyantritaśabdamaryādatayā kvacid bhāvasaundaryahānikārakatvē
satyapi prākr̥tabhāṣāvabōdhajanakatvē'nanyasadr̥śaṁ sāhāyaka vidhāyakatvamasādhāraṇō guṇaḥ । ityēnamēva guṇaṁ,
yō vartamānasamayētyupayuktatāṁ dadhāti, agrēkr̥tya mācīna rūḍhimanusarannatrāpi tādr̥śānuvāda ( chāyā )-
va vidhāya mūlagranthasyādhōbhāgē nyavīviśam ।
chāyāyāmatra yā paddhatiraṅgīkr̥tā, tasyā viṣayē'tra kriyamāṇaṁ kiñcitspaṣṭīkaraṇaṁ, vāḍhaṁ viśva-
simi, aucityaṁ nātikramiṣyati ;
1 (ka) yathā kvacidēkasyāpi tīrtha- kutūhala- br̥haspatyādēḥ saṁskr̥taśabdasya prākr̥tē'nēkarūpāṇi vyā-
karaṇaniyamēna sidhyanti tathā kvāpi samatta - patta-maya-satthaprabhr̥tēḥ prākr̥tasyāpyēkasya śabda-
rūpasya nānāvidhāni saṁskr̥tarūpāṇi bhavitumarhanti; satyapyēvam, prakaraṇasaṁgatārthakamēvaikaṁ rūpa
vihāya nānyāni tatrōpayujyanta iti suprasiddhamētat । kintu yatra prakaraṇasagatānyapyēkasya
prākr̥taśabdasya nānāvidhāni saṁskr̥tarūpāṇi saṁbhavanti, tatrāpyanyatarasyaivēhōpādānaṁ kr̥tvā -
'nyānyupēkṣitāni yathā - 'suhayara' śabdasya, ( pr̥0 3) prakaraṇāvirōdhēna saṁgamyamā-
nānāṁ śubhakara-sukhakara- śubhataraśabdānāṁ trayāṇāmapi madhya ēkatama ēva sukhakaraśabda ādr̥taḥ,
anyāvupēkṣitau, ēkēnaiva rūpēṇa paryāptaprayōjanatvāt ēvaṁ 'nivyaḍia ' prabhr̥tērapi nirvr̥tta-
niṣpatita- spaṣṭabhūtādīnāmēkatamasyaivaikatrōpādānam,
uktādēva kāraṇāt
rūpavaicitryadarśana-
syāpi sthalabhēdēnaikatamapi bhinnabhinnaṁ rūpamādāya yāvatsabhavaṁ sādhitatvāt ।
(kha) yatra ca ślēṣasaṅgastatra pakṣadvayē pr̥thaka pr̥thaka saṁvadhyamānaṁ rūpadvayamapyādr̥tam, anyathā bhinna-
1 tittha, tūha ( hē0 prā0 1, 104 ); kō ūhala, kuūhala, kōuhala ( hē0 prā0 1, 117 );
prama, puma, paduma, paḍhama ( hē0 prā0 1, 55 ), bhayasai, bhayamphai, bhayappaṛa, bahassai, baha phai,
bahampada, bihassai, biṣphai, bihampa, buhassai, buhapphai, buhapai, ( hē0 prā0 2,137 ) । 2
samasta samāpta patra, pātra, prāptaḥ mada, mata, mr̥ga, mr̥taḥ śastra, śāstra, sārtha
svastha, svāsthya,
,
śasta masta svārtha sākā svāstra |

( 3 )
pakṣē tadarthāsaṁgatē; kēvalamupamēyapakṣīyaṁ rūpaṁ mukhyataḥ, upamānapakṣīyaṁ tu rūpaṁ bhinnavarṇō
rūpāṁśō vā gauṇatayā ( ) ēvaṁbhūtē kōṣṭakē sthāpitaḥ, yathā 'sāvaya' śabdasya ( pr̥0
348) śrāvaka - śvāpadātmakasya rūpadvayasya madhya upamēyapakṣīyaṁ śrāvakarūpaṁ prathamamupādāya, upa-
mānabhūtāraṇyapakṣīyaṁ śvāpadarūpaṁ kōṣṭakē gr̥hītam ; yathā ca 'sayaṇa' śabdasya ( pr̥0 369 )
sadana - śayanarūparūpadvitayasya madhyē purapakṣīyaṁ sadanaṁ mukhyataḥ, upamānabhūtajaladhijalapakṣīya-
śayanasya bhinnavarṇōśa: 'śaya' iti kōṣṭakē, ēvamanyatrāpi sarvatra ।
(ga) yatra punaḥ ślēṣē'pi paryāptād rūpadvayādadhikasyāpi rūpasya prakaraṇa saṁgatasya saṁbhavaḥ, tatrādhi-
kasya prāguktavadanāvaśyakatayā'nupādānam, yathā 'sappāyāraṁ ' ( pr̥0 348 ) ityādau
samākāra - sarvādhārātmakasya rūpadvayasyaiva pakṣadvayē'pi paryāptatayā'dhikasya 'sarpagāra'
ityasyōpamāna bhūtāraṇyapakṣē saṁbhavatsaṁgatikasyāpyagrahaṇam ।
"
(gha) yatra tu ślēṣē pakṣadvayē'pyēkēnaiva śabdarūpēṇaikārthakēna bhinnārthakēna vā nirvāha:, tatraikasmāda-
dhikaṁ saṁbhavadapi prakaraṇasaṁgatimadapi nōpāttam, yathā 'vararayaṇā' ( pr̥0 304 ) ityatra
vararatnā' ityanēnaikēna ratnaśabdēnaiva jaladhilaharirūpōpamānapakṣē bhāryārūpōpamēyapakṣē ca
( varāṇi ratnānyābharaṇēṣu yasyāḥ sā ) paryāptatayā susaṁgatikasya saṁbhavataca 'vararacanā '
itirūpasyōpēkṣā; yathā vā 'surayaṇamahiyaṁ' ( pr̥0 369) ityatra suratnamahitēnaikēnaiva
śabdēna pakṣadvayē'pi nirvāhādabhyadhikasya 'surajanamathitaṁ ' ityasyōpamānapakṣē ghaṭamānasyādhi-
kasya rūpasyānupādānam । ēvamanyatrāpi । sarvatrāpi paryāptarūpamātrasyaiva grahaṇaṁ, nādhikasyē-
tyatra nigarvaḥ ।
2 (ka) katipayaprākr̥taśabdānāṁ niṣpadyamāna ēkārthakē'pi saṁskr̥tarūpadvaya ēkaṁ varṇaparāvr̥ttisaham,
itaracca tatparivartanarahitaṁ bhavati, yathā prākr̥tasya ' tūra' śabdasya saṁskr̥tē tūra - tayēṁ iti, mōra-
śabdasya ca saṁskr̥tē mōraṁ-mayūrāviti । ētādr̥śasthalēṣu prāyō varṇaparāvr̥ttirahitamēva rūpaṁ
chāyāyāmupāttam ।
,
(kha) yēṣāṁ tu dvē api varṇaparāvr̥ttisahē ēva yathā 'sukkha' śabdasya sukha-saukhyē, 'kōhala'
sya vā kutūhala - kautūhalē । tēṣāṁ sthānabhēdēna kutrāpi kataradupāttam, aviśēṣāt ।
3 (ka) tādr̥śā apyanēkē santi śabdāḥ yēṣāṁ prākr̥tatvē saṁskr̥tatvē vā prācyaviduṣāmapi matabhēdaḥ, yathā
'cihura' śabdasya hēmacandramatē prākr̥tatvē'pi durgastaṁ saṁskr̥taṁ manyatē । 'dra' śabdasyānyamatē
1 abhidhānacintāmaṇau 2, 200 । 2 hē0 prā0 1, 171 sūtrasya vr̥ttau । 3 abhidhāna-
cintāmaṇau 2, 590 । 4 hē0 prā0 1, 186 matravattau ।
Jain Education International
For Private & Personal Use Only
www.jainelibrary.org=== lakshmangani03output-13-to-13.json ==========================
3
saṁskr̥tatvē'pi candramatē prākr̥tatvaṁm | 'vara' śabda: kēvalārtha prākr̥tavyākaraṇēṣu nipāta
uktaḥ, bahubhirviddhi saṁskr̥tatvēna tasya prayōgaḥ kr̥ta upalabhyatē । 'caḍa' iti ruhaghātō-
rādēśō hēmacandrēṇa vihitaḥ, atha cānēkēṣu saṁskr̥tagranthēṣu 'caṭa' dhātōrvyavahārō dr̥śyatē ।
ēvamēva 'ḍa' prabhr̥tīnāṁ prākr̥taśabdānāṁ saṁskr̥tē vaikriyādivad vikurvitapramukhāṇi rūpā-
yapi dvidbhiḥ prayuktānyanēkaśō vilōkyantē । ētādr̥śēṣu vivādāpanēṣu sthalēṣu sādr̥śyā-
nuvandhitayā saṁskr̥tatvapakṣa ēvātra cchāyāyāṁ viśēṣēṇāhata: itarasyāpi matasyā'tiraskaraṇīya-
tvēna kvacit prākr̥tatvamapyurarīkr̥tam ।
(kha) 'maha' ityādīnāṁ punaḥ sādr̥śyānubandhitayā 'mahati' iti saṁskr̥tatvapakṣē kvacidupalabhyamāna-
mapyanādr̥tya prākr̥tavyākaraṇakārairvāñchārthakadhātvādēśavidhānadvārā gr̥hītaḥ prākr̥tatvapakṣa
ēvātrāpyudāttaḥ, saṁskr̥tē mahādidhātūnāṁ vāñchādyarthē prayōgasyāhr̥dayahāritvādaḥ sādr̥śyānu-
bandhasyāpi prakaraṇasaṁgatārthānupātina ēvōpādēyatvāditi ।
4 (ka) prākr̥tavyākaraṇānāmapi parasparaṁ nālpīyān matabhēda: । ayaṁ ca mukhyatō vibhāgadvayē vibhaktuṁ
śakyatē, arthaparaḥ rūpaviṣayatha । tatra prathamaprakārō yathā, 'ṇavari' śabdasya prākr̥taprakāśa-
hēmacandravyākaraṇayōrānantaryārthikatvamuktam, anyēna kēvalārthamapi । ēvaṁrūpē'rthaviṣayē
bhēdē prakaraṇasaṁga tērēvātra nirvivādaṁ niyāmakatvēna tatsaṁgata ēvārthachāyāyāmanusr̥taḥ ।
(kha) yatra punararthābhēdē'pi śabdarūpavipayakō matabhēdaḥ, yathā - vararuci: 'da ityasya 'bōlla'

prasiddhimapaśyatā kumārapālacarita ( prākr̥taddhyāśraya ) ṭīkāyāṁ prakramāgatasyāpi tasya
sthānē dēśyasyēva maryādāparyāyēṇaiva vyākhyānamālōkayatā'trāpi tadbhavatvapakṣamupēkṣya dēśyatva-

(gha) mutkalapramukhāṇāṁ tu saṁskr̥tasāhityē'pyuktavat kvacid vyavahāradarśanāt, prasiddhyabhāvāccōbhaya-
mapi - tadbhavatvaṁ dēśyatvaṁ ca - sthānabhēdēnāṅgīkr̥tam ।
(ṅa) 'aṇaha' ādīnāṁ tvarthabhēdēna tadbhavatvaṁ dēśyatvaṁ ca iti tēṣāṁ prakaraṇa saṁgatyā kvacit kiñci-
dityubhayamapyaviruddhatayā'trāśritam ।
6 (ka) dēśyaśabdānāṁ caikēnaiva dēśīnāmamālādipratipāditēna kēnacicchabdēna cchāyānuvādavi-
dhānē na kiñcid nibandhanamākalayāmaḥ, kintu tadarthakēnānyēnāpi śabdēna tatkaraṇaṁ nānucitam;
varṇasādr̥śyānubandhasya tadbhavaprākr̥taviṣayatvāt । ata ēva prācyagranthēṣu 'ghaṇia' pramukhadēśyaśa-
bdānāṁ bahu- gāḍha vāḍhādiśabdēnēvātrāpi 'paccōṇī' ādidēśyānāṁ samānārthakēnāpi bhinna-
bhinnaśabdēnānuvādō vihitaḥ, samānārthēṣvapi śabdēṣu prakaraṇānurōdhēna kvacit kasyacit
saundaryāvahatvāt । ata ēva 'hu' 'cciya' ādyavyayānāmapi vyākaraṇēṣu tadbhavaprākr̥tatvēnā-
dhikr̥tānāmapi vastutō dēśyaiprapañcāntargatānāṁ bhinnabhinnaiḥ 'hi' 'ēva' 'api' 'khalu' prabhr̥tibhiḥ
śabdairatrānuvādaḥ kr̥taḥ ।
(kha) yēṣāṁ tu pōṭṭa - mēharī - suruṁḍiyādiśabdānāṁ dēśīnāmamālāpratipāditānāṁ kramaśa udara-grāma-
pravarā - śivādyarthānāṁ prakaraṇārthēnāsaṁgatiḥ, tēṣāmanuvādē dēśīnāmamālōktamarthamagr̥hītvā prakara-
saṁgatyōdyamāna ēvārthaḥ samupāttaḥ, prakaraṇāsaṁbaddhavacanānāmanupādēyatvāt । ata ēva tadbhavamākr̥-
tānāṁ 'gaḍa' ādiśabdānāmapi gartādyananuvādēna śakaṭādyarthagrahaṇamiha vihitam ।
prakr̥tagranthē'pabhraṁśātiriktēṣu prākr̥tapadyēṣvapi bahavastādr̥śāḥ śabdā dr̥ṣṭipathamavataranti yēṣāṁ

dēśīkōṣē cānupalambhāt ; atha ca śuddhaistadbhavamākr̥tairdēśyairvā śabdaiḥ saha varṇasādr̥śyānubandhaṁ

prāguktaśailyā chāyākārṣam । katipayāni tādr̥śyatrōdāharaṇāniḥ --

( 16 )
annērhivi sō bhaṇiō sayamaṇa dilavākyassa nagarassa । ciṭṭhai lacchī saccā ihāgayā tujjha punnahiṁ ||
tā givha tumaṁ ēyaṁ, bhaṁḍārō hōi tuha jahā pōḍhō । saṁbhāvijjai ṭhāṇaṁ ēkkāē davvakōḍīē ॥ 70 ॥
lōbhēṇa sōvi savvaṁ taṁ gahiuṁ baṁchaē puṇōvi paraṁ । savayaṇamajjāyālōvaayabha (? vayasa) bhīō niyattēi ||
i anicchaō sō gr̥haṇē mōkkhē ya saṁsaiyacittō ciṁtū (1 ghittū ) ṇaṁ diṇamāṇaṁ saṁgha dhārēi tatthēva ॥
bhāṇijjatōvi diṇō (ṇē 2) visō saṁghasaṁtiyajaṇassa । nō dēi daṁsaṇaṁ, annayā ya sayaṇō maō tassa ||
tō dikkhaṇayamisēṇaṁ jēṇa muṇidēṇa tattha gaṁtūṇa । paḍivōhiūṇa ēvaṁ saṁghō mōyāviō sabbō ||74 ||
tā ūyaṁta sattuṁja ēsu titthēsu dōsuvi jiniṁdē | sirinēmi sahanāhē baṁdai saṁghō vibhūīē || 72 ||
tatyutayaṁta titthē pārutthaya addhalakkhamuṣṇannaṁ । sattuṁjayammi titthē tīsa mahassā samapannā || 76॥
jēṇa paḍivōhiūṇa bhaviyajaṇō ṭhāviō bahū dhammē । jiṇabhaṇiē sammattē dēsē saccē ya viraīē || 77 ॥৷
paṁjjatē siṁpi hu ( sā ) ṭhāṇaṁtarasaṁkamāiyā nēyā । ārāhaṇā guruṇa va sattadiṇā aṇasaṇaṁ navaraṁ ॥ 78 ॥
nīhāraṇāimahimā
nīhāraṇā mahimā dēha hēva jāva sakārō | kintu sayamēva rāyā samāgaō kē ttiryapi pahaṁ ॥ 79 ॥
1
śranyairapi sa bhaṇitaḥ svayamaṇahillapāṭakasya nagarasya । tiṣṭhati lakṣmīḥ sarvēhāgatā tava puṇyaiḥ ॥ 66 ॥
tasmād gr̥hāṇa tvamētāṁ, bhāṇḍāgārō bhavēttava yathā prauḍhaḥ । saṁbhāvyatē sthānamēkasyā dravyakōṭēḥ ॥70॥
lōbhēna sō'pi sarvaṁ tad grahītuṁ vāñchati punarapi param । svavacanamaryādālō pāpayaśōbhītō nivarttatē ॥71॥
ityakr̥taniścayaḥ sa grahaṇē mōkṣē ca saṁśayitacittaḥ । gr̥hītvā dinamānaṁ saṁgha dhārayati tatraiva ॥ 72 ॥
bhāṇyamānō'pi dinē dinē'pi sa saṁghasatkajanasya । nō dadāti darśanam, anyadā ca svajanō mr̥tastasya ॥73॥
tatō darśanamiṣēṇa yēna munīndrēṇa tatra gatvā । pratibōdhyainaṁ saṁghō mōcitaḥ sarvaḥ ॥ 74 ॥
tata ujjayanta-śatruñjayayōstiīrthayōrdvayōrapi jinēndrau । śrīnēmir̥ṣabhanāthau vandatē saṁghō vibhūtyā ॥75॥
tatrōjjayantatīrthē pārustakārdhalakṣamutpannam । śatruñjayē tīrthē triṁśatsahasrāḥ samutpannāḥ ॥76॥
yēna pratibōdhya bhavikajanaḥ sthāpitō bahurdha mēṁ । jinamaṇitē samyaktvē dēśē sarvatra ca viratau ॥77॥
paryantē'syāpi hi sā sthānāntarasaṁkramādikā śēyā । ārādhanā gurūṇāmiva saptadinādanaśanaṁ kintu ॥78॥
nissāraṇādimahimā dēhasya tathaiva yāvatsaṁskāraḥ । kintu svayamēva rājā samāgataḥ kiya tamapi panthānam ॥76॥
9 ujjayantaḥ = giranāraparvataḥ ।
1;
2 asyāpi = hēmacandrasūrērapi paryantārādhanā guruṇāmiva = abhayadēvasūrīṇāmiva ēkōnaviṁśagāthāta
ārabhya saptaviṁśagāthāparyantaṁ pratipāditaprakārēṇa jñēyā tatra prākārapaścimāṭṭālaka sthitēna rājñā gurūṇāṁ
śavaniyōṇamahōtsavō dr̥ṣṭaḥ ( gāthā 23 ), kintvatra svayaṁ rājā ( jayasiṁhaḥ ) kiyantamapi panthānaṁ
tanmahōtsavē saha calita iti viśēṣa ityarthaḥ । ētēna piṭarsanamahōdayēna prastutapraśastisārē (In his fourth
report text page9) asya hēmacandrasūrēḥ yacchatruñjayē paralōkagamanamuktaṁ, tadayuktam, samyakpāṭhānavagamēna
kalpanāmātrōdbhāvitatvāditi ।

tēsiṁ sīsō ( ? sā ) sirivijaya siṁha - siricaṁda - vibuhacaṁdati ।
jāyā tinni guṇa ( 1 gaṇa ) harā sirisiricaṁdō taō sūrī ॥ 80 ॥
dēsēsu viharamāṇō kamēṇa dhaṁvalakkaya mmi varalayarē । saṁpattō tattha ta (1ṭi) ō jaruyantrayanāmaṇibhavaṇē
utta ? ttu) gammi visālē rūvagara maṇijjamaṁḍavasaṇāhē । sirimuṇisuvvayajiṇavara paḍimā samahiṭṭiē rammē ॥ 82
saḍḍhō asthi guṇaḍḍhō dhavalō nāmēṇa pōruvāmakkulē | tēṇa jiēcaṁdasū rippanu hō saṁghō samaggōvi। 8ḥ
mēlē uṁ vinnattō sirimunisuvyayajiṇidacarisa (1) ssa । karaṇatthaṁ saṁghēṇavi siricaṁdō pamaṇiō sūrī
sō taṁ saṁdhāēsaṁ paḍivajjēuṁ viṇiggaō tattō । yāsāvallīpurīē āgaṁtūrṇa ṭhiō gēhē ॥ 85 ॥
sirimāla kulasamugbhavavarasāvayasēdvinā gilasurāṇa |
baharijaṁgasā liya saraṇayapamuhāṇa saguṇāṇa ||86 ॥
tatthaṭṭiēṇa siricaṁda sūriṇā viraiyaṁ imaṁ cariyaṁ । sirimuṇisuvvayatitthaṁkarassa samayānusārēṇa ॥ 87
jaṁ kiṁpi iha ajuttaṁ uttaṁ maimōhaō maē asthi । taṁ subaharā kayakivā majjha visōhaṁtu savrvvapi ॥ 88 ॥
paṭṭiyapōtthiyalihaṇē gaṇiṇā kayamattha pāsadēvēṇa । bahusāhējjaṁ ujjamaparēṇa varamainihāṇēṇa || 89 ||
tēṣāṁ śiṣyāḥ śrīvijayasiṁha śrīcandra- vibudhacandrā iti । jātāstrayō'pi gaṇadharāḥ śrīśrīcandrastataḥ sūriḥ॥ 80
dēśēṣu viharamāṇaḥ kramēṇa dhavalakē varanagarē । saṁprāptastatra tatō bhr̥gukacchukanāmajinabhavanē ॥ 81 ॥
uttuṅgē viśālē rūpyakaramaṇīyamaṇḍapasanāthē । śrīmunisuvratajinavarapratimāsamadhiṣṭhitē ramyē ॥ 82॥
śrāddhō'sti guṇāḍhyō dhavalō nāmnā pōruvāḍakulē । tēna jinacandrasūripramukhaḥ saṁghaḥ samagrō'pi ॥ 83 ॥
mēlayitvā vijñaptaḥ śrīmunisuvratajinēndra caritasya । karaṇārthaṁ saṁghēnāpi śrīcandraḥ prabhaṇitaḥ sūriḥ ||4||
sataṁ saṁghādēśaṁ pratipadya vinirgatastataḥ । śrāśāvallīpuryāmāgatya sthitō gēhē ॥ 85 ॥
śrīmālakulasamudbhavavaraśrāvakaśrēṣṭhināgilasutānām । śrāmraharibhāṇḍaśālikaśaraṇakapramukhāṇāṁ saguṇānām
natra sthitēna śrīcandrasūriṇā viracitamidaṁ caritam । śrīmunisuvratatīrthaṁkarasya samayānusārēṇa || 87 ॥
kimapīhā yuktamuktaṁ matimōhatō mayā'sti । tat śrutadharāḥ kr̥takr̥pā mayi viśōdhayantu sarvamapi ॥88॥
ṭṭikāpustikālēkha gaṇinā kr̥tamatra pārśvadēvēna । bahusāhāyyamudyamaparēṇa varamatinidhānēna ॥86॥
1 saṁprati gurjara dēśē 'ghōlakā' iti nāmnā khyātē । tatra bhr̥gukacchanāmni jinabhavanē, na tu piṭarasanma-
hāśayōktē mr̥gukacchē ( Broach) nagarē tādr̥śasyārthasyātrālābhāt, ananvayāt; munisuvratasvāminaḥ svasa-
tāsamayē bhr̥gukacchē nagarē'śvarakṣaṇāya saṁjātasya gamanasya śāstraprasiddhatvēna tatpratimādhiṣṭhitē jinabhavanē'pi
gucchanāmnō vyavahārasyaiaupacārikasyātvāta sāṁpratamapi tādr̥śavyavahārasyanyitra bahaśō darśanācca ।

taha vīyaguṇaccayadhāriṇā ō vidalaṁ sagōrasaṁ vajjaṁ । bhōaṇaō mahumaṁsaṁ rāhabhattaṁ ca savdēhi ॥ 1 ॥
jē uṇa rāībhattaṁ cayaṁti dattōvva muṇivi muṇivayaṇaṁ । tē iha bhavaṁtarē suvi havaṁti suhiṇō sayākālaṁ ||2||
tathāhi :-
I
suvāsaō sagōvō. bahuvaṇasaṁḍō suvacchatacchāō । atthi suraṭṭhā dēsō ghōsōnva sutitthakayasōhō ||3||
tatthatthi dhaṇasamiddhaṁ girinayaraṁ nāma paṭṭaṇaṁ tammi । rāyā rijvalamahaṇō mahaṇō nāyēṇa supasiddhō ॥ 4 ॥
taha ya mahēsaradattō siṭṭī nivasisu pauraghaṇakaliō । laliyā tassatthi piyā dattō nāmēṇa tāṇa suō।।
dullaliyagōdvikhittō piyarēhiṁ viyaraē paipuraṁpi । vilasai vēsāṇa gihē vivihavilāsēhiṁ dullaliō॥ 6 ॥
piyai suraṁ taha sarayaṁ surayapasatō gamēi diyahāī । aha annayā gaō sō ujjāṇīē saparivārō ||7||
mahumaṁḍa mōyagamaṁḍiyāṇa iḍḍariyaguṁdavaḍayāṇaṁ । gurugaḍḍīō bhari vaḍaya karaṁbāṇa ya tatra ॥ 8 ॥
vīṇāvēṇuvīṇaṁ supāulaṁ samagamēva āṇēi । tō garuyaga hirasarasītaḍampi dāūṇamāvāsaṁ ॥ 9 ॥
jā gaṁtuṁ kathaliharē pāraddhaṁ picchaṇaṁ tahiṁ tāva । tannāsāē paviṭṭō kattōvi hu durahimalagaṁdhī ||10||
dattāvahāṇacittō jāvaya pucchēī pariyaṇaṁ ēsō । kattō samēi gaṁdhō samuddharō duddharō dhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 11 ॥
tō pariyaṇamajjhāō ēgō gaṁdhāṇu sāraō tattha । jā gacchai vaṇamajjhē tā picchai muṇivaraṁ ēkkaṁ || 12 |
niṣpaḍikammasarīraṁ niviṭṭadiṭṭhi didivivammi । kaya uddhavā hujuyalēṇa dēsataṁca sivama ॥ 13 ॥
ghaṇarōmakūvaullasiyasamalava husēyasaliladhārāhiṁ । pāvamalaṁva jharataṁ tavaggitaviyā dēhāu || 14 ||
yē
1
tathā dvitīyaguṇatratadhāriṇā tu dvidalaṁ sagōrasaṁ varjyam । bhōjanatō madhumāṁsaṁ rātribhaktaṁ ca sarvaiḥ ॥1॥
punā rātribhaktaṁ tyajanti dattavajjñātvā munivacanam । ta iha bhavāntarēṣvapi bhavanti sukhinaḥ sadākālam ॥
suprajāśataḥ (supayaāśakaḥ) sagōpō bahuvana ṣaṇḍaḥ suvr̥kṣa ( suvatsa ) sacchāyaḥ ॥
asti surāṣṭrā dēśa ghōṣa iva sutīrthakr̥taśōbhaḥ ॥ 3 ॥
tatrāsti dhanasamr̥ddhaṁ girinagaraṁ nāma pattanaṁ tasmin । rājā ripubalamathanō mathanō nāmnā suprasiddhaḥ ॥ 4 ॥
tathā ca mahēśvaradattaḥ śrēṣṭhī nyavasatpracuradhanakalitaḥ । lalitā tasyāsti priyā dattō nāmnā tayōḥ sutaḥ ॥5॥
durlalita gōṣṭhīkṣiptaḥ pitr̥bhyāṁ vicarati pratipuramapi । vilasati vēśyānāṁ gr̥hē vividhavilāsairdurlalitaḥ || 6 ||
pibati surāṁ tathā sarakaṁ surataprasaktō gamayati divasāni । athānyadā gataḥ sa audyānyāṁ saparivāraḥ ॥ 7 ॥
madhumaṇḍaka mōdakamaṇḍitānāmiddarika gundravaṭakānām । guruśakaṭāni bhūtvā vaṭakakarambayōśca tathaiva ॥ 8 ॥
vīṇāvēṇupravīṇaṁ sugāyanavr̥ndaṁ samamēvānayati । tatō gurugarbhī rasarasītaṭē dattvā'vāsam ॥ 9 ॥
yāvad gatvā kadalīgr̥hē prārabdhaṁ prēkṣaṇaṁ tatra tāvat । tannāsāyāṁ praviṣṭaḥ kutō'pi hi durabhimalagandhaḥ ॥ 10॥
dattāvadhānācēttō yāvacca pr̥cchati parijanamēṣaḥ । kutaḥ samētti gandhaḥ samudadhurō durdharō gāḍham ॥ 11 ॥
tataḥ parijanamadhyādēkō gandhānusāratastatra । yāvad gacchati vanamadhyē tāvatpaśyati munivaramēkam ॥ 12॥
niṣpratikarmaśarīraṁ niviṣṭadr̥ṣṭiṁ dinēndrabimvē । kr̥tōrdhvabāhuyugalēna dēśayantamiva śivamārgam ॥ 13 ॥

supāsanāha- cariammi-
ukkaḍagaṁdhaṁ uttattakaṇayavannaṁ aṇaṁgasamarūvaṁ । taṁ daṭuṁ vimhaiō sō gaṁtuṁ kahai dattassa ॥ 15 ॥
savvaṁ taṁ vr̥ttaṁtaṁ tō sō tōsēṇa jāi muṇipāsē । pāsai pasaṁtarūvaṁ taṁ sāhuṁ vaṁdai samittō ॥ 16 ॥
tēṇavi jhāṇaṁ muttuṁ dāūṇaṁ dhammalābhamiya bhaṇiō । kiṁ datta ! dattahatthō dhammassa bhamēsi bhayarahiō ? ||
yataḥ,
1
" satyaṁ manōramāḥ kāmāḥ satyaṁ ramyā vibhūtayaḥ । kintu mattāṅganāpāṅgabhaṅgalōlaṁ hi jīvitam |
lakṣmīlatākuṭhārasya bhōgāmbhōdanabhasvataḥ । śr̥ṅgāravanadāvasya kō hi kālasya vismr̥taḥ " ||
pavaṇapahallirajalanihitaraṁgaraṁgaṁtavēviraṁgassa । aṇuhērai navari sasiṇō jīyaṁ taralattaṇaguṇēṇa ॥ 18 ॥
jarakō sāsahikkā sira viyaṇavisūyāirōgēhiṁ । āiṭṭhijjai jīyaṁ kayaṁtapāsēhiṁva sayāvi ॥ 19 ॥
ghaḍiyā muhuttapaharaddhamāsamāsāisāhikhaṁḍēhiṁ । parisaḍai junnarukkhucca dēhiṇō jīviyatthaṁvō ||20||
iya ērisampi jīē vilasasi sicchāi piyasi majjamahuṁ । jaṁ datta ! tumaṁ taṁ tuha sukuluppannassa na hu juttaṁ ॥
taha bhuṁjasi rayaṇīē khillasi jūm̐yaṁ ramēsi vēsāṇaṁ । dhammassa puṇō vattaṁpi nēya pucchēsi kaiyā vi || 22 ||
tō bhaṇiyaṁ dattē kō dōsō majjapāṇayāīsa ? | kahasu pasiūṇa jēṇaṁ caēmi, tō sāhaē sāhū ||23||
bhuvaṇōyarammi nitthāmayāē savvēvi jē aṇāyārā । tē mattavālayaṁ alliyaṁti lahu ēkakālaṁpi ||24||
aṇahigayasarūṁbāī kajjākajjāī jēṇa najjaṁti । taṁ hīrai vinnāṇaṁ majjēṇa, dhiratthu majjassa ||25||
itthatthē ditaṁ suṇēhi dō baṁdhuṇō purē kammi । nivasiṁsu, taō jiṭṭhō maō ya kālēna tabbhajjā || 26 ||
ghanarōmakūpōllasitasamalabahusvēdasaliladhārābhiḥ । pāpamalamiva jharantaṁ tapō'gnitaptād dēhāt ॥ 14 ॥
utkaṭagandhamuttaptakanakavarṇamanaṅgasamarūpam । taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā vismayitaḥ sa gatvā kathayati dattāya ॥ 15 ॥
sarva taṁ vr̥ttāntaṁ tataḥ sa tōṣēṇa yāti munipārśvē । paśyati praśāntarūpaṁ taṁ sādhuṁ vandatē samitraḥ ॥ 16 ॥
tēnāpi dhyānaṁ muktvā dattvā dharmalābhamiti bhaṇitaḥ । kiṁ datta ! dattahastō dharmē bhramasi bhayarahitaḥ ? ॥ 17॥
pavanapracalitr̥jalanidhitaraṅgaraṅgadvēpitraṅgam । anuharatē kēvalaṁ śaśinaṁ jīvitaṁ taralatvaguṇēna ॥ 18 ॥
jarākōṣṭhaśvāsahikkāśirōvēdanāvisūcikādirōgaiḥ । ākr̥ṣyatē jīvitaṁ kr̥tāntapāśairiva sadāpi ॥ 19 ॥
ghaṭikāmuhūrtapraharārdhamāsamāsādiśā khikhaṇḍaiḥ । pariśaṭati jīrṇavr̥kṣavad dēhinō jīvitastambaḥ ॥20॥
itīdr̥śē jīvitē vilasasi svēcchayā pibasi madyamadhu । yaddatta ! tvaṁ tattatva sukulōtpannasya na khalu yuktam ॥
tathā bhuṅgē rajanyāṁ ramasē dyūtaṁ ramayasi vēśyāḥ । dharmasya punarvārtāmapi naiva pr̥cchasi kadāpi ||22||
tatō bhaṇitaṁ dattēna kō dōṣō madyapānakādiṣu ? । kathaya prasadya yēna tyajāmi, tataḥ kathayati sādhuḥ ||23||
bhuvanēōdarē niḥsthāmatayā sarvē'pi yēnācārāḥ । tē mattabālamupasarpanti ladhvēkakālamapi ॥24॥
anadhigatasvarūpāṇi kāryākāryāṇi yēna jñāyantē । tad hriyatē vijñānaṁ madyēna, dhigastu madyam ||25||
atrārthē dr̥ṣṭāntaṁ śr̥ṇu dvau bandhū purē kasmin । nyavatsātāṁ, tatō jyēṣṭhō mr̥taśca, kālēna tadbhāryā ||26||

dattakahā ।
47
aṇuratā ya kaṇiṭṭhē taṁ paṛa jaṁpēi mayaṇasaravihurā । taṁ ciya saraṇaṁ dēvara ! bhuṁjasu bhōē maē saddhi ||27||
tō tēṇaṁ paḍibhaṇiyaṁ ā ammōsaṁ tayaṁ imaṁ pāvaṁ । gurubaṁdhuṇī ya bhajjā jaṇaṇītullā jaṇē bhaṇiyā ||28||
tāmā sumiṇēvi tumaṁ pāvaṁ citēsu ērisaṁ avvō ! । ihaparalōyaviruddhaṁ nirddhadhasaciṭṭhiyamaṇihaṁ ॥ 29 ॥
taṁ sōuṁ sā kāūṇa gaṁgali galiyaguṇalavā gēhē । kammāī kuṇai tīsē kathaṁ ca bahu mannaē ēsō ॥ 30॥
iya kālē vaccaṁtē kayā kayakaiyavā gihassaṁtō | ciṭṭhai maṁcayapaḍiyā naya tatti kuṇai gēhassa ॥ 31 ॥
tō bāhirā diya samāgaō taṁ naṁ picchaē tattō । pucchara gihiṇi kaha tuha na dīsaē ittha jiṭṭāṇī 1 ॥
tō sā sāhai jaṁ sā apaḍasarīrā sirassa viyaṇāē । ciṭṭhai gihassa majjhē suttā sijjāē dukkhattā ||
tō saṁtō ēsō karēi sadaṁ duvārasamma । ughāḍēsu kavāḍē kusalaṁ tuha jēṇa pucchāmi ॥ 34 ॥
ughāḍiūṇa dāraṁ majjhaviṭṭhassa tassa sā puṇavi । dēi duvāraṁ gāḍhaṁ bhuyaraṁgalaṁ taha payacchēī || 35 ॥
thālī iyapavaṁ payass puvvāṇiyaṁ ca suramaṁsaṁ । ḍhōēi tassa puraō bhaṇēi maṁsaṁ ca majjaṁ ca ॥ 36 ॥
ēyāṇaṁ ēgayaraṁ uvabhuṁjasu natthi annahā mōkkhō । tō saṁkaḍammi paḍiō ēvaṁ diyarō vikēi ||37||
ēsā jaṇaṇītulā jē jissa baṁdhuṇō bhajjā । maṁsassavi bhakkhaṇayaṁ na khamaṁ ēyaṁ visidvāṇa ॥ 38 ॥
jaō,
vilasāvaṇayamabhakkhaṁ duggaṁdhimalāvilaṁ basāliddhaṁ । jīvavahasaṁkiliḍaṁ nisāyarāsēviyaṁ maṁsaṁ ॥ 39 ॥
jō asai maṁsapēsi karagahiyaṁ tōḍiūṇa daṁtēhiṁ । sō suṇauvva achippō kuluggayāṇaṁ, na uṇa purisō ॥
I
anuraktā ca kaniṣṭhē taṁ prati jalpati madanaśaravidhurā । tvamēva śaraṇaṁ dēvara ! bhuṅkṣva bhōgān mayā sārdham ॥
tatastēna pratibhaṇitamā amarghyaṁ tadidaṁ pāpam । gurubandhōśca bhāryā jananītulyā janē bhaṇitā ||28||
tasmād mā svapnē'pi tvaṁ pāpaṁ cintayēdr̥śaṁ hanta ! | ihaparalōkaviruddhaṁ niṣṭhuracēṣṭitamaniṣṭam ||29||
tat śrutvā sā kr̥tvā tūṣṇīṁ galitaguṇalavā gēhē । karmāṇi karōti tayā kr̥taṁ ca bahu manyata ēṣaḥ ||30||
iti kālē vrajati kadācitkr̥takaitavā gr̥hasyāntaḥ । tiṣṭhati mañcapatitā na ca cintāṁ karōti gēhasya ॥ 31 ॥
tatō bahiṣṭō dēvaraḥ samāgatastāṁ na paśyati tataḥ । pr̥cchati gr̥hiṇīṁ kathaṁ tava na dr̥śyatē'tra jyēṣṭhā ? ॥32॥
tataḥ sā kathayati yatsā'paṭuśarīrā śirasō vēdanayā । tiṣṭhati gr̥hasya madhyē suptā śayyāyāṁ duḥkhārttā ॥33॥
tataḥ saṁbhrānta ēṣa karōti śabda dvāradēśē । udghāṭaya kapāṭau kuśalaṁ tava yēna pr̥cchāmi ॥ 34 ॥
udghāṭya dvāraṁ madhyapraviṣṭē tasmin sā punarapi । dadāti dvāraṁ gāḍhaṁ bhujārgalāṁ tathā prayacchati ॥ 35 ॥
sthālīsthagitapradīpaṁ prakaṭayati pūrvānītaṁ ca suramāṁsam । ḍhōkayati tasya puratō bhaṇati māṁsaṁ ca madyaṁ ca ॥ 36॥
ētayōrēkataramupabhuṅkṣva nāstyanyathā mōkṣaḥ । tataḥ saṁkaṭē patita ēvaṁ dēvarō vitarkayati ॥ 37 ॥
ēṣā jananītalyā yēna jyēṣṭhasya bandhārbhāryā। māṁsasyāpi bhakṣaṇaṁ na kṣamamētad viśiṣṭānām ||38||
yataḥ,
vilāsakamabhakṣyaṁ durgandhimalāvilaṁ vasāśliṣṭam । jīvavadhasaṁkliṣṭaṁ niśācarāsēvitaṁ māṁsam ॥ 39 ॥

supāsanāha-cariasmi ---
majjē puṇa kasiṇajalaṁ kaṇakaṭusamutrabhavaṁ na dōsillaṁ । tā aviyappaṁ pijjai viusēhivi āranālaṁva ॥ 41 ॥
iya citiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ pāyasu majjaṁ mayacchi ! lahumēva । gacchāmi jēṇa lōō bhaṇissai kipi alipi ।
jaṇaṇīēvi hu saddhiṁ rahammi japatayassa avavāō । jāyai, kiṁ puṇa mayabhibhalāē tuma samaṁ nēya ? ||
tō tīē uṭṭhē karē karēūṇa karaviyaṁ samayaṁ । taha pāiō jahicchaṁ majjaṁ jaha ghumiuṁ laggō ॥ 44॥
naya cēha kiṁpi taō ramiō sō tīē pōḍhamahilāē । asiyaṁ maṁsaṁpi taō jāō'ṇatthāṇa patthārī ||
tā datta ! dēttadōsaṁ majjaṁ vajjatu avajjasayamūlaṁ । jūyassavi diṛaṁta suṇasu tumaṁ avahiō hōuṁ ॥
iha kusumapurē nayarē dhaṇasēsuō sudaṁsaṇō āsi । savvakalā pattaṭṭhō aivasaṇī jūyavitayammi ॥47॥
nīhāriyāō kaṇayassa dōni kōḍīō piugihā tēṇa । lacchīpaḍihatthāī kayāī jūyāriyagihāī ॥
tō paṇa kālē kālakkhariō tahāvi tajjaṇaṇī । siḍidiṭṭi parvacivi appara sē kiṁci āharaṇaṁ ।।
aha kahiyē taṁ kēṇavi dhaṇassa tō tēṇa sā gihē bhinnē । nivbhacchiūṇa ṭhaviyā nivvāhaṁ kiṁpi dāuṁ ca ॥
tō annadiṇē taṇaraṇa tēṇa vahu hāriyaṁ hayāsēṇa । gāḍhaṁ gahiō jyāriēhiṁ khittō ya khaḍḍāē ||51 ||
kahiyē tajjagaṇīē kē vi ēyaṁ taō ya ruyamāṇī । pattā tāṇa sagāsa gāsaṁpi akāumavēgā ॥ 52॥
puṭṭhō yatīē sahiō kittiyadavvēṇa chuṭṭaē ēsō ? । tēṇavi bhaṇiyaṁ siṭṭiṇi ! mubai lakkhēṇa kaṇayassa ||
tō tīē saṁlataṁ taṁ pai dūrēṇa saṁpayā pattā । siṭṭigivi na vijjai bhōyaṇamittaṁpi tassēva ||24||
।
yō'śnāti māṁsapēśa karagr̥hītāṁ trōṭayatvā dantaiḥ । sa śunaka ivāspr̥śyaḥ kulōdgatānāṁ na punaḥ puruṣaḥ ॥
madyaṁ punaḥ kr̥ṣṇajalaṁ kaṇakāṣṭhasamudbhavaṁ na dōṣavat । tasmādavikalpaṁ pīyatē vidvadbhirapyāranālamiva ॥ 41 ॥
iti cintayitvā bhaṇitaṁ pāyaya madyaṁ mr̥gākṣi ! ladhvēva । gacchāmi yēna lōkō bhaṇiṣyati kimapyalīkamapi ।।
jananyāpi hi sārdhaṁ rahasi jalpatō'pavādaḥ । jāyatē, kiṁ punarmadavihvalayā tvayā samaṁ naiva ! ॥ 43 ॥
tatastayōtthāya karē kr̥tvā karavikāṁ samam । tathā pāyitō yathēcchaṁ madyaṁ yathā ghūrṇayituṁ lagnaḥ ॥ 44 ॥
naca cētati kimapi tatō ramitaḥ sa tathā prauḍhamahilayā । aśitaṁ māṁsamapi tatō jātō'narthānāṁ prastaraḥ ||
tasmād datta ! dattadōṣaṁ madyaṁ varjayāvadyaśatamūlam । dyūtasyāpi dr̥ṣṭāntaṁ śr̥ṇu tvamavahitō bhūtvā ॥ 46 ॥
iha kusumapura nagarē dhanaśrēṣṭhitaḥ sudarśana āsīt । sarvakalāsundarō'tivyasanī dyūtaviṣayē ॥47॥
nirṇāśitē kanakasya dvē kōṭī pitr̥gr̥hāttēna । lakṣmīpūrṇāni kr̥tāni dyūtakārigr̥hāṇi ॥ 48 ॥
tataḥ pitrā kālēnōpālabvastathāpi tajjananī । śrēṣṭhadr̥ṣṭiṁ pravañcyārpayati tasmai kiñcidābharaṇam || 49 ||
atha kathitaṁ tatkēnāpi vanasya tatastēna sā gr̥hē bhinnē । nirbhaya sthāpitā nirvāhaṁ kamapi dattvā ca ॥50॥
tatō'nyadinē tanayēna tēna bahu hāritaṁ hatāśēna । gāḍhaṁ gr̥hītō dyūtakāribhiḥ kṣiptaśca gartāyām ॥ 11 ॥
kathitaṁ tajjananyāḥ kēnāpyētattataśca rudatī । prāptā tēṣāṁ sakāśaṁ grāsamapyakr̥tvā'tivēgāt ॥ 52 ॥
pr̥ṣṭaśca tathā puraskr̥taḥ kiyadravyēṇa cchṭyata ēṣaḥ ? । tēnāpi bhaṇitaṁ śrēṣṭhini ! mucyatē lakṣaṇa kanakasya ॥

tō mēṁ ullē dhariūṇa muyaha ēyaṁti tīē saṁlatē । sahiēṇaṁ sā gahiyā mukkō nīhāriḍaṁ puttō ॥ 55॥
gacchaṁtēṇaṁ ākarisiūṇa jaṇaṇīē sāḍiyā tēṇa । gahiyā, sahiēṇa taō lajjāē samappiyā annā ॥
tattō sudaṁsaṇō puṇa sāḍiyaṁ milliūṇa khillēi । jūyaṁ, jaṇaṇī puṇa kuṇai sahiyagēhammi kammāī ||
tō ēsō vr̥ttō kahiō sēssi kēvi savivarō । tō sēṭṭhī niyacittē paribhāvā bhāvaṇaṁ ēvaṁ ||
jaha paḍhamaṁpi hu māūē juvvaṇaṁ hairai naṁdaṇō jāō । nāmakaraṇāiē piuṇō lacchiṁ ca avaharai ।। 59 ।।
taṇu parimāṇō harēi bhōyaṇavilēvaṇappamuhaṁ । jaṁ jaṁpi suhasarūvaṁ parigiṇhai naṁdaṇō tassa ॥ 60 ॥
tāruṇṇasamāgamaviṣphuraṁtavammahaparavasō tayaṇu । acchiṁdara gayasaṁkaṁ piuṇō vihavāiyaṁ savvaṁ ॥ 61 ॥
iya kāraṇēhiṁ piṇō duhāvō savvahā havai puttō । jaṁ tammivi paḍibaṁdhō kīrai taṁ puṇa mahacchariyaṁ ॥
ahavā kō nāma duhāvahassa taṇayassa jammasavaṇammi | harisijjā jai navi hōjja mōhamāhappasaṁpattī ? |
niyamō maha saṁpai puttaṁ vai, tammaē puṇō hiyayaṁ । tīi kaē bhajjāē kaha sā kila chuṭṭihī varaī ? |
hu nāyaṁ tīi sahōyarāṇa sāmi kassavi muhēṇa । sirinayarē, tē jēṇaṁ davvaṁ dāūṇa chōḍiti ||65 ||
tō lihiṇaṁ lēhaṁ purisō saṁpēsiō payattēṇa । pattō yēvadiṇēhiṁ tāṇaṁ sō appaē lēhaṁ ॥ 66 ॥
tatra cēdaṁ likhitam ;-
-
jalahisalilaṁva muṇiṇā mahagihadavvaṁ suēṇa ēkkapaē । nīsēsaṁpi hu gasiyaṁ jyāiduvvasaṇatisiēṇa ||
tatastayā saṁlapitaṁ taṁ prati dūrēṇa saṁpat prāptā । śrēṣṭhigr̥hē'pi na vidyatē bhōjanamātramapi tasyaiva ॥ 54 ॥
tatō māmr̥ṇē dhr̥tvā muñcataitamiti tathā saṁlapitē । puraskr̥tēna sā gr̥hītā muktō niḥsārya putraḥ ॥ 55 ॥
gacchatā''kr̥ṣya jananyāḥ śāṭikā tēna । gr̥hītā, puraskr̥tēna tatō lajjayā samarpitānyā ॥ 56 ॥
tataḥ sudarśanaḥ punaḥ śāṭikāṁ muktvā ramatē । dyūtaṁ, jananī punaḥ karōti puraskr̥tagēhē karmāṇi || 17 ||
tata ēṣa vr̥ttāntaḥ kathitaḥ śrēṣṭhinaḥ kēnāpi savivaraḥ । tataḥ śrēṣṭhī nijacittē paribhāvayati bhāvanāmēvam ॥
yathā prathamamapi hi māturyauvanaṁ harati nandanō jātaḥ । nāmakaraṇādikēṣu piturlakṣmīṁ cāpaharati ॥ 59 ॥
tadanu parivardhamānō harati bhōjanavilēpanapramukham । yad yadapi sukhasvarūpaṁ parigr̥hṇāti nandanastasya ॥ 60 ॥
tāruṇyasamāgamavisphuranmanmathaparavaśastadanu । ācchinatti gataśaṅkaṁ piturvibhavādikaṁ sarvam ॥ 61 ॥
iti kāraṇaiḥ piturduḥkhāvahaḥ sarvathā bhavati putraḥ । yattasminnapi pratibandhaḥ kriyatē tatpunarmahāścaryam ||62||
athavā kō nāma duḥkhāvahasya tanayasya janmaśravaṇē । hr̥ṣyēd yadi naiva bhavēd mōhamāhātmyasaṁpattiḥ ? || 63॥
tatō niyamō mama saṁprati putraṁ prati, tāmyati punarhr̥dayam । tasyāḥ kr̥tē bhāryāyāḥ kathaṁ sā kilacchuṭiyatē varākī ||
huṁ jñātaṁ tasyāḥ sahōdarānkathayāmi kasyāpi mukhēna । śrīnagarē, tē yēna dravyaṁ dattvā chōṭayanti ॥ 65 ॥
tatō likhitvā lēkhaṁ puruṣaḥ saṁprēṣitaḥ prayatnēna । prāptaḥ stōkādinaistabhyaḥ sō'rpayati lēkham || 66 ॥

tumha bhaiṇīva ullē dhariyā jūyāriēhiṁ tammukkā । igalakkhassa karaṇaṁ jaṁ jāṇaha taṁ karijjāsu ||
iya bāiūṇa bāhullalōyaṇā baṁdhuṇō parōpparaō । jaṁpati paṇayasāraṁ ahaha ahō dāruṇaṁ dukkha || 69 ॥
saṁjaya bhaiṇī tā ki ēēṇa davvajāēṇa । gayakannacaṁcalēṇaṁ, uvajujjara bhaiṇikajjammi || 70 ||
kō tullō bhaiṇīē havijja sayaṇāṇa majjhayārammi । jīē āsītrayaṇā duriyapabaṁdhā vilijjati ॥
savvēvi ucchavā nicchaēṇa bhaiṇīpurassarā huṁti । tā dhannāṇa gihīṇaṁ bhayaṇīō huti sīlaḍḍhā ||
iccāivāsaṇāvāsiēhiṁ savrvvapi vikkiyaṁ bhaṁḍaṁ । kicchēṇa taō lakkhō saṁpattō, taṁ gahēūṇa ॥ 73 ॥
jā pattā tamma purē sarassa pālīē baṁdhuṇō tattha । bhariyaṁbhakuṁbhaninbhara bhārōṇayakaṁdharā bhaiṇī ||74 ||
diṭṭhā sā tēhi taō paccabhināyā jhaḍatti gaṁtūṇa । uttāriūna kuṁbhō nisuṁbhiō bhūmibhāgami ||75 ||
bhūniyimatyaēhiṁ paṇayā sā lajjiyā ya tē dahum̐ । nayaṇaṁ susittanittāē jaṁpiyaṁ tīi tō ēvaṁ ॥ 76 ॥
kusala maha baṁdhūṇaṁ, atakkiyaṁ tumhadaṁsaṇaṁ jāyaṁ । kēṇa va paōyaṇēṇaṁ ihāgayā, iya nisāmē ॥77॥
mannubharabhariyavayaṇēhiṁ tēhi bhaṇiyaṁ hayamha kusalattaṁ । jīvaṁtāṇavi jēsi bhaiṇī ghaḍacēḍiyā jāyā ॥ 78 ॥
hā hā bhaiṇi ! sunayaṇē ! sahassalōyāṇa sāṁmiṇī huṁtā । iṇhiṁ dāsivva jalaṁ bahēsi rē siṁ parēsi ca ॥
hīhī aṇajjakajjujjayassa tuha divva ! kittiyaṁ bhaṇimō । jīi siraṁ sukumāraṁ bhāraṁ kusumāṇa na sahataṁ ।।
inhi jalabhariyaghaḍē vahēi taṁpi hu sunihuraṁ jāyaṁ । tuha divva ! maṇasaricchaṁ sacchaṁdapayāradullaliyaṁ ॥ 81 ॥
iccāi vilavamāṇēhi tēhimārōviyā suhāsaṇaē । nīyā sahiyassa gihē tēṇavi gahiu kaṇayalakkhaṁ ||
yuṣmadbhaginyapi r̥ṇē dhr̥tā dyūtakāribhistanmuktā । ēkalakṣasya kr̥tē yajjānīta tat kuruta ॥ 68 ॥
iti vācayitvā bāṣpavallōcanā bandhavaḥ parasparataḥ । jalpanti praṇayasāra mahaha ahō dāruṇaṁ duḥkham ॥ 69 ॥
saṁjātaṁ bhaginyāstasmāt kimētēna dravyajātēna । gajakarṇacañcalēna, upayujyatāṁ bhaginīkāryē ॥70॥
kastulyō bhaginyā bhavēt svajanānāṁ madhyē । yatyā āśīrvacanād duritaprabandhā vilīyantē ॥71॥
sarvē'pyutsavā niścayēna bhaginīpurassarā bhavanti । tasmād dhanyānāṁ gr̥hiṇī bhaginyō bhavanti śīlāḍhyāḥ॥
ityādivāsanāvāsitaiḥ sarvamapi vikrītaṁ bhāṇḍam । kr̥cchrēṇa tatō lakṣaḥ saṁprāptaḥ, taṁ gr̥hītvā ॥73॥
yāvatprāptāstasmin purē sarasaḥ pālyāṁ bandhavastatra । bhr̥tāmbhaḥ kumbhanirbharabhārāvanatakandharā bhaginī ||74॥
dr̥ṣṭā sā taistataḥ pratyabhijñātā jhaṭiti gatvā । uttārya kumbha niśumbhatō bhūmibhāgē ॥ 75 ॥
bhūnihitamastakaiḥ praṇatā sā lajjitā ca tān dr̥ṣṭā । nayanāthusiktanētrayā jalpitaṁ tayā tata ēvam ॥ 76 ॥
kuśalaṁ mama bandhūnāṁ, atarkitaṁ yuṣmadarśanaṁ jātam । kēna vā prayōjanēnēhāgatāḥ, iti niśamya ||77||
manyubharabhr̥tavadanaistabhīṇaṁta hatamasmatkuśalatvam । jīvatāmapi yēṣāṁ bhaginī ghaṭacēṭikā jātā ॥ 78 ॥
hā hā bhagini ! sunayanē ! sahasralōkānāṁ svāminyabhavaḥ । idānōṁ dāsīva jalaṁ vahasi rē ēṣāṁ parēṣāṁ ca ॥
hī hī anāryakāryōdyatasya tava daiva ! kiyadbhaṇāmaḥ । yasyāḥ śiraḥ sukumāraṁ bhāraṁ kusumānāṁ nāsahata ॥80॥
idānīṁ jalabhr̥taghaṭān vahati tadapi hi suniṣṭhuraṁ jātam । tava daiva ! manaḥsadr̥śaṁ svacchandaprakāra durlalitam ॥

tāṇa majjhāu bhaṇiyaṁ asiyakkhabhihāṇajakkharāēṇa । ahaha ahō kō ēsō sīhaṁ suttaṁ pavōi ? ||
kō niyajī kaṁḍuyai sappatuṁḍīē kaṁḍuharaṇaṭṭā ? । kō jamapurīsamāṇē samasāṇē ēvamullavai 1 ॥ 107 ॥

gurumahatthō hatthava gahīrathaṇiyabhariyadisō । hakaṁtō vaggatō samr̥ddhiō nivaiṇō samuhaṁ ॥ 110 ॥
tō taṁ daṭṭhē rāyā ūsasiyamaṇō bhaṇēi taṁ ēvaṁ । kiṁ sāhāviyakhvaṁ uya kōvavasēṇa kayamēvaṁ ? ॥ 111 ॥
jai sāhāviyamēyaṁ rūvaṁ tā gaccha rakkha ! sahāṇē । dihaṁ jaṁ daṭṭhavvaṁ dēvā suvvaṁti ramaṇīyā ॥ 112 ॥
uya kō phuriyamēyaṁ tā kiṁ kōvaraṁsa kāraṇaṁ tumha ? | aha bhaṇasi maha masāṇē samāgaō tēṇa maha kōvō ||
taṁpi na juttaṁ jamhā samudaparaṁtadharaṇināhō hūṁ । tō savvaṁ giripurakāṇaṇāī maha saṁtiyaṁ ēyaṁ ॥ 114 ॥
ja itya nivasimaṇā tubhē tā dēha maha karaṁ ihi । annaha maha paḍibaddhaṁ bhūmi sigghaṁ paricaya ||
taṁ suṇi tē kuvidhā savvē bhūyāiṇō bhaṇatēvaṁ । bhō bhūva ! saraṇamahuṇā aṇusarasu sarēsu iṭuṁ ca ॥ 116 ॥
tō asikkhō jakkhō muggaramuggīriūṇa jā caliō । tō sō sahasā thaṁbhuvtra bhiō thaṁbhavijjāē ||
aha udviō ya bhūō accanbhuaḍāmarēhiṁ vayaṇēhiṁ । khōbhaṁtō sō rannā baddhō cōruvva maṁtē ॥ 118 ॥
tō tassa pariyaṇēṇa bhaṇiō rāyā jahā imaṁ muyaha । jaṁ kiṁpi maggasi karaṁ taṁ tuha miliūṇa dāvāmō ||
|
tō bhaṇiyaṁ bhūvaiṇā jakkhō maha aṁgarakkhaō hōu । rakkhō gharēu chattaṁ bhūyapisāyāiyā annē || 120 ||
।
maha puraō picchaṇayaṁ kuṇaṁtu niccapi iya nisāmēuṁ । savvaṁ tahanti tērhivi paḍivannaṁ viṇayapaṇaēhi ||
tō asikkhaṁ utthaṁbhiūṇa rayaṇīē carimasamayammi । niyamaṁdirammi pattō naranāhō tēhi parikaliō ।।
tāva paḍupakākāsaṁkhāitūrapūrassa | atucchō ucchaliō gahiraravō tattha, ittō ya ॥ 123 ॥
tatō'sitākṣō yakṣa uccatvēna dviyōjanapramāṇam । kr̥tvā nijaśarīraṁ kṣiptvā naramuṇḍamālāṁ ca ॥ 109॥
gurumudgaragadāhastō hastīva gabhīrastanitabhr̥tadikkaḥ । niṣēdhat valgan samutthitō nr̥patēḥ saṁmukham ॥ 110॥
tatastaṁ dr̥ṣṭvā rājōcchu sitamanā bhaṇati tamēvam । kiṁ svābhāvikarūpamuta kōpavaśēna kr̥tamēvam ? ॥ 111 ॥
yadi svābhāvikamētad rūpaṁ tadā gaccha rakṣaḥ ! svasthānē । dr̥ṣṭaṁ yad draṣṭavyaṁ dēvāḥ śrūyantē ramaṇīyāḥ ॥ 112 ॥
uta kōpasphuritamētat tadā kiṁ kōpasya kāraṇaṁ tava ? | atha bhaṇāsi mama śmaśānē samāgatastēna mama kōpaḥ ॥
tadapi na yuktaṁ yasmātsamudraparyantavara ṇināthō'ham । tataḥ sarvaṁ giripurakānanādi mama sambandhyēt ॥ 114 ॥
yadyatra nivastumanasō yūyaṁ tadā datta mama karamidānīm । anyathā mama pratibaddhāṁ bhūmiṁ śīghraṁ parityajata ||
tat śrutvā tē kupitāḥ sarvē bhūtādayō bhaṇantyēvam | bhō bhūpa । śaraṇamadhunā'nusara smarēṣṭaṁ ca ॥ 116 ॥
tatōssitākṣō yakṣō mudgaramudgarītuṁ yāvaccalitaḥ । tāvatsa sahasā stambhavatstambhitaḥ stambhavidyayā ॥ 117 ॥
athōtthitaśca bhūtō'tyadbhutaḍāmarairvacanaiḥ । kṣōbhayan sa rājñā baddhaścaura iva mantrēṇa ॥। 118॥
tatastasya parijanēna bhaṇitō rājā yathēmaṁ muñcata । yaṁ kamapi mārgayasi karēṁ taṁ tubhyaṁ militvā dāpayāmaḥ !!
tatō bhaṇitaṁ bhūpatinā yakṣō mamāṅgarakṣakō bhavatu । rakṣō dharatu cchatraṁ bhūtapiśācādikā anyē ॥ 120 ॥
mama purataḥ prēkṣaṇakaṁ kurvantu nityamapīti niśamya । sarvaṁ tathēti tairapi pratipannaṁ vinayapraṇataiḥ ॥ 121 ॥
tatō'sitākṣamuttabhya rajanyāṁ caramasamayē । nijamandirē prāptō naranāthastaiḥ parikalitaḥ ॥ 122॥
tāvatpaṭupaṭahaḍhakkābukāśaṅkhāditūryapūrasya । atuccha ucchalitō gaṁbhīraravastatra, itaśca ॥ 123॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
☐
paccūsagayavarummūliyāē uḍḍīṇasasivihaṁgāē | dhavalāī galaṁti nisālayāē nakkhattakusumāī ॥ 124॥
diṇamaṇima ūhamaṁjariyadisitrahūvayaṇakamalasōhillē । paccūsē tō rāyā vihēvi āvassayaṁ tattō ।। 125 ।
vō thā pariyariō tēhi jakkharakkhēhiṁ । vēḍavviyarūvēhiṁ paccakkha maṁsacakkhaṇaṁ ॥ 126 ॥
pāraddhaṁ picchaṇayaṁ bhūyapisāēhiṁ vivibhaṁgīhiṁ । tulacēlayakayahatthō naccai ēgō mahārakkhō || 127||
kavaṇiyavēsō tō rannā pucchiō imaṁ ēsō । kiṁ buḍḍhavaṇiyavēsēṇa naccasē kahasu phuḍamēyaṁ ? ।। 128 ।
tō rakkhēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ naccēbhi khaṇaṁ taō ya paryāḍissaṁ । niyacariyē uccariḍaṁ savisēsaṁ niyayajīhāē ।
tō pikkhaṇāvasāṇē jīhaṁ nillāliūṇa aidīhaṁ । khaṇamēgaṁ gayacēṭṭō ṭhiō taō jaṁpaē ēvaṁ || 130॥
bhō naranāha ! nisāmasu jēṇaṁ ēvaṁ ahaṁ paṇañcāmi । tō kahai jahā rasaṇādōsēṇaṁ puvammammi ।। 131 |
laddhr̥ṇavi jiṇadhammaṁ maṇuyattaṁ hāriyati, tō rāyā । pucchara kahaṁti, tō sō puvvabhavaṁ sāhium̐ laggō ||
iha āsi purā siṭṭī īsaranāmā pasiddhaguṇaka liō । tabbhajjā baṁdhumaī tāṇa suō sulasanāmōti
aha jōvvaṇammi pattēṇa tēṇa sicchāē paribhamaṁtēṇa । katthavi diṭṭhō sāhū bāvīsa parīsaha sahōti ॥ 134
taṁ vaṁdiūṇa sāhuṁ nisuṇai sadēsaṇaṁ maṇabhirāmaṁ । puvvāgayaparisāē kahamāṇaṁ kahapabaṁdhēṇa ॥ 135 ॥
rāībhōpaṇaviraīguṇadōsāviyāraṇaṁ ca putrvr̥ttaṁ । suṇiuṁ tēṇavi gahiyā viraī rayaṇīē bhattassa || 136 ||
bhaddagabhāvagaēṇaṁ na uṇō sammattamāigihidhammō । tapiuṇā upavannō sammattāīvi gihidhammō || 137
puttagavēsaṇahēuṁ samāgaṇaṁ muṇissa pāsamma । taṁ namivi siṁhaṁ pattā jagahiyavayāī pālētā || 138 ।।
pratyūṣagajavêrōnmūlitāyā uḍḍīnaśaśivihaṅgāyāḥ । dhavalāni galanti niśālatāyā nakṣatra kusumāni ॥ 124 ॥
dinamaṇimayūkha mañjaritadigvadhūvadanakamalaśōbhāvati । pratyūṣē tatō rājā vidhāyāvaśyakaṁ tataḥ ॥ 125 ॥
upaviṣṭa āsthānē parikaritastairya sarakṣōbhiḥ । vikūrvitarūpaiḥ pratyakṣaṁ māṁsacakṣuṣām ॥ 126॥
prārabdhaṁ prēkṣaṇakaṁ bhūtapiśācairvividhamaṅgibhiḥ । tūlacēla kakr̥tahastaṁ nr̥tyatyēkaṁ mahārakṣaḥ ॥ 127 ॥
kr̥tavr̥ddhavaṇigvēṣastatō rājñā pr̥ṣṭa idamēṣaḥ । kiṁ vr̥ddhavaṇigvēṣēṇa nr̥tyasi kathaya sphuṭamētat 1 ॥ 128 ॥
tatō rakṣasā bhaṇitaṁ nr̥tyāmi kṣaṇaṁ tataśca prakaṭayiṣyāmi । nijacaritamuccārya saviśēṣaṁ nijajiyā ॥ 129
tataḥ prēkṣaṇāvasānē jilhnāṁ nirlālyātidīrghām | kṣaṇamēkaṁ gatacēṣṭaḥ sthitastatō jalpatyēvam || 130 ।।
।
bhō naranātha ! niśamaya yēnaivamahaṁ pranr̥tyāmi । tataḥ kathayati yathā rasanādōṣēṇa pūrvajanmani ॥ 131 ॥
labdhvāpi jinadharmaṁ manujatvaṁ hāritamiti, tatō rājā । pr̥cchati kathamiti, tataḥ sa pūrvabhavaṁ kathayituṁ lagnaḥ
ihāmītpurā śrēṣṭhīśvaranāmā prasiddhaguṇakalitaḥ । tadbhāryā bandhumatī tayōḥ sutaḥ sulasanāmēti ॥ 133
atha yauvanaṁ prāptēna tēna svēcchayā paribhramatā । kutrāpi dr̥ṣṭaḥ sādhurdvāviṁśatiparapihasaha iti ॥ 134 ॥
vanditvā sādhuṁ śr̥ṇōti saddēśanāṁ manōbhirāmām । pūrvāgata pariṣadi kathyamānāṁ kathāprabandhēna ॥ 135 ॥
rātribhōjanaviratiguṇadōṣavicāraṇaṁ ca pūrvōktam । śrutvā tēnāpi gr̥hītā viratī rajanyāṁ bhaktasya ॥ 136॥
bhadrakabhāvagatēna na punaḥ samyavattvādigr̥hidharmaḥ । tatpitrā tu prapannaḥ samyaktvādirapi gr̥hidharmaḥ ॥ 137 ॥

dattakahā ।
465
citi sayāvi maṇicchiyāī sukkhāī aṇuhavaṁtā ya । aha annadiṇē mulasō mittaṇa samaṁ nisīhammi ||
viḍacariyāē caraṁtō caccaraca uhahr̥ṭiṭasālāsu । tō mittēṇaṁ tēṇaṁ āṇēuṁ maṁḍayāīyaṁ ॥ 140 ॥
bhaṇiō sulō bhuṁja maṁḍayaiḍariyaghōlavaṭayāī । sō āha ajuttamiṇaṁ nō kappai syaṇibhattaṁ mē ॥
jamhā sugurusamī gahiō niyamō nisāra bhuktavvē । tā mā bhaṇēsu baṁdhava ! itthatthē majjha tē savahō ||
ulluṁṭhēṇaṁ tēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ rayaṇīē bhuṁjamāṇāṇaṁ । kiṁ kavalō kannatō pavisai, nō vayaṇakuhara smi ? ||
dīvaya ujjōēṇaṁ sunirikkhēūṇa mōyagāīyaṁ । kuṁthupipīliyarahiyē jai bhujjai tattha kō dōsō ? |
hā vaṁciō si baṁdhava ! ittiyakālaṁ visuddhabhujjassa | jamhā rayaṇībhattaṁ kāmakaraṁ hōṛa kāmīṇa |
tā ajja tāva bhuṁjasu maha uvarōhā vilāsiṇīhiṁ samaṁ । pacchā jaṁ tē ruccai taṁ kāyavvaṁ viyārē ॥ 146 ॥
iya bhaṇiē sē vayaṇē mōya khaṁḍaṁ balāvi pakkhittaṁ । tassanniyavēsāē sēsaṁ savvaṁ sayaṁ bhōttaṁ ॥ 147॥
tō paidipi bhuṁjai rayaṇīē mittaviṁda saṁjuttō । haṭṭapa hē vañcatō khapparakayamaṁḍayāīyaṁ ॥ 148 ॥
puddhi sustarabīhiṁ gāyamāṇīhi naccamāṇīhi । vilasai vilāsiṇīsatyaparigaō jāva paccasaṁ ॥ 149 ॥
tatō vēsāṇa gihē maṭhamaṁḍavadēulēsu vā suyai । jāva dinaddhaṁ tō uhiūṇa gacchēi piugēhē ॥ 150 ॥
tō piuṇā sō nāō bhaṇiō rē rayaṇibhattaniyamōvi । bhaggō nivbhagga ! tara hā hā hā hāriō jammō ॥
varamarigihētu kammaṁ vara maraṇaṁ suhaḍasarapahārēhiṁ । ullasiyabahalajālōlijaḍilē jalaṇē pavēsō vā ।। 152
putragavēṣaṇahētōḥ samāgatēna munēḥ pārśvē । taṁ natvā gr̥haṁ prāptau yathāgr̥hītavratāni pālayantau ॥ 138 ॥
tiṣṭhataḥ sadāpi manaīpsitāni saukhyānyanubhavantau ca । athānyadinē sulasō mittrēṇa samaṁ niśīthē ॥ 139 ॥
viṭacaryayā caraṁścatvaracaturhadr̥dyūtaśālāsu । tatō mittrēṇa tēnānīya maṇḍakādikam ॥ 140 ॥
bhaṇitaḥ sulasō bhuṅkṣva maṇḍakēḍarikā ghōlavaṭakādīn । sa āhāyuktamidaṁ nō kalpatē rajanibhaktaṁ mē ॥ 141 ॥
yasmād gurusamīpē gr̥hītō niyamō niśāyāṁ bhōktavyē । tasmānmā bhaṇa bāndhava ! atrārtha mama tē śapathaḥ ॥
ulluṇṭhēna tēna bhaṇitaṁ rajanyāṁ bhuñjānānām । kiṁ kavalaḥ karṇāntaḥ praviśati, nō vardana kuharē ? || 143 ||
dīpakō dyōtēna sunirīkṣya mōdakādikam । kunthupipīlikārahitaṁ yadi bhujyatē tatra kō dōṣaḥ ? ॥ 144 ॥
hā vañcitō'si bāndhava ! iyatkālaṁ viśuddhabhōjyāt । yasmādrajanibhaktaṁ kāmakaraṁ bhavati kāminām ॥145॥
tasmādadya tāvad bhuṅkṣva mamōparōdhād vilāsinībhiḥ samam । paścād yattē rōcatē tatkartavyaṁ vicārya ॥ 146 ॥
iti bhaṇitē tasya vadanē mōdakakhaṇḍaṁ balādapi prakṣiptam । tatsaṁjñitavēśyayā śēṣaṁ sarva svayaṁ bhuktam ॥ 147॥
tataḥ pratidinamapi bhuṅgē rajanyāṁ mittravr̥ndasaṁyuktaḥ । hr̥ṭṭapayē vrajan karparakr̥tamaṇḍakādikam ॥ 148 ॥
pr̥ṣṭhē susvaraśvapacībhirgāyantībhirnr̥tyantībhiḥ । vilasati vilāsinīsārthaparigatō yāvatpratyūṣam ॥ 149 ॥
tatō vēśyānāṁ gr̥hē maṭhamaṇḍapadēvakulēṣu vā svapitiṁ । yāvad dinārdhaṁ tata utthāya gacchati pitr̥gēhē ॥ 150 ॥
tataḥ pitrā sa jñātō bhaṇitō rē rajanibhakta niyamō'pi । bhagnō nirbhāgya ! tvayā hā hā hā hāritaṁ janma ॥
caramarigr̥hēṣu karma varaṁ maraṇaṁ subhaṭaśaraprahārai: । ullasitabahalajvālālijaṭilē jvalanē pravēśō vā ॥ 152 ॥

supāsanāha-cariammi--
tahavi na vayavigyakaraṁ rāīē bhuṁjiuṁ havai juttaṁ । vaccha ! apatthaṁ ēyaṁ pacchāyāvaṁ bahuṁ jaṇihī ||15|| 3
tō tēṇa imaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ jayaṁpi bhuṁjēi tāva rayaṇīē । mōttuṁ sāvayalōyaṁ tā tammaragamma haṁ bhaggō || 154 ||
nava kiṁcivi bhaṇiyavvaṁ tara mamaṁ paiimammi visayammi । jō jēttiyasma jōggō sō lahai tattiyaṁ atthaṁ।
ranīriō taō sō piuṇā hirivajjiō ya rayaṇīē । bhuṁjēi gihē viḍaviṁdaparigaō bhamai sacchaṁdaṁ ।
sāvayavasumittēṇaṁ aha annayā saha gaō vivāhammi | bālēmittōtti sō maha pattō rayaṇī gāmammi ||
vāhiṇa bhaṇiyaṁ kittiyalōyassa bhōyaṇaṁ paḍaṇaṁ । kuṇimō tēhivi kahiyaṁ na kōvi amhaccaō rāō ।
bhuṁjissara, tō bhaṇiyaṁ sulasēṇa ahaṁ tu bhuṁjaissāmi । pauṇaṁ karēha krūraṁ sasakaraṁ pāyasaṁ ca tahā ।। 159 /
tēhivi tahatti vihiyaṁ navaraṁ khīrē kaḍhijjamāṇammi | bahudhūmavihuriyaṁgō paḍiō nāgō tahiṁ ēgō ॥ 160 ।
aiusitāvataviōvilīṇagattō khayaṁ gaō tattha । tassa parivēsiyaṁ taṁ sasakkaraṁ pāumaṇulaggō । । 161।
paḍhamaghuṭammi khaliyā jīhā hatthāu nivaḍiyaṁ vahaṁ । vilaṁbalō ya jāō paḍiō tatthēva ṭhāṇammi |
dhāhāviyaṁ ca parivēsiyāē miliō ya tattha bahulōō । mittēṇa samaṁ pattō jannattāē ya paurajaṇō ||
dīvajjōyaṁ kāuṁ jōijjai jāva thāliyā jīē । duddhaṁ ciṭṭha kaḍhiyē tō ahiṇō khaṁḍa khaṁḍāī || 164 ||
dīsaṁti susinnāī, tammittēṇaṁ sasaṁbhramaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ । āṇaha maṇiṇō taha taṁtavāiṇō paramāruḍiyā || 165 |
tēhiṁvi tahatti vihiyaṁ ōhaliuṁ maṇigaṇaṁpi nīrēṇa । chaḍachaḍachaḍatti chaṁṭē sō taō savaṇanayaṇēsu ॥
tathāpi na vratavighnakaraṁ rātrau bhōktuṁ bhavati yuktam । vatsa ! apathyamētatpaścāttāpaṁ bahuṁ janayiṣyati || 153 |
tatastēnēdaṁ bhaṇitaṁ jagadapi bhuṅgē tāvad rajanyām । muktvā śrāvakalōkaṁ tasmāttanmārgē'haṁ bhagnaḥ ॥ 154॥
na ca kiñcidapi bhaṇitavyaṁ tvayā māṁ pratyāsmin viṣayē । yō yāvatō yōgyaḥ sa labhatē tāvantamartham ॥155॥
avadhīritastataḥ sa pitrā hrīvarjitaśca rajanyām । bhuṅgē gr̥hē viṭavr̥ndaparigatō bhramati svacchandam ॥196॥
śrāvakavasumittrēṇāthānyadā saha gatō vivāhē । bālamittramiti sa mama, prāptō rajanyāṁ grāmē ॥157॥
vaivāhikēna bhaṇitaṁ kiyallōkasya bhōjanaṁ praguṇam । kurmastairapi kathitaṁ na kō'pyasmadīyō rātrau ॥ 158 ॥
bhōkṣyatē, tatō bhaṇitaṁ sulasēnāhaṁ tu bhōkṣyē । praguṇaṁ kuruta kūraṁ saśarkaraṁ pāyasaṁ ca tathā ॥ 159 ॥
tairapi tathēti cihnitaṁ kintu kṣīrē kvathyamānē । bahudhūmavidhuritāṅgaḥ patitō nāgastatraikaḥ ॥ 160॥
atyuṣṇatāpataptō vilanigātraḥ kṣayaṁ gatastatra । tasya parivēṣitaṁ tatsaśarkaraṁ pātumanulagnaḥ ॥ 169॥
prathamapabhanē skhalitā jihvā hastānnipatitaṁ pātram । vihvalāṅgaśca jātaḥ patitastatraiva sthānē || 162 ॥
āraṭitaṁ ca parivēṣikayā militaśca tatra bahulōkaḥ । mittrēṇa samaṁ prāptō janatāyāśca pracurajanaḥ ॥ 163॥
dīpōyataṁ kr̥tvā dr̥śyatē yāvatsthālikā yasyām । dugdhaṁ tiṣṭhati kvathitaṁ tatō'hē : khaṇḍakhaṇḍāni ॥ 164 ।
dr̥śyantē suśīrṇāni, tanmittrēṇa sasaṁbhramaṁ bhaṇitam । ānayata maṇīstathā tantravādinaḥ pravaragāruḍakān ॥
tairapi tathēti vihitamabaghr̥ñya maṇigaṇamapi nīrēṇa । chaṅachaṅachaṅētyukṣati sa tataḥ śravaṇanayanēṣu ॥ 166 ॥
1 kha. ga. lavayaṁsō sō ।

ujaṁti ya gāruḍiyā taṁtāī pauṁjayaṁti jattēṇa । naya kōvi guṇō jāō picchaṁtāṇaṁ maō sahasā ||
tō sēmitta hā hā hā mitta ! mē nisiddhōvi । giddhō rayaṇībhattē na ṭhiō taṁ bhuṁjiuṁ laggō ||
tassa sumaḍḍhassa suō hōuṁ gurudinna niyamakayabhaṁgō । hā hāriyanarajammō ēmētra maō si rasa giddhōṁ ॥।
iccāi palavamāṇō mittō tahadāhamāyarai | caiūṇaṁ pariṇayaṇaṁ puṇō niyattō siṁha pattō ॥ 170 ॥
sō ddaṁ tassa kumittō mariūṇaṁ rakkhasō samppannō । vasumittaṁ niyamittaṁ daddhuṁ bhaṁḍāriyaṁ tumha || 171 ||
punvabhavanē havasaō vibhaṁganāṇēṇa attaṇō cariyaṁ । jāṇēuṁ tē kahiyaṁ saṁpara maha dēha āēsaṁ ॥ 172 ॥
taṁ sōuṁ naravaṇā vasumittō pucchiō jahā saca । jaṁ kahai imō ēyaṁ, sō bhaṇai dēva ! ēvamimaṁ ॥ 173 ॥
tō jakrakhasāī visajjiyā naravarēṇa bhīēṇa । rāībhōyaṇaviraī gahiyā taccariyamaṇusōuṁ ॥ 174॥
tā datta ! tumaṁ rayaṇīē bhōgaṇapi hu caijja sāvajjaṁ । lōiyasirddhatē suvi nisiddhamēyaṁ jaō bhaṇiyaṁ ||
nētrāhuī navā nhāṇaṁ na saddhaṁ dēvayaccaṇaṁ । dāṇaṁ vā vihiyaṁ rāō bhōyaṇaṁ tu visēsaō || 176 ||
tathā ca smr̥ti:-
1
“ divasasyāṣṭamē bhāgē mandībhūtē divākarē । naktaṁ taddhi vijānīyād na naktaṁ niśi bhōjanam ॥
divasaṁ pakṣaṁ māsaṁ cāturmāsyāyanaṁ ca abdaṁ ca । yastu na bhuṅktē rātrau kr̥tapuṇyaḥ sō'pi kr̥ṣṇamatē ||
nōdakamapi pātavyaṁ rātrāvatra yudhiṣṭhira ! | tapasvinā viśēṣēṇa gr̥hiṇāpi vivēkinā ||
sūtrōditēna vidhinā kr̥tvā rātryaśanavarjanaṁ prayataḥ । yadi mriyatē hi manuṣyō anaśanaphalamēvamāpnōti ॥
jātyakāñcanavarṇābhā udyadravisamaprabhāḥ । vaimānikāḥ prajāyantē rātrībhōjanavarjanāt ॥ "
jē uṇa gahiūṇa vayaṁ imaṁ virāhiṁti sāiyāraṁ vā । kuvvaṁti hutiṁ kivvisiya surayaṇā kicchavōhīyā ॥ 177॥
iya muṇiuṁ dattēṇaṁ rāībhattassa viramaṇaṁ vihiyaṁ । tamhā susāvaraṇaṁ bhōgaṇaō rāibhattaṁpi ॥ 178 ॥
yuñjanti ya gāruḍikāstantrāṇi prayuñjatē yatnēna । na ca kō'pi guṇō jātaḥ paśyatāṁ mr̥taḥ sahasā || 167॥
tatō vilapati tasya mittraṁ hā hā hā mitra ! mē niṣiddhō'pi । gr̥ddhō rajanibhaktē na sthitastvaṁ bhōktuṁ lagnaḥ ॥
tasya suśrāddhasya sutō bhūtvā kr̥tagurudattaniyamabhaṅgaḥ । hā hāritanarajanmaivamēva mr̥tō'si rasagr̥ddhaḥ ॥ 169॥
ityādi pralapad mitraṁ tadahadāhamācarati । tyaktvā pariṇayanaṁ punarnivr̥ttō gr̥haṁ prāptaḥ ॥ 170 ॥
sō'haṁ tasya kumitvaṁ mr̥tvā rākṣasaḥ samutpannaḥ । vasumittraṁ nijamittraṁ dr̥ṣṭvā bhāṇḍāgārikaṁ tava ॥ 171 ॥
pūrvabhavasnēhavaśatō vibhaṅgajñānēnātmanaścaritam । jñātvā tē kathitaṁ saṁprati mama dattā dēśam ॥ 172॥
tat śrutvā narapatinā vasumittraḥ pr̥ṣṭō yathā satyam । yatkathayatyayamētat sa bhaṇati dēva ! ēvamidam ॥
tatō yakṣarākṣasādayō visarjitā naravarēṇa bhītēna । rātribhōjanaviratirgr̥hītā taccaritamanuśrutya ॥174॥
tasmāddatta ! tvaṁ rajanyāṁ bhōjanamapi hi tyaja sāvadyam । laukikasiddhāntēṣvapi niṣiddhamētad yatō bhaṇitam ॥
naivāhutirnavā snānaṁ na śrāddhaṁ dēvatārcanam । dānaṁ vā vihitaṁ rātrau bhōjanaṁ tu viśēṣataḥ ॥ 176 ॥
yē punagr̥hītvā vratamidaṁ virādhayanti sāticāraṁ vā । kurvanti bhavanti kilvidhikasurajanāḥ kr̥cchrabōdhikāḥ ॥

naṁdaṇavaṇaṁ va sumaṇōvabhāsiyaṁ bahuvilāsa sōhillaṁ । suvisālasālakaliyē kusatthalaṁ asthi iha nayaraṁ ॥
tatthavi ya pavarasiṭṭī kuvalayacaṁdōtti kuvalayāṇaṁdō | āṇaṁdasirī bhajjā tāṇa suyā vimalasahadēva || 4 ||
paḍhamō guṇanilaō tavvivarīō ya baṁdhavō lahuō । tahavi ya avarōpparaō tāṇaṁ buḍhi gayā pīī ||5||
samagaṁ ramaṁti samagaṁ padaṁti samagaṁ kuṇaṁti vāṇijjaṁ । aha rahamāruhiūṇaṁ pattā tē kāṇaṇē tattha || 6 ||
kusumaphalāṇucciṇaṇaṁ kuṇaṁti jā tāva cūyatarumūlē । sirinaṁdaṇaṁva raivirahakarisiyaṁ tē niyaṁti muṇi ॥ 7 ॥
taṁda miṇā namēti taccaraṇapaṁkayaṁ payaō । tēṇavi jhāṇasamattīē bhāsiō dhammalābhōti ॥8॥
pāraddhā dhammakā muṇiṇā jā tāṇa samuciyā jamhā । muggarasajuggayāṇaṁ ahiucciya mōyagāhārō ॥ 9 ॥
tathāhi ;-
dhammō dayāpahāṇō dēvō dōnavagadōsaparihīṇō । tattakusalō ya sugurū sivamaggō rayaṇatiya miṇamō ॥ 10 ॥
savvatthavi niṇijjai jaṇēṇa nāmakkharāī dhammōtti । tāṇa puṇō paramatthaṁ sakayatthō kōvi parikalas ||
savrvvapi sattaggaṁ duggaipurapatthiyaṁ dharai jamhā | suhaṭhāṇammi ya taha dhāraē ya dhammō taō bhaṇiō || 12 ||
saggāpavaggapabhavāṇa paramasōkkhāṇa kāraṇaṁ pauṇaṁ | jīvāṇa samāyaraṇaṁ jaṁ taṁ dhammaṁ bhaṇati buhā || 13 ||
taṁ samayabhēyabhinnaṁ bhaṇati bahubhaṁgiyāhi daṁsaṇiṇō । puvtrāvarāviruddhō suhamaiṇā sa puṇa gahiyō || 14 ||
śastrāgnimuśalavastūnāṁ dāpanaṁ vitaraṇaṁ ca yadanarthārtham । tadanarthadaṇḍanāma guṇatrataṁ tr̥tīyamiha bhaṇitam ॥1॥
yō jinavacanaprasaktaḥ pālayatyaticāravarjitamētat । sa svargamōkṣasaukhyāni prāpnōti vimalaśrāddha iva ॥ 2 ॥
nandanavanamiva sumanō'vabhāsitaṁ bahuvilāsaśōbhāvat । suviśālaśālakalitaṁ kuśasthalamastīha nagaram ॥3॥
tatrāpi ca pravaraśrēṣṭhī kuvalayacandra iti kuvalayānandaḥ । ānandaśrīrbhāryā tayōḥ sutau vimalasahadēva ||4||
prathamō guṇanilayastadviparītaśca bāndhavō laghuḥ । tathāpi ca parasparatastayōrvr̥ddhiṁ gatāṁ prītiḥ ॥5॥
sabha ramētē samaṁ paṭhataḥ samaṁ kurutō vāṇijyam । atha rathamāruhya prāptau tau kānanē tatra ॥6॥
kusumaphalānāmuccayanaṁ kurutō yāvattāvacūtatarumūlē । śrīnandanamiva rativirahakarṣitaṁ tau paśyatō munim ||7||
dr̥ṣṭvā hr̥ṣṭamanasau namatastaccaraṇapaṅkajaṁ padataḥ । tēnāpi dhyānasamāptyā bhāṣitō dharmalābha iti ॥8॥
prārabdhā dharmakathā muninā yāvattayōḥ samucitā yasmāt । mudgarasayōgyānāmahita ēva mōdakāhāraḥ ॥ 9 ॥
dharmōdayāpradhāna dēvō dvinavakadōṣaparihīṇaḥ । tattvakuśalaśca suguruḥ śivamārgē ratnatrikamidam ॥ 10 ॥
sarvatrāpi śrūyatē janēna nāmākṣarāṇi dharma iti । tēṣāṁ punaḥ paramārthaṁ svakr̥tārthaḥ kō'pi parikalayati ॥ 11 ॥
sarvamapi sattvavarga durgatipuraprasthitaṁ dharati yasmāt । śubhasthānē ca tathā dhārayati ca dharmastatō bhaṇitaḥ ॥ 12 ॥
svargāpavargaprabhavāṇāṁ paramasaukhyānāṁ kāraṇaṁ praguṇam । jīvānāṁ samācaraṇaṁ yattaṁ dharmaṁ bhaṇanti budhāḥ ॥ 13 ॥

aṭṭajjhāṇaṁ vajrjjati taha ya majjā paṇavihapamāyaṁ । appaṁti na taha satyaṁ sāvajjaṁ nōva saṁti ||26||
vimala vimalasahāvō sahavō puṇa sahāvaō cavalō | dhammē pamāyabahulō sayāvi kēlī kilattaṇaō ||

1
taṁ samayabhēdabhinnaṁ bhaṇanti bahubhaṅgibhirdērśaninaḥ । pūrvāparāviruddhaḥ śubhamatinā sa punargrahītavyaḥ ॥ 14 ॥
vividhapathēṣu puruṣō gr̥hṇāti puraprāpakaṁ yathā supatham । kuśalaḥ śivapurahētuṁ bahuṣu dharmēṣu tathā dharmam ॥ 19 ॥
yathā mugdhamr̥gō mr̥gatr̥ṣṇikāyāṁ tr̥ṣitaḥ karōti jalabuddhim । tathā nirvivēkapuruṣaḥ karōtyadharmē'pi dharmabuddhim ॥
yaḥ punarvivēkāñjanagatatamōnayanō narō bhavati samyak । pūrvāparaparyālōcanēna sa gr̥hṇāti dharmam ॥ 17 ॥
yathā jīvavarjitānāṁ jīvānāṁ na kāryasādhakō dēhaḥ । saṁpadyatē tathā dharmaḥ karuṇayā parayā parihīṇaḥ || 18 ||
sā punarjinadharma ēva, iti jñātvā tamēvācarata । tathaiva svarūpamidaṁ kathyamānaṁ niśamayata ॥ 19 ॥
rāgadvēṣasamudbhavasamagrabhavadōṣasaṁgamavimuktaḥ । sa bhavati dēvadēvaścatustriśadatiśayasaṁpannaḥ || 20 ||
gauravatrikē vimukhastriguptiguptō jitēndriyō'mamaḥ । vidhivihitavihārakramō gītārthastathāca madhyasthaḥ ॥21॥
ityēvamādinirmalaguṇagrāmavibhūṣitō mahāsattvaḥ । bhavati sugururgariṣṭhō bhavajalanidhitāraṇataraṇḍaḥ ॥ 22 ॥
iti munivacanaṁ śrutvā ratnatrikaṁ pariṇataṁ manasi tayōḥ । duṣkarmavigama nirmita vimalapariṇamayuktayōḥ ॥ 23॥
tataḥ samyaktvādirgr̥hītō gharmō dvādaśavidhō'pi । asamarthābhyāṁ tābhyāṁ durdharayatidharmadhurādharaṇē ||24||
saviśēṣaṁ tr̥tīyaguṇatrataṁ tu tatpr̥ṣṭaḥ kathayati sūriḥ । caturbhēdamapi tatastau jñātvā prāptau svagēhē ॥ 25 ॥
ārtadhyānaṁ varjayatastathā ca madyādipañcavidhapramādam । arpayatō na tathā śastraṁ sāvadyaṁ nōpadiśataḥ ॥ 26 ॥
vimalō vimalasvabhāvaḥ sahadēvaḥ punaḥ svabhāvataścapalaḥ । dharmē pramāda bahulaḥ sadāpi kēlikilatvataḥ ||27||
tāvanyadā ca gr̥hītvā pravarabhāṇḍāni pūrvadēśē । saṁcalitau tataḥ pr̥ṣṭaḥ kēnāpi pathikēnārdhapathē ॥ 28 ॥

vimalō paṁjalamaggaṁ nīriṇanīraṇāisaṁjuttaṁ । vimalēṇa vimalamaiṇā tō bhaṇiyamahaṁ na yāṇāmi ॥ 29 ॥
pahiraṇa puṇō bhaṇiyaṁ tunbhēhiṁ siṭṭi । kammi nayarampi | gaṁtavvaṁ, sō sāhai paṇiyaṁ agvissaē jattha ||
pahiēṇa puṇō puḍhaṁ niyanayaraṁ kahaha maha jahiṁ vasasi । sō bhai rāyahāṇīē natthi maha saṁtiyaṁ nagaraṁ ॥
tō bhaṇiyaṁ pahiēṇaṁ api samarga samāgamissāmi । tō vimalēśaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ kiṁ bhaṇimō vayamiya vayaṁtā ||32||

hu
1
"na grāhmāṇi na dēyāni pañca dravyāṇi paṇḍitaiḥ । agnirviṣaṁ tathā śastraṁ madyaṁ māṁsaṁ ca pañcamam ॥”
tō kuviōn sa jaṁpa taṁ para rēmiṭa ! | kiṁ kubvaṁtō kūttarāī taṁ maha purō yuddha ! || 36 ||
nō lajjasi na nivijjasi iya maṇium̐ sō paḍium̐ laggō | taha jaha bhīyaṁ piva tasta kiṁcicaṁ gayē gayaṇaṁ ।
taṁ savvē hā tō vimalamālavai pahiō । yō appara maha jalaṇaṁ jaṛa kajjē tuha jīēṇa ||38||
jēṇittha maṇuyamaṁsaṁ pa jēṁmi mukkhiō vāḍhaṁ । bimalō bhaṇēi jaṁ tuha paḍihāi karēsu taṁ jamhā ||39||
jāēṇa jīvalōē mariyavvaṁ tāva nicchaō ēsa । niyamammi putra viṇḍē dhammaviṇāsō dhuvaṁ hōi ||40||
tammi viḍiāī huti dukkhāī bhavasahassēsu । niyamasahiyassa maraṇē maṇayaṁpi havēi nahu dukkha || 41 ||
tō jaṁ jaraṇasu taṁ kuṇasu na uṇa bhaṁga karēmi niyamassa । tō saṁhariya tanuṁ sō suraruvaṁ kāumāha tayaṁ ॥ 42 ॥ -

vimalaḥ prāñjalamārga nīrēndhananīraṇādisaṁyuktam । vimalēna vimalamatinā tatō bhaṇitamahaṁ na jānāmi ॥ 29 ॥
pathikēna punarbhaṇitaṁ yuṣmābhiḥ śrēṣṭhin ! kasminnagarē | gantavyaṁ, sa kathayati paṇyamardhiṣyatē yatra ॥ 30 ॥
pathikēna punaḥ pr̥ṣṭaṁ nijanagaraṁ kathayata mama yatra vamasi । sa bhaṇati rājadhānyāṁ nāsti mama saṁbandhi nagaram ॥
tatō bhaṇitaṁ pathikēnāhamapi samaṁ samāgamiṣyāmi । tatō vinalēna bhaṇitaṁ kiṁ bhaṇāmō varyamiti vrajantaḥ ||32||
prāptāḥ purād bahistatra cāvāsitā malayamadhyē | dhānyasya pacanārthamagniḥ saṁdīpitō yāvat ॥ 33 ॥
padātibhiḥ kairapi jalamapi kilānītaṁ tataḥ pathikaḥ । vimalaṁ mārgayatyagnisa tēna tata idaṁ bhaṇitaḥ ||34||
pathika ! ayi mama pārśvē bhuṅkṣva nō kalpatē jvalanadānam । jvalanādidānāni yēnaṁ niṣiddhāni samayē ||35||
tataḥ kupita iva sa jalpati taṁ prati rē ghr̥ṣṭa duṣṭadharmiṣṭha ! । kiṁ kurvan kūṭōttarāṇi tvaṁ mama purō mugdha ! ॥ 36 ॥
nō lajjasē na nirvidham̐sa iti bhaṇitvā sa pravardhituṁ lagnaḥ । tathā yathā bhītamiva tasmātkiñciducaṁ gataṁ gaganam ॥
tad dr̥ṣṭvā sarvē'pi hi naṣṭā tatō vimalamālapati pathikaḥ । bhō arpayata mama jvalanaṁ yadi kārya tava jōvitēna ॥
yēnātra manujamāṁsaṁ paktvā bhuñjīya bubhukṣitō bāḍham । vimalō bhaṇati yattava pratibhāti kuruṣva tadyasmāt ॥ 39 ॥
jātēna jīvalōkē martavyaṁ tāvad niścaya ēṣaḥ । niyamē punarvinaṣṭē dharmavināśō dhruvaṁ bhavati ॥ 40 ॥
tasmin vinaṣṭē'niṣṭāni bhavanti duḥkhāni bhavasahasra । niyamasahitasya garaṇē manāgapi bhavati nahi duḥkham 41

supāsanāhacariammi-
dhannō si tumaṁ sāvaya ! tujjha suladdhaṁ ca māṇusa jammaṁ । jō dhuvvasi surapahuṇā surāṇa majjhami ēvamahō ||
dēvō va dāṇavō vā naya sakkō kōvi khōbhiuṁ bharahē । vimalaṁ saḍḍhaṁ gāḍhaṁ tajhyāu guṇavvayāhitō || 44 ॥
taṁ sōuṁ asahaṁtō samāgaō tujjha khōhaṇanimittaṁ । sāvajjavayaṇamaggēvi nō gaō taṁ ca puṭṭhōvi ॥45॥
tō tuṭṭhō haṁ maggasu maṇassa jaṁ kiṁci tujjha paḍihāi| tō vimalēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ savvaṁ ciya mē taē dinnaṁ ॥ 46 ॥
niyadēhaṁ payatēṇa niyamakasavaṭṭayaṁ vahatēṇaṁ । tahavi imaṁ patthijjasi dhammammi samujjamaṁ kuṇaṣu ||47 ||
kiñca ।
sarpati tavamaṇēgē jayaṁti maṁtē tahā suvijjāō । viyaraṁti daṁsaṇaṁ puṇa dēvā kē siṁci viralāṇa || 48 ॥
mō dēvō bhai tumaṁ jaivi nirīhō tahāvi maṇimēgaṁ । pasiūṇa imaṁ giṇhasu sappavisukchēyaṇapavīṇaṁ ॥
tō'ṇicchaṁtassavi tassa uttarīyampi baṁdhiūṇa maṇi । saggaṁ gaō surō sō sāhai savvaṁ suridassa || 50 ॥
vimalōvi kuṇai saddaṁ sahadēvāīṇa tēvi taṁ suṇiuṁ । saṁpattā tappāsē pucchaṁti ya pahiyavr̥ttaṁ ॥ 51 ॥
sōcihu sāha savvaṁ savittharaṁ tāṇa harisiyā savvē । tō baṁdaṁti jiṇidē tatthēva ṭhiyā sumattī || 52 ||
avalōyaṇaṁ muṇīṇaṁ kāuṁ bhujaṁti pariyaṇasamēyā । bhuttattarammi puraparisarāō majjhammi saṁcaliyā || 53 ||
pattā nayara duvārē suṇaṁti hasu khaḍahaḍārāvaṁ । uttālatālayāṇaṁ vaṇiēhiṁ dijjamāṇāṇaṁ ॥ 54 ॥
pēkkhati ya pakkhariē turaṁgamē suhaḍasōhiyara hē ya । taha guḍiyagayaghaḍāō iō taō paribhramaṁtīō ||
taha talavaraṁ ca sannahiyasaha sahiyaṁ bhamatamittō ya | vimalēṇaṁ kōvi narō puṭṭhō bhō kahasu kahamitya ।। 56 ।
tatō yajjānīyāstat kuryā na punarbhaṅgaṁ karōmi niyamasya । tataḥ saṁhr̥tya tanuṁ sa surarūpaṁ kr̥tvā''ha tam ॥ 42 ॥
dhanyō'si tvaṁ śrāvaka ! tava sulabdhaṁ ca mānuṣaṁ janma । yaḥ stūyasē suraprabhuṇā surāṇāṁ madhya ēvamahō॥ 43 ॥
dēvō vā dānavō vā naca śaktaḥ kō'pi kṣōbhayituṁ bharatē । vimalaṁ śrāddhaṁ gāḍhaṁ tr̥tīyād guṇavatāt ॥44॥
tat śrutvā'śradadhat samāgatastava kṣōbhaṇanimittam । sāvadyavacanamārgē'pi nō gatastvaṁ ca pr̥ṣṭō'pi ॥ 45 ॥
tatastuṣṭō'haṁ mārgaya manasō yatkiñcittava pratibhāti । tatō vimalēna bhaṇitaṁ sarvamēva mē tvayā dattam ||46 ॥
nijadēhaṁ prakaṭayatā niyamakaṣapaṭṭē vahatā । tathāpīdaṁ prārthya sē dharmē samudyamaṁ kuru ॥ 47 ॥
tapyantē tapō'nēkē japanti mantrāṁstathā suvidyāḥ । vitaranti darśanaṁ punardēvāḥ kēṣāṁcidviralānām ॥ 48 ॥
tatō dēvō bhaṇati tvaṁ yadyapi nirīhastathāpi maṇimēkam । prasadyēmaṁ gr̥hāṇa sarpaviṣōcchēdana pravīṇam ॥49॥
tatō'nicchatō'pi tasyōttarīyē badadhvā maṇim । svargaṁ gataḥ suraḥ sa kathayati sarva surēndrasya ॥ 50 ॥
vimalō'pi karōti śabdaṁ sahadēvādīnāṁ tē'pi taṁ śrutvā । saṁprāptāstatpārśvē pr̥cchanti caṁ pathikavr̥ttāntam |
sō'pi hi kathayati sarvaṁ savistaraṁ tēṣāṁ harṣitāḥ sarvē । tatō vandantē jinēndrāṁstatraiva sthitāḥ subhaktyā ||
avalōkanaṁ munīnāṁ kr̥tvā bhuñjatē parijanasamētāḥ । bhuktōttarē puraparisarād madhyē saṁcalitāḥ ॥53॥
prāptā nagaradvārē śr̥ṇvanti haṭṭēṣu khaṭakhaṭārāvam । uttālatālakānāṁ vaṇigbhirdīyamānānām ॥54॥
prēkṣantē ca saṁnaddhāṁsturaṁgamāt subhaṭaśōbhitarathāṁśca । tathā guḍitagajaghaya itamtataḥ paribhramantīḥ ॥99॥

khuddha savtrōva jaṇa paribhamai puramma gōuraduvārē । dijjaṁti kavāḍāī kuṭuvari bhaḍā ṭhavijjati ? ||
kiṁ paracakkāu bhayaṁ sacakkaō vā duhāvi bhayamahavā । naravaiṇō vā kiṁcivi jāyaṁ ahimarakayamaṇi ? ||
tō tēṇaṁ parikahiyaṁ savaṇaduvārammi tarasa jaha ittha । nivasai rāyā purisōttamōtti bhuvaṇattayapasiddhō ॥
ēkkucciya tassa ō arimallō nāma mayaṇasamarūvō । sō suttō vāmaharē ahiṇā duṭṭēṇa daṭṭhōtti ॥ 60 ॥
tō tassa piyamā puriē dhātriō pariyaṇōvi । jāva palōyai savvaṁ tā sappō katthavi palāṇō ||
iya kumaravaiyaraṁ nisuṇiūṇa rāyāvi tattha saṁpattō । dīharanidapasuttaṁva picchiuṁ niyasuyaṁ sahasā ||62 ||
mucchānimīliyacchō luḍhiō puḍhavīē gāḍhakuṁḍhaunca । niyasuyapāṇavahārissa pihimadhāvaṇanimittaṁ ॥
avarōhakāmiṇīō nivarasa kumarassa uvari paḍiyāō । rōyaṁti ya aikaruṇaṁ purapaurajaṇōvi savvattō ॥
hakkārijjati naridavidavidāragā amacēhi । tēvi niyamatatē āgaṁtu saṁpaujjaṁti ॥ 65 ॥
naya yēvōvi visēsō visassa nigghāyaṇē va kōvi । rāyāvi kahavi satthōṁ jāō jalavāudāṇēṇa ||
bhai sacivāijaṇaṁ jaṛa kahavi virūvayaṁ kumārassa । saṁpajjissaivassaṁ tō ciyakaṭṭēṇa paḍhamēṇa ॥67॥
hōyavvamissa maē, aṇumannaha ēsa nicchaō majjha । iya sōuṁ paurajaṇō saṁbhaṁtō ēvamāyara || 68॥
aha rāyāvi hu paḍayamuhēṇa imaṁ ghōsāvaē nayarē । jō jīvāvaē kumaraṁ tassaddhaṁ dēmi rajassa ।। 69 ।।
taṁ sōuṁ sahadēvō vimalaṁ pabhaṇē kuṇasu uvayāraṁ । maṇimōhaliuṁ chaṁṭasu kumaraṁ, ujjīvaē jēṇa ॥70॥
tathā purārakṣakaṁ ca saṁnaddhasubhaṭasahitaṁ bhramantamitaśca । vimalēna kō'pi naraḥ pr̥ṣṭō bhōḥ kathaya kathamatra ||16||
kṣuḥ sarvō'pi janaḥ paribhramati purē gōpuradvārē । dīyantē kapāṭāni durgōpari bhaṭāḥ sthāpyantē ? || 57 ॥
kiṁ paracakrād
bhayaṁ svacakratō vā dvidhāpi bhayamathavā । narapatērvā kiñcidapi jātamabhimarakr̥tamaniṣṭam ? || 18 ||
tatastēna parikathitaṁ śravaṇadvārē tasya yathā'tra । nivasati rājā puruṣōttama iti bhuvanatrayaprasiddhaḥ ॥ 59॥
ēka ēva tasya sutō'rimallō nāma madanasamarūpaḥ । sa suptō vāsagr̥hē'hinā duṣṭēna daṣṭa iti ॥ 60 ॥
tatastasya priyatamayā pūtkr̥tē dhāvita: parijanō'pi । yāvatpralōkatē sarvaṁ tāvatsarpaḥ kvāpi palāyitaḥ ॥ 61॥
iti kumāravyatikaraṁ śrutvā rājāpi tatra saṁprāptaḥ । dīrghanidrāprasuptamiva dr̥ṣṭrā nijasutaṁ sahasā ॥ 62 ॥
mūrcchānimīlitākṣō luṭhitaḥ pr̥thivyāṁ gāḍhānugata iva । nijasutaprāṇāpahāriṇaḥ pr̥ṣṭhē'nudhāvananimittam ॥
avarōdhakāminyō nr̥pasya kumārasyōpari patitāḥ । rudanti cātikaruṇaṁ purapracurajanō'pi sarvataḥ ॥ 64 ॥
kāryantē narēndravr̥ndavr̥ndārakā amātyaiḥ । tē'pi nijamantratantrāṇyāgatya saṁprayuñjatē ॥ 65 ॥
na ca stōkō'pi viśēṣō viṣasya nirghātanē bhavati kō'pi । rājāpi kathamapi svasthō jātō jalavāyudānēna ॥
prabhaṇati sacivādijanaṁ yadi kathamapi virūpaṁ kumārasya । saṁpatsyatē'vaśyaṁ tataścitā kāṣṭhēna prathamēna ॥67॥
bhavitavyamasya mayā, anumanyadhvamēṣa niścayō mama । iti śrutvā paurajanaḥ saṁbhrānta ēvamācarati ॥ 68 ॥
atha rājāpi hi paṭahamukhēna ghōṣayatīṁda nagarē । yō jīvayati kumāraṁ tasmā artha dadāmi rājyasya ॥ 69 ॥

supāsanāha- carijammi--
ahigaraṇamiṇaṁ baṁdhava ! mahappamārṇa na hōi kāyavvaṁ । kiṁ rajjēṇa kajjē sajjō sāvajjamūlēṇa ? || 7 ||
iya vimalavaṇamāyanniūṇa jaṁpēi sō taō ēvaṁ । ucchidaha dālidaṁ amhakulassāvi pasiūṇa ॥ 72 ॥
jīvāvasu rāyasūyaṁ maṇimāhappaṁpi picchima tāva | taha dhammaṁṣi pavajjai jaṛa kahavi hu jīvaē ēsō ||
iccāi ta bhaṇirē vimalō nō kivi uttaraṁ dēi । jā tāva tēṇa sahasā vatthāō chōḍiō gaṁṭhī ||
gahiō maṇī taō lahaṁ chitō paḍō paṭṭacittēṇa । nīō kumarasamī sō nivapurisēhiṁ tō tēṇa ॥
ōhaliūṇa marṇi sō nīrēṇa jhaḍatti chaṁṭiō kumarō । suttavidvēva tēṇa tō disāō niyaṁtē ॥ 76 ॥
diṭṭhō sahadēvō naravaībisaṁtēurō purajaṇō ya । tō pucchiyā sajaṇaṇī kiṁ ammō ! ēsa mēlāvō? ॥77॥
harisuttinittāē tīē kahiyē savittharaṁ savaṁ । tō rannā sahadēvō niyaṁtiō addharajjēṇa ॥ 78 ॥
tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ narēsara ! mahatthi baṁdhū sahōparō vimalō । tassa pabhāvō ēsō kumarastujjīvaṇē jāō ॥ 79 ॥
camma sōvi uvi ciē saparivārō । sadāviūṇa sigvaṁ tassa pasāyaṁ kuṇau dēvō || 80 ॥
tō tattha sayaṁ gaccha saha sahadēvēṇa karivarārūḍhō । rāyā vimalaṁ da avagr̥hivi pabhaṇaē ēvaṁ ॥ 81 ॥
bhō ma pāṇabhikkhā dinā tumaē sudīṇahiyayassa । tō pasiūṇa saṁpai āgacchasu taṁ maha gimmi ||
jaha jaha ullavai nicō puṇō puṇō paṇayamāravayaṇāī । taha taha vimalassa maṇē sallai vayavisayaaiyārō ||
tō lēsana rāyē para jaṁpiyaṁ jahā dēva ! | sahadēvavilasiyamaṇaṁ tā kijjau jamuciyamimassa ||
hu
।
tat śrutvā sahadēva vimalaṁ prabhaṇati kuruvvōpacāram । maṇimavavr̥ṣyōkṣa kumāraṁ, ujjīvati yēna ॥ 70 ॥
adhikaraṇamidaṁ bāndhava ! mahāpramāṇaṁ na bhavati kartavyam । kiṁ rājyēna kāryaṁ sadyaḥ sāvadyamūlēna ? ॥71॥
iti vimalavacanamākarṇya jalpati sa tata ēvam | ucchinta dāridryamasmatkulasyāpi prasadya || 72 ।।
jīvaya rājasutaṁ maṇimāhātmyamapi paśyāmastāvat । tathā dharmamapi prapadyatē yadi kathamapi hi jīvatyēṣaḥ ॥73॥
ityādi tasmin bhaṇitari vimalō nō kimapyuttaraṁ dadāti । yāvattāvattēna sahasā vastrācchōṭitō granthiḥ ॥74॥
gr̥hītō bhaṇistatō laghu spr̥ṣṭaḥ paṭahaḥ prahr̥ṣṭacittēna । nītaḥ kumārasamīpaṁ sa nr̥papuruṣastatastēna ॥ 75 ॥
avakr̥ṣya maṇi sa nīrēṇa jhaṭityukṣitaḥ kumāraḥ । sutaviddhēnēva tēna tatō diśaḥ paśyatā ॥ 76 ॥
dr̥ṣṭaḥ sahadēvō narapatirapi sāntaḥ puraḥ purajanaśca । tataḥ pr̥ṣṭā svajananī kimamba ! ēṣa mēlakaḥ ? ||77||
harṣāśruktinētrayā tayā kathitaṁ savistaraṁ sarvam । tatō rājñā sahadēvō nimantritō'rgharājyēna ॥ 78 ॥
tēna bhaṇitaṁ narēśvara ! mamāhita bandhuḥ sahōdarō nilaḥ । tasya prabhāva ēṣa kumārasyōjjīvanē jātaḥ ॥79॥
caturhaṭṭakē sō'pi khalvupaviṣṭāstiṣṭhati saparivāraḥ । śabdayitvā śīghraṁ tasmai prasādaṁ karōtu dēvaḥ ॥ 80 ॥
tatastatra svayaṁ gacchati saha sahadēvēna karivarārūḍhaḥ । rājā vimalaṁ dr̥ṣṭrā'vaguhya prabhaṇatyēvam ॥81॥
bhō mama prāṇabhikṣā dattā tvayā sudīnahr̥dayasya । tataḥ prasadya saṁpratyāgaccha tvaṁ mama gr̥hē ॥ 82 ॥
yathā yathōllapati nr̥paḥ punaḥ punaḥ praṇayasāravacanāni । tathā tathā vimalasya manasi śalyati vrataviṣayāticāraḥ ॥
tī vimalēna samayaṁ rājānaṁ prati jalpitaṁ yathā dēva ! | sahadēvavilasitamidaṁ tasmātkriyatāṁ yaducitamasya ॥

tō dharivi karēṇa karaṁ karēṇuyārōviōya sō rannā । nīō gimmikārāviō ya sō majjaṇāīyaṁ ॥
sahiō sahadēvēṇa bhaṇiō bhutattarammi sō rannā । rajjassaddhaṁ giṇhasu uvaṇīyaṁ niyayapunnēhiṁ ॥ 86 ॥

niyagāmabhūribhūmi paḍiyaṁ khēḍāvaē lahu karēṇa । dēi dhāḍīu bahuhā haṇēi gāmāi annāṇaṁ ॥ 94 ॥
fares pāgarsē tassa naridasta jaha imō lōō। lhasijjaḍa dhaṇakaliō viulakarō kijjaḍa iyarō ॥

tataḥ sajigīṣaṁ jñātvā sahadēvaṁ prati prajalpitaṁ rājñā । pratyāsannōpakāryasmākaṁ tvamēva tataśca ॥ 89 ॥
gr̥hāṇēdaṁ tvaṁ rājyaṁ yathābhaṇitaṁ tatō bhaṇati sa ēvam । nijavākpratipannaṁ vitīryatāṁ tēna tatō dattam ||10||
dhavalagr̥haṁ rathaturagān karivararathaprabhr̥ti vibhajya sarvam । vimalaḥ punaḥ śrēṣṭhapadē saṁsthāpitō'nicchannapi ॥ 91 ॥
nijajanakādilōkaḥ samānatistaistatra tatō vimalaḥ | śrāvakadharmaṁ samyakpālayan gamayati bahukālam ॥92॥
itarō rājyē rāṣṭrē viṣayasukhē mōhitō mahāgr̥ddhaḥ । niṣṭhuraśca jātō nirapēkṣōṁ vratamālinyē ॥93॥
nijagrāmabhūribhūmiṁ patitāṁ karṣayati laghu karēṇa । dadāti ghāṭīrbahudhā hanti grāmādyanyēṣām ॥94॥
vitarati pāpōpadēśāṁstasmai narēndrāya yathā'yaṁ lōkaḥ । luṇṭhyatāṁ dhanakalitō vipulakaraḥ kriyatāmitaraḥ || 95 ||
ityādi caran sa bhaṇitō vimalēnānarthadaṇḍavratam । aticarasi kiṁ svayamēva gr̥hītvā yēna manujabhavē ॥ 96 ॥
ēkatō vikarālā mattā vyānīva ghughurāyamāṇā । jarārākṣasī pracaṁṇḍā''krāmati tanuṁ jīvānām ||97||
anyatō vyāyō dāruṇarūpāḥ kila kīḍantaḥ । dēhē sthitā nityaṁ nr̥tyanti ca ḍākinya iva ॥ 98 ॥

tāṇatthadaṁḍaviraī mā baṁdhava ! aiyarēsu aidulahaṁ । piccabhavē paramasuhaṁ jai mahasi tumaṁti ki bahuṇā ? ||
iya suṇiuṁsō jaṁpaṛa jaṛa haṁ ēvaṁviha uvaisēmi । nō naravaṇō tā maha avasāō havai niyarmēṇa ॥ 102 ॥

abhimaraprayōgapūrvaṁ pañcatvaṁ prāpitō'kr̥tadharmaḥ । prathamapr̥thivyāṁ prāptastata udvr̥ttaḥ san ॥ 106 ॥
bhramitvā bhavē katyapi hi sutīkṣṇaduḥkhānyanubhūya । sētsyati dhutakarmā prāptacaraṇaḥ samādhinā ॥ 107 ॥
vimalaḥ punarvimalamatiraskhalitaṁ pālayitvā gr̥hidharmam । vidhinā''rādhya paralōkamārgamatha sa gataḥ svargam ॥
yathaivaṁ vimalēna pālitaṁ niraticāratratamētat । tathānyairapi bhavyaiḥ pālayitavyaṁ sadākālam ॥109 ॥

taha pārēra siyaṁ kuṇai tahāmuddiyaṁ lahuṁ jēṇa । diusīlāuvi nārīu huti kaṁdappavagāō ||15||
tō kumarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ tayabhimuhaṁ mā karēsu tumamēvaṁ । taiyaguṇavvayapaḍhamō aiyārō ēsa jaṁ bhaṇiō || 16 ||
taṁ sōuṁ sō kaṁdaṇabhāvaō nē kahavi uvaramaī । kēlīra siyattaṇaō kumarēṇa ubēhiō tattō ||17||
kassavi bhaḍassa bhajjaṁ pautyavaiyaṁ ahannayā dayuṁ । taha kahavi kuṇai sō surayakūtriyaṁ tappurō jēṇa ॥ 18 ॥
kaṁdappapīḍiyā sā sahasā tassēva vilaiyā kaṁṭhē । tō taddiyarō daṭṭuṁ ruṭṭō tajjēi taṁ ēvaṁ ॥ 19 ॥
rē | tara ēsā kaṁdappāsvasā kayā muddhā | sussīlāvi varāī tō sō taṁ baṁdhaē dhaṇiyaṁ ||20||
bhai ya kumāramittaṁ tapasi jaō tō haṇēmi nō sahasā । taṁ sōūṇaṁ kumarō mōyāvara tassa pāsāō ||
āī yahiṁ baṁdhēhiṁ pīḍiyaṁ taṁ bhaṇēi tō kumarō । baṁdhava ! iṣi pattaṁ vayaaiyaraṇatarukusumaṁ ||22||

tā ajjavitaṁ sumara arihaṁ dēvō guruya nāṇadharā । ālōyasu duccariyaṁ taha khāmasu pāṇisaṁghāya || 24||
tēvi kumarō bhaṇiō baṁdhava ! baṁdhēhi pīḍiō gāḍhaṁ । na sarēmi ahaṁ kiṁcivitā kicivi kuṇasu paḍiyāraṁ ॥
iya bhatō mariḍaṁ vavannō kariva savijhami । tattō bhavammi bhami bhaṭṭa tō sa sijjhihihī ।।
kumarōvi niraiyāraṁ sāvagadhammaṁ ciraṁpi pālēḍaṁ । vihiṇā pavanacaraṇō sāsayasōkkhaṁ gaō mōkkhaṁ ||27|
॥ iti tr̥tīyaguṇavatē prathamāticāravipākē mittrasēnakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
tathā pārāpatarasitaṁ karōti tathāmudritaṁ laghu yēna । dr̥ḍhaśīlā api nāryō bhavanti kandarpavaśāḥ ॥ 15 ॥
tataḥ kumārēṇa bhaṇitaṁ tadabhimukhaṁ mā kuruṣva tvamēvam । tr̥tīyaguṇavrataprathamō'ticāra ēpa yad bhaṇitaḥ || 16 |
tat śrutvā sa kandarpabhāvatō naiva kathamapyuparamati । kēlī rasikatvataḥ kumārēṇōpēkṣitastataḥ ।। 17 ।।
kasyāpi bhaṭasya bhāryāṁ prōṣitapatikāmathānyadā dr̥ṣṭvā । tathā kathamapi karōti sa suratakūjitaṁ tatpurō yēna ॥
kandarpapīḍitā sā sahasā tasyaiva vilagitā kaṇṭhē । tatastadēvarō dr̥ṣṭvā ruṣṭastarjayati tamēvam ॥ 19 ॥

dhr̥ṣṭa ! tvayaiṣā kandarpaparavaśā kr̥tā mugdhā । suśīlāpi varākī tataḥ sa taṁ badhnāti gāḍham ॥ 20 ॥
bhaṇati ca kumāramittraṁ tvamasi yatastatō hanmi nō sahasā । tat śrutvā kumārō mōcayati tasya pārśvat |21|

sō uṇa avisannamaṇō tikkālaṁ kuṇaṛa bhāvaō pūyaṁ । saikāriyajiṇamaṁdira jigapaḍimāē jahāsattiṁ ॥ 15 ॥

ihalōicci dihaṁ pūyāi phalaṁ jiṇidarvivāṇaṁ । tahavi na viramasi ēīē nūṇa mūḍhō si taṁ būḍha ! || 18 ||
tō tāṇaṁ paṛa jaṁpara māmēvaṁ vayaha dhammacāēṇaṁ | jamhā na kajjasiddhī jāyaṛa jīvāṇa kaiyāvi ||19||
jaṁ puṇa dāridaduhaṁ samāgayaṁ amha ēttha janmammi । taṁ puvvajammavāvassa vilasiyaṁ jēṇimaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 20॥
suṁdaradhammarayāṇavi trisamaṁ vihivilasiyaṁ samāvaḍai । jaṁ tattha kāraṇamiṇaṁ annabhavē khaṁḍiō dhammō ||
tō jāu sirī viḍaṁtu baṁdhavā hōu lōyaavamāṇaṁ । tahavi na jidipūyaṁ vajjissamahaṁ jaō bhaṇiyaṁ ॥
pūyāē jiniṁdāṇaṁ phaṟamiha saggāpāsōkkhāī । tamhā tumhēvi hu ittha āyaraṁ kuṇaha iya bhaṇiē ||
tayabhimuhaṁ bhaṇai jaṇō jaha jaha jiṇapūyaṇaṁ tumaṁ kuṇasi । taha taha dālidatarū suphalaphalaṁ phalai tuha gēhē ॥
iya muṇiuṁ jaṇavāyaṁ dhammakkhisatti mannamāṇō sō । caiūṇa puraṁ pattō pañcāsannapi gāmammi ||25||
tatthavi piḍimā tikkālaṁ kuṇai pūyamaṇavajjaṁ । aha caumāsagadivasē sō pattō mahuranagarīē ||26||
jiṇamaṁdirarasa dārē tō mālākāriṇī bhaṇai siddhiṁ । causara mēgaṁ kusumāṇa givha pr̥ēsa jiṇarvivaṁ ||
।
tō gioes nō siṭṭī davvābhāvā bhaṇēi sā ēvaṁ । tujjha pasāēṇa imēlaṁkārā amha dēhami ||28||
lōkānāṁ bandhūnāṁ narapatērnijasutānāṁ bhāryāyāḥ । kiṁ bahunā, prativacanamapi tasya nō dadāti kō'pi tatra ॥ 14 ॥
sa punaraviṣaṇṇa manāstrikālaṁ karōti bhāvataḥ pūjām । svakāritajinamandirajinapratimāyā yathāśakti ||15||
tattanayāstataḥ śrēṣṭhinaṁ sīdantaṁ bruvanti virama pūjāyāḥ । iyatkālaṁ haṭṭē yadi tvaṁ tiṣṭhasi vāṇijyakr̥tē ॥
tatō na khalu kṣūṇaṁ jāyatē bhōjanataḥ, vastrādikaṁ sarvam । vayaṁ punaḥ paragēhē karma kr̥tvōpārjayiṣyāmaḥ ॥ 17 ॥
ihalōka ēva dr̥ṣṭaṁ pūjāyāḥ phalaṁ jinēndrabimbānām । tathāpi na viramasyētasyā nūnaṁ mūḍhō'si tvaṁ vr̥ddha ! ॥ 18॥
tatastān prati jalpati mā maivaṁ vadata dharmatyāgēna । yasmānna kāryasiddhirjāyatē jīvānāṁ kadāpi ॥19॥
yatpunardāridryaduḥkhaṁ samāgataṁ mamātra janmani । tatpūrvajanmapāpasya vilasitaṁ yēnēdaṁ bhaṇitam ||20||
sundaradharmaratānāmapi viṣamaṁ vidhivilasitaṁ samāpatati । yattatra kāraṇamidamanyabhavē khaṇḍitō dharmaḥ || 21 |
tatō yātu śrīvighaṭantāṁ bāndhavā bhavatu lōkāpamānaḥ । tathāpi na jinēndrapūjāṁ varjayiṣyāmyahaṁ yatō bhaṇitam |
pūjāyā jinēndrāṇāṁ phalāmiha svargāpavargasaukhyāni । tasmād yūyamapi khalvatrādaraṁ kurutēti bhaṇitē ||23||
tadabhimukhaṁ bhaṇati janō yathā yathā jinapūjanaṁ tvaṁ karōṣi । tathā tathā dāridryataruḥ suphalaphalaṁ phalati tava gēhē ।
iti jñātvā janavādaṁ gharmahēlēti manyamānaḥ saḥ । tyaktvā puraṁ prāptaḥ pratyāsannē grāmē ||25||
tatrāpi gr̥hapratimāyāstrikālaṁ karōti pūjāmanavadyām । atha caturmāsadivasē sa prāptō mathurānagaryām ॥ 26 ॥
jinamandirasya dvārē tatō mālākāriṇī bhaṇati śrēṣṭhinam । caturmālāmēkāṁ kusumānāṁ gr̥hāṇa pūjaya jinabimbam ।
1 ka. kha. phalihī tumāvi ya gēhammi |

sīhakahā ।
511
cārakaraṇa tumaē kusumāī gihiyāī sayakālaṁ । tā giṇhasu ēyāī puṇṇaṁ tumhāṇa mē dinaṁ ॥ 29 ॥
pūyasu jiṇidabiṁbaṁ tō siṭṭī kuṇai tāī nihatthē । nissīhiyaṁ bhaṇēuṁ pavisa vihiṇā jiṇasamīvē ॥।
bhaktivbhara nivbharunbhinnavahalarōmaṁcakaṁcuijjatō । pūyai jiṇidarbivaṁ iya bhāvatō paṇē siṭṭhī ||31||
dhannō haṁ jēṇa maē aṇōrapāram bhavasamuddammi | bhavasayasahassadulahaṁ laddhaṁ saddhammajāṇaṁti ||32||
ēyassa pabhāvēṇaṁ pālijaṁtassa saha payattēṇa । jammaṁtarēvi jīvā pārśvati na dukkhadōhaggaṁ ||33||
ciṁtāmaṇī aḍavō ēsa auvvō ya kapparukkhōti । ēsō paramō maṁtō ēyaṁ paramāmayaṁ ittha ||34||
tēsi namō tērsi namō bhāvēṇa puṇō puṇōvi tērsi namō । aṇuvakayapara hiyarayā jīvāṇa karhiti jē dhammaṁ ।।
sulahō vimāṇavāsō ēgacchattāvi mēiṇī sulahā । lōgammi navari dulahō jaṇēṇa jinadēsiō dhammō ||
tā dullabhō laḍō dhammō sanvannupūyaṇāīō । anēṇa mē na kajjaṁ iya citivi vaṁdaē dēvē ||37||
jiṇavaṁdanāvasāṇē piccha cakkhāṇamaṁḍavē sūriṁ । vāgaramāṇaṁ dhammaṁ sammaṁ bhavvāṇa tō siṭṭhī ||38||
vaṁda dūrahiō taṁ sūrīvi hu sāyaraṁ gurugirāē । dāūṇaṁ dhammalābhaṁ tappuraō sāhaē ēvaṁ ||39||
jalaviḍayaṁtra rayaṇaṁ dulahaṁ maṇuyattamittha saṁsārē । tā laḍūṇaṁ ēyaṁ jaiyavvaṁ sugamammi ||40||
sa cāyam ;
pūyā jiṇidēsu raī vasu jattō ya sāmāiyapōsa ।
dāṇaṁ supattē savarṇa sutitthē susāhasēvā sumaīi maggō || 41॥
tatō gr̥hṇāti nō śrēṣṭhī dravyābhāvadbhaṇati saivam । tava prasādanēmē'laṅkārā mama dēhē ||28||
icchākrayēṇa tvayā kusumāni gr̥hītāni sadākālam । tasmād gr̥hāṇaitāni puṇyaṁ yuṣmabhyaṁ mayā dattam ॥ 29॥
pūjaya
jinēndrabimba, tataḥ śrēṣṭhī karōti tāni nijahastē । naiṣēdhikīṁ bhaṇitvā praviśati vidhinā jinasamīpē ॥
bhaktibharanirbharādbhinnabahalarōmāñcakañcukāyamānaḥ । pūjayati jinēndrabimbamiti bhāvayanmanasi śrēṣṭhī ॥ 31 ॥
dhanyō'haṁ yēna mayā'nādipārē bhavasamudrē । bhavaśatasahasradurlabhaṁ labdhaṁ saddharmayānamiti ||32||
ētasya prabhāvēṇa pālyamānasya sadā prayatnēna । janmāntarē'pi jīvāḥ prāpnuvanti na duḥkhadaurbhāgyam ||33||
cintāmaṇirapūrva ēṣō'pūrvaśca kalpavr̥kṣa iti । ēṣa paramō mantra ētat paramāmr̥tamaṁtra || 34॥
tēbhyō namastēbhyō namō bhāvēna punaḥ punarapi tēbhyō namaḥ । anupakr̥taparahitaratā jīvānāṁ kathayanti yē dharmam ॥
sulabhō vimānavāsa ēkacchatrāpi mēdinī sulabhā । lōkē kēvalaṁ durlabhō janēna jinadēśitō dharmaḥ || 36 ||
tasmād durlabhō labdhō dharmaḥ sarvajñapūjanādikaḥ । anyēna mē na kāryamiti cintayitvā vandatē dēvān ॥37॥
jinavandanāvasānē paśyati vyākhyānamaṇḍapē sūrim । vyākurvantaṁ dharmaṁ samyag bhavyēbhyaḥ, tataḥ śrēṣṭhī ॥38॥
vandatē dūrasthitastaṁ sūrirapi hi sādaraṁ gurugirā । dattvā dharmalābhaṁ tatpurataḥ kathayatyēvam ||39||
jaladhipatitamiva ratnaṁ durlabhaṁ manujatvamatra saṁsārē । tasmāllabdhvaitad yatitavyaṁ sugatimārgē ॥40॥
pūjā jinēndrēṣu ratitratēṣu yatnaśca sāmāyika pauṣadhēṣu ।

supāsanāha-cariammi-
iccāvityarēṇa kahiyāē dēsaṇāē surīhiṁ । siṭṭhī jaṁśi saṁvēganibbharaṁ sūrihamaṇaṁ ॥ 42 ॥
tujjha pasāēṇa mahaṁ nicaṁ nivvaha nāha ! jiṇapūyā । kiṁpuṇa pahu ! aṁgaruhā kuṇaṁti apattiyaṁ bahuyaṁ ॥
jaṁpati tahā vijjai na kiṁpi pūyāē tuha phalaṁ tāya ! | puṇvajjiyāvi lacchī navaraṁ nōharai nēhāō ||
lōōvi bhai ēvaṁ dhammēṇa dharṇa imassa hāraviyaṁ । mama puṇa maṇayaṁpi na kiṁpi māṇasē phurai tavvayaṇaṁ ।
tā thirakaraṇōvāō havijja jai kōvi tāṇavi muṇida ! | tō nivvahija dhammō suhēṇa maha nāha ! iya vōttu ।।
mōṇēṇa ṭhiō siṭṭhī uvayāraṁ jāṇiūṇa sūrīvi । uvaisai tassa maṁtaṁ niravajjaṁ paḍhiyasiddhaṁ ca ॥ 47॥
kasiṇaca udasirayaṇī addharattammi pēyavaṇamajjhē । kāussaggēṇa ṭiō sumarijjatu taṁ imaṁ mataṁ ॥ 48 ॥
tō cakkhō hōhī kaḍijakkhō muhuttamittēṇa । bhaṇihī sō tuha samuhaṁ abhiruiyaṁ maggasu varaṁti ||49 ॥
tō
tumala
sō ēvaṁ ēvaṁ vattavyaōtti bhaṇiūṇa | sūrīvi vihārēṇa annattha gaō taō siṭṭī ॥ 50 ॥
bhaṇiya divasamma pattō masāṇabhūmīē kahiyavihiputraṁ । kāussaggampiṭiō tō punmuttaṁ samagaṁṣi ||
taha jāyaṁ jaha bhaṇiyaṁ jakkhābhimu bhaṇē tō siṭṭhī । caupāsadiṇē pūyā jā vihiyā causarēṇa maē ||
tīi phalēṇa pasāyaṁ kuṇasu tumaṁ asthi tujjha jai sattī । ina suṇiuṁsō jakkhō uvaōgē dēi avahīē ||
ullaviyaṁ tō tēṇa tīē phalaṁ biyariḍaṁ asatō haṁ | jamhā jiṇassa pūyāē ēkkassi bhāvavihiyāē ||
saggasirīvi hu labbhai aivitthinnā mamaṁ ca sā natthi | vaṁtarajāīō hūṁ tā annaṁ bhaṇasu taṁ kiṁpi ॥
dānaṁ supātrē śravaṇaṁ sutīrthē susādhusēvā sugatē mārgaḥ || 41 ॥
ityādivistarēṇa kathitāyāṁ dēśanāyāṁ sūribhiḥ । śrēṣṭhī jalpati saṁvēganirbharaṁ sūrisammukhamidam ॥42॥
tava prasādēna mama nityaṁ nirvahati nātha ! jinapūjā । kintu prabhō ! aṅgaruhāḥ kurvantyapratyayaṁ bahum ||43||
jalpanti tathā vidyatē na kimapi pūjāyāstava phalaṁ tāta ! | pūrvārjitāpi lakṣmīḥ kintu nissarati gēhāt ||44 ||
lōkō'pi bhaṇatyēvaṁ dharmēṇa dhanamasya nāśitam । mama punarmanāgari na kimapi mānasē sphurati tadvacanam ॥45॥
tasmātsthira karaṇōpāyō bhavēdyadi kō'pi tēṣāmapi munīndra ! । tatō nirvahēd dharmaḥ sukhēna mama nātha ! ityuktvā ||
maunēna sthitaḥ śrēṣṭhyupakāraṁ jñātvā sūrirapi । upadiśati tasya mantraṁ niravadyaṁ paṭhitasiddhaṁ ca ॥ 47 ॥
kr̥ṣṇa cartudaśīraṁjanyāmardharātrē prētavanamadhyē | kāyōtsargēṇa sthitaḥ smarastvamimaṁ mantram || 48 ॥
tataḥ pratyakṣō bhaviṣyati kapardiyakṣa muhūrtamātrēṇa । maṇiṣyati sa tava saṁmukhamabhirucitaṁ mārgaya varamiti ॥ 49 ॥
tatastvayā sa ēvamēvaṁ vaktavya iti bhaṇitvā । sūrirapi vihārēṇānyatra gatastataḥ śrēṣṭhī ॥ 50 ॥
bhaṇitadivasē prāptaḥ śmaśāna bhūmau kathita vidhipūrvam । kāyōtsargē sthitastataḥ pūrvōktaṁ samagramapi ॥ 51 ॥
tathā jātaṁ yathā bhaṇitaṁ yakṣābhimukhaṁ bhaṇati tataḥ śrēṣṭhī । caturmāsadinē pūjā yā vihitā caturmālēna mayā ॥ 52॥
tasyāḥ phalēna prasādaṁ kuruṣva tvamasti tava yadi śaktiḥ । iti śrutvā sa yakṣa upayōgaṁ dadātyavadhēḥ ॥ 53॥
ullapitaṁ tatastēna tasyāḥ phalaṁ vitarītumaśaktō'ham । yasmājjinasya pūjayaikayā bhāvavihitayā || 14 ||
svargaśrīrapi hi labhyatē'tivistīrṇā mama ca sā nāsti । vyantarajātīyō'haṁ tasmādanyadbhaṇa tvaṁ kimapi ॥ 55 ॥
