sā bhai jakkha ! tuha daṁsaṇēṇa tuṭṭhō ahaṁ vayasu ṭhāṇaṁ । jiṇadhammabhāvēṇa kiṁ maha taṁ jaṁ na hōḍitti ? ||
tō taṁ para sō jaṁpa samattiō tuha karēmi vacchallaṁ | sāhammiutti kāuṁ tēṇāṇumaē bhāi jakkhō ||
tuha gēhē catuvi kōṇaēsa cihnaṁti gurunihāṇāī | giṇyavvāī tara iya bōpadaṁsaṇaṁ pattō ॥ 58 ॥
pacchimanisā siṭṭhī pattō gēhammi bhai niyataṇaē । jai dhammē kuha maī tō iha jammēvi tumhāṇaṁ ||
daṁsēmi phalamuyāraṁ, tō tē jaṁpati jai imaṁ kuṇasi । tō niuṇataraṁ dhammaṁ tujjha sayāsāu pakarēmō || 60 ॥
dāūṇa tāṇa savahaṁ tikkālaṁ jiṇagihasta gamaṇammi । pūyāīkaraṇammiya payaṁsiō tō nihī ēgō ॥ 61 ॥
dahuṁ mahapamāṇaṁ paḍipuṇṇaṁ ṭaṁkayāṇa tē hiṭṭhā। savvaṁ citra tatrvayaṇaṁ kurṇati bhāvēṇa paidiyahaṁ ||62 ||
tatō kamēṇa nihiṇō sēsāvi paryaṁsiyā gihasta । aha annayā ya pattō sōcciya sūrī tarhi tattō ॥
niyasa ēhi samaṁ mahaṁta riddhīē tāṇa namaṇatthaṁ । siṭṭī pattō annōvi purajaṇō biyisiṁgārō ||64 ||
ti payāhiṇīkarēuṁ namium̐ sūriṁ na yāidūrammi । uvaviṭṭhā saccēvi hu tō siṭṭhī bhaṇai samayampi || 65 ||
bhayavaṁ ! sajjha suyāṇaṁ sammattāī gityasaddhammō | ubaisiūṇaṁ dijjau sūrīvi tahēva taṁ kuṇai ||66 ||
iya sōūṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ sīhēṇaṁ nāha ! majjhavi kahēha | vittharaō gimmiṁ jēṇāhaṁ taṁ pavajjēmi ॥ 67 ॥
tō kahai gurū tassava annērsipi hu taō ya kēṇāvi | sammattaṁ paḍivannaṁ taha kēṇaviṇuvtrayāṇi ॥ 68 ॥
sahadēvēṇa samaṁ puṇa sīhō givhēiṇatthadaṁḍavayaṁ । sammatta juaṁ sāhai tassa sakhvaṁ gurūvi imaṁ ।। 69 ।।
pāvōva ēsasippayāṇaō aṭṭajhāṇakaraṇāō | majjāipamāyāō aṇatthadaṁḍō bhavē cauhā ॥ 70 ॥
। ॥
sa bhaṇati yakṣa ! tava darśanēna tuṣṭō'haṁ vraja sthānam | jinadharmaprabhāvēṇa kiṁ mama tadyanna bhaviṣyatīti ? ॥56॥
tatastaṁ prati sa jalpati svaśaktitastava karōmi vātsalyam । sādharmika iti kr̥tvā tēnānumatē bhaṇati yakṣaḥ ॥
tava gēhē caturṣvapi kōṇēṣu tiṣṭhanti gurunidhānāni । grahītavyāni tvayētyuktvā'darśanaṁ prāptaḥ ॥ 58 ॥
paścimaniśāyāṁ śrēṣṭhī prāptō gēhē bhaṇati nijatanayānū । yadi dharmē kuruta matiṁ tata iha janmanyapi yuṣmākam ॥
darśayāmi phalamudāraṁ, tatastē jalpanti yadīdaṁ karōṣi । tatō dviguṇataraṁ dharmaṁ tatra sakāśātprakurmaḥ ॥ 60 ॥
dattvā tēṣāṁ śapathaṁ trikālaṁ jinagr̥hasya gamanē । pūjādikaraṇē ca pradarśitastatō nidhirēkaḥ ॥ 61 ॥
dr̥ṣṭvā mahāpramāṇaṁ paripūrṇa ṭaṅkakānāṁ taṁ hr̥ṣṭāḥ । sarvamēva tadvacanaṁ kurvanti bhāvēna pratidivasam ॥ 62 ॥
tataḥ kramēṇa nidhayaḥ śēṣā api pradarśitā gr̥hasyāntaḥ । athānyadā ca prāptaḥ sa ēva sūristatra tataḥ ॥ 63 ॥
nijasarvasutaiḥ samaṁ mahaddhardhyā tēṣāṁ namanārtham । śrēṣṭhī prāptō'nyō'pi purajanō vihitaśr̥ṅgāraḥ ॥ 64 ॥

triḥ pradakṣiṇīkr̥tya natvā sūriṁ na cātidūrē । upaviṣṭāḥ sarvē'pi hi tataḥ śrēṣṭhī bhaṇati samayē ॥ 62 ॥
bhagavan ! mama sutānāṁ samyaktvādirgr̥hasthasaddharmaḥ । upadiśya dīyatāṁ sūrirapi tathaiva tatkarōti ॥ 66 ॥
iti śrutvā bhaṇitaṁ siṁhēna nātha ! mamāpi kathayata । vistaratō gr̥hidharma yēnāhaṁ taṁ prapadyē ॥ 67 ॥

supāsanāha - cariammi-
ahigaraṇapauṇakaraṇaṁ bhōguvabhōgāṇa ahiyakaraṇaṁ ca । aṇavarathaṁ mōhariyaṁ kaṁdaṣpaṁ taha ya kukkuiyaṁ ॥ 71 ॥
vajjēva gihiṇā aṇatthadaṁḍavyayaṁ dharatēṇa । iya nisamiūṇa samagaṁ bhattīē sīhasahadēvā ॥ 72॥
tattō namiūṇa guruṁ gimmi pattā kuṇati jiṇadhammaṁ । aha annayā ya sīhō haṭṭē vavaharai jā tāva ||
rāyasuhāsiyāsī bhaṁḍō pattō bhai tayabhimuhaṁ । kaṭṭhēsu vēṇiya ! kōḍiṁ vaihiyāvadvāṇa daḍḍhāṇa ||74 ||
tō karē sō sōva hu appē viṭayaṁ tassa । mullaṁ ṭhaviūṇa taō phālāvara kannamūlammi || 75॥
savvēvi vaiviṭṭē bhāi ya na kayāvi savaṇavivarēsu । majjha paviḍō ēsō caracarasahō savaṇasuhaō ||
tō hasai sīhavaṇiō saha vaṇiuttēhi millaē mōllaṁ । tāṇaṁ taṁbōlāī dāūṇa visajjaē bhaṁḍa || 77 ||
tō paidi bhaṁḍō āgacchā sīhapāsammi akkhaliō । kugai vivihē viyārē taha bhūbhaṁgāi rihā sē ||
taha viḍavijjaṁ payaḍai hasati sīhāiyā jahā savvē । muttaṇaṁ sahadēvaṁ sīhō tō dūrayahiyaō || 79 ||
muhanayaṇāiviyārē aṇavarayaṁ kuṇai tasma pāsaṭhiō । kiṁ bahuṇā sō jāō taōvi garuō mahābhaṁḍō ।
sahadēvō uṇa vārai aṇavarayaṁ sō na viramai tahāvi । ramaṇīmaṇaānaṁda karēi vivihāhiṁ ciṭṭhāhiṁ ॥ 81 ॥
muddhatā na yāṇai aiyāramimaṁ sumittakahiyapi । hāsarasāulahiyaō hasāvaē savvamavi lōyaṁ ॥ 82 ॥
kannaḍa yauttassa bhāriyā kappaḍassa kiṇaṇatthaṁ । aha kaiyāvi hu haṭṭē pattā sīhassa pāsamma || 83 ||
kannaḍayarāyauttassa
vatthaṁ hatthē appara tīē nayaṇāiēhiṁ vivikariyaṁ । kuṇaṛa jaha bhōliyā sā mullaṁ bahuyaṁ payacchēī ||84 ॥
I
pāpōpadēśa hiṁsapradānata ārtadhyānakaraṇāt । madyādipramādādanarthadaṇḍō bhavēccaturdhā ॥ 70 ॥
adhikaraṇapraguṇakaraṇaṁ bhōgōpabhōgānāmadhikakaraṇaṁ ca । anavarataṁ maukharya kandarpastathā ca kaukucyam ॥ 71 ॥
varjayitavyaṁ gr̥hiṇā'narthadaṇḍavataṁ dharatā । iti niśamya samaṁ bhaktyā siṁhasahadēvau ॥ 72 ॥
tatō natvā guruṁ gr̥hē prāptau kurutō jinadharmam । athānyadā ca siṁhō haṭṭē vyavaharati yāvattāvat ॥73॥
rāgasubhāṣitabhāṣī viṭaḥ prāptō bhaṇati tadabhimukham । karṣa vaṇik ! kōṭiṁ vahikā vr̥ttānāṁ dagdhānām ||74||
tatastathā karōti siṁhaḥ sō'pi khalvarpayati pōṭṭalaṁ tasya । mūlyaṁ sthāpayitvā tataḥ sphālayati karṇamūlē |
sarvānapi vahikāvr̥ttān bhaṇati ca na kadāpi śravaṇavivarēṣu । mama praviṣṭa ēṣa caracaraśabdaḥ śravaṇasukhadaḥ ॥
tatō hasati siṁhavaṇik saha vaṇikputrairmuñcati mūlyam । tēṣāṁ tāmbūlādīn dattvā visr̥jati viṭam ||77 |
tataḥ pratidinaṁ viṭa āgacchati siṁhapārśvē'skhalitaḥ । karōti vividhāvikārāṁstathā bhrūbhaṅgādiparihāsān ||
tathā viṭavidyāṁ prakaṭayati hasanti siṁhādikā yathā sarvē । muktvā sahadēvaṁ siṁhastatō dūrahatahr̥dayaḥ ॥ 79 ॥
mukhanayanādivikārāna'navarataṁ karōti tasya pārśvasthitaḥ । kiṁ bahunā sa jātastatō'pi gururmahāviṭaḥ ॥ 80 ॥
sahadēvaḥ punarvārayatyanavarataṁ sa na viramati tathāpi । ramaṇīmana ānandaṁ karōti vividhābhiścēṣṭābhiḥ ॥ 81 ॥
mugdhatvānna jānātyaticāramimaṁ sumitra kathitamapi । hāsyarasākulahr̥dayō hāsayati sarvamapi lōkam ॥82॥
karṇāṭaka rājaputrasya bhāryā karpaṭasya krayaṇārtham । atha kadāpi hi haṭṭē prāptā siṁhasya pārśvē ॥ 83 ॥
1 ga. paṇayakō । 2 ka. vihi° ।

haṇai kavōlapaē sē bhaṇaiya rē rē aṇajja ! vaṇiōvi । bhaṁḍāṇavi ahiō taṁ jō maha mahilāpurō ēvaṁ ।।

karōṣi vividhānvikārāniti bhaṇitvā yāvannihaniṣyati tāvat । vaṇikputraiḥ sahasā ghr̥tō bāhunā bhaṇitaśca ॥
kṣamaya mahāyaśaḥ ! idānīṁ kṣamāpradhānāśca bhavanti satpuruṣāḥ । ityādi prajalpya kōpa uttāritastasya ॥ 88॥
siṁhapēṭāghātēna pīḍitō mūcchitaśca kṣaṇamēkam । khaṇḍitaikanayanagōlaka upacaritaścandanādibhiḥ ॥89॥

āppāyaṁ mōhariyabhāvaō jō palappaē saḍḍhō । taiyaguṇavvayadhārī duhāī sō lahaṛa paumōvva || 1 ||
tathāhi;

puramatthi purimatālaṁ taṁ pālai patthitrō vijayapālō । tassatthi piyā raṁbhā raṁbhavva vibhiyasubhōyā || 2 ||
aha annā nariṁdō karidakhaṁghaggaō saparivārō । rāyavaḍiyāi gaccha tō picchara vaṇigi kammi ||
paḍhamullasaṁtajōvvaṇarasāulaṁ lacchināmiyaṁ kannaṁ । gayarūvaṁ, tō taduvari tassaṇurāō kahavi jāō || 4 ||
tajjayāī maggāviūṇa pariṇēi taṁ sahatthē । aṁtēurammi khiviḍaṁ tīi samaṁ vilasai nariṁdō ||5||
na kuṇa kassaviṁ tatti purasta atēurassa rajjassa । tīi paribhōgarasiō rāōdivasaṁpi tīi gihē || 6 ||
cihna paḍiō naḍiō tīē siṇēhēṇa hāriyavivēō । parihariyasavvakajjō bhaṇiō tō maṁtiṇā ēvaṁ ||
iyarōvi jaṇō rāgassa vasagaō bahu vigupaē nr̥ṇaṁ । kiṁ puṇa puhaīvaiṇō aṁtara riuchakka akaṁtā ? ॥8॥
dhammaṁ atthaṁ kāmaṁ nīīē nisēvayaṁti naravaṇō । jē tāṇaṁ purisatthā diti phalaṁ niṣphalā iharā ||9||
kiñca ।
dūraṁ nāsaṁti guṇā duraṁ ci vīsaraṁti satthatthā । dūraṁ guruvaēsā rāgaṁdhāṇaṁ narāṇa taō ॥ 10 ॥
।
taramma bhullō dēvō caiūṇa rajjarahaṁ ca । dhammaṁ ca jaṁ imīē āsattō ci sāvi ॥ 11 ॥
tō bhaṇiyaṁ naravaṇā saciva ! tumaṁ mā bhaṇēsu maha samuhaṁ । kiṁcivi jamimaṁ rajjaṁ tuha dinaṁ pālasu tamēva ॥
jāvēsā miganayaṇā mahanayaṇa hē payaṭṭai sayāvi । tāvacciya maha jīyaṁ kiṁ kajjaṁ rajjamāīhi ? || 13 ||
piccha kaha ēsa rāyā rāgēṇa viḍaṁbiō na cēēi । appāṇaṁ gayalajjō iya sacivō citaē jāva ॥ 14 ॥
ālaprāyaṁ maukharyabhāvatō yaḥ pralapati śrāddhaḥ । tr̥tīyaguṇavratadhārī duḥkhāni sa labhatē padma iva ॥ 1 ॥
puramasti purimatālaṁ tatpālayati pārthivō vijayapālaḥ । tasyāsti priyā rambhā rambhēva vijr̥mbhitasubhōgā ||

tajjanakādīnmārgayitvā pariṇayati tāṁ svahastēna । antaḥpurē kṣiptvā tayā samaṁ vilasati narēndraḥ ||5||
na karōti kasyāpi cintāṁ purasyāntaḥpurasya rājyasya । tasyāṁ paribhōgarasikō rātridivasamapiṁ tasyā gr̥hē ||
tiṣṭhati patitō naṭitastasya snēhēna hāritavivēkaḥ । parihr̥tasarvakāryōṁ bhaṇitastatō mantriṇaivam ||7||
itarō'pi janō rāgasya vaśagatō bahu vigupyatē nūnam । kiṁ punaḥ pr̥thivīpataya āntararipuṣaṭkākrāntāḥ ? ॥
dharmamartha kāmaṁ nītyā niṣēvantē narapatayaḥ । yē tēṣāṁ puruṣārthā dadati phalaṁ niṣphalā itarathā ||9||
dūraṁ naśyanti guṇā dūramēva vismaryantē śāstrārthāḥ । duraṁ gurūpadēśā rāgāndhānāṁ narāṇāṁ tataḥ ॥ 10 ॥
mahāntarē bhraṣṭō dēvastyaktvā rājyarāṣṭraṁ ca । dharmaṁ ca yadasyāmāsaktastiṣṭhati sadāpi ॥ 11 ॥ .
tatō bhaṇitaṁ narapatinā saciva ! tvaṁ mā bhaṇa mama saṁmukham । kiñcidapi yadidaṁ rājyaṁ tava dattaṁ pālaya tvamēva ॥

tā tī carimajāmē vāsiyamaṇaṁ kahaṁdhi saṁjāyaṁ । tō rāyā saṁbuddhō vijjē vāharai tēvi taō || 15 ||
chaḍḍāvaṇāī vivihāī jāva pauṁjaṁti tāva sahasāvi । sā mukkā pāṇēhiṁ mihirassa samuggamē tattō ||
mucchā nimīliyacchō rāyā dharaṇīē nivaḍiō dahūṁ । gayapāṇaṁ pāṇaviyaṁ ṭiō ya kaṭuṁba niciṭṭhō ||
caṁdaṇarasēṇa sitō pīō tālaviṭaēṇa niyō । pattē cēyaṇabhāvē vilavara gurumukapukārō ||18||
hā lacchi mayacchi sudacchi kimiha pucchaṁtayassa paḍivayaṇaṁ । na hu dēsi majjha chaṇasasivayaṇē ruṭṭhāsi kiṁ suyaṇu
iccāi palavamāṇō na mui pāsa karēi naya gāsaṁ । naya dēī avagāsaṁ kassavi tō pabhaṇē maṁtī ||20||
dēva ! mayacciya ēsā maṁcasu pāsa karēmi sakkāraṁ । ēīē jēṇāhaṁ kuviō tō naravaī bhai ||21||
sakkāraha niyadēhaṁ puttapaputtāiēhiṁ saha tumayaṁ । maha pāṇapiyā daiyā jīvissara kōḍivāsāī ||22||
maha kanakaḍuyavayaṇaṁ amaṁgalaṁ jō bhaṇissai imīē । sō nicchaēga marihī tō vaṁcēūṇa taddihiṁ ॥ 23॥
maṁtī kammarāō sakkārāvara kaḍēvaraṁ tīsē । ummukkagaruyapukō tamapēcchaṁtō naravarōvi ॥ 24 ॥
viess bhai ēvaṁ bhuṁjissamahaṁ piyāē diṭṭhāē । jēṇavahariyā dēvī jamagēhammi ya gaē tammi ||25|
ēvaṁ arousal didasagaṁ gamai naravarō tattō । sikkhaviṁḍaṁ sacivēṇaṁ tapāsē pēsiō purisō ||26||
tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ narāhiva ! vaddhāvijjaha piyāē suddhīē । sō bhaṇai sāhasu karhi uvaladdhā tīi suddhitti ||
sō āha nāha ! dēvī saṁpai saggammi suravaisamīvē । ciṭṭhara suhēṇa tīē tuha pāsē pēsiō ahayaṁ ||28||
I
paśya kathamēṣa rājā rāgēṇa viḍambitō na cētati । ātmānaṁ gatalajja iti sacivaścintayati yāvat ॥ 14 ॥
tāvattasyāścaramayāmē vāsitavamanaṁ kathamapi saṁjātam । tatō rājā saṁkṣubdhō vaidyānāhvayati tē'pi tataḥ ||15||
mōcanāni vividhāni yāvatprayuñjatē tāvatsahasāpi । sā muktā prāṇairmihirasya samudgamē tataḥ ॥ 16 ॥
mūrcchānimīlitākṣō rājā dharaṇyāṁ nipatitō dr̥ṣṭvā । gataprāṇāṁ prāṇapriyāṁ sthitaśca kāṣṭhamiva niścēṣṭaḥ ॥
candanarasēna siktaḥ pravījitastālavr̥ntēna nr̥paḥ । prāptē cētanabhāvē vilapati muktaguruputkāraḥ ॥ 18 ॥
hālakṣmi mr̥gākṣi sudakṣē kimiha pr̥cchataḥ prativacanam । na hi dadāsi mama kṣaṇaśaśivadanē ruṣṭāsi kiṁ sutanu ||
ityādi pralapanna muñcati pārśva karōti naca grāsam । naca dadātyavakāśaṁ kasyāpi tataḥ prabhaṇati mantrī ||
dēva ! mr̥taivaiṣā muñca pārśvaṁ karōmi saṁskāram । ētasyā yēnāhaṁ, kupitastatō narapatirbhaṇati ॥21॥
saṁskuruta nijadēhaṁ putrapraputrādikaiḥ saha tvam । mama prāṇapriyā dayitā jīviṣyati kōṭivarṣāṇi ॥ 22 ॥
mama karṇakaṭukavacanamamaṅgalaṁ yō bhaṇibhyatyasyāḥ । sa niścayēna mariṣyati tatō vañcitvā tadṣṭim ॥ 23 ॥
mantrī karmakarātsaṁskārayati kalēvaraṁ tasyāḥ । unmuktagurupūtkārastāmapaśyannarabarō'pi ॥24॥
vilapati bhaṇatyēvaṁ bhōkṣyē'haṁ priyāyāṁ dr̥ṣṭāyām । yēnāpahr̥tā dēvī yamagr̥hē ca gatē tasmin ||25||
ēvaṁ kr̥tapratijñō dinadaśakaṁ gamayati naravarastataḥ । śikṣayitvā sacivēna tatpārśvē prēṣitaḥ puruṣaḥ || 26 ॥
tēna bhaṇitaṁ narādhipa ! vardhyadhvē priyāyāḥ śuddhayā । sa bhaṇati kathaya kutrōpalabdhā tasyāḥ śuddhiriti ||27||
sa āha nātha ! dēvī saṁprati svargē surapatisamīpē । tiṣṭhati sukhēna tathā tava pārśvē prēṣitō'ham ||28||

supāsanāha - cariammi-
taha saṁdiṭṭhē ēyaṁ tumhāṇaṁ nāha ! ētyavatthāṇaṁ । na hu jutta jēṇēsō maṇustalōō adugaṁdha ||29||
vāhijarāduhakaliō, saggō uṇa ēyavirahiō rammō । taha jai maēvi kajjē tā sigghaṁ ējja iha nāha ! ||
tō bhaṇiyaṁ naravaiṇā daṁsaha saggassa vattaṇī majjha । picchāmi piyayamāē jēṇāhaṁ vimalamuhakamalaṁ ||31||
tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ narāhiva ! bhuṁjasu majjēsu kuṇasu siṁgāraṁ । rajjaṁ rahūṁ kōsaṁ saṁbhālasu ramasu dhammammi ||
jātra ahaṁ dēvīē gaṁtuṁ sāhēmi tumha āgamaṇaṁ । tō tavvayaṇēṇa nivō bhōyaṇamāī kuṇai sabbaṁ ||33||
yataḥ,
|
vivīvi buddhikaliōvi puinā hōtra hōu dakkhōva । gururāgagahagahiō aliyaṁpi viyāṇaē saccē ।
dēvī virakkatō paidiṇamavalōyaē purisamagaṁ । sōvi hu cirakālāō samāgaō nivāsamma ||35||
|
appēvi kaṣpapāyavaphalōtramē sakkarukkararasaḍḍhē । nāraṁgaphalē namiūṇa naravarō tō imaṁ bhaṇiō || 36 ||
dēvīē pēsiyāī dēva ! phalāī imāī saggāō । tuha bhaṇiyaṁ taṁ kahiyaṁ taha saṁdiṭṭhē ca maha jōgaṁ ||37|
maggēyō dēvō āharaṇaṁ jēṇa amararamaṇīṇaṁ । majjhē sōhāmi ahaṁ sālaṁkārā visēsēṇa ||38||
tō takkhaṇēṇa sacivē pabhaṇai rāyā imassa purisassa । dēvīē jamāihaṁ lahu āharaṇaṁ tamappēha ||39||
maṁtīhi tahā vihiyaṁ tassa niyaṁtassa tayaṇu bhaṁḍārē । pakkhiviḍaṁ sō purisō nigūhiō kaśvayadiṇāī ||
puṇaratri ēi vaēi ya gahium̐ āharaṇamāiyaṁ kiṁci । tō kēṇavi dhuttēṇaṁ nāō iya vaiyarō kavi || 41 |
tō tēṇa kaṇayapattaṁ bhujjava karāviūṇa ukkiriyā । tatthakkharāu bhariyā suyaṁdhakatthūriyara sēṇa ॥ 42 ॥
।
tathā saṁdiṣṭamētad yuṣmākaṁ nātha ! atrāvasthānam । na khalu yuktaṁ yēnaiṣa manuṣyalōkō'tidurgandhaḥ ॥ 29 ॥
vyādhijarāduḥkhakalitaḥ, svargaḥ punarētadvirahitō ramyaḥ । tathā yadi mamāpi kāryē tadā śīghramēyā iha nātha !
tatō bhaṇitaṁ narapatinā darśaya svargasya vartanīṁ mama । paśyāmi priyatamāyā yēnāhaṁ vimalamukhakamalam ॥ 31 ॥
tēna bhaṇitaṁ narādhipa ! bhuṅkṣva majja kuru śr̥ṅgāram । rājyaṁ rāṣṭraṁ kōśaṁ saṁbhālaya ramasva dharmē ||32||
yāvadahaṁ dēvīṁ gatvā kathayāmi tavāgamanam । tatastadvacanēna nr̥pō bhōjanādi karōti sarvam ||33||
vibhavyapi buddhikalitō'pi pr̥thivīnāthō'pi bhūtvā dakṣō'pi । gururāgagrahagr̥hītō'līkamapi vijānāti satyam
dēvīvirahākrāntaḥ pratidinamavalōkatē puruṣamārgam । sō'pi khalu cirakālātsamāgatō nr̥patipārśvē ॥ 35॥
arpayitvā kalpapādapaphalōpamāni śarkarōtkararasāḍhyāni । nāraṅgaphalāni natvā naravarastata idaṁ bhaṇitaḥ ||
dēvyā prēṣitāni dēva ! phalānīmāni svargāt । tava bhaṇitaṁ tatkathitaṁ tathā saṁdiṣṭaṁ ca mama yōgyam ॥37॥
mārgayitavyō dēva ābharaṇaṁ yēnāmararamaṇīnām । madhyē śōbhē'haṁ sālaṅkārā viśēṣēṇa ||38||
tatastatkṣaṇēna sacivān prabhaṇati rājā'sya puruṣasya । dēvyā yadādiṣṭaṁ ladhvābharaṇaṁ tadarpayata ॥ 39 ॥
mantribhistathāvihitaṁ tasya paśyatastadanu bhāṇḍāgārē । prakṣipya sa puruṣō nigūhitaḥ katipayadināni ॥
punarapyēti vanati ca gr̥hītvā''bharaṇādikaṁ kiñcit । tataḥ kēnāpi dhūrtēna jñāta iti vyatikaraḥ kathamapi ॥
tatastēna kanakapātraṁ bhūrjāmēva kārayitvōtkīrṇāni । tatrākṣarāṇi bhr̥tāni sugandhakastūrikārasēna || 42 ||

saṁvaṭṭi lēpi taṁ pattō sō nivassa pāsammi । bhaṇai ya dēvīē ahaṁ paviō lēhavāhōti ||43||
tō harisiō nariṁdō lēhaṁ gahiūṇa ciṁtaē nūṇaṁ । saggabhujaṁ khu ēyaṁ masīvi na hu maccalōīyā ॥ 44 ॥
kusala dēvīē taō sō purisō kahai pucchiō saṁtō। tō chōḍiūṇa lēhaṁ vāyai rāyā imaṁ tattha || 45 ॥
tadyathā; — svastiśrī purimatālē mahārājādhirājaśrīvijayapālapādāna śrīsvargād mahārājñī lakṣmīnāmā
-
sasnēhaṁ sōtkaṇṭhaṁ praṇamya vijñapayati yathā, kuśalamatra, kāryaṁ cēdam;
nicaṁ yiyagaṇaṁ dēva ! taē garuyabhārabhariyantra । ukkaṁṭhiyāvi dūraṁ na caēmi ahaṁ samāgamiuṁ ॥ 46 ॥
tā kāūna pasāyaṁ niyaṁgalaggaṁ samaggamābharaṇaṁ । niyataṇupharisapavittaṁ appēyavvaṁ mahanimittaṁ ॥ 47 ॥
kiśca ।
surasuṁdarīṇa majjhē lajjijjai tuhapasāyavirahēṇa । taha nivchaṇa mahaī sajāya majjhatā ittha ||48 ||
pakvatō mātō pēsijjasu jaṁtra taṁva vatthāī । iha buḍḍhapurisahatthē niyataṇukusalaṁ ca pasiūṇa ॥ 49 ॥
tō rannā maṁtiyaṇō bhaṇiō jaha majjha sāramābharaṇaṁ । varavatthakuṁkumāī pēsaha ēyarasa pāsamma ||50 ||
yataḥ,
saṁdēsagassa lakkhaṁ mullē lēhassa hōi dhaṇakōḍī । diṭṭhīē kōḍisayaṁ piyassa vayaṇaṁ puṇa amōllaṁ ॥ 51 ॥
maṁtīhini paḍivannaṁ tavvaṇaṁ citiuṁ jaha viṇaṭuṁ । kajjamiṇaṁ, tō maṁtivi tēhivi ēvaṁ nivō bhaṇiō ॥
kaha gamihī samima nivēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ jahāgaō, tēhiṁ । bhaṇiyaṁ dēviṣabhāvā samāgaō tō nivō bhaṇai ||
puvvillō jaha pagaō taha ēsōvi hu gamissaē tattha । maṁtīhiṁ tō bhaṇiyaṁ sihidaḍḍhō sō gaō saggē ||
saṁvartya lēkhamiva tatprāptaḥ sa nr̥pasya pārśvē । bhaṇati ca dēvyāhaṁ prasthāpitō lēkhavāha iti ॥ 43 ॥
1
tatō harṣitō narēndrō lēkhaṁ gr̥hītvā cintayati nūnam । svargabhūrjaṁ khalvētad maṣyapi na khalu martyalōkīyā ॥
kuśalaṁ dēvyāstataḥ sa puruṣaḥ kathayati pr̥ṣṭaḥ san । tataichōṭayitvā lēvaṁ vācayati rājēṁda tatra || 45 ॥
nityaṁ hr̥dayagatēna dēva ! tvayā gurubhārabhr̥tēva । utkaṇṭhitāpi dūraṁ na śaknōmyahaṁ samāgantum ||46 ||
tasmātkr̥tvā prasādaṁ nijāṅgalagnaṁ samagramābharaṇam । nijatanusparśapavitramarpayitavyaṁ mannimittam ||47 ||
surasundarīṇāṁ madhyē lajjyatē tvatprasādavirahēṇa । tathā nirbhatsanā mahatī saṁjāyatē mama tasmādatra || 48 ॥
pakṣāntō māsāntaḥ prēṣayēryadvā tadvā vastrādi । iha vr̥ddhapuruṣahastē nijatanukuśalaṁ prasadya ॥49॥
tatō rājñā mantrijanō bhaṇitō yathā mama sāramābharaṇam । varavastrakuṅkumādi prēṣayatētasya pārśvē ॥10॥
saṁdēśakasya lakṣaṁ mūlyaṁ lēkhasya bhavati dhanakōṭiḥ । dr̥ṣṭēḥ kōṭiśataṁ priyasya vacanaṁ punaramūlyam ॥ 51 ॥
mantribhirapi pratipannaṁ tadvacanaṁ cintayitvā yathā vinaṣṭam । kāryamidaṁ tatō mantrayitvā tairapyēvaṁ nr̥pō bhaṇitaḥ॥
kathaṁ gamiṣyati svargamayaṁ nr̥pēṇa bhaṇitaṁ yathāgataḥ taiḥ । bhaṇitaṁ dēvīprabhāvātsamāgatastatō nr̥pō bhaṇati ॥ 53॥
pūrvīyō yathā pragatastathaiṣō'pi hi gamiṣyati tatra । mantribhistatō bhaṇitaṁ śikhidagdhaḥ sa gataḥ svargam ॥ 54 ॥

supāsanāha - cariammi-
I
ēyassavi taha kijjau niṣēṇa iya jaṁpiyammi maṁtīhi । pajjaliyaciyābhimuhaṁ sō nijjatō kahavi divō ||
tattha va vasaṁtē paramabhihāṇēṇa mōhariyabhāvā । bārasavayajuttēṇavi, tō bhaṇiyaṁ tēṇa nivabhimuhaṁ ॥ 56 ॥
dēva ! imō aibūḍhō bahusaṁdēsēhi bhāriō dhaṇiyaṁ । na hu sakkistai gaṁtuṁ tā pēsasu kamavi taruṇanaraṁ ॥
maṁtīhi taō bhaṇiyaṁ dēva ! imōcciya saduttarō taruṇāṁ । muharō sigghagaī tō pahāvasu dēvipāsamma ||
ranā bhayaṁ ēvaṁ karēha tō takkhaṇēṇa maṁtīhi । baṁdhāviūṇa bāhi nijjai sō vilavāṇō ॥ 59॥
tō sē sayaṇā pucchati kēṇa dōsēṇa baṁdhiō bhāya ! । sō bhaṇai samuhadōsēṇa kōci nannō kaō dōsō ||
tō tunbhēhi niyatuṁḍa rakkhaṇaṁ savvahā u kāyavvaṁ । jēṇaṁ aṇatthadaṁḍa mōhariyattāu nō lahaha || 61 ||
aha sayaṇēhiṁ bhaṇi maṁti mōyāviō ya sō kahavi । tēṇavi sō karuṇāē mukkō paḍhamōvi sikkhaviō ।
annamma diṇē rāyā maṁtiyaṇa bhaṇai kahavi iha dēviṁ । āṇāvaha saggāō tabbirahē dukkhaō ahayaṁ ।
tō tēhi maṁtiūṇaṁ kamalasirīnāmiyā suruvavaī । nivaialaṁkāradharā navataruṇī vāhirujāṇē || 64 ॥
mukkā sikkhaviūrṇa, kahiyē tēhi nivassa jaha purisō | paṭṭaviō dēvīē āvahaṇatthaṁ harisamīvē ॥
tō vīyadi pattō sō purasō sāhaē narridassa । vaddhāvijjaha tubbhē ujjāṇē āgayā dēvī ||66 ||
vr̥ddhāvayassa niyaaṁgalaggamābharaṇamaha payacchēi । mahayā sāmaggīē paccōṇīē gaō rāyā ||67 ||
tō diṭṭhā sā dēvī jāō hiṭṭhō bhaṇēi bhō sacivā ! | dēvīē saggavāsō saccaviō rūvasōbhāē ||
purvitra tu imā sāmā ṭapparakannā ya visamagurudaṁtā । laṁbō civiḍanāsā saṁpa anēva paḍihāī || 69 ॥
ētasyāpi tathā kriyatāṁ nr̥pēṇēti jalpitē mantribhiḥ । prajvalitacitābhimukhaṁ sa nīyamānaḥ kathamapi dr̥ṣṭaḥ || 55 |
tatraiva vasatā padmābhidhānēna maukharyabhāvāt । dvādaśatratayuktēnāpi, tatō bhaṇitaṁ tēna nr̥pābhimukham ॥56॥
dēva ! ayamativr̥ddhō bahusaṁdēśaibharitō gāḍham । na khalu śakṣyati gantuṁ tasmātprēṣaya kamapi taruṇanaram ||17|
mantribhistatō bhaṇitaṁ dēva ! ayamēva saduttarastaruṇaḥ । mukharaḥ śīghragatistataḥ prasthāpaya dēvīpārśvē ||18||
rājñā bhaṇitamēvaṁ kuruta tatastatkṣaṇēna mantribhiḥ । bandhayitvā bahirnīyatē sa vilapannapi ||19||
tatastasya svajanāḥ pr̥cchanti kēna dōṣēṇa baddhō bhrātaḥ ! । sa bhaṇati svamukhadōṣēṇa kō'pi nānyaḥ kr̥tō dōṣaḥ ।
tatō yuṣmābhirapi nijatuṇḍarakṣaṇaṁ sarvathā tu kartavyam । yēnānarthadaṇḍaṁ maukharyānnō labhadhvam ||61||
atha svajanairbhaṇitvā mantriṇaṁ mōcitaśca sa kathamapi । tēnāpi sa karuṇayā muktaḥ prathamō'pi śikṣitaḥ |
anyasmindinē rājā mantrijanaṁ bhaṇati kathamapīha dēvīm । ānāyayata svargāttadvira hē duḥkhitō'ham ॥ 63 ॥
tatastairmantrayitvā kamalaśrīnāmikā surūpavatī । nr̥patyalaṅkāradharā navataruṇī bāyōdyānē ॥ 64 ॥
muktā śikṣayitvā kathitaṁ tairnr̥pasya yathā puruṣaḥ । prasthāpitō dēvyā āhvānārthaṁ harisamīpē ॥ 65 ॥
tatō dvitīyadinē prāptaḥ sa puruṣaḥ kathayati narēndrasya । vardhyadhvē yūyamudyāna āgatā dēvī ||66 ॥
vardhakāya nijāṅgalagnamābharaṇamatha prayacchati । mahatyā sāmagryā saṁmukhaṁ gatō rājā ॥ 67 ॥
tatō dr̥ṣṭā sā dēvī jātō hr̥ṣṭō bhaṇati bhō saciva ! | dēvyāḥ svargavāsaḥ satyāpitō rūpaśōbhayā ॥ 68 ॥

iya kavaḍavacaṇāvi hu caiyavvā sāvaēhiṁ savisēsaṁ । asamaṁjasabhāsāvi hu mōhariyattā na bhaṇiyantrā ।

॥ iti tr̥tīyapurāta maukharyāticāra vipākē padmakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥

tatastuṣṭēna rājñā nijakaryardhāsanē saṁsthāpya । gurupuraśōbhāpurassaramānītā mandirē nijē ||72 |
bhuṅktē vipulān bhōgāṁstayā samamasamarāgagatacittaḥ । pr̥cchati ca svargavārtā kathayati sā pūrvaśikṣitā ॥ 73 ॥
tatō bhō varjayata rāgaṁ yēna samāliṅgitā na jānanti । madhumattamānavā iva kāryākāryādikaṁ kimapi ॥74॥

yē gatavivēkavacanā padma iva labhantē duḥkhasaṁghātam । ta ihāpi paratra narakagatiṁ yānti niyamēna ॥ 76 ॥
tasmānmaukharyaṁ varjayitvā madhuranipuṇasaṁbaddham । niravadyamēva kathayata tarata bhavajalanidhiṁ yēna ||77 ||

saṁjutē jō gharaghaṭṭamusalukkhalāi ahigaraṇē । sō dulahōvva lahēī duhāī narayāipabhavāī || 1 ||
tathāhi;-
muṇijiṇavara supavittaṁ nicaṁ ciya usavēhiṁ avittaṁ । paracakaīicattaṁ āsi puraṁ pāḍalīputtaṁ ||2||
tatthathi vijayasiṭṭhī ajaō chajjīvakāyavahaṇampi । tassa piyā paumasirī sirivva jaṇanayaṇamaṇaharaṇī ॥
tāṇa taṇaō dulahā dulahō jassāsi sugurusaṁjōgō । sō jōvvaṇammi pattō aha annayā khillaē jūyaṁ ||
chinnōkannanāsēṇa saha taō jiṇai dammasayapaṇagaṁ । sō ya suvanaṁ viyarai pēyavaṇāō samāuṁ ॥ 5 ॥
tō puṭṭhō dulahēṇaṁ jūyakarō kassa pāsaō kahasu । pēyavaṇāō tuma āṇīyaṁ kaṇagamēyaṁti ? || 6 ||
sō bhai tēṇa kiṁ tē payaṇaṁ givha taṁ jiṇiyadavvaṁ । citai dulahō nūṇaṁ pēēṇava ahava bhūṣaṇa ||7||
siddhēṇa vāvi kēṇavi dinaṁ ēyassa tuṭṭacittēṇa । tō bhaṇai tassa samuhaṁ kaṇayaṁ giṇhasa tumaṁ cēva ||8||
pasiūṇaṁ kahasu phuḍaṁ dāyāraṁ puṇa imassa, sō bhai | jhāṇaṭhiō sō ciṭṭhai iṇhi tō jaṁgaē dulahō ||
jhāṭhiyē pihū daṁsasu tō tēṇa samuṭṭhēūṇa pēyavaṇē । ēgō muṇī mahayā padasiō tastra jhāṇaṭiō ||10||
tēṇaṁ namasiō sō iyarēṇavi tō gayā niyagihēsu । paidivasaṁ ciya dulahō muṇirūpa payapaṁkayaṁ namaḥ ||
paharadurga va ciṭṭha ciṭṭhiyaṁ pariniyaṁtō । aha muṇiṇā sō bhaṇiō sōma ! sudhammaṁ samajjiṇahi ॥
tō sō bhai sāmiya ! tuha payasēvāē kō parō dhammō ? । kiṁtu karuṇaṁ karēuṁ lūgassa va maha pasīya |
tō sō muṇiṇā bhaṇiō tēṇa tumaṁ bhōliō mahābhāga ! । na maē kiṁcivi dinnaṁ vayassa puṇa kāraṇa majjha ।।
saṁyuktāni yō dharatyaraghaṭṭamuśalōdūkhalādyadhikaraṇāni । sa durlabha iva labhatē duḥkhāni narakādiprabhavāṇi ॥1॥
munijinavarasupavitraṁ nityamēvōtsavairaviyuktam । paracakrētityaktamāsītpuraṁ pāṭalīputram ॥2॥
tatrāsti-vijayaśrēṣṭhī ayataḥ ṣaḍjīvakāyavadhē । tasya priyā padmaśrīḥ śrīriva jananayanamanōharaṇī || 3 ||
tayōstanayō durlabhō durlabhō yasyāsīd gurusaṁyōgaḥ । sa yauvanaṁ prāptō'thānyadā ramatē dyūtam ||4||
chinnauṣṭhakarṇanāsēna saha tatō jayati drammaśatapañcakam । sa ca suvarṇa vitarati prētavanāt samānīya || 5 ||
tataḥ pr̥ṣṭō durlabhēna dhūtakaraḥ kasya pārśvataḥ kathaya । prētavanāt tvayā''nītaṁ kanakamētaditi ? ॥ 6 ॥
sa bhaṇati tēna kiṁ tē prayōjanaṁ gr̥hāṇa tvaṁ jitadravyam । cintayati durlabhō nūnaṁ prētēna vāthavā bhūtēna ॥ 7 ॥
siddhēna vāpi kēnāpi dattamētasya tuṣṭacittēna । tatō bhaṇati tasya sammukhaṁ kanakaṁ gr̥hāṇa tvamēva ॥ 8 ॥
prasadya kathaya sphuṭaṁ dātāraṁ punarasya, sa bhaṇati । dhyānasthitaḥ sa tiṣṭhatīdānīṁ tatō jalpati durlabhaḥ ||9||
dhyānasthitamapi hi darśaya tatastēna samutthāya prētavanē । ēkō munirmahātmā pradarśitastasmai dhyānasthitaḥ ॥ 10 ॥
tēna namasthitaḥ sa itarēṇāpi tatō gatau nijagr̥hayōḥ । pratidivasamēṣa durlabhō munēḥ padapaṅkajaṁ namati ॥11॥
praharadvikamupaviṣṭastiṣṭhati taccēṣṭitaṁ paripaśyan । atha muninā sa bhaṇitaḥ sōma ! sudharmaṁ samarjaya ॥12॥
tataḥ sa bhaṇati svāmin ! tava padasēvāyāḥ kaḥ parō dharma: ? । kintu karuṇāṁ kr̥tvā lūnāṅgasyēva mayi prasīda
tataḥ sa muninā bhaṇitastēna tvaṁ vañcitō mahābhāga ! । na mayā kiñcidapi dattaṁ vratasya punaḥ kāraṇaṁ mama ॥

sō jāō tō sō bhaṇēi kaha nāha ! tumha vayagahaṇē । saṁjāō sō hēū, tō sūrī kahai tassa imaṁ ||
itthēva āsi siṭṭī sāgaradattōtti nāma daviṇaḍḍhō । aidaviṇarakkhaṇajjaṇaparāyaṇō savvakālaṁpi ॥
aha annayā sa maṁtai niyataṇayaṁ sōhaḍaṁ jahā vaccha ! । dukkhēṇa imā lacchī samajjiyā jāṇasi tumaṁpi ||
tamhā kīra rakkhā imī bāhiṁ gihassa dūrammi । gēhammi ṭhiyā saṁtī sāhīṇā savvalōyassa || 18 ||
tā pēyavaṇē gaṁtuṁ nihaṇijjau kammi rahapaēsammi । āvaigayāṇa jēṇaṁ sāhijjaṁ kuṇai amha imā ॥ 19 ॥
ēvaṁ rahampri maṁtivi taṇaēṇa samaṁ gaō masāṇammi | khaniūṇa guruṁ gataṁ nihaṇaṁti tarhi daviṇakala sē ||
pūrēūṇaṁ gataṁ bhaṇiō tō sēṭṭiṇā imaṁ taṇaō । putta ! palōēsa tumaṁ gaṁtuṁ savrvvapi disikaṁ ||21||
jara puṇa kēṇavidihaṁ havijja, sō bhaṇai tāya ! niuṇō taṁ । aibhīsaṇē masāṇē ramaṇīē ēikō ēttha ? ||
tō bhai piyā suniruviyassa iha hōi vaccha ! kō dōsō ? । iya bhaṇiē puttēṇaṁ gaṁtr̥ṇa nirūviyaṁ savvaṁ ।।
dō tō kapaḍiō paḍiō mayakhiḍḍa ēṇa gayaciṭṭhō । sāsaṁ niraṁbhiūṇaṁ davtradvāṇaṁ palōyaṁtō ||24||
drituṁ kahiyaṁ gayasāsō kōvi ciṭṭhaē tattha । tō siṭṭiṇāvi bhaṇiyaṁ jai puṇa sō davvalōbhēṇa ||
sunibhiūṇa sāsa paḍiō mayakhēḍḍayaṁ vihēūṇa । tā kiṁpi tassa agaṁ chēttuṁ churiyāē lahum̐ ēhi ||26||
iya kahiē takanaṁ chittūṇa samāgaō taō bhaṇiō । vīryapi chiṁda savaṇaṁ jai puṇa dhuttō iya sahēi ||
tēvi tava vihiyaṁ chinnā nāsāvi uṭṭauḍasahiyā । tēṇavi savvaṁ sahiyaṁ davvaṭṭā jēṇa iya bhaṇiyaṁ ॥
taṁ natthi jaṁ na kuvvaṁti pāṇiṇō sāhasaṁ daviṇakajjē । niyajīviyapi vicaṁti kiṁ puṇō chēvaṇaṁ taguṇō ? ||
sa saṁjātaḥ, tataḥ sa bhaṇati kathaṁ nātha ! tava vratagrahaṇē । saṁjātaḥ sa hētuḥ, tataḥ sūriḥ kathayati tasyēdam ॥
atraivāsīt śrēṣṭhī sāgaradatta iti nāma draviṇāḍhyaḥ । atidraviṇarakṣaṇārjana parāyaṇa: sarvakālamapi ॥ 16 ॥
athānyadā sa mantrayati nijatanayaṁ śōbhaṭa yathā vatsa ! | duḥkhēnēyaṁ lakṣmīḥ samarjitā jānāsi tvamapi ॥
tasmātkriyatāṁ rakṣā'syā bahirgr̥hād dūrē । gēhē sthitā satī svādhīnā sarvalōkasya ॥ 18॥
tasmātprētavanē gatvā nidhīyatāṁ kasminrahaḥ pradēśē । āpatānāṁ yēna sāhāyyaṁ karōtyasmākamiyam ॥19॥
ēvaṁ rahasi mantrayitvā tanayēna samaṁ gataḥ śmaśānē । khanitvā guruṁ garta nighattastatra draviṇakalaśān ॥20॥
pūrayitvā gartaṁ bhaṇitastataḥ śrēṣṭhinēdaṁ tanayaḥ । putra ! pralōkaya tvaṁ gatvā sarvamapi dikcakram ॥21॥
yadi punaḥ kēnāpi dr̥ṣṭaṁ bhavēt sa bhaṇati tāta ! nipuṇastvam | atibhīṣaṇē śmaśānē rajanyāmēti kō'tra ! ॥
tatō bhaṇati pitā sunirūpitasyēha bhavati vatsa ! kō dōṣa: ? । iti bhaṇitē putrēṇa gatvā nirūpitaṁ sarvam ।।
dr̥ṣṭastataḥ kāpaṭikaḥ patitō mr̥tacēṣṭayā gatacēṣṭaḥ । śvāsaṁ nirudhya dravyasthānaṁ pralōkamānaḥ ||24||
tēnāgatya kathitaṁ gataśvāsaḥ kō'pi tiṣṭhati tatra । tataḥ śrēṣṭhināpi bhaṇitaṁ yadi punaḥ sa dravyalōbhēna ||25||
sunirudhya śvāsaṁ patitō mr̥tacēṣṭāṁ vidhāya । tasmātkimapi tasyāṅgaṁ chittvā kṣurikayā lōhi ||26||
iti kathitē tatkarṇaṁ chittvā samāgatastatō bhaṇitaḥ । dvitīyamā chinddhi śravaṇaṁ yadi punardhūrta iti sahatē ||
tēnāpi tathaitra vihitaṁ chinnā nāsāpyōṣṭhapuṭasahitā । tēnāpi sarva sōḍhaṁ dravyārthaṁ yēnēdaṁ bhaṇitam ||28||

supāsanāha-cariasmi -
1
tō kapaḍiyaṁ mayaṁ kaliūṇa gaō gimmi sō siṭṭī । suyaparikaliō, ittō kappaḍiēṇāvi hu jhaḍatti ||
uṭṭhēūṇaṁ gahiyaṁ taṁ davvaṁ gōviyaṁ ca annattha । gahiuṁ kittiyamittaṁ pattō nayarammi givhēi ||31||
tyāgurukappūrappamuhāī nivasaṇēṇa suhumēṇa । pacchāiyaluyaaṁgō vilasai vēsāṇa gēhēsu ||32||
aha annayāya sōvi hu gaccha ujjōṇiyāē ujjāṇē । mōyagamaṁḍagavaḍayāī nēi tatthapaṇā saddhiṁ ||
nayarassa pāulāīvi tēṇaṁ sadāviyāī savvāī । hiṭṭhō tāṇa payacchai bhōyaṇavatthāiyaṁ savvaṁ ||34||
taha maggaṇāṇa jammaggirāṇa dīṇāiyāṇavi jahicchaṁ । tēvi hu tuṭṭhāvannati kannanāmaṁ vihēūṇa || 35 ॥
tō jaṇaparaṁparāē taṁ sōuṁ tassa saṁkiō siṭṭī । mama davvaṁ nō gahiyaṁ taṭṭāṇāō imēti || 36 ||
jaṛa puṇa sō kapaḍiō taiyā sāsaṁ niraṁbhiḍaṁ thakkō । iya ciṁtatō tassavi palōyaṇatthaṁ gaō tattha ||
pēcchai ya tayaṁ kuṁkumarpijariyē vēsalōyapariyariyaṁ । varavatthapihichinnōnāsiyaṁ citaē tattō ॥ 38 ॥
dukkhēṇa jō vippa atyō dukkhēṇa sujjaē sō u । cōracaraḍāṇa pāyaṁ cariyaṁ ēvaṁvihaṁ hōi ||39||
isa ciṁtiya samatāṇē pattō sō picchaē tayaṁ gattaṁ । kalasajyalēṇa rahiyaṁ ahiyē tō cilavium̐ laggō ||
hā divya ! davvanāsō kaha jāō majjha maṁdapunnassa ? | saccē ciya jaṁ kēvi viusē paḍhiyamēvaṁti ||
" dānaṁ bhōgō nāśastisrō gatayō bhavanti vittasya । yō na dadāti na bhuṅgē tasya tr̥tīyā gatirbhavati || "
naya mē dinaṁ dāṇaṁ na vilasiyaṁ vivihabhōgabhaṁgīhi । nāsōvi ya lacchīē jāō tō jāmi rāyaulē ||
savvaṁ kami rannō javi hu appāvara imāu dhaṇaṁ । tō kōsalliyaputraṁ sāhai rannō jahā dēva ! |
I
tannāsti yanna kurvanti prāṇinaḥ sāhasaṁ draviṇakāryē । nijajīvitamapi viyanti kiṁ punaśchēdanaṁ tanōḥ ? ॥
tataḥ kārpaṭikaṁ mr̥takaṁ kalayitvā gatō gr̥hē sa śrēṣṭhī । sutaparikalitaḥ, itaḥ kārpōṭikēnāpi hi jhaṭiti ||
utthāya gr̥hītaṁ tad dravyaṁ gōpitaṁ cānyatra । gr̥hītvā kiyanmātraṁ prāptō nagarē gr̥hṇāti ॥ 31 ॥
vastrāgurukarpūrapramukhāṇi nivasanēna sūkṣmēṇa । pracchāditalūnāṅgō vilasati vēśyānāṁ gēhēṣu ||32||
athānyadā ca sō'pi khalu gacchatyudyānika yōdyānē । mōdakamaṇḍakavaṭakāni nayati tatrātmanā sārdham ||33|
nagarasya gāyanā api tēna śabditāḥ sarvē । hr̥ṣṭastēbhyaḥ prayacchati śōbhanavastrādikaṁ sarvam ॥ 34 ॥
tathā mārgaṇēbhyō yanmārgayitr̥bhyō dīnādikēbhyō'pi yathēccham । tē'pi hi tuṣṭā varṇayanti karṇanāma vidhāya ॥ 35 ॥
tatō janaparamparayā tat śrutvā tasya śaṅkitaḥ śrēṣṭhī । mama dravyaṁ nō gr̥hītaṁ tatsthānādanēnēti ॥ 36 ॥
yadi punaḥ sa kāpaṭikastadā śvāsaṁ nirudhya sthitaḥ । iti cintayaṁstasyāpi pralōkanārthaṁ gatastatra ||37||
paśyati ca taṁ kuṅkamapiñjaritaṁ vēśyālōkaparikaritam । varavastrapihitacchannauṣṭhanāsikaṁ cintayati tataḥ ॥ 38॥
duḥkhēna yō'yētē'rthō duḥkhēna bhujyatē sa tu । cōracaraṭānāṁ prāyaścaritamēvaṁvidhaṁ bhavati ॥ 39 ॥
iti cintayitvā śmaśānē prāptaḥ sa paśyati taṁ gartam । kalaśayugalēna rahitamadhikaṁ tatō vilapituṁ lamaḥ ॥
hā daiva ! dravyanāśaḥ kathaṁ jātō mama mandapuṇyasya ! | satyamēva yatkēnāpi viduṣā paṭhitamēvamiti ॥ 41 ॥
naca mayā dattaṁ dānaṁ na vilasitaṁ vividhabhōgamaṅgībhiḥ । nāśō'pi ca lakṣmyā jātastatō yāmi rājakulē ||

525
ujāṇē jō vilasai vivipayārēhiṁ sō dhuvaṁ cōrō । maha davvaṁ ukkhaṇium̐ gahiyē imiṇā masāṇāō ||
iya suṇiuṁ naravaiṇā bhaṇiō ārakōi jahā simyaṁ । āṇē majjha pāsē baṁdhēuṁ taṁ mahācōraṁ || 45 ॥
tēvi tahēva vihiē tēṇō jaṁpēi majjha kō dōsō ? | bhai niyō tara atthō gahiō ēyassa ukkhaṇiuṁ ॥
sō bhai dēva ! imiṇā gahiyaṁ mama saṁtiyaṁ kimavi asthi । taṁ appāsu tō haṁ daviṇaṁ ēyarasa apissaṁ ||
rannā divē kammi vajjarai sō vaṇī na maē । gahiyaṁ kiṁcivi ēyassa jaṁpaē tō imaṁ tēṇō ॥ 48 ॥
pahasamakhinō narapahu ! tatthāhaṁ āsi nivbharaṁ suttō । nāsāvaṁsō savaṇā ya kaḍḍiyā maha imēṇēvaṁ ||
tāmaha ēsō savaṇāī apiḍaṁ lēu appaṇō davvaṁ । iya bhaṇiō sō siṭṭhī savilakkhō ṭhāi, ittō ya ॥
jayā isa apahasi siddhi ! savaṇāiyaṁ tathā davvaṁ । lahihasi taṁ ii bhaṇiḍaṁ visajjiyā dōvi naravaiṇā ॥
tō siṭṭī pitta puttaṁ pannavai jāyavēraggō । jaha lacchī vaccha ! gayā khaṇēṇa taha jīviyaṁ jāhī || 52 ||
jammāu jarā lōē jarāu maccū avassa dēhīṇaṁ । tamhā maccumuhagayā jīvā jīvaṁti vadiṇē || 53॥
tā jai tē paralōē gahiṁu saddhammasaṁbalē jati । tā dhuvamasōyaṇijjā suhiyā ya havaṁti tattha gayā || 54 ||
kiñca ।
pipatiṣuradya śvō vā jarāghuṇōtkīrṇadēhasā'pi । dharmaṁ prati nōdyacchati vr̥ddhapaśuḥ paśyata nirāśaḥ ॥
bālyē'sti yauvanāśā spr̥hayati ca yauvanē'pīha vr̥ddhatvam | mr̥tyūtsaṅgagatō'yaṁ vr̥ddhaḥ kimapēkṣya nirdharmā ? ||"
tāvaccha ! nicchaō mē gahiyantrō kōvi vayavisēsutti । caiūṇaṁ gihivāsaṁ duhavāsaṁ tā tumaṁ inhi ।। 55 ।।
niyajaṇaṇīpamuhajaṇaṁ pālatu dīṇēsu kuṇasu aṇurūpaṁ । davvēṇa na tuha khūṇaṁ hōhitti taō ō bhai ||26||
sarvaṁ kathayāmi rājñē yadi khalvarpayatyasmād dhanam । tataḥ kōśalikāpūrvaṁ kathayati rājñē yathā dēva ! ॥ 43 ॥
udyānē yō vilasati vividhaprakāraiḥ sa dhruvaṁ cauraḥ । mama dravyamutkhāya gr̥hītamanēna śmaśānāt ॥44॥
iti śrutvā narapatinā bhaṇita ārakṣikō yathā śīghram | ānaya mama pārśvē caddhvā taṁ mahācōram ||45 ॥
tēnāpi tathaiva vihitē stēnō jalpati mama kō dōṣa: ? । bhaṇati nr̥pastvayārthō gr̥hīta ētasyōtkhāya ॥ 46 ॥
sa bhaṇati dēva ! anēna gr̥hītaṁ mama saṁbandhi kimapyasti । tadarpaya tatō'haṁ draviṇamētasyāpayiṣyāmi ॥47॥
rājñā dr̥ṣṭikṣēpē kr̥tē kathayati sa vaṇig na mayā । gr̥hītaṁ kiñcidapyētasya jalpati tata idaṁ stēnaḥ ॥ 48 ॥
pathiśramakhinnō naraprabhō ! tatrāhumāēm̐ nirbharaṁ suptaḥ । nāsāvaṁśaḥ śravaṇau ca karṣitā mayānēnaivam ||49||
tasmānmamaiṣa śravaṇādyarpayitvā lātvātmanō dravyam । iti bhaṇitaḥ sa śrēṣṭhī savailakṣyastiṣṭhati, itaśca ॥50॥
yadā'syārpayasi śrēṣṭhin ! śravaṇādikaṁ tadā dravyam | lapsyasē tvamiti bhaṇitvā visarjitau dvāvapi narapatinā ॥
tataḥ śrēṣṭhī gr̥haprāptaḥ putraṁ prajñāpayati jātavairāgyaḥ । yathā lakṣmīrvatsa ! gatā kṣaṇēna tathā jīvitaṁ yāsyati ॥
janmanō jarā lōkē jarātō mr̥tyuravaśyaṁ dēhinām । tasmānmr̥tyumukhagatā jīvā jīvanti stōkadinān ॥53॥
tasmādyadi tē paralōkē gr̥hītvā saddharmaśambalaṁ yānti । tadā dhruvamaśōcanīyāḥ sukhitāśca bhavanti tatra gatāḥ ॥
tasmād vatsa ! niścayō mē grahītavyaḥ kō'pi vrataviśēṣa iti । tyaktvā gr̥hivāsaṁ duḥkhavāsaṁ tasmāttvamidānīm ॥

supāsanāha - variammi-
kēsi sayāsē givhihisi taṁ vayaṁ tāya ! kahasu, sō bhaṇai । niggacchaṁtassa gihāō hōrhiti ya majjha jēbhimuhaṁ ॥
iccāī paryapēḍaṁ caliō taṇaēṇa saha vahiṁ sēṭṭhī । tō suṭṭiyaāyariyā nāṇēṇābhōgi samuhā ||58 ||
pattā siṭṭhissa, ōsiṭṭhī tē vaṁdiuṁ bhaṇai ēvaṁ । niyadikkhā dāṇēṇaṁ kuṇasu pasāyaṁ tumaṁ bhaṁtē ! ||59 ||
tō vihiṇā tē siddhiṁ dikkhaṁti pabhāvaṇāē jiṇabhavaṇē । duvihaṁ sikkha vihiṇā giṇhai navadikkhiō sāhū ||
uciyasamaē patrajjai ēkkallavihāra paḍimamappaḍimaṁ । sō haṁ suvannadāyā jō kahiō tēṇa tēṇēṇa ||61 ||
iya taccariyaṁ sōuṁ saṁviggō dullahō bhāi ēvaṁ । bhayavaṁ ! bhavannavāō nityāraha dāum̐ gihidhammaṁ ||62 ||
tō muṇiṇāpannaviō sammattāī duvālasavihōvi । sāvayadhammō aṁgīkaō ya tēṇāvi vihipuvvaṁ ।। 63 ।।
piṇōvi vīryādivasē gurupāsāō davāvara dhammaṁ । pālaṁti payattēṇaṁ piyaputtā dōvi uvattā ॥ 64 ॥
aha dulahō kālē khalai pamāēṇa guṇavvaē taiē । savvāhigaraṇapaḍalaṁ payaḍatō paidiṇaṁ ēvaṁ ||65 ||
tathāhi ;-
--
khaggapharayāisatthē saṁjuttē gharai samuhabhittīē । savvāī vāhaṇāī taha pauṇāī gharaduvārē ||66 ||
musalukkha lahalaṁ tālakuṁṭikudāla muhasatthāṇaṁ | saṁjuttāṇaṁ dharaṇaṁ karēi abhimānaḍiō sō ||67 ||
kiṁ sōvi gihī bhannai jassa gihē nō imāī paḍaṇāī | ciṭṭhati sayākāla iya bhaṇai samudadhurō ni ||
sāhaṁkāraṁ nāuṁ nakōvi sikkhaṁ payaccha tassa । iya vañcatē kālē kēṇavi tabbālamittē ||69 ॥
nāmaṁkiyatakkhaggaṁ āsaṁghēṇaṁ amaggiuṁ nīyaṁ । samuhagharabhittīē vilaṁbamāṇaṁ palōēvaṁ ॥ 70 ॥
1
nijajananīpramukhajanaṁ pālaya dīnēṣu kuruṣvānukampām । dravyēṇa na tava bhrūṇaṁ bhaviṣyatīti tataḥ sutō bhaṇati ॥ 26 ॥
kēṣāṁ sakāśē grahīṣyasi tvaṁ vrataṁ tāta ! kathaya, sa bhaṇati । nirgacchatō gr̥hādbhaviṣyanti ca mama yē'bhimukham ||57॥ -
ityādi prajalpya calitastanayēna saha bahiḥ śrēṣṭhī । tataḥ susthitācāryā jñānēnābhōjya saṁmukhāḥ ॥ 18॥
prāptāḥ śrēṣṭhinaḥ, tataḥ śrēṣṭhī tān vanditvā bhaṇatyēvam । nijadīkṣādānēna kuru prasādaṁ tvaṁ bhadanta ! || 59॥
tatō vidhinā tē śrēṣṭhinaṁ dīkṣantē prabhāvanayā jinabhavanē । dvividhāṁ śikṣāṁ vidhinā gr̥hṇāti navadīkṣitaḥ sādhuḥ ॥
ucitasamayē prapadyata ēkākivihārapratimāmapratimām । sō'haṁ suvarṇadātā yaḥ kathitastēna stēnēna ॥ 61 ॥
iti taccaritaṁ śrutvā saṁvignō durlabhō bhaṇatyēvam । bhagavan ! bhavārṇavānnistārayata dattvā gr̥hidharmam ||62॥
tatō muninā prajñāpitaḥ samyaktvādirdvādaśavidhō'pi । śrāvakadharmō'ṅgīkr̥taśca tēnāpi vidhipūrvam ||63 ||
piturapi dvitīyadivasē gurupārśvāddāpayati dharmam । pālayataḥ prayatnēna pitāputrau dāvapyupayuktau ॥64॥
atha durlabhaḥ kālēna skhalati pramādēna guṇavatē tr̥tīyē । sarvādhikaraṇapaṭalaṁ prakaṭayanpratidinamēvam ॥65॥
khaḍgapharakādiśastrāṇi saṁyuktāni gharati saṁmukhabhittau । sarvāṇi vāhanāni tathā praguṇāni gr̥hadvārē ||66 ||
muśalōdūkhalahaladantālakuntikā kuṭhārapramukha śastrāṇām । saṁyuktānāṁ dharaṇaṁ karōtyabhimānanaṭitaḥ saḥ ||67||
kiṁ sō'pi gr̥hī bhaṇyatē yasya gr̥hē nō imāni praguṇāni । tiṣṭhanti sadākālamiti bhaṇati samuddharō nityam ||
sākāraṁ jñātvā na kō'pi śikṣāṁ prayacchati tasya । iti vrajati kālē kēnāpi tadbālamitrēṇa ॥69॥

niyagāmē gacchaṁtassa tassa khisiūṇa vāhaṇāhitō | paḍiyaṁ na tēṇa nāyaṁ taṁ pattaṁ ahimarēṇa taō ||
taṁ gahium̐ sō pattō pāḍaliputtammi rāyavahaṇatthaṁ । vaṭhāṇa jujjhaṇakaē puggāī davāvaē tattha ||72 ||
tō rāya ḍiyāē gaēṇa nisuyāī tassa puggāī । rannā tō āhūō sabhāsēuṁ samāhattō ||13||
tō tēṇa tēṇa khaggēṇa kōsakhittēṇa vāhiō ghāō । rannō sahasā tattō paḍikhaliō aṁgarakkhēṇa || 74 ॥
abhēṇa taō khagrga uddālēūṇaṁ ahimarō baddhō । haṇiō ya, tassa khaggaṁ samappiyaṁ nivaiṇō sōvi ।। 75 ।।
taṁ pātō pāsai dullahanāmakkharāī tattha nivō । tō rōsāruṇanayaṇō sacivaṁ sō bhai lahumēva ||76 ||
kō sō dulahanāmā ēvaṁ muṇiūṇa majjha sāhēsu । khaggavaḍayāṇa sigdhaṁ sō daṁsai jēṇa ghaḍiyaṁ taṁ ॥ 77 ॥
sō bhai maē ghaḍiyaṁ ēvaṁ sirisiddhivijayataṇayassa । dullahanāmassa kaē sēsaṁ tu na kiṁpi jāṇēmi ॥
tō sacivēṇaṁ rannō nivēyaṁ sō bhai saṁbhavai । tassa sayāsē ēyaṁ jamhā sō rāyamāṇī ya ॥ 79 ॥
tō aṁgarakkhalōyaṁ nirūar taggihammi haṭṭammi । muddāō dāvāvara āṇāvara taṁpi baṁdhēuṁ ॥ 80 ॥
puṭṭīēsiḍivijaō sayaṇajuō naravariṁdapāsammi । kōsalliyaṁ vihēuṁ paṇamiya vinnava naranāhaṁ ॥ 81 ॥
kiṁ dēva! majjha taṇaō cōrōvva niyaṁtiuṁ ihāmīō ? । tivalīta raṁgabhaṁgurabhālō tō bhūvaī bhai ||82||
maha ahimaraṁ nirūvai vaṇiōvi hu rajjakaṁkhirō bhamai । tō siṭṭī pāēsuṁ laggēuṁ bhaṇai jaha dēva ! ||83 ||
nō ghara imaṁ kavi hu tō rāyā daṁsaē kivāṇaṁ taṁ । tō saṁbhaṁtō siṭṭī vinnavai nivassa jaha dēva ! ॥ 84॥

taṁ gr̥hītvā sa prāptaḥ pāṭalīputrē rājavadhārtham । bhr̥tyānāṁ yōdhanakr̥tē pūtkr̥tāni dāpayati tatra ॥ 72 ॥
tatō rājavāṭikāyāṁ gatēna śrutāni tasya pūtkr̥tāni । rājñā tata āhūtaḥ saṁbhāṣituṁ samārabdhaḥ ॥73॥
tatastēna tēna khaḍgēna kōśakṣiptēna vyāhitō ghātaḥ । rājñaḥ sahasā tataḥ pratiskhalitō'ṅgarakṣaṇa ॥ 74 ॥
anyēna tataḥ khaḍgamuddālyābhimarō baddhaḥ । hataśca tasya khaḍgaḥ samarpitō nr̥patayē sō'pi ॥ 75 ॥

taṁ paśyanpaśyati durlabhanāmākṣarāṇi tatra nr̥paḥ । tatō rōṣāruṇanayanaḥ sacivaṁ sa bhaṇati ladhvēva ॥76॥
kaḥ sa durlabhanāmaitajjñātvā mama kathaya । khaṅgaghaṭakēbhyaḥ śīghraṁ sa darśayati yēna ghaṭitaḥ saḥ ॥77॥
sa bhaṇati mayā ghaṭita ēṣa śrīśrēṣṭhivijayatanayasya । durlabhanāmnaḥ kr̥tē śēṣaṁ tu na kimapi jānāmi ॥78॥
tataḥ satrivēna rājñē nivēditaṁ sa bhaṇati saṁbhavati । tasya sakāśa ēṣa yasmātsa rājamānī ca || 79 ||
tatō'ṅgarakṣakalōkaṁ nirūpayati tadgr̥hē haṭṭē | mudrā dāpayatyānāyayati tamapi baddhvā ॥ 80 ॥
pr̥ṣṭhē śrēṣṭhivijayaḥ svajanayutō naravarēndrapārśvē । kauśalikāṁ vidhāya praṇamya vijñapayati naranātham ॥ 81 ॥
kiṁ dēva ! mama tanayaścaura iva niyantryēhānītaḥ ? । trivalītaraṅgabhaṅgurabhālastatō bhūpatirbhaṇati ॥ 82॥
manābhimaraṁ nirūpayati vaṇigapi khalu rājyakāṅkṣitā bhramati । tataḥ śrēṣṭhī pādayōrlagitvā bhaṇati yathā dēva ! ॥83॥
nō ghaṭata idaṁ kathamapi hi tatō rājā darśayati kr̥pāṇaṁ tam । tataḥ saṁbhrāntaḥ śrēṣṭhī vijñapayati nr̥pāya yathā dēva ! ॥

gayabaṁdhaṁ kāūṇaṁ dulahaṁ iha āṇavēsu pasiūṇa । jēṇa jahatthaṁ sāhai sōcciya khaggassa vr̥ttaṁtaṁ ॥ 85 ॥
tō rāyāsēṇaṁ dulahō tatthāgaō nivaṁ namiuṁ । uvavihō tō puṭṭhō nivēṇa khaggaṁ tuha kimēvaṁ 1 || 86 ॥
sō bhai dēva ! āmaṁ kiṁtu imaṁ gāmavāsimittēṇa । amugēṇaṁ āsi nīyaṁ maēvi pacchāṁ imaṁ nāyaṁ ॥ 87 ॥
tō takkhaṇēṇa cariyē pēsēuṁ sōvi āṇiō minō । puṭṭō ya nariṁdēṇaṁ dullahakhaggaṁ tumē nīyaṁ ॥ 88 ॥
jaṁ taṁ kattha iyāṇi, sō sāhai dēva ! majjha pāsāō । khisiūṇa tathā paḍiyaṁ jāṇāmi na kēṇa taṁ pattaṁ ॥
tō rannā tasta karē samappiyaṁ taṁ imaṁ tu sō puṭṭhō khaggamiṇaṁ taṁ nō yā, taṁ caiva imaṁti sō bhai ॥ 90 ॥
tō saciva bhaṇa: imaṁ hōi jugatēvi nēya ēyāṇaṁ । dēu karaṁ puṭṭhīra dēvō gacchaṁtu sadvāṇaṁ ॥ 91 ॥
tō dulahaṁ para jaṁpai rāyā rē tujjha vaṇiyamittassa । kiṁ naṇu hōhī kajjaṁ kiṁvāṇarayaṇēhiṁ ēēhi ? ॥ 92 ॥
āṇāviya savvāī khaggāī nivēṇa tassa gēhāō । niyagēhē ṭaviyāī, mukkō sō niyagihē pattō ॥ 93 ॥
baṁdhē pīḍiyēgō bhariō ruhirassa sattamadiṇammi | apaḍikkatō yamaō sahihī bahudukkha lakkhāī ||94||
vijaō siṭṭī ārāhiūṇa saṁmpattamāigihidhammaṁ । sōhammē uvannō taiyabhavē sajjhihī ittha || 95|
॥ iti tr̥tīyaguṇavatē caturthāticāravipākē durlabhakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
gatabandhaṁ kr̥tvā durlabhamihānāyaya prasadya । yēna yathārtha kathayati sa ēva khaḍgasya vr̥ttāntam ||85||
tatō rājādēśana durlabhastatrāgatō nr̥paṁ natvā । upaviṣṭastataḥ pr̥ṣṭō nr̥pēṇa khaḍgastava kimēṣaḥ ? ॥ 86 ॥
sa bhaṇati dēva ! āma kintvayaṁ grāmavāsimittrēṇa । amukēnāsīd nītō mayāpi paścādidaṁ jñātam ॥87॥
tatastatkṣaṇēna caryaṁ prēṣya tadapyānītaṁ mittram । pr̥ṣṭaṁ ca narēndrēṇa durlabhakhagastvayā nītaḥ ॥ 88 ॥
1
• yaḥ sa kutrēdānīṁ, sa kathayati dēva ! mama pārśvāt । satvā tadā patitō jānāmi na kēna sa prāptaḥ ॥89॥
tatō rājñā tasya karē samarpitaḥ sa idaṁ tu sa pr̥ṣṭaḥ । khaḍgō'yaṁ sa nō vā, sa ēvāyamiti sa bhaṇati ||9||
tataḥ sacivō bhaṇatīdaṁ bhavati yugāntē'pi naivaitēṣām । dadātu karaṁ pr̥ṣṭhē dēvō gacchantu svasthānam ॥91॥
tatō durlabhaṁ prati jalpati rājā rē tava vaṇikputrasya । kiṁ nanu bhaviṣyati kāryaṁ kr̥pāṇaratnairētaiḥ ? ॥92॥
ānāyya sarvē khaḍḍā nr̥pēṇa tasya gēhāt । nijagēhē sthāpitāḥ, muktaḥ sa nijagr̥hē prāptaḥ ||93 ||
bandhaiḥ pīḍitāṅgō bhr̥tō rudhirēṇa saptamadinē । apratikrāntaśca mr̥taḥ sahiṣyatē bahuduḥ khalakṣāṇi ॥ 94 ॥
vijayaḥ śrēṣṭhyārādhya samyaktvādigr̥hidharmam । saudharma upapannastr̥tīyabhavē sētsyatyatra ॥95॥

tathāhi: --
parapurisōvadavarakakhagēṇa sakkhāiēṇa tuṁgēṇa । sappurisēṇava sālēṇa sōhiyā āsi bharahami ||2 ||
kaṁcī nāmēṇa purī tattha nivō rāyasēharō sōmō । jahavaṭṭiyābhihāṇō gayavasaṇō bhūikaliō ya || 3 ||
siṭṭhī vivō basa tarhi nāmaō ya guṇakaliō | vēsamaṇō, tassa suā nāmēṇaṁ mūladēvōtti ॥4॥
sō jōvvaṇamaṇupattō nīō kēṇāvi sāhumūlammi । vimhayaparantrasō sō taṁ paṇamai paramabhattīē ||5||
sāhūvi sajalajalahara guruga hiraravēṇa dēi āsīsaṁ । uvavisiya dharaṇiva suṇai dhammaṁ taō sōvi || 6 ||
pucchai i patthāvē bhayava ! vēraggakāraṇaṁ garuyaṁ । kiṁti tuha jēṇa niyataṇunirakhakkhō carasi tavacaraṇaṁ ? |
bhai muṇivariṁdō saṁsārē pauradukkhabhaṁḍārē । vēraggakāraṇaṁ kimiha nēya, sammaṁ vicitēha ||8||
iha jaṁ jaṁ ciya dīsai rāganimittaṁ sarāgapurisāṇa । taṁ taṁ ciya nīsēsaṁ vēraraṁgakaraṁ vivēīṇa ॥ 9 ॥
niyacittaviyappēṇaṁ mr̥ṇaṁti jaha suṁdaraṁ maha sarīraṁ । asuibhariyaṁpi taha cēva suṁdaraṁ ēttha savrvvapi ॥ 10 ॥
paramatthasuhavihīṇē niyama parikapaṇākayasuhammi | paramatyapaṁḍiyāṇaṁ saṁsārē hōi nivvēō || 11||
sō puṇa sanimittōtā susu jaṁ ittha majjhavi nimittaṁ । asthi avaṁtīvisaē ujjēṇī puravarī rammā || 12 |
maṇaharalāyaṇṇubbhaḍajōvvaṇavararūvasuṁdaravilāsā | vēsā vilāsavasahī nāmēṇa guṇēṇa tatthatthi || 13 ||
agra bhinnaṁjaṇapuṁjapēsalā vēṇivallarī jīē । mahumitta vallahāē vilōyaṇaṁjaṇa salāyantra || 14 ||
kiṁ bahunā ।
tr̥tīyaguṇavratadhāryatirēkīṇi yaḥ karōti bhōgāṅgāni । sa prāpnōti paramaduḥkhamihāpi vaṇigmūladēvavat ॥ 1॥
parapuruṣōpadravarakṣakēṇa sakhā ( khyā) tikēna tuṅgēna । satpuruṣēṇēva śālēna śōbhitā''sīdbharatē ॥2॥
kāñcī nāmnā purī tatra nr̥pō rājaśēkharaḥ sōmaḥ । yathāvr̥ttābhidhānō gatavyasanō bhūtikalitaśca ||3||
śrēṣṭhī viśiṣṭavibhavō vasati tatra nāmataśca guṇakalitaḥ । vaiśramaṇaḥ, tasya sutō nāmnā mūladēva iti ॥4॥
sa yauvanamanuprāptō nītaḥ kēnāpi sādhumūlē । vismayaparavaśaḥ sa taṁ praṇamati paramabhaktyā ॥5॥ -
sādhurapi sajalajaladharagurugabhīraravēṇa dadātyāśiṣam । upaviśya dharaṇipaṭṭē śr̥ṇōti dharma tataḥ sō'pi ॥ 6 ॥
pr̥cchatīti prastāvē bhagavan ! vairāgyakāraṇaṁ guru । kimiti tava yēna nijatanunirapēkṣaścarasi tavaścaraṇam ? || 7 |
tatō bhaṇati munivarēndraḥ saṁsārē pracuraduḥkhabhāṇḍāgārē | vairāgyakāraṇaṁ kimiha naiva, samyag vicintaya ॥8॥
iha yadyadēva dr̥śyatē rāganimittaṁ sarāgapuruṣāṇām । tattadēva niḥśēṣaṁ vairāgyakaraṁ vivēkinām ||9||
nijacittavikalpēna jānanti yathā sundaraṁ mama śarīram | aśucibhr̥tamapi tathaiva sundaramatra sarvamapi ॥10॥
paramārthasukhavihīnē nijamatiparikalpanākr̥tasukhē । paramārthapaṇḍitānāṁ saṁsārē bhavati nirvēdaḥ ॥11॥

avirayacāvayaṭṭhaṇapagāḍhamuṣṭiyassa kusumacāyassa | mannāmi hatthabhallī jayavijayatthaṁ imāṁ siṭṭā ||15||
vīravilāsabhihāṇō tatthavi ya vaṇī dhaṇī sayākālaṁ । bhōgī cāī viusō aha annayā tēṇa sā diṭṭhā ।
vimviyaṁtī bahupariyaṇaparigayā rahārūḍhā । gāḍhaṁ suratacittō tīē pāsammi pēsēi ||17||
niyamāṇusa gahēḍaṁ kaṇayasyaṁ ēgarattagahaṇammi | sā bhaṇai mattahatthiṁ ēgaṁ mē dēhi rattī || 18 ||
jai mē paōyaṇaṁ tuha ēvaṁ gaṁtūṇa kahasu niyapahuṇō | tēṇavi āgaṁtr̥ṇaṁ kahiyaṁ savvaṁpi tayabhimuhaṁ ||19|
iya sōūṇa sōvi hu aidiḍharāgō u tīi uvarimmi । gayahēḍatthaṁ caliō viṁjhāḍavisamuha jamhā ||20|
taṁ natthi jaṁ na kuvrvvati itthaṁ itthīkaraṇa rādhā । taha bhaṇiyaṁ satthēsuṁ viusēhivigahā ēvaṁ || 21 ||
“yad gāyanti ca vādayanti caṁ nr̥ṇāṁ nr̥tyanti cāgrē sadā, nīcānāmapi citracāṭuracanāstōtrāṇi kurvanti ca ।
ārōhanti ca rōhaṇādriśikharaṁ krāmanti cāmbhōnidhiṁ, martyāstaṁtra nimittamuttamatamā mattēbhakumbhastanī
apahr̥tahr̥dayānāṁ kāmināṁ kāminībhiḥ kimiha bhavati kāmaṁ duṣkaraṁ hrīkaraṁ ca ।
vahati śirāsa gaṅgāṁ śaṅkarō, dānavāriḥ punarurasi salīlāṁ lōlanīlōtpalākṣīm ॥"
aha pattō viṁjhagirissa aṁtiē sō kamēṇa tattha puṇō । bahuvarisēhiṁ laddhā pahāṇakariṇō taō caliō ।
niyapuravarīē samuhaṁ pattō ya kamēṇa nidhayagēhammi । pucchēi tīē vēsāē ēsa pati viḍē bahuē ||23||
tēvi ya bhaṇati nō asthi kāi iyanāmiyā ihaṁ bēsā । tō sō divāṇē sayaṁ gaō vēsapāsmi ||24
pucchai vēsāva kattha gayā sā vilāsavasahitti ? | amugammi gihē ciṭṭhā iya bhaṇiē jāi sō tattha ||
ōṇā miuttamaṁga hatthāyilaṭṭhivihiyavaṁ । nāṇāvalisayakaliyē sasikara siya kē sapa-bhāraṁ ||26||
•
rājatē bhinnāñjana putra pēśalā vēṇīvallarī yasyāḥ । madhumistravallabhāyā vilōcanāñjanaśalāṁkēva ॥ 1-4 ॥
aviratacāpāvartanapragāḍhaśrāntasya kusumacāpasya । manyē hastabhallī jagadvijayārthamiyaṁ sr̥ṣṭā ॥15॥
vīravilāsābhidhānastatrāpi ca vaṇig dhanī sadākālam । bhōgī tyāgī vidvān, athānyadā tēna sa dr̥ṣṭā ||
vipaṇipathē vrajantī bahuparijanaparigatā rathārūḍhā । gāḍhaṁ suraktacittastasyāḥ pārśvē prēṣayati ||17||
nijamānuṣaṁ gr̥hītvā kanakaśatamēkarātragrahaṇē । sā bhaṇati mattahastinamēkaṁ mē dēhi rātryai ॥ 18 ॥
yadi mē prayōjanaṁ tavaitadgatvā kathaya nijaprabhōḥ । tēnāpyāgatya kathitaṁ sarvamapi tadabhimukham ॥19॥
iti śrutvā sō'pi khalvatidr̥ḍharāgastu tasyā upari । gajaghaṭārtha calitō vindhyāṭavīsaṁmukhaṁ yasmāt ॥ 20 ॥
tannāsti yanna kurvantyatra strīkr̥tē rāgāndhāḥ । tathā bhaṇitaṁ śāstrēṣu vidvadbhirapyanēkadhaivam ॥21॥
atha prāptō vindhyagirērantikaṁ sa kramēṇa tatra punaḥ । bahuvarṣērlabdhāḥ pradhānakariṇastataścalitaḥ ॥22॥
nijapurīvarāyāḥ saṁmukhaṁ prāptaśca kramēṇa nijagēhē । pr̥cchati tasyā vēśyāyā ēṣa pravr̥ttiṁ vidānbahūn ॥ 23 ॥
tē'pi ca bhaṇanti nō asti kāciditināmikēha vēśyā । tataḥ sa diṣṭasthānē svayaṁ gatō vēśyāpāṭakē ||24|
pr̥cchati vēśyāvarga kutra gatā sā vilāsavasatiriti ! | amuṣmin gr̥hē tiṣṭhatīti bhaṇitē yāti sa tatra ||25|
avanamitōttamāṅgāṁ hastasthitayaṣṭivihitāvaṣṭambhām । nānāvaliśatakalitāṁ śaśikarasitakēśaprāgbhārām ॥

lāyannavajjiyataṇū lālilla yadasaṇara hiyamuhabhāyaṁ । ullaṁbiyabuka saricchadīhalaṁbaṁ tathaṇajuyalaṁ ||27||
dūsiyamayanayaṇaṁ thēri daṭṭūṇa taṁpi pucchēi । vattaṁ vilāsatrasahīē sāvi jaṁpēṛa taya bhimu ||28||
।
kiṁ kajjai tuha tīē, sambhāvē sāhiyammi sā bhaṇai । ēsā sāhaṁ vasahī haḍḍukaraḍassa ciṭṭhāmi ||29||
ō ! patthiyā vilāsā tava hē atthi saṁpai vilāsā । tō takkhaṇēṇa jāō tassa virāgō maṇē garuō ॥
tō sōcita dhiddhī caṁcalayā jōvvaṇassa payaīē । jaṁ daṭhṭhē rattō haṁ tī avasthā imā jāyā ॥ 31 ॥
tathāhi--
1
aisa ralataraladhavalā imīē jē āsi acchivicchōhā | taruṇajaṇahiyayaharaṇā tē saha acchīrhivi paṇaṭṭā ॥
aliulakajjalakasiṇō imīē jō āsi kuṁtalakalāvō । sō saṁpai camarīsēyapucchalacchiṁ viḍaṁbēi ||33||
kuṁdaliyāvalikibhamā ēīē āsi jē dasaṇā । jararakkhasīya bhīyā tē saṁpai dūraō naṭṭhā ||34||
iya bhāviūṇa pattō gimmi dāūṇa tattha bahudāṇaṁ । jiṇamaṁdirēsu mahimaṁ kāuṁ pañcayai, sō ya ahaṁ ॥
iya suṇivi mūladēvō jaṁpai jīvāṇa hutigāī । vēraggakāraṇāī paraṁ tumaṁ cētra iya kuṇasi ॥ 36 ॥
kāraṇē saṁtēvi majjha natthi nivvēō । bhōgapivāsānaḍiyassa nāha! tā disasu gihidhammaṁ ।
tō kahiō sē muṇiṇā gihatyadhammō duvālasavihōvi । tēṇavi sō paḍivō tō taṁ nami siṁha pattō ॥
pālai kittiyakālaṁ bhōgapivāsāē vinaḍiō pacchā । lacchīpa urattaṇaō pamāyavasagō visēsēṇa ||39||
airēgabhōgaaṁgēsu mucchiō kāravēi aipauraṁ । ōyaṇarvajaṇa muddē pahāṇaṁgaṁ khalijalāīyaṁ ॥ 40 ॥
lāvaṇyavarjitatanuṁ lālāvaddaśanarahitamukhabhāgām । ullambitamuṣṭisadr̥kṣa dīrghalambamānastanayugalām ॥27॥
dūṣitadāvitanayanāṁ sthavirāṁ dr̥ṣṭrā tāmapi pr̥cchati । vr̥ttaṁ vilāsavasatēḥ sāpiṁ jalpati tadabhimukham ||28||
kiṁ kāryaṁ tava tasyāḥ, sadbhāvē kathitē, sā bhaṇati । ēṣā sāhaṁ vasatirasthyutkarasya tiṣṭhāmi ॥29॥
āḥ ! prasthitā vilāsā tava hētōrasti saṁprati vilāsyā । tatastatkṣaṇēna jātastasya virāgō manasi guruḥ ॥
tataḥ sa cintayati vigdhik cañcalatā yauvanasya prakr̥tyā । yāṁ dr̥ṣṭvā raktō'haṁ tasyā avasthēyaṁ jātā ॥ 31 ॥
atisaralataraladhavalā asyā ya āsannakṣivikṣōbhāḥ । taruṇajanahr̥dayaharaṇāstē sahākṣibhyāmapi pranaṣṭāḥ ||32||
alikulakajjalakr̥ṣṇō'syā ya āsītkuntalakalāpaḥ । sa saṁprati camarīśvētapucchalakṣmīṁ viḍambayati ||33||
kundakalikāvalīvibhramā ētasyā āsan yē daśanāḥ । jarārākṣasyā bhītāstē saṁprati dūratō naṣṭāḥ ||34||
iti bhāvayitvā prāptō gr̥hē dattvā tatra bahudānam | jinamandirēṣu mahimānaṁ kr̥tvā pravrajati, sa cāham ॥35॥
iti śrutvā mūladēvō jalpati jīvānāṁ bhavantyanēkāni । vairāgyakāraṇāni paraṁ tvamēvēti karōṣi ॥36॥
vairāgyakāraṇēṣu saṁtsvapi mama nāsti nirvēdaḥ । bhōgapipāsānaṭitasya nātha ! tasmāddiśa gr̥hidharmam ||37||
tataḥ kathitastasya muninā gr̥hasthadharmō dvādaśavidhō'pi । tēnāpi sa pratipannastatastaṁ natvā gr̥haṁ prāptaḥ ॥
pālayati kiyatkālaṁ bhōgapipāsayā vinaṭitaḥ paścāt । lakṣmīpracuratvataḥ pramādavaśagō viśēṣēṇa ||39||
atirēkabhōgāṅgēṣu mūrcchitaḥ kārayatyatipracuram | ōdanavyañjanapramukhaṁ snānāṅgaṁ khalijalādikam ॥40॥

bhai ya ki sō bhōgī jassaṁganimittabhōgaaṁgēsu । uvvariēsu na vilasai sēvayalōō jahicchāē ? ||
tō tassa lahu bhaiṇī gihidhammaṭhiyā bhaṇēi tayabhimuhaṁ । jai atthakhayaṁ na gaṇasi tā kiṁ bīhasina pāvāō ? ।।

hu
sō bhai jahā bhaiṇīvaissa maha bhaiṇi kivaṇasiramaṇiṇō । nitthāraē na kāōvi paḍēi taha maha gihē kuṇasi ||

marai chuhāē nicca kahakahavi hu bhuṁjaē viyālammi | vāsiyamattañcariyassa dūraō tāva vattāvi ||46 ||
iya sunivi sēvayajaṇō tayabhimuhaṁ bhaṇai lōyapaccava । krūrasamuddō amhāṇa sāmiō mūladēvōti ||47 ||
anējaṇa savvēvi niyauyaraṁ pūrayaṁti kaṭṭhēṇa । tavtrayaṇēṇuddhasiō sō bhaiṇi bhaṇai mā ēvaṁ ॥ 48 ॥
kaiyāvi dijjaṁ sikkhaṁ abhikkhaṇaṁ ditalitayastra mahaṁ । gacchaṁtu imē divasā kharṇādihaviṇavihavassa ॥
phalamēyaṁ ciyajaṁ sayaṇaparijaṇō upayarijjai sayāvi । iya bhaṇiyā sā bhaiṇī mōrṇa avalaṁbiūṇa ṭhiyā ||
aha saṇavārē pattē tillāmalayāī āṇavāvēḍaṁ । vāhiṁ naīē pattō nhāṇatthaṁ saparivārō sō ॥51॥
tattha ya sēvayalōō abbhaṁguṇamivatō । jā ciṭṭā tā kattō pattō pahiyāṇa saṁghāō || 52 ||
tammajjhāō kēvi khalitēlluvvaṭṭaṇāī daṭṭṇaṁ । aipaurayaraṁ bhaṇiō krūrasamuddassa kōvi narō ॥ 53 ॥
thēvaṁ maha tēllāī jai appara tumha sāmiō kahavi । tā majjaṇaṁ karēmō iya suṇiuṁ mūladēvēṇa || 54 ||
bhaṇati ca kiṁ sa bhōgī yasyāṅganimittabhōgāṅgēṣu । udvr̥ttēṣu na vilasati sēvakalōkō yathēccham ॥41॥
tatastasya laghubhaginī gr̥hidharmasthitā bhaṇati tadabhimukham । yadyarthakṣayaṁ na gaṇayasi tataḥ kiṁ bibhyasi na pāpāt ? ||

bhaṇiyāṇamapsu jattiya jāitēllābhiīyaṁ । iya sōuṁ tē saccē sicchāē liti tillāī ||55 ||

kūrasamudaṁ bhaṇiuṁ tō tēṇa tāṇa bhōgaṇaṁ dinaṁ । gēhāō tattha mōyagaōyaṇamaṁḍāi āṇaviuṁ ॥ 57 ॥
iya bahutē kattō tēsiṁ pahiyāṇa vērisaṁghāō । haṇa haṇa haṇattibhaṇirō pattō tāvari paharaṁtō ||58||

iya bhaṇiyāvi hu tēṇaṁ pahiyā jhaḍajhaḍatti paharaṁti । tēsipi jō pahuppai sō samuhō hōi vērīṇaṁ || 63 ||

hra annavatthaṁ vimukkavāṇēṇa āhaō tattha । kūrasamuddō tattō paṁcataṁ jhatti saṁpattī ||35||

sāmāiyaṁvtrayaṁ jō karēi sāvajjajōgapaḍivakvaṁ । sō nāgadattakumaravva pāvaē paramasukkhāī ॥1॥
tathāhi —
tuṁga jiṇabhavaṇasiharaggabhaggaravirahaturaṁgagaipasaraṁ । sīhauraṁ nāma puraṁ iha bharahē āsi supasiddhaṁ ||2||
tammi nivō riumallō nimmūlīkayamahallamallōhō । tassatthi paṇaiṇī pēmakulaharaṁ vasumaī nāma || 3 ||
sā annayā pasuttā pāsai sumiṇammi pacchimanisāē । phāraṣphaṇākaḍappaṁ sappaṁ dippaṁtamaṇiruiraṁ ||4||
tatō sāpaḍabuddhā sāhai sumiṇaṁ piyassa sō bhaṇai । daiē ! ēsō sumiṇō suputtalābhaṁ phuḍa kahai ||
tā tuha taṇaō hōhī dharavalaē ēgachattarajjakarō । sā bhaṇai nāha ! ēyaṁ saccē tuha bhāsiya hōu || 6 ||
taṁ ciya diṇaṁ pamāṇaṁ gabhāharaṇassa tīē dēvīē । jāō kamēṇa puttō paḍipunnadiṇēhiṁ suhadivasē ॥7॥
sumiṇāṇusāraō tō mahāvibhūīē nāgadattōtti । tāṇa taṇayassa nāmaṁ vihiyaṁ vihiṇā guruyaṇēṇa ॥8॥
aha kamasō vaḍhatēṇa tēṇa acirēṇa nāgadattēṇa । gahiō kalākalāvō guruṁ samakkhaṁ karēūṇa ||9||
tassatthi vālamittamitta iva paumakōsabuḍhikarō | amaragurūmaṁtitaṇaō nayacaṁdō nāma samarūvō ॥ 10 ॥
buddhisamiddhō guṇēhiṁ niddhō dharāē supasiddhō । sō annayā pasuttō rayaṇīē kumarapāsamma || 11 ||
tō avarattasamaē sō taṁ nō pāsaē sasijjāē । tō saṁbhatō sahasā savvattha gavēsa kumaraṁ ||12||
jā tāva vāsabhavaṇassa uvaribhāgammi rahasi maṁtataṁ । taṁ picchai ēgāē taruṇī itthiyāē samaṁ ॥ 13॥
āharaṇa pahāpiṁjariyadisivahūvayaṇiyā miyaṁkamuhī। kiṁ ēsā mayaṇapiyā raṁbhā vā lacchidēvī vā ।।
sāmāyikavrataṁ yaḥ karōti sāvadyayōgapratipakṣam । sa nāgadattakumāra iva prāpnōti paramasaukhyāni ॥ 1 ॥
,
tuṅgajina bhavana śikharāgrabhagnaravirathaturaṅgagatiprasaram । siṁhapuraṁ nāma puramiha bharata āsītsuprasiddham ||2||
tasmin nr̥pō ripumallō nirmūlīkr̥tamahāmallaughaḥ । tasyāsti praṇayinī prēmakulagr̥haṁ vasumatī nāma ||3||
sā'nyadā prasuptā paśyati svapnē paścimaniśāyām । sphāraphaṇāsaṁghātaṁ sarpa dīpyamānamaṇiruciram ||4॥
tataḥ sā pratibuddhā kathayati svapnaṁ priyasya sa bhaṇati । dayitē ! ēṣa svapnaḥ suputralābhaṁ sphuṭaṁ kathayati ||5||
tasmāttava tanayō bhaviṣyati dharāvalaya ēkacchatrarājyakaraḥ । sā bhaṇati nāṁtha ! ētatsatyaṁ tava bhāṣitaṁ bhavatu ॥
tadēva dinaṁ pramāṇaṁ garbhavaraṇasya tasyā dēvyāḥ । jātaḥ kramēṇa putraḥ paripūrṇadinaiḥ śubhadivasē ||7||
svapnānusāratastatō mahāvibhūtyā nāgadatta iti । tayōstanayasya nāma vihitaṁ vidhinā gurujanēna ॥ 8 ॥
atha kramaśō vardhamānēna tēnācirēṇa nāgadattēna । gr̥hītaḥ kalākalāpō guruṁ samakṣaṁ kr̥tvā ॥9॥
tasyāsti bālamitraṁ mitra iva padma (jhā) kōśavr̥ddhikaraḥ । amaragurumantritanayō nayacandrō nāma samarūpaḥ ॥ 10॥
caturvidhabuddhisamr̥ddhō guṇaiḥ snigdhō gharāyāṁ suprasiddhaḥ । sō'nyadā prasuptō rajanyāṁ kumārapārśvē ॥ 11 ॥
tatō'rdharātrasamayē sa taṁ nō paśyati svaśayyāyām । tataḥ saṁbhrāntaḥ sahasā sarvatra gavēṣayati kumāram ॥ 12 ॥
yāvattāvad vāsabhavanasyōparibhāgē rahasi mantrayantam । taṁ paśyatyēkayā taruṇyā striyā samam ||13||

supāsanāha-caritrasmi --
iya citatō tīē bhaṇiō āgaccha kumarapāsammi । nīatthaṁ mā sumarasu dōṇḍaṁ taiō havai mukkhōṁ ||15||
jamhā dēhavibhinnā tumhē cittēṇa puṇa abhinnā ya । tā uvasappasu pahupādapaṁkayaṁ, bhagai kumarōvi ॥ 16 ॥
āgaccha, taō pattō tāṇa samīvammi uvavisai jāva । tāva sahasatti kattō vīyāvi hu bāliyā pattā ||
namiūṇaṁ sā pucchai sāmiṇi ! siddhaṁ paōyaṇaṁ nōvā ? | sā bhaṇai bhaṇatumaṁ ciya lajjā avarujjhaē majjha ॥
na maē kiṁcivi kahiyaṁ paōyaṇaṁ tō bhaṇai sā ēvaṁ । kumara ! nimuṇēsu kajjaṁ avahiyacittō khaṇaṁ hōuṁ ॥
jā pāra kahi kiṁcivi tā takkhaṇēṇa annāvi । iṁṭatabhamirabhamara ulamāliyaṁ māliyaṁ gahiraṁ ॥ 20 ॥
pattā visakaṁdōvayaṇiyā sā bhaṇēi tayabhimuhaṁ । givha imaṁ varamālaṁ khivēsu kumarasma kaṁṭhami ||21||
sā bhai halē! sutharā bhavēsu, tō bhaṇai maṁtinayacaṁdō । huṁ vinnāyaṁ ēvaṁ parismamaṁ mā tumaṁ kuṇasu ||22||
kahasu puṇa ūsugattassa kāraṇaṁ tō kahēi sā duiyā । jaha malayakēurannō kannāṇa caukathaṁ ēhī ||23||

sapariggahōvi sagihōvidārajuttōvi dēsaviraōvi । pāvai muṇīṇa uvamaṁ jattha ṭiō tattha ki bhaṇimō ? ||
sāmāiyaṭṭhiyāṇaṁ jaha jaha ullasai suddhapariṇāmō taha taha aṇēyabhavasaṁciyāṇi kammāṇi jhijjati ॥
māṇasasaranīraṁ jaha kalusijjai kāsarēhiṁ vimalaṁpi । aiyārēhiṁ sāmāiyaṁpi taha cēva, tē ya imē ॥ 74 ॥
aṇavadviyakaraṇaṁ taha maṇatraikāyāṇa duppaṇihāṇaṁ । sāmaiyaṁ vihiyaṁ vā navatti iya saṁsaō taha
iya nāūṇaṁ sammaṁ kumarō sāmāiyassa sambhāvaṁ । aṭṭhamicaudasīsuṁ giṇhēyavvaṁ maē ēyaṁ ॥ 76 ॥
1
|| 75 ॥
kumārō'pi saparivāra upaviṣṭaḥ śuddhadharaṇipaṭṭē । itō dharmaḥ kathayituṁ prārabdhaḥ sūriṇaivam || 63 ॥
pr̥cchati saviśēṣamēva śrāvakadharma gururapi taṁ kathayati । kumārō'pi mantrisahitastaṁ gr̥hṇāti dvādaśavidhamapi ॥64॥
tatō vanditvā sūriṁ kumāraḥ saṁcalati nijapurābhimukham | mārgē ca trajañjalpati mittrēṇa sahaivam ||65 ||
śakunaiḥ phalaṁ dattaṁ yathā nirdiṣṭaṁ purā tvayā mitra ! | prāptō'prāpta pūrvī yajjinadharmō mayā'dya ॥ 66 ॥
iti jalpanprāptō gr̥hē pūjayitvā tatra jinapratimām । vanditvā vidhinā mitrēṇa parigatō bhōjanaṁ karōti ॥
bhuktōttarē tatra ca parasparaṁ cintayatō gr̥hidharmam | samyaksamyaktvādi sāmayikē kiñcitsaṁmūḍhau ॥68॥
tataḥ prabhātasamayē jinapūjanavandanaṁ vidhāya । prāptau sūrisakāśaṁ vidhinā vanditvā bhaktyā ॥69॥
sāmāyikasvarūpaṁ sūriṁ pr̥cchataḥ kumāranayacandrau । tayōśca hitārtha sūrirapi kathayatyēvam ॥70॥
yatra samaśatru mittraḥ samatr̥ṇamaṇikāñcanō bhavati jīvaḥ । sāmāyikābhidhānaṁ prathamaṁ śikṣātrataṁ tadiha ॥ 71 ॥
saparigrahō'pi sagr̥hō'pi dārayuktō'pi dēśaviratō'pi । prāpnōti munīnāmupamāṁ yatra sthitastatra kiṁ bhaṇāmaḥ ? ॥
sāmāyikasthitānāṁ yathā yathōllasati śuddhapariṇāmaḥ । tathā tathānēkabhavasaṁcitāni karmāṇi kṣīyantē ॥ 73 ॥
mānasasarōnīraṁ yathā kaluṣyatē kāsarairvimalamapi । aticārai: sāmāyikamapi tathaiva tē cēmē ॥74॥
anavasthitakaraṇaṁ tathā manōvacaḥ kāyānāṁ duṣpraṇidhānam । sāmpradhikaṁ vihitaṁ vā navētīti saṁśayastathā ca ॥
iti jñātvā samyak kumāraḥ sāmāyikasya sadbhāvam । aṣṭamīcaturdaśyōrgrahītavyaṁ mayaitat ॥76॥

iya kāūṇa painna namiuṁ sūriṁ gimmi saṁpattō । āsattō jiṇadhammē mittēṇa samaṁ gamai kālaṁ ||77||
aha malayakēurannō kannacaukkaṁ samāgayaṁ tattha । taṁ sōhaṇē muhuttē kumarō pariṇē, ittō ya ॥ 78 ॥
paṁcamārōē paṁcahiṁ bhajāhi sahaṇurbhujaṁtō । piuṇāvi carimasamaē ahisitō sō niyapayammi ॥
kārai jidibhavaṇē rahajattāō pavattara dēsē | sāhammiyavacchallaṁ kuṇai samittōvi uvauttō ॥ 80 ॥
iya
kālē bacatē kayāi kassavi nivassa uvarimmi । jayajattāē caliō pattō kammivi mahānayarē ॥
uccasiē jakkhēṇaṁ, kavi vinnava nivaṇō ēvaṁ | jaha ittha kōvi na lahai basiuṁ rayaṇipi, tā ittō ॥
gaccha dēvō, tō bhaṇai bhūvaī ajja caudasī tāva । itthēva ciṭṭiyanvaṁ na payāṇa ajja dāyantraṁ ॥ 83 ॥
ṭhāi tattha rāyā kkhagihē givhaē ya sāmaiyaṁ । pihiūṇa tassa dāraṁ sajhāyaṁ kuṇai, ittō ya ॥
tatthēva taṁ piccha vēgavaī garuyasārasiṁgāraṁ । jakkhā gārassaṁtō pabhaṇati ērisaṁ vayaṇa || 85 ||
tō
hā sāmi ! kimiha naṭṭō maṁ duhiyaṁ mōttamittha rannasmi । kiṁ na muṇasi maha hiyayaṁ tuha vira hē phuṭṭa taḍati ।।
iya sōuṁ savisēsaṁ saṁvēgakarāī guṇai kulayāī । naranāhō vēgavaī tō iya bhaṇiuṁ samārā ||87||
hā daiya ! kaha saṁpai maha hiyayāō khaṇēṇa kaha nahō । sō tārisōvi paṇaō savvaṁgōvaṁgalīṇōvi 9 ॥
dūmē majjha hiyayaṁ dahai sarīraṁ karēi raṇaraṇayaṁ । tuha virahō tā sāmiya! muṁcasu iya gaḍavarḍa ihiṁ ॥ 89 ॥
jaha ēyaṁ maha dukkha avēi taha nāha ! kuṇasu kiṁpi tumaṁ । na hu nāma mahāpurisā duhiēsuṁ huṁti nikaruṇā ||
tō rāyā paricita vihīsiyā kāvi uṭṭiyā ēsā । akkhayanihi vihīē samukkhaṇaṁtassa kimu kāhī ? ||
|
iti kr̥tvā pratijñāṁ natvā sūriṁ gr̥hē saṁprāptaḥ । āsaktō jinadharmē mitrēṇa samaṁ gamayati kālam ॥ 77 ॥
atha malayakēturājasya kanyācatuṣkaṁ samāgataṁ tatraṁ । tacchōbhanē muhūrttē kumāraḥ pariṇayati, itaśca ॥78॥
pañcaprakārabhōgān pañcabhirbhāryābhiḥ sahānubhuñjānaḥ । pitrāpi caramasamayē'bhiṣiktaḥ sa nijapadē ||79||
kārayati jinēndrabhavanāni rathayātrāḥ pravartayati dēśē । sādharmika vātsalyaṁ karōti samittrō'pyupayuktaḥ ॥ 80॥
iti kālē vrajati kadācitkasyāpi nr̥pasyōpari । jayayātrayā calitaḥ prāptaḥ kasminnapi mahānagarē ॥ 81 ॥
usitē yakṣēṇa, kō'pi vijñapayati nr̥patērēvam । yathātra kō'pi na labhatē vastuṁ rajanimapi, tasmāditaḥ ॥ 82॥
gacchatu dēvaḥ, tatō bhaṇati bhūpatiradya caturdaśī tāvat । atraiva sthātavyaṁ na prayāṇamadya dātavyam ॥ 83 ॥
tatastiṣṭhati rājā yakṣagr̥hē gr̥hṇāti ca sāmāyikam । pidhāya tasya dvāra svādhyāyaṁ karōti, itaśca ॥ 84 ॥
tatraiva ca tāṁ paśyati vēgavatīṁ gurusāraśr̥ṅgārām । yakṣāgārasyāntaḥ prabhaṇantīmīdr̥śaṁ vacanam ॥89॥
hā svāmin ! kimiha naṣṭō māṁ duḥkhitāṁ muktvā'vāraṇyē । kiṁ na jānāsi mama hr̥dayaṁ tava virahē sphuṭati taḍiti |
iti śrutvā saviśēṣaṁ saṁvēgakarāṇi gaṇayati kulakāni । naranāthaḥ, vēgavatī tata iti bhaṇituṁ samārabdhā ॥87॥
hā dayita ! kathaya saṁprati māṁ hr̥dayātkṣaṇēna kathaṁ naṣṭaḥ । hā tādr̥śō'pi praṇayaḥ sarvāṅgōpāṅgalīnō'pi ॥88॥
dunōti mama hr̥dayaṁ dahati śarīraṁ karōti raṇaraṇakam । tava virahastasmātsvāmin ! muñcatyāṭōpamidānīm ॥ 89 ॥
yathaitanmama duḥkhamapaiti tathā nātha ! kuru kimapi tvam । na hi nāma mahāpuruṣā duḥkhitēṣu bhavanti niṣkaruṇāḥ ॥

supāsanāha - cariśrammi

ityaṁtarē sayaṁ ciya sō jakkhō gaḍayaḍaṁ pakubvaṁtō । pattō nivassa pāsē viuvviraṁ ruvamabhīmaṁ ॥ 92 ॥
bhaṇai niyapōrisēṇaṁ mannasi bhuvarṇapi taṇasamaṁ mūḍha ! | mā pabhaṇasu nō kahiyaṁ taṁ mārissāmi ahamihi ।
tā sarasu iṭṭhadēva sēvaṁ vā majjha taṁ pavajjēsu । iya bhaṇiuṁ ujgāmai muggara mēgaṁ nivassuvari ||94 ||
bhaṇai ya muṁcasu nayaraṁ sajjō vā pōrisaṁvalavēsu । aha niyasirakamalēṇaṁ pūyasu maha pāyakamalaṁ vā ॥ 95|
iya sōuṁ savisēsaṁ sajjhāyaṁtō sa ciṭṭhaī jāva । tā tattha kavaḍijakkhō naravairakkhākaē pattō || 96 ||
bahusurakathaṁgarakkhō kamaladalakkhō raṇammi niru dakkhō । taṁ daṇaṁ naṭṭō bhayabhīō sōvi purajakkhō
tō rāyā sāmayaṁ pāra vihiṇā karita saṁbhā । kavaḍijakkhēṇa samayaṁ bhaṇai imaṁ tumhabhayanahaṁ ॥ 98 ॥
hakārāsu jakkhaṁ paḍivōhissāmi taṁ ahaṁ jēṇa । uvvāsiyapuralōō vasaī dukkhēṇa annattha ॥ 99 ॥
tō takkhaṇēṇa sō tattha āṇiō tassa suravisēsērhi । paṇamitta mahārāyaṁ kayaḍḍijakva ca nirvābhimu
bhai ahō taṁ purisō dhīrataṁ tujjha caiva dharaṇīē । majjhuvasaggēhi jō pavaṇēhiṁ girivva nō khuhiō ।। 101
kiñca ।
sutthāvatthāē jaṇō niyakajjasahō havēi savvōvi । sō viralō visamadasāi jō puṇō sattamāruhai ||102
tā tuṭṭhō haṁ naravara ! pasiūṇaṁ bhaṇasu kiṁpi taṁ kajjaṁ । tō bhai kavaḍijakkhō ajjavi taṁ puccha sē ēvaṁ
niyamāṇēṇaṁ sayamavi paribhāvasu jaṁ imassa maṇaiṭuṁ । tō takkhaṇēṇa jakkhō uvaōgaṁ dēvi bhaṇai ima ||
tujjha pasāēṇa sō puralōō lahau appaṇō riddhiṁ । taṁ sāmiyaṁ vihēḍaṁ kavaḍḍijakkhassa sāhijjā |
tatō rājā paricintayati vibhīṣikā kāpyutthitaiṣā । akṣatanidhiṁ vidhinā samutkhanataḥ kimu kariṣyati ? || 91
atrāntarē svayamēva sa yakṣō gaḍagaḍaṁ prakurvan । prāptō nr̥pasya pārśvē vikr̥tya rūpamatibhīmam ॥92 ||
bhaṇati nijapauruṣēṇa manyasē bhuvanamapi tr̥ṇasamaṁ mūḍha ! | mā prabhaṇa nō kathitaṁ tvāṁ mārayiṣyāmyaha madhunā ॥ 93
tasmātsamarēṣṭadēvaṁ sēvāṁ vā mama tvaṁ prapadyasva । iti bhaṇitvōtthāpayati mudgaramēkaṁ nr̥pasyōpari ||94 ॥
bhaṇati ca muñca nagaraṁ sadyō vā pauruṣamavalambasva । atha nijaśiraḥ kamalēna pūjaya mama pādakamalaṁ vā ॥95|
iti śrutvā saviśēṣaṁ svādhyāyansa tiṣṭhati yāvat । tāvattatra kapardiyakṣō narapatirakṣā kr̥tē prāptaḥ ॥ 96 ॥
bahusurakr̥tāṅgarakṣaḥ kamaladalākṣō raṇē niścitaṁ dakṣaḥ । taṁ dr̥dvā naṣṭō bhayabhītaḥ sō'pi purayakṣaḥ ||97 ||
tatō rājā sāmāyikaṁ pārayati vidhinā kr̥tvā saṁbhāṣam । kapardiyakṣēṇa samaṁ bhaṇatīmaṁ yuṣmadbhayanaṣṭam ||98||
hakkāraya yakṣaṁ pratibōdhayiṣyāmi tamahaṁ yēna । udvasitapuralōkō vasati duḥkhēnānyatra ॥ 99 ॥
tatastatkṣaṇēna sa tatrānītastasya suraviśēṣaiḥ । praṇamya mahārājaṁ kapardiyakṣaṁ ca nr̥pābhimukham ॥100॥
bhaṇatyahō tvaṁ puruṣō dhīratvaṁ tavaiva dharaṇyām । mamōpasargairyaḥ pavanairgiririva nō kṣubhitaḥ ॥ 101 ॥
susthāvasthāyāṁ janō nijakāryasahō bhavati sarvō'pi । sa viralō viṣamadaśāyāṁ yaḥ punaḥ samārōhati ॥ 102
tasmāttuṣṭō'haṁ naravara ! prasadya bhaṇa kimapi tvaṁ kāryam । tatō bhaṇati kapardiyakṣō'dyāpi tvaṁ pr̥cchasyētat ॥
nijajñānēna svayamapi paribhāvaya yadasya manaiṣṭam । tatastatkṣaṇēna yakṣa upayōgaṁ dattvā bhaṇatīdam ॥ 104 ॥

tō sō suralōō nirūviō tappurasta lōyāṇaṁ । āhavaṇatthaṁ tēṇavi samāṇiō sō imaṁ bhaṇiō ।।
niyaniyahisāmittaṁ kuṇaha jaṇā ! nitrapaē namēūṇa । ēsō tumhāṇa pahū tēvi hu taha caitra kuvvaṁti ||
tō bhai nighaṁ jakkhō ēyapurasāmiēṇa taṁ vihiyaṁ । maha kiṁpi jaṁna kahiṁu pārijjai tō nivō bhaṇai ॥
pāēṇa niravarāhē jaṇampina hu kōvi maṁgulaṁ kuṇai । muttr̥ṇaṁ khudajaṇaṁ avāṇuyaṁ maccharāinaṁ ॥ 109 ॥
kiñca ।
1
garuyāvarāhiṇapi hu aṇupaṁtīha jē mahāsattā । jamhā jē karuṇavarā tēhi ciya bhūsiyā dharaṇī ॥ 110 ॥
tā khamasu purajaṇammī puranāhassāvi, tō bhāi jakkhō । sō pāviō maē cciya paralōyaṁ tō bhaṇai rāyā ||
tattaṇayaṁ āṇēuṁ ṭhavē rajjammi, tēṇa taṁ vihiyaṁ । tō rāyā sē sikkha tāṇa samakkha ima dēi ॥ 112 ॥
nayavaṁtē jō pālai duḍē nigahai nīivaddharaī । dīṇāṇāhaṁ samarṇa pōsai taha sayaṇavagaṁ ca ॥ 113 ॥
sō hō frately jahatthanāmō narāṇa pālaṇaō । niyapōṭabharaṇatuṭṭhō na hōi nēva ya pamaīvi ॥ 114 ॥
kiṁ tāṇa jīviēṇaṁ kiṁvā lacchīē kiṁva rajjēṇa । picchatāṇavi jāṇaṁ nivāṇa duhiō jaṇō hōi ? ||
iyavasāya purajakva bhai naravaī ēvaṁ । jiṇathammaṁ paḍivajjasu tō jakkhō bhai taṁ kahasu ||
niyajīyanivvisēsā savvēvi visēsaō duhiyasattā । savvēṇaghi daṭṭhavvā vivēgiṇā puṇa visēsēṇa ||
dēvaṁ dhammaṁ tattaṁ savittharaṁ sē kahē tō rāyā । paḍivajjivi sō savvaṁ rāyābhimuhaṁ imaṁ bhaṇai ||118||
bhūsiyapuhaitalāṇaṁ mahāṇubhāvāṇa daṁsaṇaṁpi suhaṁ । saṁsaggī saṁbhāsō ya suhayarō punnapurimāṇa ॥ 119 ॥
tava prasādēna sa puralōkō labhatāmātmana r̥ddhim । tvāṁ svāminaṁ vidhāya kapardiyakṣasya sāhāyyāt ॥ 105॥
tataḥ sarvaḥ suralōkō nirūpitastatpurasya lōkānām । āhvānārthaṁ tēnāpi samānītaḥ sa idaṁ bhaṇitaḥ ॥ 106 ॥
nijanijagr̥hasvāmitvaṁ kuruta janāḥ ! nr̥papādān natvā । ēṣa yuṣmākaṁ prabhustē'pi hi tathaiva kurvanti ॥ 107 ॥
tatō bhaṇati nr̥paṁ yakṣa ētatpurasvāminā tad vihitam । mama kimapi yanna kathayituṁ pāryatē tatō nr̥pō bhaṇati ॥
prāyēṇa niraparādhē janē na khalu kō'pyaniṣṭaṁ karōti । muktvā kṣudrajanamajñāyakaṁ matsarākīrṇam ॥ 109 ॥
gurvaparādhamapi hyanukampanta iha yē mahāsattvāḥ । yasmādyē karuṇāparāstairēva bhūṣitā dharaṇī ॥ 110 ॥
tasmātkṣamasva purajanaṁ puranāthamapi tatō bhaṇati yakṣaḥ । sa prāpitōṁ mayaiva paralōkaṁ tatō bhaṇati rājā ॥ 111 ॥
tattanayamānīya sthāpaya rājyē, tēna tadvihitam । tatō rājā tasmai śikṣāṁ tēṣāṁ samakṣamimāṁ dadāti ॥ 112 ॥
nayavatō yaḥ pālayati duṣṭān nigr̥hṇāti nītibaddha ratiḥ । dīnānāthaṁ śramaṇaṁ pōṣayati tathā svajanavarga ca ॥
sa bhavati nr̥pō lōkē yathārthanāmā narāṇāṁ pālanataḥ । nijōdarabharaṇatuṣṭō na bhavati naiva ca pramādyapi ॥ 114 ॥
kiṁ tēṣāṁ jīvitēna kiṁvā lakṣmyā kiṁvā rājyēna । paśyatāmapi yēṣāṁ nr̥pāṇāṁ duḥkhitō janō bhavati ? ॥ 115 ॥
iti navanr̥pamanuśāsya purayakṣaṁ bhaṇati narapatirēvam | jinadharmē pratipadyasva tatō yakṣō bhaṇati taṁ kathaya ॥ 116 ॥
nijajīvanirviśēṣāḥ sarvē'pi viśēṣatō duḥkhitasattvāḥ । sarvēṇāpi draṣṭavyā vivēkinā punarviśēṣēṇa ॥117॥
dēvaṁ dharmaṁ tattvaṁ savistaraṁ tasya kathayati tatō rājā । pratipadya sa sarva rājābhimukhamidaṁ bhaṇati ॥ 118 ॥

supāsanāha-cariammi-
aha puramutthaṁ kāuṁ kavaḍḍijakkhāiyē visajjēuṁ । rāyā puraō caliō tā purajakkhēṇa iya bhaṇiō ||
jassōvaritaṁ caliō nivassa sō saṁpayaṁ tuha samīvē । sayamiha baddhō ēhī tā taṁ mā vacca tassuvariṁ ।।
taṁ ca tahēva ya jāyaṁ sēvaṁ mannāviūṇa sō mukkō । aha niyanayarābhimuhaṁ caliō rāyāvi pattō ya ॥
vēgavaī puttaṁ niyarajjē ṭhāviūṇa samayammi | paṁcataṁ saṁpatō taiyabhavē sijjhihī ēttha || 123 ||
iya sāmaiē bhāvā ihapi hu nāgadattanaranāhō । jāō sāḍihērō tā karaṇīyaṁ imamavasaṁ ॥ 124 ॥
sāmāiyagayacittō sē vijjai dēvadāṇavērhipi । pōrāṇayabahukammaṁ khavēi thēvēṇa kālēna || 125 ||
॥ iti sāmāyikadr̥ṣṭāntē nāgadattanr̥pakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
bhūṣitapr̥thivītalānāṁ mahānubhāvānāṁ darśanamapi śubham । saṁsargaḥ saṁbhāṣaśca śubhataraḥ puṇyapuruṣāṇām ॥ 119 ॥
atha purasausthyaṁ kr̥tvā kapardiyakṣādikaṁ visr̥jya । rājā purataścalitastāvatpurayakṣēṇēti bhaṇitaḥ ॥ 120॥
yasyōpari tvaṁ calitō nr̥pasya sa sāṁprataṁ tava samīpē । svayamiha baddha ēṣyati tasmācaṁ mā vraja tasyōpari ||
tacca tathaiva ca jātaṁ sēvāṁ mānayitvā sa muktaḥ । atha nijanagarābhimukhaṁ calitō rājāpi prāptaśca ॥ 122॥
vēgavatyāḥ putraṁ nijarājyē sthāpayitvā samayē । pañcatvaṁ saṁprāptastr̥tīyabhavē sētsyatyatra || 123 ||
iti sāmāyikē bhāvādihāpi hi nāgadattanaranāthaḥ । jātaḥ saprātihāryastasmātkaraṇīyamidamavaśyam ॥ 124॥
sāmāyikagatacittaḥ sēvyatē dēvadānavairapi । purāṇabahukarma kṣapayati stōkēna kālēna ॥ 125॥

tathāhi;
jassā lōṇakara mannē sakkēṇa lōyaṇasahassaṁ । vihiyaṁ tamatthi nayaraṁ rayaṇapuraṁ nāma vikkhāyēṁ ॥2॥
tatthavi ya dhaṇagariṭṭō siṭṭhī nāmēṇa gaṁgadattōtti । bhajjā guṇamaināmā puttī māṇōti tāṇatthi ||3||

tā sōvidē kannaṁ gurūṇa vayaṁṇē taḍiṭṭiō saṁtō। tō kēṇavi saḍḍhēṇaṁ pañcabhināūṇa sō. bhaṇiō ||
uvavisa ittha bhaṇiūṇa sāhiyaṁ sāhunāhapāyāṇaṁ । jaha gaṁgadattataṇaō ēsō māṇōtti vaṁdē ||7||
tō savisēsa sūrī sāhai akśvēvaṇi kahaṁ tassa । bhadagabhāvattāō sugēi sō avahiō hōuṁ ||8||
aggāhārō nāmēṇa atthi gāmō dhaṇēṇa paḍipunnō । niṣpunnagābhihāṇō ēgō kulaputtaō tattha ||9||
vasaī vavasāyasahiō navaraṁ jaṁ kiṁpi kuṇai bavasāyaṁ । tattha aṇatthaṁ pāvaṛa viḍhavēi na kavaḍḍiyaṁ kahavi ।।
tō anyāya bhaṇiō kēṇavi sayaṇēṇa pāusē paḍhamē । majjha baladē gahiraṁ halamēgaṁ kuṇasu kiṁtu taē || 11 ||
saṁjhāsamaē pattē majjha baladā purōhaḍassaṁtō । maha diṭṭhīē daṁsivi ṭhāēyavvā paidipi ||12||
tēṇavi taṁ paḍivannaṁ paidiyahaṁ khēḍiūṇa khittammi । taggōṇē taha kuṇaī aha vāvai sō tahiṁ paḍhamaṁ || 13 ||
mugacāvalayāidhannaṁ kattariyaṁ kattarēhiṁ jāyaṁpi । taṁ tatthavi tō tusaliṁ vāvai sō kiṇivi varavīyaṁ ॥ 14 ॥
sāmāyikaṁ gr̥hītvā duṣpraṇidhānaṁ karōti yō manasā । sa māna iva pramattō niruṇaddhyātmanaḥ sugatim ॥ 1॥ -
yasyāvalōkanakr̥tē manyē śakrēṇa lōcanasahasram । vihitaṁ tadasti nagaraṁ ratnapuraṁ nāma vikhyātam ||2||
tatrāpi ca dhanagariṣṭhaḥ śrēṣṭhī nāmnā gaṅgadatta iti । bhāryā guṇamatīnāmā putrō māna iti tayōrasti || 3 ||
kiñcidapi kalāsu kuśalō vicarati svēcchayā kānanādiṣu । durlalitamittrasahitō'thānyadā jinagr̥hē prāptaḥ ॥
paśyati prabhūtalōkaṁ bhaktyā sūrinidhānē । śr̥ṇvantaṁ gr̥hidharmaṁ samyaktvādi prayatnēna ||5||
tataḥ sō'pi dadāti karṇa gurūṇāṁ vacanē taṭīsthitaḥ san । tataḥ kēnāpi śrāddhēna pratyabhijñāya sa bhaṇitaḥ || 6 ||
upaviśātra bhaṇitvā kārthataṁ sādhunāthapādānām । yathā gaṅgadattatanaya ēṣa māna iti vandatē ||7||
tataḥ saviśēṣaṁ sūriḥ kathayatyākṣēpaṇīṁ kathāṁ tasya । bhadrakabhāvatvācchr̥ṇōti sō'vahitō bhūtvā ॥8॥
agrādhārō nāmnā'sti grāmō dhanēna paripūrṇaḥ । niṣpuṇyakābhidhāna ēkaḥ kulaputrakastatra ||9||
vasati vyavasāyasahitaḥ kēvalaṁ yaṁ kamapi karōti vyavasāyam । tatrānarthaṁ prāpnōtyarjayati na kapardikō kathamapi ॥
tatō'nyadā ca bhaṇitaḥ kēnāpi svajanēna prāvr̥ṣi prathamāyām । mama balīvardī gr̥hītvā halamēkaṁ kuru kintu tvayā ॥
sandhyāsamayē prāptē mama balīvardō vāṭakasyāntaḥ । mama dr̥ṣṭayā darśayitvā sthāpayitavya pratidinamapi ॥ 12॥

mudgataṇḍulādidhānyaṁ kr̥taṁ kartaraijātamapi । tat tatrāpi tatō dhānyaṁ vapati sa krītvā varabījam ॥14॥

iya

cintayatō gōturagādhipāvapīha nayanajihvāsattāyām । bhavantyāmanyē'pi hi bhaviṣyanti gōturagādayaḥ ॥ 44 ॥

sa truṭiṣyati yatō mē pīnaṁ vastraṁ, kathamapi trōṭayitvā । nipatatā'pi prāṇā naiva mayā tasya gamiṣyantē ||

gr̥hṇīta ubhayakālaṁ, haṭṭē vyavaharati māna ēva । parityakta bālalīlō dharmaprabhāvēṇa sa jātaḥ ॥ 51 ॥
vyavaharati tasya haṭṭē prajādilōkaḥ sadāpi prāyēṇa । labdhē bhaktē tē tasya prayacchanti tad drvyam ॥52॥
iti vrajati kālē kēnāpi bhaktē labdhē sati । nō mānasya dattaṁ kiñcidapi mārgayatō'pi ॥ 53 ॥
anyēna punarardhamanyēnārdhasyārdhaṁ dattam । tāvad yāvad daśa sahasrāṇi jātāni cchēdē mānasya ॥ 54 ॥
asamādhānaṁ jātaṁ tathāpi hi sāmāyikaṁ na muñcati । gr̥hītē'pi sāmayikē manasi mānō vicintayati ॥ 55 ॥
ētēna duṣṭēna prajādivargēṇa mama bahudravyam । gamitaṁ saṁpratibhaktē, bhaviṣyadbhaktē punaraham ||16||
dattvā kimapi vaikaraṇikēbhya ētēṣāṁ sarvamapi bhaktam । uparyapi hi grahīṣyē tatō mē sarvamapi tad dravyam ||

yataḥ ।

acchariyāṇa kulaṁ piva lacchīē nivāsavāsabhavarṇava । vijjāṇa nihāṇaṁ piva nayaraṁ iha asthi sākēyaṁ ॥

551
tō bhai muṇī gāmāyaṇa paḍhamō ya davvamaggōtti । nāṇāiyāṇa bīō vinnēō bhāvamaggōti ||15||
jīvāiyā patthā jāṇijjaṁtīha jēṇa taṁ nāṇaṁ । taṁ puṇa paṁcapayāraṁ maināṇāī muṇēyavvaṁ ॥ 16 ॥
sammattaṁ puṇa vr̥ttaṁ jīvāipayatya satyasandahaṇaṁ । dēvā arihaṁtā ciya guruṇō ya musāhuṇō caiva ॥ 17॥
taṁ puṇativihaṁ khāiga khāōvasamaṁ ca uvasamasamutthaṁ । ahavā kāragarōyagadīvagabhēṇa taṁ tivihaṁ ॥ 18 ॥
cāritapi yadi paṁcavihaṁ samaiyāiēṇa । iya kiṁci vittharēṇa kahiō bhō bhāvamaggōvi ||19||
jaha tumhēhi kahiō paṁjalaō amha davvamaggōtti । taha tumhāṇaṁ kahiō amhēhivi bhāvamaggōti ॥ 20 ॥
tumhakahiyammi maggē gacchassaṁ vaṭṭamāṇajōgēṇa । amhakahiyammi maggē tumhēvi payaṭṭaha jaicchā ||21||
visaḍhē ta bhaṇiyaṁ kahēha dēsēṇa bhāvamaggapi । paḍipunnabhāvamaggē gaṁtumasattā jaō nāha ! ||22||
sammattassa sakhvaṁ dhūlayapāṇāivāyavirayāī । bārasa vihagihidhammaṁ kahēi sāhū savivaraṁpi ॥ 23 ॥
tēhivi taṁ paḍivannaṁ sammaṁ avahāriḍaṁ visēsēṇaṁ । aha muṇiṇō saṁcaliyā takka hiyapaṇa, tēvi taō ||24||
namiuṁ abhiruiyapurē pattā tatthavi ya thēvadiyahēhiṁ । pattamaṇicchiyalābhā caliyā tō niyapuraṁ pattā ||25||
kuvvaṁti jahākahiyaṁ sammaṁ sammattayāigihidhammaṁ । sāmāiē visēsēṇa tāṇaṁ jattō imaṁ suṇiuṁ ||26||
sāmāiyammi ukaē samaṇō iva sāvaō havai jamhā । ēēṇa kāraṇēṇaṁ bahusō sāmāiyaṁ kujjā ||27||
sāmāiyaṭṭhiyāṇaṁ jaha jaha ullasai suddhapariṇāmō । taha taha aṇēyabhavasaṁciyāṇi kammāṇi niddala ॥ 28 ॥
iya sāmaiyarayāṇaṁ tāṇaṁ vaccati vāsarā bahuyā । kiṁtu visaḍhō pamāī rāyakahāīvi bhāsē ॥ 29 ॥
tatō bhaṇati munirgrāmādikānāṁ prathamaśca dravyamārga iti । jñānādikānāṁ dvitīyō vijñēyō bhāvamārga iti ॥ 15॥
jīvādikāḥ padārthā jñāyanta iha yēna tajjñānam । tat punaḥ pañcaprakāraṁ matijñānādi jñātavyam ॥16॥
samyaktvaṁ punaruktaṁ jīvādipadārthasārtha śraddhānam । dēvā arhanta ēva guravaśca susādhava ēva ॥17॥
tat punastrividhaṁ kṣāyikaṁ kṣāyōpaśamikaṁ cōpaśamasamuttham । athavā kārakarōcakadīpakabhēdēna tat trividham ॥
cāritramapi ca diṣṭaṁ pañcavidhaṁ sāmāyikādibhēdēna । iti kiñcidvistarēṇa kathitō bhō bhāvamārgō'pi ॥19॥
yathā yuvābhyāṁ kathitaḥ prāñjalō'smākaṁ dravyamārga iti । tathā yuvayōḥ kathitō'smābhirapi bhāvamārga iti ॥ 20 ॥
yuṣmatkathitē mārgē gamiṣyāvō vartamānayōgēna । asmatkathitē mārgē yuvāmapi prayatētāṁ yadīcchā ||21||
visaḍhēna tatō bhaṇitaṁ kathayata dēśēna bhāvamārgamapi । paripūrṇa bhāvamārgē gantumaśaktau yatō nātha ! ॥22॥
samyaktvasya svarūpaṁ sthūlaprāṇātipātaviratādim । dvādaśavidhagr̥hidharmē kathayati sādhuḥ savivaramapi ॥23॥
tābhyāmapi sa pratipannaḥ samyagavadhārya viśēṣēṇa । atha munī saṁcalitau tatkathitapathēna tāvapi tataḥ ॥24॥
natvā'bhirucitapuraṁ prāptau tatrāpi ca stōkadivasaiḥ । prāptamanaīpsitalābhōṁ calitau tatō nijapuraṁ prāptau ॥
kurutō yathākathitaṁ samyak samyaktvādigr̥hidharmam । sāmāyikē viśēṣēṇa tayōryatna idaṁ śrutvā ॥26॥
sāmāyikē tu kr̥tē śramaṇa iva śrāvakō bhavati yasmāt । ētēna kāraṇēna bahuśaḥ sāmāyikaṁ kuryāt ||27||
sāmāyikasthitānāṁ yathā yathōllasati śuddhapariṇāmaḥ । tathā tathānēkabhavasaṁcitāni karmāṇi nirdalati ॥ 28 ॥
।

nimaḍhasurabhicamajjhē, tattō daddūṇa tassa gururiddhiṁ । nāūṇa putrajammaṁ tattō jhūrai bahuṁ visaḍhō ॥ 51 ॥
sarisēhivi gihidhammō dōhivi paripāliō tahavi jāō । ajjhavasāyavasēṇa ēsō sāmī ahaṁ bhiccō ||
haddhī muddhē maē dhammaviruddhaṁ samāyaraṁtēṇa । hāsuvahāsaparēṇaṁ hā hā hā hāriō jammō || 53 ||
baivagghī saṁjamaṇaṁ kāurisēṇaṁ na sakkiyaṁ kāuṁ । sāmaiyamittakālaṁpi ahaha ahō mōhamā || 54 ||
vārijjatēvi nibaṁdhuṇā jaṁpiyē imaṁ tathā । taṁ hōsi mahiḍdīō surō ahaṁ tujjha mahaliō || 55 ||
taṁ saccaṁ ciya jāyaṁ nisadasurō javi puvvanēhēṇa । aigauravēṇa pāsai tahāvi puvvakkiyavasē || 56 ॥
garuō gavalaṁba maddalaō tassa picchaṇayakālē । tō taha jhijjara hiyaē jaha dukkhaṁ kēvalī muṇai ||
caṭatu vivāhamaṇḍapē śūlyāṁ vāpi tāvadahaṁ na kimapi jalpiṣyāmi । yāvannaiṣā raṇḍā mama gēhātu niḥsr̥tā ॥
tatō bhaṇitaṁ tanayaiḥ 'raṇḍā' mā bhaṇa tāta ! prathamamapi । sa bhaṇati yuṣmajjananī sadāpi raṇḍā mayā bhaṇitā ॥
tathāpi na jātā raṇḍā, kiṁ rē dugdhāni maṅgalaśataiḥ । jāyantē, ēvamāditadbhaṇitānāṁ tu nō saṁkhyā ॥45॥
ēvaṁ mamāpi prakr̥tiḥ kēlikaraṇē karmamūḍhasya । tathāpi yatanāṁ kariṣyē sāmāyikaṁ punarna hi tyakṣyāmi ॥ 46 ॥
nisaḍhaḥ pravr̥ttaśraddhaḥ sāmāyikaṁ gr̥hītvā pārayati । aticārapaṅkamuktaṁ śrāvakadharmamapi tathā sarvam ॥47॥
prakr̥tyā śaṁṭhō visaḍhaḥ kr̥tasāmāyikō'pi duṣpraṇidhānam । vācā karōti tatastaṁ nisaḍhō vārayati pratidivasam ॥
tatō bhaṇatīmaṁ visaḍhō bhavasi tvaṁ suravarō maharddhikaḥ । bhaviṣyāmyahaṁ mārdaṅgikastvadīyastathāpīti hasati ||
iti visaḍhanisaḍhaśrāddhau kālēna kavalitau samādhinā । saudharma upapannau visaḍhō'lparddhikō jātaḥ ॥10॥
nisaṭasurabhr̥tyamadhyē, tatō dr̥ṣṭvā tasya gurur̥ddhim । jñātvā pūrvajanma tataḥ khidyatē bahu visaḍhaḥ ॥ 51 ॥
।
sadr̥śābhyāmapi gr̥hidharmō dvābhyāmapi paripālitastathāpi jātaḥ । adhyavasāyavaśēnaiṣa svāmyahaṁ bhr̥tyaḥ ॥52॥
hā dhig mugdhēna mayā dharmaviruddhaṁ samācaratā । hāsōpahāsaparēṇa hā hā hā hāritaṁ janma ॥53॥
vacōvyāghrīsaṁyamanaṁ kāpuruṣēṇa na śakyaṁ kartum । sāmāyikamātrakālamapyahaha ahō mōhamāhātmyam ॥ 54 ॥
vāryamāṇēnāpi nisaḍhabandhunā jalpitamidaṁ tadā । tvaṁ bhavasi maharddhikaḥ surō'haṁ tava mārdaṅgikaḥ ॥ 55 ॥
tatsatyamēva jātaṁ nisadasurō yadyapi pūrvasnēhēna । atigauravēṇa paśyati tathāpi pūrvakriyāvaśēna ॥56॥
gururgalē'valambatē mr̥daṅgastasya prēkṣaṇakālē । tatastathā kṣīyatē hr̥dayē yathā duḥkhaṁ kēvalī jānāti ॥57॥

caṁpayajaṁdhā kamalāṇaṇā ya unnayaōharā nayarī | kaṁkillipallavakarā malayapurī āsiramaṇivva || 2 ||

ēgē bhaṇati ōsahamanē kuvvaṁti siddhiāīyē । kēi gurumukkapukkā yaṁti kuṭṭati hiyayāī || 8 ||
tō puṭṭhō kōvi narō kuladharavaṇiṇā kimittha bahulōō । akkaṁdaparō dīsara, sō jaṁvara saṁpayaṁ ēttha ॥
kīlatthaṁ saṁpattō pattarutrō dhaṇēsavaṇitaṇaō । nāmēṇa malayacaṁdō iṁdō iva accharāhiṁ samaṁ ॥ 10 ॥

tuha taṇayaṁ jīvāvara ēsō anbhatthiō iha lahuṁpi । gaṁtr̥̄ṇa bhaṇasu ēyaṁ karuṇā gurusāyaraṁ sāhuṁ || 14 ||
apratilēkhitasthānē sthānādi karōtyanupayuktō yaḥ । kr̥tasāmāyikaḥ sa śyāmala iva śōcati kugatigataḥ ॥ 1 ॥
campakajaṅghā kamalakā ( lā ) nanōnnatapayōdharā nagarī । kaṅkallipallavakarā malayapuryāsīd ramaṇī ||2||
tatra nr̥pō nayasāraḥ svacchaḥ saguṇaśca tathāpi gatatrāsaḥ । caturjaladhimēkhalāmahīmahilā vakṣastalahāra iva ॥ 3 ॥
kuladharaśyāmalanāmānau vaṇijō nivasatastatrātidhaninau । dvāvapi pattiyuktāvaviyuktau bhramataḥ sarvatra || 4 ||
atha prāptē vasantē śāntānapi khalu yaḥ karōtyanupaśāntān । ratisundarābhidhāna udyānē tau gatau dvāvapi ॥5॥
krīḍatō vividhakrīḍābhiḥ suhr̥tkalatraiḥ parigatau yāvat । tāvadākrandaravaughaḥ samutthitaḥ pūrvadigabhimukham ॥ 6 ॥
kiṁ kimiti jalpantāvuttālagatyā yāvad gacchataḥ । tāvatpaśyataḥ prabhūtaṁ lōkaṁ piṇḍīkr̥taṁ tatra ॥7॥

nijabhāryābhiḥ samētaḥ krīḍan kānanē kr̥ṣṇēna । sarpēṇa sa daṣṭastatō vilapatyēṣa iti lōkaḥ ॥ 11 ॥

tēvi tahēva vihiyaṁ gaṁtūṇabhatthiō jaha muṇiṁda ! | maha puttō sappēṇaṁ kayaṁtaka pēṇa ḍasiutti ||15||

jā kiṁci muṇivariṁdō na bhaṇai vijjāharēṇa tō bhaṇiyaṁ । jaha ēē muṇivasahā virayā bhī tāṇa ||

tēnāpi tathaiva vihitaṁ gatvābhyarthitō yathā munīndra ! | mama putraḥ sarpēṇa kr̥tāntakalpēna daṣṭa iti ॥ 15 ॥

upadēśa dadāmyahaṁ karuṇayā tava yathā nijaṁ tanayam । muñca munipādayōḥ puratō gharaṇyāmānīya || 18॥

tatō bhaṇati munirbhō bhōḥ ! ēkasyāstava viṣaṁ naṣṭam । adyāpi mōhāhērviṣēṇa grastō'si nanu bāḍham ॥23॥

ētēna jagaddaṣṭaṁ cētati na ca kiñcidātmanaḥ kr̥tyam । ajñānagaralaghātitahāritanijakārya paraṁmārtham ॥25॥
yadi kathamapi gurunarēndraḥ sadēśanāmr̥tavāridhārābhiḥ । abhiṣiñcati taddaṣṭaṁ tathāpi na samyakparicchinatti ॥
yadi punaḥ sa karṇajāpamupadēśasumantradānatō dadāti । tathāpi hi śirō dhunāti samyama śr̥ṇōti, atha kathamapi ॥
bhavitavyatāvaśēna kasyāpi puṇyānubhāvata ēva । gurugāruḍakaprayuktō mantrō'panayati mōhaviṣam ||28||
