tā ajjavi mōhamada ahivisavēgā phuraṁti tuha bāḍhaṁ । tāṇuttāraṇahēḍaṁ tamhā jattaṁ kuṇasu bhadda ! ||29 ॥
bhai malayacaṁdō tumha pasāēṇa tēvi visavēgā । gacchissaṁti sudūrē ravikaranihayanvaṁ tamaniyarā ||
jamhā tu matthā mōhavisucchāyaṇēvi, tā pasiuṁ । tappaḍiyāraṁ taṁ kuṇaha jēṇa sō maṁ na pīḍēi ||31||
tō bhai guru nisuṇasu sammaṁ sammattamaṁḍalaṁ paḍhamaṁ । lihium̐ sikkhābaṁdhō kāyavvō tujjha amhēhi ||32||
jaidhammaparamamaṁtō dāyavvō tujha sō vihīē taō | sēvēyavvō tō sō mōhavisaṁ savvamavi harihī ||33||
iccāidēsaṇāē paḍivōhēuṁ kalattasaṁttaṁ । taṁ malapacaṁdanāmaṁ siṭṭhiyaṁ dikkhaē sāhū || 34॥
kuladharasālavaṇiṇō tēvi hu sammata dētacaraṇaṁ ca । paḍivannā annēvi hu sammattaṁ kēvi kiṁpi vayaṁ ||35||
siṭṭighaṇēsōvitahā paḍivajjai dēsaviraimakkhaṁḍaṁ । saha malayacaṁdamuṇiṇā viharai sāhūvi annattha ||36||
kuladharasāmalasaḍḍhā pasaṁsamāṇā muṇi malayacaṁdaṁ । niyaniyagihēsu pattā pāliti vihīē gihidhammaṁ ||37||
savisēsaṁ sāmaiē kuṇaṁti jattaṁ suṇaṁti siddhataṁ । gīyatyasāhumūlē sāmaiyaguṇē ya taha ēē ||38||
jaha samabhāvō sāhū sāvajjaṁ cayai kuṇai niravajjaṁ । taha sāvagōvi sammaṁ rāgadōsē pariharaṁtō ||39||
sāhuvva sō ya taiyā kammaṁ nijjarai baṁdhaī appaṁ । parimiyakālaṁ jāvai iriyāsamiyāiguṇajuttō ॥ 40 ॥
sō hu taha bhāsāō khaviūṇaṁ caraṇamōhaṇīyapi । acirēṇaṁ ciya pāva savvacaritaṁpi pāēṇa ||41 ||
i kāraṇāu niccaṁ kāyavvaṁ sāvagēṇa sāmaiyaṁ । iya sōuṁ paidiyahaṁ taṁ tē giti savisēsa ||42 ||
paha kālēṇa pamāyai sāmaiē sāmalō kukammavasā । appaḍilēhiyaapamajjiēvi ṭhāṇē nisīēi ||43||
smādadyāpi, mōhamahāhiviṣavēgāḥ sphuranti tava bāḍham । tēṣāmuttāraṇahētōstasmādyatnaṁ kuruṣva bhadra ! ॥ 29 ॥
tō bhaṇati malayacandrastava prasādēna tē'pi vipavēgāḥ । gamiṣyanti sudūrē ravikaranihatā iva tamōnikarāḥ ॥
yasmādyūyaṁ samarthā mōhaviṣōcchādanē'pi, tasmātprasadya । tatpratikāraṁ taṁ kuruta yēna sa māṁ na pīḍayati ॥21॥.
tō bhaṇati guruḥ śr̥ṇu samyaksamyaktvamaṇḍalaṁ prathamam | likhitvā śikṣābandhaḥ kartavyastavāsmābhiḥ || 32॥
pratidharmuparamamantrō dātavyastava sa vidhinā tataḥ । sēvitavyastataḥ sa mōhaviṣaṁ sarvamapi hariṣyati ॥ 33 ॥
ityādidēśanayā pratibōdhya kalatrasaṁyuktam । taṁ malayacandranāmānaṁ śrēṣṭhitaṁ dīkṣatē sādhuḥ ||34||
kuladharaśyāmalavaṇijau tāvapi hi samyaktvaṁ dēśacaraṇaṁ ca । pratipannāvanyē'pi hi samyaktvaṁ kē'pi kimapi vratam ॥
śrēṣṭhidhanēśō'pi tathā pratipadyatē dēśaviratimakhaṇḍām । saha malayacandramuninā viharati sādhurapyanyatra ॥ 36 ॥
kuladharaśyāmalaśrāddhau praśaṁsantau muniṁ malayacandram | nijanijagr̥hēṣu prāptau pālayatō vidhināṁ gr̥hidharmam ||37||
saviśēṣaṁ sāmāyikē kurutō yatnaṁ śr̥ṇutaḥ siddhāntam । gītārthasādhumūlē sāmāyikaguṇāṁśca tathaitān ॥38॥
yathā samabhāvaḥ sādhuḥ sāvadyaṁ tyajati karōti niravadyam । tathā śrāvakō'pi samyagrāgadvēṣau pariharan ॥39॥
sādhuriva sa ca tadā karma nirguṇāti baghnātyalpam । parimitakālaṁ yāpayatīryāsamityādiguṇayuktaḥ ॥ 40 ॥
sa khalu tadabhyāsātkṣapayitvā caraṇamōhanīyamapi । acirēṇaiva prāpnōti sarvacāritramapi prāyēṇa ॥ 41 ॥
iti kāraṇānnityaṁ kartavyaṁ śrāvakēṇa sāmayikam । iti śrutvā pratidivasa tattau gr̥hṇītaḥ saviśēṣam ||42 ||

||
vōsira kāiyāī apamajjiyathaṁḍilammi ṭhāēi । kāussaggēṇa tahā kaṁḍuyai pamajjiḍaṁ nēya ||44 ||
tō kuladharō nisēes mā mā duṣpaṇihiyattaṇaṁ kuṇasu । sāmaiē aiyārō hōi kuṇaṁtassa tuha ēvaṁ || 45 ||
anirikkhiyāpamajjiyathaṁḍillē ṭhāṇamāi sētō । hiṁsābhāvēvi na sō kaḍasāmaiō pamāyāō || 46 ॥
• sō bhai ki karēmī takkālē sumaraī na mē kiṁpi । paḍilēhaṇāi tō saṁbaṁdha ! pēhēsi maha chiḍḍuṁ || 47॥
tō kuladharō vikkhaṛa tahavi hu sāmāiyassa gahaṇammi । na ya sō cayai payattaṁ muṇiūṇa phalaṁ imarasa taō ||
duppaṇihiyakāraṇaṁ karēi sāmāiyaṁ tahavi ēsō । iya saiyāraṁ kāuṁ sāmaiyaṁ sō divaṁ pattō ॥ 49 ॥
apaḍhiō ya jāō iyarō sāmāiyaṁ niraiyāraṁ । pālēḍaṁ pajjētē aṇasaṇavihiṇā marēūṇa ||20||
sōhammē uvavō harisāmāṇiyasurō sarēūṇa । niyamittaṁ saṁpattō tassa samāsē tarhi caiva ॥ 51 ॥
sō taṁ picchiya pucchara kō si tumaṁ, sō bhaṇēi tuha mittaṁ । sō haṁ kuladharanāmā avahinnāṇēṇa sō muṇiraṁ ||
savvaṁ niyavr̥ttaṁtaṁ tō jhūrai tassa pāsiuṁ riddhiṁ । haddhī majjha pāō phaliō ēssa apanāō || 53 ||
sarisēhiṁ sammattaṁ paḍivanaṁ dēsavirairayaṇaṁ ca । ēgaguruṇō samīvē tahavi hu iya aṁtaraṁ jāyaṁ ॥ 54 ॥
iccā jhūriṇaṁ paṇa baṁdhava ! tayā maē tujjha । uvaēsāmayavāṇaṁ na kayaṁ kannēvimūḍhē || 55 ||
tatō vi dōnivi mahāvidēhammi saṁjamaṁ pappa | saṁpāviyavaranāṇā tē sijjhissaṁti taiyabhavē ॥ 56 ॥
॥ iti sāmāyikatratē tr̥tīyāticāravipākē sāmalakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
|
atha kālēna pramādyati sāmāyikē śyāmalaḥ kukarmavaśāt । apratilēkhitāpramārjitē'pi sthānē niṣīdati ॥
vyutsr̥jati kāyikyādyapramārjitasthaṇḍilē tiṣṭhati । kāyōtsargēṇa tathā kaṇḍūyati pramāyaṁ naiva ॥ 44 ॥
tataḥ kuladharō niṣēdhati mā mā duṣpraṇihitaṁ kuru । sāmāyikē'ticārō bhavati kurvatastavaivam ॥45॥
anirīkṣitāpramārjitasthaṇḍilē sthānādi sēvamānaḥ । hiṁsābhāvē'pi na sa kr̥tasāmāyikaḥ pramādāt ॥ 46 ॥
sa bhaṇati kiṁ karōmi tatkālē smaryatē na mayā kimapi । pratilēkhanādi tatastvaṁ bāndhava ! prēkṣasē mama cchidram ॥
tataḥ kuladhara upēkṣatē tathāpi hi sāmāyikasya grahaṇē । na ca sa tyajati prayatnaṁ jñātvā phalamasya tataḥ ॥
duṣpraṇihitakāyēna karōti sāmāyikaṁ tathāpyēṣaḥ । iti sāticāraṁ kr̥tvā sāmāyikaṁ sa divaṁ prāptaḥ ॥ 49 ॥
alparddhikaṁśca jāta itaraḥ sāmāyikaṁ niraticāram । pālayitvā paryantē'naśanavidhinā mr̥tvā ॥50॥
saudharma upapannō harisāmānikasuraḥ smr̥tvā । nijamittraṁ saṁprāptastasya sakāśē tatraiva ॥51॥
,
sa taṁ dr̥ṣṭrā pr̥cchati kō'si tvaṁ sa bhaṇati mittram । sō'haṁ kuladharanāmā'vadhijñānēna sa jñātvā ||12||
sarva nijavr̥ttāntaṁ tataḥ khidyatē tasya dr̥ṣṭyā r̥ddhim । hā dhig mama pramādaḥ phalita ētasyāpramādaḥ ॥ 53 ॥
sadr̥śābhyāṁ samyaktvaṁ pratipannaṁ dēśa viratiratnaṁ ca । ēkagurōḥ samīpē tathāpi khalvityantaraṁ jātam ||14||
ityādi khittvā prabhaṇati bāndhava । tadā mayā tava । upadēśāmr̥tapānaṁ na kr̥taṁ karṇē'pi mūḍhēna ॥ 55 ॥
tataścyutvā dvāvapi mahāvidēhē saṁyamaṁ prāpya । saṁprāptavarajñānau tau sētsyatastr̥tīyabhavē ॥ 56 ॥

kālāvahiṁ na pūrai gōhēu sāmāiya jāṁhēcchō vā । takkaraṇē varuṇō iva sahēi kumaīsu dukkhāī ॥ 1 ॥
tathāhi ;-
paribhamiraramaṇikaracaraṇaraṇiramaṇivalayanēuraravēhiṁ । pāhāuyatūravō khalijjaē jammi taṁ naraṁ ||2||
nāmē naṁdivaddhagamiha purasāmī ravivva sūranivō । paḍiyaaritimirōhō tahavi hu nō kahavi sattāsō ॥
vaha siḍī purasiṭṭhī vasaī tarhi suṁdarōtti nāmēṇa । varuṇadharaṇābhihāṇā tassa ya taṇayā nayavahāṇā ||
aha annayā naīē kūlē kēlīē jāva kīlaṁti । tāva sahasatti kattō pattō cāraṇamuṇī tattha || 5 |
paṇaō tēhi taō sō dhammaṁ sāhēi mahuravāṇīē । sammattāī savvaṁ jaigihibhēēhiṁ tō tēhi || 6 ||
saat gimmi paḍhasamatthēhi thēvadiyahēhi । nāō jahaḍiō sōrhati parāē bhattīē || 7 ||
sāmayahaṇaṁ para paidiyahamahiggahaṁ vihēūṇa । giṇhaṁti dōvi samagaṁ varuṇō dharaṇō ya tē vihiṇā ॥ 8 ॥
kiṁtu avarhi na pūrai varuṇō sāmāiyaṁ gahēūṇaṁ । kajjammi samupapannē punna innōvva pārē ॥ 9 ॥
tō gharaṇō pannavaī varuṇaṁ ēvaṁ na jujjaē kāuṁ । ghaḍiyadurgapi na pālasi sāmaiyaṁ sammabhāvēṇa || 10 ||
anyatrāpyuktam ;-
kāūṇa takkhaṇaṁ ciya pārēi karēi vā jahicchāē । aṇavadviyasāmaiyaṁ aṇāyarāō na taṁ suddhaṁ ॥ 11 ॥
aṇavadviyassa kajjaṁ sijjhai ihalōiyaṁpi nō jamhā । iha atthē cārahaḍō dihaṁtō cāhuyāṇōti ॥ 12 ॥
tathāhi ;-
gāmammi sāligāmē nivasaī ēgō samudadhurō sūrō। nāmēṇa guṇēṇa ya tassa bhāriyā sirimaī nāma ॥
kālāvadhiṁ na pūrayati gr̥hītvā sāmāyikaṁ yathēcchō vā । tatkaraṇē varuṇa iva sahatē kugatiṣu duḥkhāni ॥ 1 ॥
paribhramitr̥ramaṇīkaracaraṇarāṇatamaṇivalayanūpuraravaiḥ । prābhātikatūryaravaḥ svalyatē yasmiṁstannagaram ॥2॥
nāmnā nandivardhanamiha purasvāmī raviriva sūranr̥paḥ । pratihatāritimiraughastathāpi hi nō kaścamapi satrāsaḥ ॥
tathā śrēṣṭhī puraśrēṣṭhī vasati tatra sundara iti nāmnā | varuṇadharaṇābhivānau tasya ca tanayau nayapradhānau || 4 |
athānyadā nadyāḥ kūlē kēlyā yāvatkrīḍataḥ । tāvatsahasēti kutaḥ prāptaścāraṇamunistatra ॥5॥
praṇatastābhyāṁ tataḥ sa dharmaṁ kathayati madhuravāṇyā । samyaktvādi sarva yatigr̥hibhēdābhyāṁ tatastābhyām ||6||
pratipannōṁ gr̥hidharmaḥ prathamāsamarthābhyāṁ stōkadivasaiḥ । jñātō yathāsthitaḥ sō'nutiṣṭhataḥ parayā bhaktyā ||7||
sāmāyikagrahaṇaṁ prati pratidivasamabhigrahaṁ vidhāya । gr̥hṇītā dvāvapi samaṁ varuṇō dharaṇaśca tau vidhinā ||8||
kintvavadhiṁ na pūrayati varuṇaḥ sāmāyikaṁ gr̥hītvā । kāryē samutpannē pūrṇapratijña itha pārayati ॥9॥
tatō dharaṇaḥ prajñāpayati varuṇamēvaṁ na yujyatē kartum । ghaṭikādvikamapi na pālayasi sāmayikaṁ samyagbhāvēna ||
kr̥tvā tatkṣaṇamēva pārayati karōti vā yathēccham । anavasthitasāmāyikamanādarānna tacchuddham ॥11॥
anavasthitasya kāryaṁ sidhyatyaiha lōkikamapi nō yasmāt । ihārthē cārabhaṭō dr̥ṣṭāntaścāhumāna iti ॥ 12॥
grāmē śāligrāmē nivasatyēkaḥ samuddhuraḥ śūraḥ । nāmnā guṇēna ca tasya bhāryā śrīmatī nāma ॥ 13॥

supāsanāha-cariammi - .
tāṇa suō cārahaḍō nāmēṇa guṇēga atthi supasiddhō । sō jōvvaṇammi pattō ōlāi naravaī bhīmaṁ ॥
annōvi tassa mittō nāmēṇaṁ mōhaṇō naravaissa । alaggai sōvi taō abhōyaṇa visēsēṇa ॥ 15 ॥
paccūsē uṭṭhēuṁ dōvi hu gacchēti rāyapāsampi । namiūṇaṁ cārahaḍō khaṇāu uṭṭhēvi gacchēi || 16 ||
bīō mōhanāmā tā ciṭṭai naravarassa pāsammi । jā jimiūṇaṁ rāyā sijjāē ṭhāi samayasmi || 17 ||
tō uṭṭhaūṇa vāhi gaṁtuṁ bhuṁjē puṇavi samayampi | āgaccha nivapāsē tahēva picchē taṁ rāyā ||18||
cārahaḍō uṇa aṁtaṁtarāō kajjaṁtarēṇa gacchēi । tō picchai bhūvālō sēvāē aṁtaraṁ tāṇa ॥ 19 ॥
aha annapā nariṁdō bhōtuṁ sijjāē ṭhāi jā tattō । nisuṇai purassa majjhē lōyāṇaṁ vahalatumularakhaṁ ||20||
tō saṁtō rāyā mōhaṇamāisai jaha tumaṁ gaṁtuṁ । puramajjhē avalōyasu kō hēū tumulasadassa ||21||
tō mōhaṇōvi gaṁtuṁ jā picchai karivaraṁ vigayamiṁṭha । bhajataṁ cūraṁtaṁ gharahaṭṭāīṇi purama ||22||
tō hakkaō kariṁdō tēṇa taō saṁmuhaṁ samucchalium̐ । gayasikkhākusalēṇaṁ vasīkaō mōhaṇēṇa lahuṁ ||
tō paḍihārō gaṁtuṁ sāhai savrvvapi naravaissa tayaṁ । kōūhalēṇa rāyā saṁpattō tattha ṭhāṇammi ||24||
karikhaṁdhagayaṁ baddhuṁ taṁ tō ciṁtēi naravaī ēvaṁ । tumulaparijāṇaṇaṭṭā paṭṭaviō na uṇa ii kāuṁ ||25||
tō raṁjiēṇa rannā dinnō sō caiva tassa varahatthī । saha visayāvāsēhi maṁḍaliyapayammi saṁṭhaviō || 26॥
tō cārahaḍō cita ēēṇa maēvi sēviō ēsō । ēyassa iyapasāyaṁ viyarai nō prajjha puṇa kiṁpi ||27||
tahavihu sō alagga va aṇavaḍiō, taō rāyā । majjhanē paricitai cārahaḍassāvi viyarēmi ||
1
tayōḥ sutaścārabhaṭō nāmnā guṇēnāsti suprasiddhaḥ । sa yauvanē prāptō'valagati narapatiṁ bhīmam ॥ 14 ॥
anyō'pi tasya mittraṁ nāmnā mōnō narapatim । avalagati sō'pi tatō'bhōjanēna viśēṣēṇa ||15||
pratyūṣa utthāya dvāvapi hi gacchatō rājapārśvē । natvā cārabhaṭaḥ kṣaṇādutthāya gacchati ॥ 16 ॥
dvitīyō mōhananāmā tāvattiṣṭhati naravarasya pārśvē । yāvajjāmitvā rājā śayyāyāṁ tiṣṭhati samayē ॥ 17 ॥
tata utthāya bahirgatvā bhuṅktē punarapi samayē । āgacchati nr̥papārśvē tathaiva paśyati taṁ rājā ॥ 18 ॥
cārabhaṭaḥ punarantarāntarā kāryāntarēṇa gacchati । tataḥ paśyati bhūpālaḥ sēvāyāmantaraṁ tayōḥ ॥19॥
athānyadā narēndrō bhuktvā śayyāyāṁ tiṣṭhati yāvattataḥ । śr̥ṇōti purasya madhyē lōkānāṁ bahalatumularavam ||
tataḥ saṁbhrāntō rājā mōhanamādiśati yathā tvaṁ gatvā । puramadhyē'valōkasva kō hētustumulaśabdasya ॥ 21 ॥
tatō mōhanō'pi gatvā yāvatpaśyati karivaraṁ vigatahastipakam । bhañjantaṁ cūrṇayantaṁ gharahaṭṭādīni puramadhyē ||
tatō hātkr̥taḥ karīndrastēna tataḥ saṁmukhaṁ samucchalya । gajaśikṣākuśalēna vaśīkr̥tō mōhanēna laghu ॥ 23 ॥
tataḥ pratihārō gatvā kathayati sarvamapi narapatēstat । kutūhalēna rājā saṁprāptastatra sthānē ||24||
kariskandhagataṁ dr̥ṣṭrā taṁ tataścintayati narapatirēvam । tumulaparijñānārthaṁ prasthāpitō na punariti kartum ||25||
tatō rañjitēna rājñā- dattaḥ sa ēva tasmai varahastī । saha viṣayāvāsa maṇḍalikapadē saṁsthāpitaḥ ॥ 26 ॥
tataścārabhaṭaścintayatyētēna mayāpi sēvita ēṣaḥ । ētasmā iti prasādaṁ vitarati nō mahyaṁ punaḥ kimapi ||27||

varuṇakahā ।
566
kiṁcivi gāmāīyaṁ hakkārāvara tayaṁpi tō tattha । paḍihārāō, sō natthi tattha iya kahai sō rannō ।। .
aṇavadaḍiō ya ēsō paḍihārō vinnavē nivaissa । dēva ! pasāyaajōggō, tō rāyā bhaṇai ēvamiṇaṁ ।।
tō kēvi sē kahiyaṁ jaha taṁ rannā nirūviō ajja । sō bhai ahaṁ bhāgya ! paōyaṇēṇa gaō āsi ।।
dō tinni diṇāī tō niraṁtaraṁ rāyasaṁnihāṇammi | ṭhāuṁ puṇōvi tahavi hu uṭṭhēuṁ jāi ēmēva ||32||
tō mōhaṇēṇa bhaṇiō baṁdhava ! aṇavaḍiō si sēvāē । supāḍilaggō jai havasi kahavi tō taṣphalaṁ lahasi ।।
tō tēṇaṁ sō bhaṇiō vinnavasu narēsaraṁ sarasu paṇayaṁ । jēṇa pasīyai majjhavi vinnattō tēṇa tō rāyā ॥
jaha pahu ! cārahaḍassavi kuṇasu pasāyaṁ visīyara ēsō । bukkaṁtō bahukālō tuha payasēvaṁ kuṇaṁtassa ||35||
tassa rōhēṇa taō dinaṁ gāmaṁ nivēṇa tassavi ya । tā bhō ! suppaḍilaggō tumapi sāmāiē havasu || 36 ||
saggāpavaggavisayaṁ jai sōkkhaṁ mahasi tā thirō hōuṁ । sāmāiyamavi pālatu iya bhaṇiuṁ vigmaē dharaṇō ॥
tō varuṇēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ēvamiṇaṁ kiṁtu kammavasagōtti । na havāmi supaḍilaggō sāmāiē ki karēmi ahaṁ ? ||
tadagrahaṇēvi na sakkō ṭhāumahaṁ jaha tahēva givhēmi । tā tuha sikkhāēṁ ahaṁ arihō na havāmi iya vōttuṁ ॥
puṇaravi tahā payaṭṭara kālēṇaṁ kavaliō sa kālēṇa । jōisiēsuvavannō ajjavi bhamihī bhavē suciraṁ ॥
dharaṇēṇaṁ cirakālaṁ sāmaiyaṁ pāliyaṁ niraiyāraṁ । pāṇē vihiṇā caiuṁ īsāṇē suravarō jāō || 41||
tattō cuō vidēhē sijjhissai caraṇasaṁ । yaṁ lahiuṁ । tā jattō kāyavvō sāmaiē savvakālaṁpi ||42 ||
॥ iti caturthāticāravipākē varuṇakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
tathāpi khalu sō'valagati tathaivānavasthitaḥ, tatō rājā । madhyāhnē paricintayati cārabhaṭāyāpi vitarāmi ॥
kiñcidapi grāmādikaṁ hakkārayati tamapi tatastatra । pratihārāt sa nāsti tatrēti kathayati sa rājñē ॥29॥
anavasthitaścaiṣa pratihārō vijñapayati nr̥patayē । dēva ! prasādāyōgyaḥ, tatō rājā bhaṇatyēvamidam ॥ 30 ॥
tataḥ kēnāpi tasmai kathitaṁ yathā tvaṁ rājñā nirūpitō'dya । sa bhaṇatyahaṁ bhrātaḥ ! prayōjanēna gata āsam ॥31॥
dvē trīṇi dināni tatō nirantaraṁ rājasaṁnidhānē । sthitvā punarapi tathāpi hyutthāya yātyēvamēva ॥ 32 ॥
tatō mōhanēna bhaṇitō bānvava ! anavasthitō'si sēvāyām । supratilammō yadi bhavasi kathamapi tatastatphalaṁ labhatē ॥
tatastēna sa bhaṇitō vijñapaya narēśvaraṁ smara praṇayam । yēna prasīdati mayyapi vijñaptastēna tatō rājā ॥ 34 ॥
yathā prabhō ! cārabhaṭāyāpi kuru prasādaṁ viṣīdatyēṣaḥ । vyutkrāntō bahukālastava padasēvāṁ kurvataḥ ||35||
tasyānurōdhēna tatō dattō grāmō nr̥pēṇa tasmā apica । tasmād bhōḥ supratilagnastvamapi sāmāyikē bhava || 36 ||
svargāpavargaviṣayē yadi saukhyaṁ kāṅkṣasi tadā sthirō bhūtvā । sāmāyikamapi pālayēti bhaṇitvā viramati dharaṇaḥ ॥
tatō varuṇēna bhaṇitamēvamidaṁ kintu karmavaśa iti । na bhavāmi supratilagnaḥ sāmāyikē kiṁ kurvē'ham ||38||
tadagrahaṇē'pi na śaktaḥ sthātumahaṁ yathā tathaiva gr̥hṇāmi । tasmāttava śikṣāyā ahamahōṁ na bhavāmītyuktvā ॥
punarapi tathā pravartatē kālēna kavalitaḥ sa kālē । jyōtiṣkēṣūpapannō'dyāpi bhramiṣyati bhavē suciram ॥40॥
dharaṇēna cirakālaṁ sāmāyikaṁ pālitaṁ niraticāram । prāṇānvidhinā tyaktvēśānē suravarō jātaḥ ॥41॥
tataścyutō vidēhē sētsyati caraṇasaṁpadaṁ labdhvā । tasmādyatnaḥ katarvyaḥ sāmāyikē sarvakālamapi ॥ 42 ॥

sunnattaṇaō gahiyaṁ sāmāiyamaṇuṭṭiyapi sutrēṇa । sāṁmēṇava jēṇa tayaṁ apaṁ citra sō phalaṁ lahai ॥ 1 ॥
tathāhi ;-
asthi puraṁ kaṁpillaṁ bhārahavāsamma gayaṇasamasōhaṁ । gurubuhakavikamaṇīyaṁ diyarāyavirāiyaṁ ca tahā ||2||
taṁ pālai bhūvālō jayavālō vissavissuō, tassa । piyakaṁtā nāmēṇaṁ guṇaōnya samatthi suphala || 3 ||
taha asthi vaṇipāṇō sumaibhihāṇō piyā ya sē sulasā । tēsiṁ puttō sōmō sōmō iva baṁdhukumuyāṇaṁ ||4||
kumayavaṇē aṇavarayaṁ paribhamaṁtō samaṁtabhadassa । bhaṭṭassa saṁnihāṇē pattō paṇamit taccaraṇē ||5||
pucchara kahēsu kiṁcivi kahāvisēsa visēsaō majjha । jamuciyadhammāṇugayaṁ bhaṇēi vippō nisā mēsu || 6 ||
kamma giridugganayarē duggō nāmēṇa māhaṇō vasai । nivvinnakāmabhōgō karēi bahutitthajatāō ||7||
aha annayā bhatō pattō ēkkammi vaṇaniguṁjammi | vēllahalavēllipallavasaṁchāiyasayala bhūbhāgē ||8||
tatthanēsai salilaṁ tavhāsusiōṭṭhakaṁṭhaō jāva । tō niyaha aṁdhakūvaṁ vallitriyāṇēhi saṁchannaṁ ॥9॥
aiguruvallivarataṁ valiuṁ karabattiyāṁē baṁdhēi । taṁ khibai kūvamadhyē tā caḍiō tattha lahubālō ॥ 10 ॥
uttariō tēṇa taō paṇaō vippō taō yasō bhaṇai । kō si tumaṁ kaha paḍiō ēttha, taō kahai sō ēvaṁ ॥
mālāgārassa suō mahurāṉayarīē rāyamalayāō । cōrēṇaṁ āṇīō vagghabhaēṇēha kummi || 12 ||
dōdivi khittō appā taha sunnārēṇa nīratisiēṇa । gāruḍiēṇāvi tahā khittō appā iha lahuṁpi ॥ 13 ॥
ciṭṭhēti tēvi kūvē tō taṁ suṇiuṁ puṇōvi vippēṇaṁ । khittā tattha varattā tā gāruḍiōvi ṇikktō ||
।
śūnyatvatō gr̥hītaṁ sāmāyikamanuṣṭhitamapi śūnyēna । sōmēnēva yēna tadalpamēva sa phalaṁ labhatē ॥1॥
asti puraṁ kāmpilyaṁ bhāratavarṣē gaganasamaśōbham । gurubudhakavikamanīyaṁ dvijarājavirājitaṁ ca tathā ॥2॥
tat pālayati bhūpālō jayapālō viśvāvaśrutaḥ, tasya । priyakāntā nāmnā guṇataśca samasti sukalatram ||3||
tathāsti vaṇikpradhānaḥ sumatyabhidhānaḥ priyā ca tasya sulasā । tayōḥ putraḥ sōmaḥ sōma iva bandhukumudānām ||4||
kumatavanē'navarataṁ paribhramansamantabhadrasya । bhaṭṭasya saṁnidhānē prāptaḥ praṇamya taccaraṇau ||5||
pr̥cchati kathayati kañcidapi kathāviśēṣaṁ viśēṣatō mama । ya ucitadharmānugatō bhaṇati viprō niśamaya ॥ 6 ॥
kasmin giridurganagarē durgōṁ nāmnā brāhmaṇō vasati । nirviṇṇakāmabhōgaḥ karōti bahutīrthayātrāḥ ||7||
athānyadā bhramanprāpta ēkasmin vanānikuñja । kōmalēvallipallava saṁchāditasakala bhūbhāgē ॥ 8 ॥
tatrānvēṣyati salilaṁ tr̥ṣṇāśuṣkōṣṭhakaṇṭhakō yāvat । tataḥ paśyatyandhakūpaṁ vallivitānaiḥ saṁchannam ॥9॥
atiguruvallivastrāṁ valayitvā karapatrikayā badhnāti । tāṁ kṣipati kūpamadhyē tadā caṭitastatra laghubālaḥ ॥ 10 ॥
uttāritastēna tataḥ praṇatō viprastataśca sa bhaṇati । kō'si tvaṁ kathaṁ patitō'tra, tataḥ kathaṁyati sa ēvam ॥
mālākārasya sutō mathurānagaryō rājamalayāt । caurēṇā nītī vyāghrabhayēnēha kūpē ॥ 12 ॥
dvābhyāmapi kṣipta ātmā tathā suvarṇakārēṇa nīratr̥ṣitēna । gāruḍikēnāpi tathā kṣipta ātmēha ladhvapi ॥ 13 ॥
? ga kumuya ।

sāvi kamēṇa taō namiuṁ viṣpaṁ bhaṇati taṁ jaṇaō | ahava gurū saṁjāō amhāṇaṁ pāṇadāṇāō || 15॥
savvēvi hu mahurāē vatthavvā pāyaṁḍā ya tatthamhē । titthāvagāhanatthaṁ āgaṁtavyaṁ taē tattha ॥ 16 ॥
tujvāraṁ kāuṁ amhē niraṇīkayā bhavissāmō । aha pāṇadāyagāṇaṁ uvayārō dukkarō kāuṁ ||17||
tō bhaṇiō bhaṭṭaṇaṁ cōrō jaha ēsa bālaō milai । niyapīūṇaṁ tumaē kāyavvaṁ taha taē sigyaṁ ॥ 18 ॥
ēvaṁ karēmi bhaṇiuṁ tattō tēṇō gaō tahanēvi । kittiyakālāō taō viṣpōvi samāgaō tattha ||19||
mahurāē bahuvihakusumaphalabharōnamiyamalayachāyāē । pahasaṁtō uvavihō jā ciṭṭhā tattha tō diṭṭhō ||20||
mālāgārasugaṁ hiṭṭēṇaṁ paṇamiō sasaṁbhataṁ । nāraṁga kēlidakkhādā ḍimaphalaphulamāīhi ||21||
kāraviya pāṇavitti nīō niyamaṁdirammi malayaṁtō । tō tēṇaṁ tēṇassavi kahiō tassāgamō tayaṇu ॥ 22 ॥
sōvi lahuṁ saṁpatō ēgatē paṇamiūṇa cōrēṇa । cōriyanivaāharaṇaṁ bahumullaṁ tassa taṁ dinaṁ ||23||
tō sunnārasiṁhaṁ sō pattō nāūṇa tassa pāsāō । taṁ bhaṇai mēṁ viyāṇasi, sō bhaṇai ahaṁ na yāṇēmi ||
tō kahiyaṁ bhaṭṭaṇaṁ sōhaṁ iccāi jāva sāhēi । tō uṭṭiūṇa dinnaṁ niyāsaṇaṁ saṁbhamavimukaṁ ||25||
tō bhaṭṭē rahasmī taṁ āharaṇaṁ nirdēsiya tassa | vikkīya imaṁ appasu maha mullaṁ kipi taṁ ginha || 26॥
sōhi āharaṇaṁ hi gaō māhaṇōvi jamuṇāē । nisuṇai sō sunnārō paḍahayasa vivaṇimaggē |
jō kōvi kaha cōraṁ rāyasuyaṁ jēṇa māriuṁ gahiyaṁ । āharaṇaṁ tastra nivō lakkhaṁ viyarēḍa iya sōuṁ ॥
tiṣṭhanti tē'pi kūpē tatastat śrutvā punarapi viprēṇa । kṣiptā tatra varatrā tadā gāruḍikō'pi niṣkrāntaḥ ॥ 14 ॥
śēṣā api kramēṇa tatō natvā vipraṁ bhaṇanti tvaṁ janakaḥ । athavā guruḥ saṁjātō'smākaṁ prāṇadānāt ॥ 15 ॥
sarvē'pi hi mathurāyāṁ vāstavyāḥ prakaṭāca tatra vayam | tīrthāvagāhanārthamāgantavyaṁ tvayā tatra ॥ 16 ॥
tavōpakāraṁ kr̥tvā vayaṁ nirr̥gīkr̥tā bhaviṣyāmaḥ । atha prāṇadāyakānāmupakārō duṣkaraḥ kartum ॥ 17 ॥
tatō bhaṇitō bhaṭṭēna caurō yathēṣa bālō milati । nijapitrōstvayā kartavyaṁ tathā tvayā śīghram ॥ 18 ॥
ēvaṁ karōmi bhaṇitvā tataḥ stēnō gatastathānyē'pi । kiyatkālāt tatō viprō'pi samāgatastatra ॥19॥
mathurāyāṁ bahuvidhakusumaphalabharāvanatamalayacchāyāyām । pārthaśrānta upaviṣṭō yāvattiṣṭhati tatra tatō dr̥ṣṭaḥ ॥20॥
mālākārasutēna hr̥ṣṭēna praṇataḥ saṁsaṁbhrāntam । nāraṅgakēlidrākṣādāḍimaphalapuṣpādibhiḥ ॥21॥
kārayitvā prāṇavr̥tti nītō nijamandirē malayāntaḥ । tatastēna stēnasyāpi kathitastasyāgamastadanu ||22||
sō'pi laghu saṁprāpta ēkāntē praṇamya caurēṇa । cōritanr̥pābharaṇaṁ bahumūlyaṁ tasmai tad dattam ||23||
"
•
tataḥ suvarṇakāragr̥haṁ sa prāptō jñātvā tasya pārśvāt । taṁ bhaṇati māṁ vijānāsi sa bhaṇatyahaṁ na jānāmi ||
tataḥ kathitaṁ bhaṭṭēna sō'hamityādi yāvatkathayati । tata utthāya dattaṁ nijāsanaṁ saṁbhramavimuktam ॥25॥
tatō bhaṭṭēna rahasi tadābharaṇaṁ nidarśitaṁ tasmai । vikrīyēdamarpaya mahyaṁ mūlyaṁ kimapi tvaṁ gr̥hāṇa ||26||
sa gr̥hītvābharaṇaṁ bahirgatō brāhmaṇō'pi yamunāyām । śr̥ṇōti sa suvarṇakāraḥ paṭahaśabdaṁ vipaṇimārgē ॥ 27 ॥
yaḥ kō'pi kathayati cauraṁ rājasutaṁ yēna mārayitvā gr̥hītam । ābharaṇaṁ tasmai nr̥pō lakṣaṁ vitaratīti śrutvā ||
॥

sunnārō paribhāvaī taṁ āharaṇaṁ visēsaō jāva । rāyataṇayastra taṇayaṁ ghaḍiyaṁ ca imaṁ maē caiva ||29||
tāgaṁtuṁ sāmō nissa appēvi taha alaṁkārē । giṇhāmō taṁ lakkhaṁ kiṁ kajjaṁ tēṇa vippēṇa 1 ||30||
tō taha kahē savvaṁ rāyā pucchē kattha sō inhiṁ । sōvi kahai jamuṇāē bhaṇai nivō daṁsasu imāṇa ||
ārakkhiyāṇa gaṁtuṁ sōvi hu daṁsēi tāṇa dūratthō । jamuṇāō uttinaṁ vēyajjhayaṇaṁ sarataṁ taṁ ||32||
tō pacchimavāhāhiṁ baṁdhēuṁ pabhaṇiō jahā tumaē । vāvāiuṁ kumāraṁ gahiyaṁ savrvvapi ābharaṇaṁ ||33||
nīō rāyasamīvaṁ ēēṇaṁ nihaṇiō maha kumārō | hē sunnayāra ! imiṇā tuha āharaṇaṁpi dinaṁti ||34||
sō bhai dēva ! ēvaṁ tattō aṁtēurēṇa taṁ daddhuṁ । vihiō mahāmahaṁtō akkaṁdō dukkhaduhiē ||35||
vārē akkaṁdaṁ bahussuyā māhaṇā samāhūyā । puṭṭhā kahēha daṁḍaṁ jaṁ uciyaṁ hōi ēyassa || 36 ||
tēhi bhaṇiyaṁ narēsara ! tuhasuyavahagō suvannacōrō ya । jaivi hu vippabhāsō tahāvi vajjhō dhuvaṁ ēsa ॥ 37॥
tathā ca smr̥tiḥ, "suvarṇataskaraṁ vipram" ityādi ।
tō rannā sō vajjhō āṇatō rattakusumagalamālō । kharapuṭṭhīē ṭhaviō paḍhēi sa subhāsiyaṁ ēyaṁ ॥ 38 ॥
" naśyanti guṇaśatānyapi puruṣāṇāmaguṇavatsu puruṣēṣu । añjanagiriśikharēṣviva niśāsu candrāṁśavaḥ patitāḥ”
vivagimmi jaṁtō gāruḍiēpi sō taō dihō । paramupayārī ēsō uvayariyacvō mayā nr̥ṇaṁ || 39॥
tō siddhacēḍaēṇaṁ gāruḍiēṇaṁ jhaḍatti nivakannā । sappāu ḍasāvēuṁ bhūmīē pāḍiyā jhati ॥ 40 ॥
Ferral art car skkatti kannagā tattō । rāyāvi tattha pattō silōyamēyaṁ paḍhaṁtō ya ॥ 41 ॥
suvarṇakāraḥ paribhāvayati tadābharaṇaṁ viśēṣatō yāvat । rājatanayasya saṁbandhi ghaṭitaṁ cēdaṁ mayaiva ॥ 29 ॥
tasmād gatvā kathayāmō nr̥pāyāpayitvā tathā'laṁkārān । gr̥hṇīmastallakṣaṁ kiṁ kāryaṁ tēna viprēṇa ? ||20||
tatastathā kathayati sarvaṁ rājā pr̥cchati kva sa idānīm ? । sō'pi kathayati yamunāyāṁ bhaṇati nr̥pō darśayaibhyaḥ ॥
ārakṣikēbhyō gatvā sō'pi hi darśayati tēbhyō dūrasthaḥ । yamunāta uttīrṇa vēdādhyayanaṁ smarantaṁ tam ॥32॥
tataḥ paścimabāhubhyāṁ baddhvā prabhaṇitō yathā tvayā । vyāpādya kumāraṁ gr̥hītaṁ sarvamapyābharaṇam ||33||
nītō rājasamīpam, ētēna nihatō mama kumāraḥ । hē suvarṇakāra ! anēna tavābharaṇamapi dattamiti ॥ 34 ॥
sa bhaṇati dēva ! ēvaṁ tatō'ntaḥ purēṇa taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā । vihitō mahāmahānākrandō du:khaduḥkhitēna ॥ 35 ॥
vārayitvā''kandaṁ bahuśrutā brāhmaṇāḥ samāhūtāḥ । pr̥ṣṭāḥ kathayata daṇḍaṁ ya ucitō bhavatyētasya || 36॥
tairbhaṇitaṁ narēśvara ! tvatsutaghātakaḥ suvarṇacauraśca । yadyapi hi viprābhāsastathāpi badhyō dhruvamēṣaḥ ||37||
tatō rājñā sa vadhya ājñaptō raktakusumamālāgalaḥ । kharapr̥ṣṭhē sthāpitaḥ paṭhati sa subhāṣitamētat ॥38॥
vipaṇimārgē yān gāruḍikēnāpi sa tatō dr̥ṣṭaḥ । paramōpakāryēṣa upakartavyō mayā nūnam ॥ 39 ॥
tataḥ siddhacēṭakēna gāruḍikēna jhaṭiti nr̥pakanyā । sarpēṇa daṁśayitvā bhūmau pātitā jhaṭiti ॥ 40 ॥
hāhāravaḥ pravr̥ttōṁ daṣṭā daṣṭēti kanyā tataḥ । rājāpi tatra prāptaḥ ilōkamētaṁ paṭhaśca ॥ 41 ॥

ēvaṁ vicitiūṇaṁ paḍahayasaddēṇa savvaō nayarē । āhūyā gāruḍiyā jīvāvai jō ya nivakannaṁ ॥ 42 ॥
sō lahai lakkhavitti tō sō sōūṇa puvvagāruḍiō | paḍaddaṁ chivēvi pattō rāyasamīvammisaṁtuṭṭō ||43||
bhaṇai narēsara ! kannaṁ jīvāvissāmi nicchaō ēsa। jō kiṁtu vajjhaṭhāṇē nijjai sō māhaṇō suddhō || 44 ||
rakkhāvasu taṁ sighaṁ rannā āṇāviō tahiṁ vippō । puvvattō vr̥ttaṁtō tēṇavi kahiō samaggōvi ॥ 46 ॥
gāruḍiēṇavi vālā uṁjiya jīvāviyā khaṇadvēṇa । rāyāvi paḍha ēvaṁ muṇium̐ sunnāvuttaṁtaṁ ॥ 46 ॥
"upakāriṇi viśrabdha āryajanē ya: samācarati pāpam । taṁ janamasatyasaṁdhaṁ bhagavati vasudhē ! kathaṁ vadasi ? ||
ii paribhāviya rannā suvannayāraṁ dharāviḍaṁ jhattiṁ । gāruḍiō sammāṇiya suvannalakkhēṇa mukkōti ॥47॥
vippōvi khamāvēḍaṁ sammāṇēūṇa bahuyadavvēhiṁ । bhaṇiō bhaṇēsu annaṁpi jēṇa kajjaṁ tuha ihajja ॥48॥
tō baṁbhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ millēsu majjha uvayāriṁ । annaha kaha tuha daṁsaṇamēsō ēvaṁ jaṛa na kāhī ? ॥ 49 ॥
tatō rājā subhāṣitamapaṭhat ;-
"upakāriṇi vītamatsarē vā sadayatvaṁ yadi tatra kō'tirēkaḥ ? |
ahitē sahasāparādhalabdhē saghr̥ṇaṁ yasya manaḥ satāṁ sa dhuryaḥ ॥
pratyupakurvan pūrvaṁ kr̥tōpakārō'pi lajjayati cētaḥ ।
yastu vihitāpakārādupakāraḥ sō'dhikō mr̥tyōḥ || ”
tavtrayaṇēṇaṁ rannā mukkō jīēṇa sō ya sunnārō । niyadēsāō niddhāḍiūṇa daviṇaṁ gaūṇa ॥ 50 ॥
gāruḍiēṇaṁ laddhaṁ jaṁ rannāō suvanna lakkhāī । taṁ baṁbhaṇassa dinaṁ paccuvayāritti paḍhaī ya ॥ 51 ॥
"pratyupakurvanbahvapi na bhavati pūrvēpakāriṇā tulyaḥ । ēkō'nukarōti kr̥taṁ niṣkāraṇamēva kurutē'nyaḥ ॥ "
ēvaṁ vicintya paṭahaśabdēna sarvatō nagarē । āhūtā gāruḍikā jīvayati yaśca nr̥pakanyām ॥42॥
sa labhatē lakṣavr̥tti tataḥ sa śrutvā pūrvagāruḍikaḥ । paṭahaṁ spr̥ṣṭvā prāptō rājasamīpē saṁtuṣṭaḥ ॥ 43 ॥
bhaṇati narēśvara ! kanyāṁ jīvayiṣyāmi niścaya ēṣaḥ । yaḥ kintu vadhyasthānē nīyatē sa brāhmaṇaḥ śuddhaḥ ॥
rakṣaya taṁ śīghraṁ rājñā''nāyitastatra vipraḥ । pūrvōktō vr̥ttāntastēnāpi kathitaḥ samagrō'pi ॥ 45 ॥
gāruḍikēnāpi bālā yuktvā jīvitā kṣaṇārdhēna । rājāpi paṭhatyēvaṁ jñātvā suvarṇakāravr̥ttāntam ॥ 46 ॥
iti paribhāvya rājñā suvarṇakāraṁ dhārayitvā jhaṭiti । gāruḍikaḥ sammānya suvarṇalakṣēṇa mukta iti ॥47॥
viprō'pi kṣamayitvā sammānya bahudravyaiḥ । bhaṇitō bhaṇānyadapi yēna kāryaṁ tavēhādya ॥48॥
tatō brāhmaṇēna bhaṇitamēnaṁ muñca mamōpakāriṇam | anyathā kathaṁ tava darśanamēṣa ēvaṁ yadi nākārṣīt ||49॥
tadvacanēna rājñā muktō jīvitēna sa ca suvarṇakāraḥ । nijadēśād nirdhāṭya draviṇaṁ gr̥hītvā ॥ 50 ॥
gāruḍikēna labdhaṁ yad rājñaḥ suvarṇalakṣādi । tad brāhmaṇāya dattaṁ pratyupakārīti paṭhati ca ॥51॥

supāsanāha-cariasmi -
I
taṁ nattha kiṁpi vatthaṁ uyariḍaṁ jaṁ bhavāmi niraṇō haiṁ । aha pāṇadāyagāṇaṁ dukkhaṁ niraṇattaṇaṁ kāuṁ ॥ 52 ॥
iccā papē tapāē paṇamiuṁ niyagihammi । kaivayadiṇāṇi dhariḍaṁ visajjiō sō ihaṁ pattō ||53॥
sibhikkhurūvārī ujjāṇē ajja sō maē diṭṭhō । tēṇa iyaṁ niyacariyaṁ kahiyaṁ vatthavvalōyassa ॥54॥
kēṇa puṇa kāraṇēṇaṁ sēyaṁvarasaṁtiyaṁ vayaṁ gahiyē ? । sōmēṇa imō puṭṭhō sō bhaṇaī nō imaṁ puḍhaṁ ॥ 65 ॥
āgaccha tattha jāmō pucchēmō taṁpi kāraṇaṁ gaṁtuṁ । iya bhaṇiuṁ dōvi gayā tassa muṇidassa pāsamma || 56 ॥
nami pucchara sōmō bhayavaṁ ! kiṁ kāraṇaṁ vayaggahaṇē ? । sō bhaṇai sōma ! mahurāsuvannayārō ihaṁ hēū ॥57॥
jaha puvviṁ taccariyaṁ kahiyaṁ taha caiva kahai tā jāva । nivvisaō āṇatō sō sunnārō nivēṇa taō ॥ 58 ॥
sō una paribbhamatō pattō ēgammi puravaēsamma । tatthēgō muṇivasabhō diṭṭhō jhāṇaḍiō tēṇa ॥59॥
taṁ paṇamiya uvaviṭṭhō muṇiṇā jiṇadhammadēsaṇā vihiyā । paḍibuddhēṇaṁ gahiyā jiṇadikkhā sunnayārēṇa || 60||
gahiūṇa duvihasikkhaṁ ēkkallavihārapaḍimapaḍivannō । viharatēṇaṁ diṭṭhō ahaṁ niyattō a mahurāē ॥ 61 ॥
paḍiuvayāramaīē puvvakkiyadukkaḍassa samaṇaṭṭhā। pavvāviō ya tēṇaṁ paḍivōhivi duvihasikkhāē || 62 ||
vihiō aīvakusalō kāṇēkkallapa ḍimapaḍivannō । viharaṁtō iha pattō iya kahiyē tumha niyacariyaṁ ॥ 63 ॥
tā bhō mahāṇubhāvā! lōiyatitthēsu paribhamaṁtēṇa । pattamiṇaṁ punnēhiṁ paramapavittaṁ sumuṇititthaṁ ॥ 64 ॥
tasṇubhāvēṇa maē tinō saṁsārasāyarō ghōrō। tumhēhivi jiṇadhammē jaiyanvaṁ ēvama immi ||65 ||
bhattī jiṇēsu mittī jiēsu tattī ya gurubaēsēsu । pīī sīlaguṇaḍ ṭṭhēsu taha maī dhammasavaṇammi ||66॥
tad nāsti kimapi vastūpacarya yadbhavāmi nirr̥ṇō'ham । atha prāṇadāyakānāṁ duḥkhaṁ nirr̥ṇatvaṁ kartum ॥52॥
ityādi prajalpya tatpādau praṇamya nijagr̥hē । katipayadināni dhr̥tvā visarjitaḥ sa iha prāptaḥ ||13||
sitabhikṣurūpadhāryudyānē'dya sa mayā dr̥ṣṭaḥ । tēnēdaṁ nijacaritaṁ kathitaṁ vāstavyalōkasya ||14||
kēna punaḥ kāraṇēna śvētāmbara saṁbandhi vrataṁ gr̥hītam ? | sōmēnāyaṁ pr̥ṣṭaḥ sa bhaṇati nō idaṁ pr̥ṣṭam ||55॥
āgaccha tatra yāvaḥ pr̥cchāvastadapi kāraṇaṁ gatvā । iti bhaṇitvā dvāvapi gatau tasya munīndrasya pārśvē ॥ 56
natvā pr̥cchati sōmō bhagavan ! kiṁ kāraṇaṁ vratagrahaṇē : sa bhaṇati sōma ! mathurāsuvarṇakāra iha hētuḥ ॥57॥
yathā pūrvaṁ taccaritaṁ kathitaṁ tathaiva kathayati tāvadyāvat । nirviṣaya ājñaptaḥ sa suvarṇakārō nr̥pēṇa tataḥ ॥ 58॥
sa punaḥ paribhraman prāpta ēkasminpurapradēśē । tatraikō munivr̥ṣabhō dr̥ṣṭō dhyānasthitastēna || 19॥
taṁ praṇamyōpaviṣṭō muninā jinadharmadēśanā vihitā । pratibuddhēna gr̥hītā jinadīkṣā suvarṇakārēṇa ॥ 60 ॥
gr̥hītvā dvividhaśikṣāmēkākivihārapratimāpratipannaḥ । viharatā dr̥ṣṭō'haṁ nivr̥ttaśca mathurāyāḥ || 61 ॥
pratyupakāramatyā pūrvakr̥taduṣkr̥tasya śamanārtham । pratrājitaśca tēna pratibōdhya dvividhaśikṣāyām ॥62॥
vihitō'tīva kuśalaḥ kālēnaikākipratimāpratipannaḥ । viharanniha prāpta iti kathitaṁ yuvayōrnijacaritam ॥ 63 ॥
tasmādbhō mahānubhāvau ! laukikatīrthēṣu paribhramatā । prāptamidaṁ puṇyaiḥ paramapavitraṁ sumunitīrtham ||64 ॥
tasyānubhāvēna mayā tīrṇaḥ saṁsārasāgarō ghōraḥ । yuvābhyāmapi jinadharmē yatitavyamēvamādau ||65 ||

sōmakahā
567
parauvayārē vittaṁ cittaṁ paralōyakajjaciṁtāē । dhammapahāṇō jammō niruvamapunnāṇa jai hōi ॥ 67॥
laddhēvi dullahē māṇumattaṇē dhammaguṇavihūṇāṇa । vōliṁti jāṇa diyahā vihalacciya tāṇa tē nāyā ||68 ||
tāṇa varamajagaṇaṁ ciya jaṇaṇēvi hu varamaraṇṇapasubhāvō । dhammaguṇavirahiēhi jēhi sajammō kaō vihalō ||
āsanna ciya jēsiṁ mahāṇubhāvāṇa bhāvibhaddattaṁ । dhammapavittipahāṇāī jaṁti tērsi ciya diṇāī || 70॥
ticciya dhannā tē punnabhāyaṇā tāṇa jīviyaṁ sahalaṁ । dhammujjayāṇa jēsiṁ ramai maī nēya pāvē ॥ 71 ॥
tō sōmēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ kaibhēō ittha hōi jiṇadhammō ? । āha muṇī duvihō sō jaigihidhammappabhēṇa ॥72॥
tāṇa saru kahiē sōmēṇa samaṁtabhadasahiēṇa । paḍivannō gimmi sambhaṁ sammattamūlavi ॥ 73 ॥
paidivasa sāmaiē kāyavvēbhiggahō kaō tēhi । kuvvaṁti paidiṇapi hu sāvayadhammaṁ payattēna ||74||
aha sōmēṇa haṭṭē vavaharamāṇēṇa dinnamuddhārē । bahudavvaṁ pagaīṇaṁ tāō davvaṁ gahēūṇa || 75 ||
annattha gayā tattō sōmō cittēṇa āulō jāō । tahavi hu jiṇabhavaṇāisa paidiyahaṁ jāi niyamēṇa ॥
sāmāiyaṁpi giṇhai sunnattaṇaō sarēi nō gahiyaṁ । kaiyā vā kāyavvaṁ sāmaiyaṁ iya na yāṇē || 77 ||
tō bhaṭṭēṇa bhaṇiō samaṁtabhadēṇa sōma ! na hu juttaṁ । sunnattaṁ vayavisaē jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ āgamē ēvaṁ ॥ 78 ॥
na sarai pamāyajuttō jō sāmaiyaṁ kayā u kāyavvaṁ । kayamakathaṁ vā tassa hu kapi vihalaṁ tayaṁ nēyaṁ ॥ 79 ॥
sōmō bhaṇēi bhāuya ! jaddivasāō ya dhaṇassa mē nāsō । taddiyahāō jāō sunnō haṁ hā kahaṁ kuṇimō ? ||
bhaktirjinēṣu maittrī jīvēṣu tatparatā ca gurūpadēśēṣu । prītiḥ śīlaguṇāḍhyēṣu tathā matirdharmaśravaṇē ॥ 66 ॥
parōpakārē vittaṁ cittaṁ paralōkakāryacintāyām । dharmapradhānaṁ janma nirupamapuṇyānāṁ yadi bhavati ॥ 67 ॥
labdhē'pi durlabhē mānuṣatvē dharmaguruvihīnānām । gacchanti yēṣāṁ divasā viphalā ēva tēśaṁ tē jñātāḥ ||68 ||
tēṣāṁ varamajananirēva jananē'pi hi varamaraṇyapaśubhāvaḥ । dharmaguṇavirahitairyaiḥ svajanma kr̥taṁ viphalam ॥ 69 ॥
āsannamēva yēṣāṁ mahānubhāvānāṁ bhāvibhadratvam । dharmapravr̥ttipradhānāni yānti tēṣāmēva dināni ॥ 70 ॥
ta ēva dhanyāsta ēva puṇyabhājanāni tēṣāṁ jīvitaṁ saphalam । dharmōdyatānāṁ yēṣāṁ ramatē matirnaiva pāpēṣu ॥71॥
tataḥ sōmēna bhaṇitaṁ katibhēdō'tra bhavati jinadharma: ? । āha munidvividhaḥ sa yatigr̥hidharmaprabhēdēna ॥72॥
tayōḥ svarūpē kathitē sōmēna samantabhadrasahitēna । pratipannō gr̥hidharmaḥ samyak samyaktvamūlō'pi ॥73॥
pratidivasaṁ sāmāyikē kartavyē'bhigrahaḥ kr̥tastābhyām । kurutaḥ pratidinamapi hi śrāvaka prayatnēna ||74 ||
atha sōmēna haṭṭē vyavaharamāṇēna dattamuddhārē । bahudravyaṁ prakr̥tibhyastā dravyaṁ gr̥hītvā ॥75॥
anyatra gatāstataḥ sōmaścittēnākulō jātaḥ । tathāpi hi jinabhavanādiṣu pratidivasa yāti niyamēna ॥ 76 ॥
sāmāyikamapi gr̥hṇāti śūnyatvataḥ smarati nō gr̥hītam । kadā vā kartavyaṁ sāmayikamiti na jānāti ॥77॥
tatō bhaṭṭēna bhaṇitaḥ samantabhadrēṇa sōma ! na hi yuktam । śūnyatvaṁ vrataviṣayē yadbhaṇitamāgama ēvam ॥78॥
na smarati pramādayuktō yaḥ sāmāyikaṁ kadā tu kartavyam । kr̥tamakr̥taṁ vā tasya khalu kr̥tamapi viphalaṁ tajjñēyam ॥
sōmō bhaṇati bhrātaḥ ! yaddivasācca dhanasya mē nāśaḥ । tadivasājjātaḥ śūnyō'haṁ hā kathaṁ kurmaḥ 1 ॥ 80 ॥

khidyantē rudanti smaranti tathā ca vilapanti yānti ca viṣādam । dr̥ṣṭavinaṣṭē dravyē na punaḥ satpuruṣacaritadharāḥ ।
pavanāndōlitakuvalayadalāvalīcañcalēti matyā । kriyatē kṣagēna lakṣmīḥ pātravibhaktā supuruṣaiḥ ||86 ॥
ityādidēśanayā vibōdhitastathāpi sa mahābhāgaḥ । śūnyamanā anuṣṭhānaṁ sāmāyikādikaṁ karōti ॥ 87 ॥
karmavaśēna kramaśaḥ paryantē prāptaṁ tad maraṇam । jyautiṣikasaukhyalābhaḥ prāpyatē yēnātistōkaḥ ॥88॥
vipraḥ punaḥ pālayitvā śrāvakadharmaṁ viśēṣataḥ samyak । sāmāyikānuṣṭhānamanuṣṭhāya samādhimaraṇēna ॥ 89 ॥
utpannaḥ saudharmē tataścyutō bhāratē varṣē । sētsyati kusumapurē gr̥hītatrataḥ kṣapita karmāśaḥ ॥90॥
pañcadōṣavipramuktaṁ niṣkampaṁ yaḥ karōti sāmāyikam । sa dēvadānavānāmapi vandanīyaḥ sadā bhavati ॥ 91 ॥
yataya iva śamitapāpāḥ susvabhāvā ullasacchubhabhāvāḥ । kr̥tasāmāyikāstē śrāvakā apyabhivādanīyāstu ॥

pāyaṁ savvavayāṇaṁ savitrāṇapi gahiyaniyamassa । saṁkhēvō jaṁ kīrai taṁ dēvagāsiyaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 1 ॥
dēsāvagāsiṁya jō karēi suddhaṁ khaṇē 'khaṇē payaō । sō dēvāsuramr̥ṇuēhiṁ pūiō hōi saṁkhōnya ||2||

bahudalasujuttavr̥ttā pattasurālayasirī susadā ya | vijayaghaṭavva nayarī vijayapurī nāma iha asthi || 3 ||
tasyatthi daṁtidataggabhinnaca ujalahikūlapariklaō । nīsēsaviyaḍa paḍivakkhanayakkamō vikamō rāyā ||4||
tassatthi paṇaiṇī paṇayavacchalā malaya maṁjarī nāma । tiṇayaṇahuyāra saṁdaḍhamayaṇatarumaṁjarivva varā ||5||
tāṇaṁ ca parupparapī saṁjuyāṇaṁ uvāiyasaēhiṁ । parisaiō ya kahamavi saṁjāō annayā putō || 6 ||
ruṁkhō nāmēṇa asaṁkhasaṁkhaparimuṇiyasayala satyatyō । viyaḍārivāravikvēva pauṇasaṁkhō asaṁkhaguṇō ||7||
sō paramaṁtisāmaṁtakōḍimuḍēhiṁ parivuḍē viyaḍē | atyāmi niviṭṭassa sāmiṇō vikaṇassa ||8||
paṇa mittu pāyaparamaṁ jāva nimaṇṇō niyampi ṭhāṇammi । ucchaṁgiya piupāē saṁvāhai viyaputraṁ tā ॥9॥
mhāvi amhā kiṁpi kasiṇagayaṇaṁgaṇā avayarataṁ । sabvēvi unnayamuhā picchaṁti ya cittajuyacittā ॥
vāmakarakaliyakhēḍayaphaḍaphaḍāḍōvaḍa riyavara suhaḍaṁ । vara suhaḍaviyaḍapāyaḍiyabhiuḍitaḍakhaṁḍa paḍē ||11||
khaṁḍaṇaparyaṁḍakara maṁḍalagga saṁkamiyasuhaḍapaḍirvivaṁ । suhaḍapaḍivibaphuḍapāḍaṇatthataḍḍa viyabhuyadaṁḍē || 12 ||
bhuyadaṁḍavaddhavaravīravalayaṁ nīsēsabhuvaṇasōṁḍīraṁ । sōṁḍīra suhaḍabhiḍaṇikalaṁparḍa suhaḍavaramēgaṁ ॥ 13 ॥
taṁ picchipa accabhuyabhayarasakaliyā parōpparaṁ suhaḍā । picchaṁti muhāī jāva tāva niyaḍīhūō suhaḍō ॥
prāyaḥ sarvavratānāṁ savistarāṇāmapi gr̥hītaniyamasya । saṁkṣēpō yaḥ kriyatē tada dēśāvakā śikaṁ bhaṇitam ॥ 1 ॥
dēśāvakāśikaṁ yaḥ karōti śuddhaṁ kṣaṇē kṣaṇē prayataḥ । sa dēvāsuramanujaiḥ pūjitō bhavati śaṅkha iva ॥2॥
bahudalasuyuktavr̥ttā prāptasurālayaśrīḥ suśabdā ca । vijayaghaṇṭēva nagarī vijayapurī nāmēhāsti || 3॥
tatrāsti dantidantāgrabhinnacaturjaladhikūlaparivalayaḥ । niḥśēṣavikaṭapratipakṣanatakramō vikramōrājā ॥4॥
tasyāsti praṇayinī praṇatavatsalā malayamañjarī nāma । trinayana hutāśasaṁdagdha madanatarumañjarīva varā ||5||
tayōśca parasparaprītisaṁyutayōrupayācitaśataiḥ । parisūcitaśca kathamapi saṁjātō'nyadā putraḥ || 6 ||
śaṁkhā nāmnā parijñātāsāṁkhya sāṁkhya sakalaśāstrārthaḥ । vikaṭārivāravikṣēpapraguṇasaṁkhyō'saṁkhyaguṇaḥ ॥ 7॥
sa pracuramantrisāmantakōṭisubhaṭaiḥ parivr̥tē vitatē । āsthānē niviṣṭasya svāminō vikramavanasya ॥8॥
praṇamya pādapadmaṁ yāvanniṣaṇṇō nijē sthānē । utsajya pitr̥pādau saṁvāhayati vinayapūrvaṁ tāvat ॥9॥
kasmādapyakasmātkamapi kr̥ṣṇagaganāṅgaṇādavatarantam । sarvē'pyunnatamukhāḥ paśyanti ca citrayutacittāḥ ॥ 10 ॥
vāmakarakaṁlitakṣvēṭakaphaḍaphaḍāṭōpadīrṇavarasubhaṭam । varasubhaṭavikaṭaprakaṭitabhr̥kuṭitaṭakhaṇḍana pracaṇḍam ॥11॥
khaṇḍanapracaṇḍakaramaṇḍalāgrasaṁkrāntasubhaṭapratibimbam । subhaṭapratibimbasphuṭapāṭanārthatatabhujadaṇḍam ॥12॥
bhujadaṇḍabaddha varavīravalayaṁ niḥśēṣabhuvanaśauṇḍarim । śauṇḍīrasubhaṭabhēdanaikalampaṭaṁ subhaṭavaramēkam ॥13॥

rāyāvi kamaladadīharāē diṭṭhīē niyai niyamuhaḍē । suhaḍāvi diti diṭṭhi niyanikhagāisatsu ||
kivi tattha jamajīhasamataralu vikarālu, raṇarasiyabhaḍapisiyagiddhālu karavālu ।
kari karivitālēti vāyaṁti bhuyadaṁḍa, paḍiraviṇa bahiraṁta sayalaṁpi bhaṁḍu || 16 ॥
kivi dharahiṁ nārāu payaḍaṁta bhaḍavāu, sumahaṁtu kivi kuṁtu daṁsaṁti sunisāu ।
jaṁpati āēsa amhāṇa pahu ! dēhi, jiva nēhu lahu ēhu amhēvi jamahi ||17||
iya vikamasuḍāṇaṁ parōpparaṁ jāva hōṁti ullāvā । īsīsiha siyavayaṇō tāva bhaḍō sōvi saṁpattī || 18 ||
āgaṁtūṇaṁ pabhaṇēi tattha rē tumha ēttha kō hēū । niyaniyaāuhagahaṇē atthāṇēsuṁ nivāṇaṁ ? ॥ 19 ॥
tētriya bhaṇati amhē niyahupāyāraviṁdapāsamma । ciṭṭhāmō jaha taha tujjha tattha rē mūḍha ! kā tattī ? |
taṁ puṇa aṇaṇunnāō samāgaō kēṇa kāraṇēṇēha hai । amhapahuṇō gihāō tā nīhara jhatti vēgēṇa ॥ 21 ॥
pabhaṇai ki kōvipaṭū annōtriya asthi ēttha bhuvaṇampi ? । sāmī vijagammivi natthi kōī annō mamaṁ mōttuṁ ॥
tā gaṁtūṇaṁ pabhaṇaha tumhē niyanāyagaṁ imaṁ vayaṇaṁ । jai jīviēṇa kajjaṁ tā dēsu isassa niyarajjaṁ ||23||
aha hiya tumhapahussa huē ittha kōvi ahimāṇō । jaṁ kira kulakamā gayamēyaṁ rajjaṁ kaha dēmi ||24||
taṁpi na juttaṁ kiṁkēṇa kassa puhaīvi sāsaṇē lihiyā । aha kulakamā gayā vā, navaraṁ puṇa khaggabalu gijjhā ||
jai puṇa tumhapahussavi tumhāṇaṁ vāvi atthi khaggabalaṁ । tā pahuṇāvi tummēhivi samagaṁ samaraṁ karēmi ahaṁ ॥
taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā'tyadbhutabhayarasakalitāḥ parasparaṁ subhaṭāḥ । paśyanti mukhāni yāvattāvannikaṭībhūtaḥ subhaṭaḥ ॥ 14 ॥
rājāpi kamaladaladīyā dr̥ṣṭyā paśyati nijasubhaṭān । subhaṭā api dadati dr̥ṣṭiṁ nijanijakhaṅgādiśastrēṣu ||
kēṁ'pi tatra yamajihvāsamataralaṁ vikarālaṁ, raṇarasikabhaṭapiśitagr̥ddhaṁ karavālam ।
karē kr̥tvā tāḍayanti vādayanti bhujadaṇḍaṁ pratiravēṇa bavirayantaḥ sakalamapi brahmāṇḍam ॥16॥
kē'pi dharanti nārācaṁ prakaṭayantō bhaṭavādaṁ sumahāntaṁ kē'pi kuntaṁ darśayanti suniśātam ।
'
jalpantyādēśamasmākaṁ prabhō ! dēhi, yathā nayēma ladhvētaṁ vayamapi yamagēham ||17||
itiṁ vikramasubhaṭānāṁ parasparaṁ yāvadbhavantyallāpāḥ । īṣadīṣaddhasitavadanastāvadbhaṭaḥ sō'pi saṁprāptaḥ || 18 ||
āgatya prabhaṇati tatra rē yuṣmākamatra kō hētuḥ । nijanijāyudhagrahaṇa āsthānēṣu niviṣṭānām ॥19॥
tē'pi ca bhaṇanti vayaṁ nijapramupādāravindapākhēṁ । tiṣṭhāmō yathā tathā tava tatra rē mūḍha ! kā cintā ! ||20||
tvaṁ punarananujñātaḥ samāgataḥ kēna kāraṇēnēha ? | asmatprabhōgr̥hāt tasmānniḥsara jhaṭiti vēgēna ||21||
prabhaṇati kiṁ kō'pi prabhuranyō'pi cāstyatra bhuvanē । svāmī trijagatyapi nāsti kō'pyanyō māṁ muktvā ॥
tasmād gatvā prabhaṇata yūyaṁ nijanāyakāmidaṁ vacanam | yadi jīvitēna kārya tadā dēvasmai nijarājyam ||23||
atha hr̥dayē yuṣmatprabhōrvartatē'tra kō'pyabhimānaḥ । yatkila kulakramāgatamētad rājyaṁ katha dadāmi ||24||
tadapi na yuktaṁ kiṁ kēna kasya pr̥thivyapi śāsanē likhitā । atha kula kramāgatā vā, kēvalaṁ punaḥ khaḍgabalagrādyā ॥
1 kha. ga. tōlaṁta vā° ।

saṁkhakahā ।
571
iya bhaṇiē gururōsambhavaṁta bhiuḍīkarālabhālayalā । raṇarasiyasuhaḍavayaṇubbhavaṁtarā maṁcacayakavayā ||27||
jaṁpati tēvi rē dudhi nikiṭa ! ērisaṁ vayaṇaṁ । suhaḍā hama ! jē jaṁpasi taṁ muṇimō jāsi jamabhavaṇaṁ ||
anirikkhiūṇa jīhaṁ niyatrayaṇē kaha tumaṁ imaṁ bhaṇasi । jaṁ tumhē tumhapahū jujjhaṁtu maē samaṁ dōvi ॥ 29 ॥
kiṁ ēgēvi dariyāriviyaḍakarikara ḍadalaṇamiyariṇā । suhaḍēṇa samaṁ samaraṁ kāuṁ tuha asthi rē sattī ? ॥
jaṁ amhē apavidhivayaṇēhi niṣphalēhiṁ tumaṁ । akvivasi sarayariusamayamēhagalagajjiēhiva ? |
sō bhai ahaṁ ēgō tujhē savvēvi sāmisaṁjuttā । paharaha paḍhamaṁ pacchā raṇakaṁḍuṁ tumha avaṇissaṁ || 32॥
iya bhaṇiē nivaḍā bhallīnārāyakhaggacāvakarā । pabhaṇaṁti tumaṁ ēkōtti na haṇiō amhasuhaḍēhi ||
tā inhiṁpi palāyatu ahavā sumarēsu dēvayaṁ iṭuṁ । paṁcattaṁ pattōvi ya jēṇa tumaṁ lahasi suhaṭhāṇaṁ ||34||
tō bhai bhaḍō sōṁḍīranāḍayā saraha dasadisācakkaṁ । savvēvi ya maha raṇabhairavampi paḍiūṇa mā maraha ||
gōvi jahā sīhō kara ḍighaḍāḍōvavihaḍaṇaparyaṁḍō । havai ahaṁpi tahacciya tā savvē paharaha jahicchaṁ || 36॥
iya bhaṇiē suhaḍāvi hu samakālē jāva tassa paharaṁti । tāva akamhāvi ya tē jaha jāyā taha nisāmēha ||
saṁmūcchiyantra lihipanna ubalakiṇṇavva kaṭṭavaḍiyantra | paṁcataṁ pitra pattā dhasatti dharaṇīyalē paḍiyā ||
tō rāyā daṭṭū bhaḍapaḍalaṁ nivaḍiyē gharaṇipīḍhē । rōsāruṇanayaṇō karayalammi paḍaṇē karavālaṁ ||39||
sayamāyadviyakhaggō laggō uvasappaupi tayabhimuhaṁ । tā jāva saṁkhakumarōvi vikamaṁ bhaṇi umādattō ॥ 40 ॥
।
yadi punaryuṣmatprabhōrapi yuṣmākaṁ vāpyasti khaḍgabalam । tadā prabhuṇāpi yuṣmābhirapi samaṁ samaraṁ karōmyaham ||
iti bhaṇitē gururōpōdbhavadbhr̥kuṭikarālabhālatalāḥ । raṇarasikasubhaṭavacanōdbhavadrōmāñcacayakavacāḥ ||27||
jalpanti tē'pi rē duṣṭa ghr̥ṣṭa nikr̥ṣṭa ! īdr̥śaṁ vacanam । subhaṭādhama ! yajjalpasi tajjānīmō yāsi yamabhavanam ॥
anirīkṣya jihvāṁ nijavadanē kathaṁ tvamidaṁ bhaṇasi । yadyayaṁ yuṣmatprabhuryudhyētāṁ mayā samaṁ dvāvapi ||29||
kimēkēnāpi dr̥ptārivikaṭakarikaraṭadalana mr̥garipuṇā । subhaṭēna samaṁ samaraṁ kartuṁ tavāsti rē śaktiḥ ? ||30||
yadasmānasmatprabhumapi ghr̥ṣṭavacanairniṣphalaistvam । ākṣipasi śaradr̥tusamaya mē bagala garjitairiva : ॥31॥
sa bhaṇatyahamēkō yūyaṁ sarvē'pi svāmisaṁyuktāḥ । praharata prathamaṁ paścād raṇakaṇḍūṁ yuṣmākamapanēṣyē ||32||
iti bhaṇitē nr̥pasubhaṭā bhallīnārācakhaṅgacāpakarāḥ । pramaṇanti tvamēka iti na hatō'smatsubhaṭaiḥ ||33||
tasmādidānīmapi palāyasvāthavā smara dēvatāmiṣṭām । pañcatvaṁ prāptō'pi ca yēna tvaṁ labhasē śubhasthānam ॥
tatō bhaṇati bhaṭaḥ śauṇḍīryanāṭakāt sarata daśadikcakram । sarvē'pi ca mama raṇabhairavē patitvā mā mriyadhvam ॥
ēkō'pi yathā siṁhaḥ karaṭighaṭāṭōpavighaṭanapracaṇḍaḥ । bhavatyahamapi tathaiva tasmātsarvē praharata yathēccham ॥ 36 ॥
iti bhaṇitē subhaṭā api hi samakālaṁ yāvattaṁ praharanti । tāvadakasmādapi ca tē yathā jātāstathā niśamayata ॥
saṁmūrcchitā iva likhitā ivōpalakīrṇā iva kāṣṭhaghaṭitā iva । pañcatvamiva prāptā dhasēti dharaṇītalē patitāḥ ॥
tatō rājā dr̥ṣṭvā bhaṭapaṭalaṁ nipatitaṁ gharaṇipīṭhē । rōṣāruṇanayanaḥ karatalē praguṇayati karavālam ||39||
svayamākr̥ṣṭakhaḍgō lagna upasarpitumapi tadabhimukham । tāvadyāvacchaṁkhakumārō'pi vikramaṁ bhaṇitumārabdhaḥ ||40||

supāsanāha- cariammi-
kusu pasāyaṁ maha uvari dēva na hi ittha tumhaahigārō । kittiyamittaṁ ēsō mamāvi sajjhō tuha pasāyā ||
tāhi dēvō ēvaṁ dudvaṁ ahaṁ haṇissāmi । picchau pavarhataṁ majjha karayalaṁ kaliyakaravālē ||42||
iya pabhaṇatō rannā bhujjō bhujjō nisijjhamāṇōvi । āyaṭṭiyakhaggalaō saṁkhō jujhēumārō ||43||
jugavaṁ paritōlatā khaggaṁ samaraṁgaṇammi tō dōvi । rēhati tappalaluddha bhīmajamajīha kalin ||44 ||
tō bhaṇiō kumarēṇaṁ paḍhamaṁ paharēsu rē tumaṁ majjha । bhagai tumaṁ paharasu tō asiṇā muyai sē ghāyaṁ ॥ 45 ॥
।
tō sōcā vitō kuṁmarapahāraṁ vaēi puravāhi । tapiṭṭhīē kumarōvi dhāvaē jāva ujjāṇaṁ ||46 ||
picchai sūriprayāṇaṁ saraṇagayaṁ taṁ taō kumārōvi । kōsamma khivai khaggaṁ paṇamai sūrissa payakamalē ||
bhaṇai ya abhayaṁ tuha hōu bhadda ! itthaṁ pavannasaraṇassa | sugurupayapaṁkayāṇaṁ, mukkō gacchasu saicchāē ||48 ॥
tō nāṇēṇa nāuṁ guruṇā bhaṇiyaṁ kumāra ! tuha ēsō । dēvabhavē kila mittaṁ āsi imō paramanēharā ||49 ॥
iya sōuṁ suraruvaṁ payaḍai suhaḍō taō kumārōvi । paribhāvā mē mannē puvvabhavē divvōti ||20||
iya īhaṁ kuvrvatassa tassa saṁjāyajāisaraṇassa | saṁjāō paccakkhō savvōviya surabhavō vō ॥51॥
jaha ōsaṁkēō dēvabhavē maraṇakālasamayammi । jaha putri pīīē sōhammē vilasiṁga samagaṁ ॥ 52 ॥
tō uū dōnivi parōpparaṁ harisaparavasā dhaṇiyaṁ । sūrīṇa samavakhaṁ ciya āliṁgaṇayāī kuvvaiti ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ kumarēṇa taō suṭṭa kayaṁ jaṁ taē imaṁ vihiyaṁ । paḍivannapālaṇaṁ ciya mahavvayaṁ dhīrapurisāṇa ||
dēvēṇa taō bhaṇiyaṁ khamiyavyaṁ savvamavi mahābhāga ! | dhammammi pamāyaparaṁ taṁ nāumimaṁ maē vihiyaṁ ॥
।
kuru prasādaṁ mamōpari dēva ! na hyatra yuṣmadadhikāraḥ । kiyanmātramēṣa mamāpi sādhyastava prasādāt ॥41॥
tasmāttiṣṭhatviha dēva taṁ duṣṭamahaṁ haniṣyāmi । paśyatu pradhnad mama karatalaṁ kalitakaravālam ॥42॥
iti prabhaṇan rājñā bhūyō bhūyō niṣidhyamānō'pi | āṣṭakr̥khaṅgalataḥ śaṁkhō yōddhumārabdhaḥ ||43||
yugapatparitōlayantau khaṅgaṁ samarāṅgaṇē tatō dvāvapi । rājatastatpalalubdhabhīmayama jihvā kalitāviva ॥ 44 ॥
tatō bhaṇitaḥ kumārēṇa prathamaṁ prahara rē tvaṁ mām । sa bhaṇati tvaṁ prahara tatō'sinā muñcati tasya cātam ॥
tataḥ sa vañcayankumāraprahāraṁ vrajati purabahiḥ । tatpr̥ṣṭhē kumārō'pi dhāvati yāvadudyānam ॥ 46 ॥
paśyati sūripadānāṁ śaraṇagataṁ taṁ tataḥ kumārō'pi । kōśē kṣipati khaṅgaṁ praṇamati sūrēḥ padakamalam ॥47॥
bhaṇati cābhayaṁ tava bhavatu bhadra ! atra prapannaśaraṇasya | sugurupadapaṅkajānāṁ, muktō gaccha svēcchayā ||48||
tatō jñānēna jñātvā guruṇā bhaṇitaṁ kumāra ! tavaiṣaḥ । dēvabhavē kila mitramāsīdayaṁ paramasnēhaparaḥ || 49||
iti śrutvā surarūpaṁ prakaṭayati subhaṭastataḥ kumārō'pi । paribhāvayati mayā manyē pūrvabhavē dr̥ṣṭapūrva iti ॥50॥
।
itīhāṁ kurbatastasya saṁjātajātismaraṇasya । saṁjātaḥ pratyakṣaḥ sarvē'pi ca surabhavaḥ pūrvaḥ ॥51॥
yathā vihitaḥ saṁkētō dēvabhavē maraṇakālasamayē । yathā pūrvaṁ prītyā saudharmē vilasitaṁ samam ॥52॥
tata utthāya dvāvapi parasparaṁ harṣaparavaśau gāḍham । sūrīṇāṁ samakṣamēvāliṅganādi kurutaḥ ||13||
bhaṇitaṁ kumārēṇa tataḥ suṣṭhu kr̥taṁ yattvayēdaṁ vihitam । pratipannapālanamēva mahāvrataṁ dhīrapuruṣāṇām ॥ 54 ॥

lēkhakahā ।
573
harisaparasahiō tō saṁkhō bhaṁgara disasu taṁ majjha । kiñcamakiccaṁ baṁdhava ! tō dēvō bhai jaṁ guruṇō ॥
sāhati tujjha kicaṁ kicaṁ ciya taṁ taē payattēṇa । jalacaṁcalammi jīē na pāō bhadda ! kāyanvō ॥
tō afra haṇāṇagāradhammō savittharō tattha । nāhaṁ nāha ! samatthō iya kumarō bhaṇai jā tāva ||
sahati faraafrat kumarapautti sayaṁ gavēsaṁtō । cauraṁgiṇīsēnāē parigaō āgaō tattha ॥ 59 ॥
ha ha haṇatti bhaṇirō rōsabasāvēsaō caudisipi । viṁṭai taṁ ujjāṇaṁ hayagayarahasuhaḍakōḍīhiṁ ॥ 60 ॥
saṁnaddhavaddhakavaō kaivabhaḍaparigaō gaō majjhē । tō rāyā taṁ nāṇi kumarasurāīhiṁ pariyariyaṁ ॥ 61 ॥
picchittā bhaṇai suyaṁ vaccha ! kahiṁ sō bhaḍō durāyārō ? | jāva paryaṁpai kruddhō tā kumarō bhaṇai mā tāya ! ॥
akkhivasu imaṁ, duvvayaṇabhāsurō jaṁ bhaḍō ṭhiō amarō । paramuvayārī jaṁmaha iya bhaṇijaṁ kahai puvvabhavaṁ ॥
tō harisiō nariṁdō vaṁda sūriṁ suraṁ tu khāmēi | nisuṇai jiṇidadhammaṁ sammattāisamapi ॥ 64 ॥
saṁkhakumarēṇa saddhiṁ saddhāsuddhamāṇasō rāyā । bārasavihagihidhammaṁ paḍivajjaivajjabhayabhīō ॥ 65 ॥
dēvōni khamāvēḍaṁ rāyakumārē muṇipi vaṁdēḍaṁ । sahāṇaṁ saṁpattō rāyakumārāvi niyagēhaṁ ॥ 66 ॥
bhaṇiyavihiṇā kuṇatiya giridhammaṁ niccamēva ujjuttā । dēsāvagāsiē puṇa kumarō savisēsamujjamā ||
aha annā kumārō disivayama saṁkaḍaṁ nisīhammi । giṇhai maē na bāhiṁ gaṁtavvaṁ vāsabhavaṇāō || 68 ॥
jāva na diyaraviṁva diṭṭhē udayālammi ārūḍhaṁ | kaṁtāsijjaṁpi na saṁkhyēmi cauhāraparihārō || 69॥
dēvēna tatō bhaṇitaṁ kṣantavyaṁ sarvamapi mahābhāga ! | dharmē pramādaparaṁ tvāṁ jñātvēdaṁ mayā vihitam ॥15॥
harṣaparavaśahr̥dayastataḥ śaṅkhō bhaṇati diśa tvaṁ mama । kr̥tyamakr̥tyaṁ bāndhava ! tatō dēvō bhaṇati yad guravaḥ ||
kathayanti tava kr̥tyaṁ kr̥tyamēva tattvayā prayatnēna । jalacañcalē jīvitē na pramādō bhadra ! kartavyaḥ ॥57॥
tataḥ kathitaḥ kēvalināṁ'nagāradharmaḥ savistarastatra । nāhaṁ nātha ! samartha iti kumārō bhaṇati yāvattāvat ॥
sahasēti vikramanr̥paḥ kumārapravr̥tti svayaṁ gavēṣayan । caturaṅgasēnayā parigata āgatastatra ॥19॥
jahi jahi jahīti bhaṇitā rōṣavaśāvēśataścaturdikṣvapi । vēṣṭayati tadudyānaṁ hayagajarathasubhaṭakōṭibhiḥ ॥ 60॥
saṁnaddhabaddhakavacaḥ katipayabhaṭaparigatō gatō madhyē । tatō rājā taṁ jñāninaṁ kumārasurādibhiḥ parikaritam ॥ 61 ॥
dr̥ṣṭrā bhaṇati sutaṁ vatsa ! kva sa bhaṭō durācāraḥ । yāvatprajalpati kruddhastāvatkumārō bhaṇati mā tāta ! ॥ 62॥
ākṣipēmaṁ, durvacanamāsurō yadbhaṭaḥ sthitō'maraḥ । paramōpakārī yanmamēti bhaṇitvā kathayati pūrvabhavam ॥ 63 ॥
tatō harṣitō narēndrō vandatē sūriṁ suraṁ tu kṣamayati । śr̥ṇōti jinēndradharma samyaktvādisamagramapi ॥ 64 ॥
śaṅkhakumārēṇa sārdhaṁ śraddhā saṁśuddhamānasō rājā । dvādaśavivagr̥hidharma pratipadyatē'vadyabhayabhītaḥ ||65||
dēvō'pi kṣamayitvā rājakumārau munimapi vanditvā । svasthānaṁ saṁprāptō rājakumārāvapi nijagr̥ham ॥ 66॥
bhaṇitavidhinā kurutaśca gr̥hidharmaṁ nityamēvōdyuktau । dēśāvakāśikē punaḥ kumāraḥ saviśēṣamudyacchati ॥67॥
athānyadā kumārō digvratamatisaṁkaṭaṁ niśīthē । gr̥hṇāti mayā na bahirgantavyaṁ vāsabhavanāt ॥68॥
yāvatra dinakarabimbaṁ dr̥ṣṭamudayācala ārūḍham । kāntāśayyāmapi na saṁspr̥śāmi caturāhāraparihāraḥ ||19||

supāsanāha caritryammi-
aha kē dēvēṇaṁ suriṁdavaṇaṁ nisāmiyaṁ ēyaṁ । cālijjai na surēhiṁ saṁkhō dēsāvagāsāō || 70 ||
taṁ sōuṁ saṁpatō kumārabhavaṇassa dāradēsammi । avaharai tassa bhajjaṁ ruyamāṇi gasyāhāhiṁ ॥ 71 ॥
jaha niṇai sō kumarō sāmiyaṁ । maṁ rakkha rakkha nijjati । kēṇatri ahammiēṇaṁ taṁ suṇiuṁ citaē kuma ||
kassā kila bhajjā kassa va taṇaō sahōyarā kassa । iccāibhāvaṇāē apagamappēṇa bhāvē || 73 ॥
vratra frursat sōgiṭṭāṇa nivaṇahēū | dhammōciya saṁsārē saraṇaṁ tāṇaṁ ca jīvāṇa ॥ 74॥।
iya bhāvaṁtasa taō jāō kōlāhalō vahiṁ bahuō | haṇa-haṇa-haṇattigandhō bahubala kaliyāṇa sattana ॥
tēhiṁ viṣayāṇaṁ ca pariyaṇaṁ sōuṁ । bhāvēi bhāviyappā bhavabhayabhīō suṇi ॥76॥
ēvāmahaṁ nāhō ēē yaha sēkyatti jā buddhī । abhimāṇamittajaniyā kēvalamalamiha kilēsōya || 77 ||
ēsa maha sajakō ēē sattū kubuddhī maha ēsā । nahi yaṇō ya parō vā pasāhaō hōi sugaīē || 78 ||
ēkōciya jimyō sāhai suhariddhisiddhisukkhāī । tā tatthacciya jattō kāyavya kiṁ viyappēṇa ? ||
iya citiūṇa vilasamāhimāvisa saṁkhakumaravarō । tō dēvō tammākaṁ nāūṇaṁ hōī paccarakhō || 80 ॥
|
bhagara mahāya ! tē ci dhannō dhīrāṇa dhuri tumaṁ caiva । dēvēhivi jassa maṇō na caijjara niyapainnāō ||
sāṁgaṇāsaṇāhō surāṇa nāhōvi tujjha guṇagahaṇā । appāṇaṁ sakayatthaṁ mannai mannē tihuvi ॥ 82 ॥
।
taṁ ciya dhīrō saddhammatapparō taṁ ca bhuvaṇamaṇikaṁ । tā maggasu kiṁpi varaṁ tuṭṭhō haṁ tujjha cariēhi ||83 ||
paṇa saṁkhakumārō ki yaha kajjaṁ varēṇa anēṇa । tumhāṇa daṁsaṇaṁ ciya varaṁ barō sarau annaṇa ||84||
||
atha kēnacidēvēna surēndravacanaṁ niśamitamētat । cālyatē na suraiḥ śaṅkhō dēśāvakāśāt ॥ 70
tat śrutvā saṁprāptaḥ kumārabhavanasya dvāradēśē । apaharati tasya bhāryā rudatīṁ gurvākrandaiḥ ॥71॥
yathā śr̥ṇōti sa kumāraḥ svāminmāṁ rakṣa rakṣa nīyamānām । kēnāpyadhārmikēṇa tat śrutvā cintayati kumāraḥ ॥
kasyaiṣā kila bhāryā kasya vā tanayaḥ sahōdarāḥ kasya । ityādibhāvanayā''tmānamātmanā bhāvayati ॥ 73 ॥
ēkō'tra jinādiṣṭa iṣṭō'niṣṭānāṁ niṣṭhāpanahētuḥ । dharma ēva saṁsārē śaraṇaṁ trāṇaṁ ca jīvānām ॥ 74 ॥
iti bhāvayatastatō jātaḥ kōlāhalō bahirvahaḥ । jahi-jahi-jahītigarbhō bahubala kalitānāṁ śatrūṇām ॥75॥
tairapi lupyamānamākrandantaṁ ca parijanaṁ śrutvā । bhāvayati bhāvitātmā bhavabhayabhītō munirivēdam ॥ 76 ॥
ētēṣāmahaṁ nātha ētē mama sēvakā iti yā buddhiḥ । abhimānamātrajanitā kēvalamalamiha klēśaśca ॥77॥
ēṣa mama svajanavarga ētē śatravaḥ kubuddhirmamaiṣā । nahi svajanaśca parō vā prasādakō bhavati sugatēḥ ॥ 78 ॥
ēka ēva jinadharmaḥ sādhayati suraddhisiddhisaukhyāni । tasmāttatraiva yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ kiṁ vikalpēna ? ॥79॥
iti cintayitvā niścalasamādhimāviśati śaṁkhakumāravaraḥ । tatō dēvastadbhāvaṁ jñātvā bhavati pratyakṣaḥ ॥ 80 ॥
bhaṇati mahāyaśaḥ ! tvamēva dhanyō dhīrāṇāṁ dhuri tvamēva । dēvairapi yasya manō na tyājyatē nirjapratijñātaḥ ॥81॥
svargāṅganāsanāthaḥ surāṇāṁ nāthō'pi tavaṁ guṇagrahaṇāt । ātmānaṁ svakr̥tārtha manyatē manyē tribhuvanē'pi ॥82॥
tvamēva dhīraḥ saddharmatatparastvaṁ ca bhuvanamāṇikyam । tasmānmārgaya kamapi varaṁ tuṣṭō'haṁ tava caritaiḥ ॥ 83॥

saṁkhakahā ।
565
tō sō tōsēṇa surō sarōyadaladahalōyaṇa kumaraṁ । bhaṇai mahāyasa ! tahavi hu dēvāṇaṁ daṁsaṇamōhaṁ ॥ 85 ॥
hōi, taō tuha ēsō hōu barō jō tara sakaruṇāē । diṭṭhō diṭṭhīē khaṇaṁ sō khala rōgēhi succēhī ॥ 86॥
iya bhaṇi sahāṇaṁ jāi surō diṇayarassa udayati । paḍipunnaniyamaavahī vihīē sijjaṁ taō mō ||
kumarō araateefariō kiriyākalāvakaliyāṇa । sāhūṇa jāi pāsē vaṁdai tē paramaviṇaṇa ॥ 88 ॥
nisuṇēi samayasāraṁ tamaṇiyaṁṇuhuē jahāsatti । aha anayā nariṁdō tajjaṇaō pīḍiō sahasā ॥ 89॥
amūlavēpaṇā pacakhāō ya savvavijjēhiṁ । hakārāvai kumaraṁ bhaṇai jahā vaccha ! maha ihi ॥ 90 ॥
baṭṭai samaō maraṇassa tā tumaṁ saṁpayaṁ payānāhō । iha bhaṇiē tō kumarō sarēi suradina āṇapiō ॥ 91 ॥
karuṇābharaṁciyāē niyadihīē palōyaē dēhaṁ । jaṇayassa tāva sahasā himava ravikiraṇatāvahayē ||12||
naṭaṁ mūlaṁ dēhē nissaṁdēhaṁ taō bhai rāyā । jāō nirāmaō ha diṭṭō diṭṭhīē tuha baccha ! ॥93॥
ēmēva maō hutō sāmunnavivajjiō iyāṇi tu । tuhamā hijjavasēṇaṁ saṁpai sāhēmi niyakajjaṁ ॥94॥
muṁca mamaṁ jēṇāhaṁ karēmi sugurūṇa pāyamūlammi । saṁjamamupāracittō hōūṇa gharēsu rajjabharaṁ ||15||
jā kila kumarō kiṁcitri kāhī paccuttaraṁ taō rāyā । ghariḍaṁ taṁ bāhāē ṭhaviḍaṁ sīhāsaṇē paṇaō ॥ 96 ॥
sāmaṁtāī lōō bhaṇiō jaha namaha saṁkharāyassa । payapaṁkayamihi jaṁ sāmī tumhāṇa. ēsa niyō ||97||
iya tēhivi taha vihiē sīhōvba kariṁdagurūghaḍāṇuvariṁ । nikkhamai higuhāō vikamarāyā mahiddīē ||
|
1
prabhaṇati śaṁkhakumāraḥ kiṁ mama kāryaṁ varēṇānyēna । yuṣmākaṁ darśanamēva varaṁ varaḥ saratvanyēna ॥84॥
tataḥ sa tōṣēṇa suraḥ sarōjadaladīrghalōcanaṁ kumāram । bhaṇati mahāyaśaḥ ! tathāpi hi dēvānāṁ darśanamamōtram ॥
bhavati, tatastavaiṣa bhavatu varō yastvayā sakaruṇayā । dr̥ṣṭō dr̥ṣṭyā kṣaṇa sa khalu rōgaimakṣyatē ॥86॥
iti bhaṇitvā svasthānaṁ yāti surō dinakarasyōdayē । paripūrṇaniyamāvadhirvidhinā śayyāṁ tatō muktvā ॥ 87॥
kumāraḥ kr̥tāvaśyakakriyaḥ kriyākalāpakalitānām । sādhūnāṁ yāti pārśvē vandatē tān paramavinayēna ॥88॥
śr̥ṇōti samayasāraṁ tadbhaṇitamanutiṣṭhati yathāśakti । athānyadā narēndrastajanakaḥ pīḍitaḥ sahasā ||89 ॥
atiśūlavēdanayā pratyākhyātaśca sarvavaidyaiḥ । hakkārayati kumāraṁ bhaṇati yathā vatsa ! mamēdānīm ॥ 90 ॥
vartatē samaya maraṇasya tasmāttvaṁ sāṁprataṁ prajānāthaḥ । iti bhaṇitē tataḥ kumāraḥ smarati suradattājñāmitaḥ ॥ 91 ॥
karuṇābharāñcitayā nijadr̥ṣṭyā pralōkatē dēham | janakasya tāvatsahasā himamiva ravikiraṇatāpahatam ॥92॥
naṣṭaṁ śūlaṁ dēhē nissaṁdēhaṁ tatō bhaṇati rājā | jātō nirāmayō'haṁ dr̥ṣṭō dr̥ṣṭyā tava vatsa ! ॥93॥
ēvamēva mr̥tō'bhaviṣyaṁ śrāmaṇyavivarjita idānīṁ tu । tvatsāhāyyavaśēna saṁprati sādhayāmi nijakāryam ॥ 94 ॥
muñca māṁ yēnāhaṁ karōmi sugurūṇāṁ pādamūlē । saṁyamamudāracittō bhūtvā ghara rājyabharam ॥ 95||
yāvatkila kumāraḥ kiñcidapi kariṣyati pratyuttaraṁ tatō rājā । dhr̥tvā taṁ bāhau sthāpayitvā siṁhāsanē praṇataḥ ॥
sāmantādilōṁ kō bhaṇitō yathā namata śaṅkharājāya । padapaṅkajamidānīṁ yatsvāmī yuṣmākamēṣa nr̥paḥ ॥ 97 ॥
iti tairapi tathā vihitē siṁha iva karīndragurughaṭānāmupari । niṣkrāmati gr̥hagr̥hāta vikramarājō mahada ॥98॥

kōsaṁvavajjāṇē pattō sirivijayasūripayapāsē । giṇhai vihiṇā dikkha sikkhapi duhāvi sō dhīrō ||
sirisaṁkhanāradōvi hu aṭṭhā hiyamāiyē jaṇayakiccaṁ । kāūṇa vihāṇēṇa sāvayadhammammi daḍhacittō ॥ 100 ॥
pālai payāvakaliō payāu supayattaō taō kamhā | annammi diṇē nisuṇai sīhaduvārammi gururōlaṁ ॥
vivihaguruvāhivihuriyadēhāṇa jaṇāṇa dīṇakaruṇayaraṁ । sōuṁ rāyā pucchara paḍihāraṁ kēsimō sadō ? || 102॥
sō bhai dēva ! dārē duraṁtaduriōhapīḍiyaṁgāṇaṁ | jariyāṇaṁ kuṭṭhīṇaṁ khaīṇa khāsīṇa siṁbhīṇa ॥103॥ .
ēmāirōgiyāṇaṁ nāṇādēsāgayāṇa ēsa sarō। sīhaduvāraṭhiyāṇaṁ tuha kitti nisuṇiḍaṁ ēvaṁ ॥ 104 ॥
jaṁ jaṁ piccha dēvō karuṇābhara maṁtharāē diṭṭhīē । taṁ taṁ rōgaviuttaṁ karēi gururōgajutaṁpi ॥ 105 ॥
tō bhaṇiō paḍihārō rannā savvaṁpi rōgisaṁghāyaṁ । āṇāvasu jaha sigghaṁ āgacchai vaggaṭhavaṇāē ।
paḍhamaṁ kuṭṭhiyavaggō jarīṇa vaggō kamēṇa savvēvi । kāūṇa vaggavaragaṁ samāgayā rāyapāsamma || 107 ||
paḍhamavaggō nivēṇa bhaṇiō mahumajjamaṁsamāīṇa । kāyavvā bhō viraī jāvajjīvapi sammataṁ ॥ 108 ॥
kēsipi hu paḍhamatrayaṁ vīyavayāīvi kē simuddisium̐ । avalōiyā ya savvē karuṇārasasarasadiṭṭhīē ॥ 109 ॥
tō takkhaṇēṇa mukkā savvē savvēhi uggarōgēhiṁ । caiuṁ nikāiyakammē, viyaṇā tāṇavi kayā appā ||
ēvaṁ paraṁ pasiddhiṁ pattō thēvēhiṁ caiva diyahēhiṁ । paṭṭamahādēvīē jāyaṁ puttaṁ utriya rajjē ॥ 111 ॥
jiṇasāsaṇaṣpabhāvaṇapucvaṁ giṇi savvaō viraī । saṁpattakēvalō sō kamēṇa pattō siksamiddhiṁ ॥ 112 ॥
kōśāmbavanōdyānē prāptaḥ śrīvijayasūripadapārśvē । gr̥hṇāti vidhinā dīkṣāṁ śikṣāmapi dvivāpi sa vīraḥ ॥ 99 ॥
śrīśaṅkhanarēndrō'pi hyaṣṭāhikādikaṁ janakakr̥tyam । kr̥tvā vidhānēna śrāvakadharmē dr̥ḍhacittaḥ ॥100॥
pālayati pratāpakalitaḥ prajāḥ suprayatnatastatō'kasmāt । anyasmindinē guṇōti siṁhadvārē gurukalakalam ॥
vividhaguruvyādhividhuritadēhānāṁ janānāṁ dīnakaruṇataram । śrutvā rājā pr̥cchati pratīhāraṁ kēṣāmayaṁ śabdaḥ ? |
sa bhaṇati dēva ! dvārē durantaduritautrapīḍitāṅgānām । jvaritānāṁ kuṣṭhināṁ kṣāyaṇāṁ kāsināṁ ślēṣmiṇām ॥
ēvamādirōgiṇāṁ nānādēśāgatānāmēṣa svaraḥ । siṁhadvārasthitānāṁ tava kīrtti śrutvaivam ॥ 104 ॥
yaṁ yaṁ paśyati dēvaḥ karuṇābharamantharayā dr̥ṣṭyā । taṁ taṁ rōgaviyuktaṁ karōti gururōgayuktamapi ॥ 109 ॥
tatō bhaṇitaḥ pratihārō rājñā sarvamapi rōgasaṁghātam । ānāyaya yathā śīghramāgacchati vargasthāpanayā ॥ 106 ॥
prathamaṁ kuṣṭhivargōṁ jvariṇāṁ vargaḥ, kramēṇa sarvē'pi । kr̥tvā vargavarga samāgatā rājapārśvē ॥ 107॥
prathamavargō nr̥pēṇa bhaṇitō madhumadyamāṁsādīnām । karttavyā bhō viratiryāvajjīvamapi samyaktvam ॥ 108॥
kēṣāmapi khalu prathamavrataṁ dvitīyavatādīnyapi kēṣāmuddiśya । avalōkitāśca sarvē karuṇārasasarasadr̥ṣṭayā ॥ 109॥
tatastatkṣaṇēna muktāḥ sarvē sarvairugrarōgaiḥ । tyakvā nikācitakarmaṇō, vēdanā tēṣāmapi kr̥tālpā ॥ 110 ॥
ēvaṁ parāṁ prasiddhiṁ prāptaḥ stōkairēva divasaiḥ । paṭṭamahādēvyāṁ jātaṁ putraṁ sthāpayitvā rājyē ॥ 111 ॥
jinaśāsanaprabhāvanāpūrva gr̥hṇāti sarvatō viratim । saṁprāpta kēvalaḥ sa kramēṇa prāptaḥ śivasamr̥ddhim ॥192॥

gāmagihāigāṇaṁ vatthūṇaṁ jō karēi āṇavaṇaṁ । gahiyāvahīē paraō viṁjhō iva sō duhaṁ lahai ||1||

pariṇayaṇē jaṁ vaiyaṁ kappaḍataṁvōlabhōyaṇāīsu । dāyavvamimassa maē iya buddhīē nirucchāhō ||13||
viṁjhōttiviyināmō viyarai savvattha kāṇaṇāīsu । aha annayā ya tēṇaṁ diṭṭhō sūrī surammavaṇē ॥ 14 ॥
taṁ vaṁdiya uvaviṭṭō pucchara sūriṁ sudhammaparamatthaṁ । bhayavaṁpi kahai dhammaṁ jaigihibhēēṇa tēṇāvi || 15 ||
grāmagr̥hādigatānāṁ vastūnāṁ yaḥ karōtyānāyanam । gr̥hītāvadhēḥ paratō vindhya iva sa duḥkhaṁ labhatē ॥ 1 ॥
sugajagataṁ (sugatagarda) vibudhamata (ya) mamr̥tamiva samastyamr̥ta kuṇḍapuram । tatrāsīdvidhuśrēṣṭhī bhāryā ratisundarī tasya ॥

madhyamavayasi tatō jātaḥ putra upayācitaśataiḥ । rajanyāmardharātrē yāvatsuptastiṣṭhati śrēṣṭhī ॥ 4 ॥
atha tasya gr̥hē prāptaṁ vyantarayugalaṁ parasparōllapitr̥ । ēkō bhaṇati jānāsi śrēṣṭhagr̥hē yaḥ sutō jātaḥ ॥ 5॥
dvitīyō bhaṇati samyag jānāmina, kathaya kaḥ sphuṭamēṣaḥ ? । tataḥ sa kathayatyēṣa pūrvabhava āsīcchrēṣṭhinaḥ ॥ 6 ॥
vyavahāraka ētasya ca r̥ṇagrahaṇē dharatyēkalakṣam । putracchalēnaiṣa ētasya gr̥hē samanujātaḥ ॥7॥

gahiō sāvayadhamma sammattāī duvālasavihōvi । pālatō saṁttīē gamēi diyahāī sō tattha ॥ 16 ॥
aha annayā sa jāō rōgagvatthō taō ya sayaṇēhiṁ । bhaṇiō siṭṭī āṇasu bijjaṁ paḍijāgaraṭṭhāē ||
siṭṭī bhai nahu kiṁpi majjha taṇayassa hōhihīṇihaṁ । kaivayadiṇāṇa uvariṁ gihista pacchamaviyappaṁ ॥
tō taṁ tava nāyaṁ jāyā kittīvi tassa savvattō । jaha savvaṁpi viyāṇai sēṭṭī nēmittamittō ya || 19 ॥
nivasta aggamahisī aparurīrā aīva saṁjāyā । tō kahiyē kēṇāvi hu jahavi jāṇaē satraṁ ॥
tō rannā āhūō sō pattō pāhuḍāī ghēttūṇa । namiūṇa bhaṇai siṭṭī āēsaṁ disasu maha nāha ! || 21 ||
tō rannā sō bhaṇiō gaṁtūṇatēura mmi maha dēviṁ । paḍijāgarasu vihīē ōsahadāṇāiṇā jhatti ||22||
tō siṭṭī bhai nivaṁ nāhaṁ vijjō na saṁtataṁtannū । dēvō puṇa āēsaṁ dēi imaṁ kaha ṇu, tō rāyā ॥ 23 ॥
bhai tara niyataṇaō ōsaha bhēsajjamaṁtataṁtēhiṁ । jīvāviō rasaṁtō naya vijjō kōī āhūō || 24॥
iccā kahatē naravarammi siṭṭhī bhara hasiūṇa । kīrau majjha pasāō rahēṇa tō takkhaṇā caiva ||25||
rannā bhūsannāē lōē ōsāriyammi sō kahara | jahavittaṁ vr̥ttaṁtaṁ tō rannā pucchiō ēvaṁ ||26||
kittiyamittaṁ davvaṁ dāyavvaṁ tassa ajjavi kahēsu | pannāsasahassāī ajjavi thakkaṁti dāu sē ||27|
iccā kaha kahi siṭṭī baccē rāyaāṇāē । niyagēhē puttōvi hu vihiṇā pālēi gimmiṁ ॥ 28 ॥
navaraṁ sō ahiyayaraṁ nicaṁ dēsāvagāsiē ramai । aha annayā sa bāhi ujjāṇē jāva gacchēi ||29||
taṁ vanditvōpaviṣṭaḥ pr̥cchati sūriṁ sudharmaparamārtham । bhagavānapi kathayati dharma yatigr̥hibhēdēna tēnāpi ॥ 15 ॥
gr̥hītaḥ śrāvakadharmaḥ samyaktvādirdvādaśavidhō'pi । pālayan śaktyā gamayati divasāni sa tatra ॥ 16 ॥
athānyadā sa jātō rōgagrastastataśca svajanaiḥ । bhaṇitaḥ śrēṣṭhī ānaya vaidya pratijāgarārtham ॥17॥
śrēṣṭhī bhaṇati na hi kimapi mama tanayasya bhaviṣyatyaniṣṭam । katipayadinānāmupari grahīṣyati pathyamavikalpam ||
tatastattathaiva jātaṁ jātā kīrttirapi tasya sarvataḥ । yathā sarvamapi vijānāti śrēṣṭhī nimittamitaśca ॥ 19 ॥
nr̥patēragramahiṣyapaṭuśarīrā'tīva saṁjātā । tataḥ kathitaṁ kēnāpi hi yathā vidhurjānāti sarvam ॥ 20 ॥
tatō rājñā''hūtaḥ sa prāptaḥ prābhr̥tāni gr̥hītvā । natvā bhaṇati śrēṣṭhī ādēśaṁ diśa mama nātha ! ||21||
tatō rājñā sa bhaṇitō gatvāntaḥpurē mama dēvīm । pratijāgaraya vidhinauṣadhadānādinā jhaṭiti ॥22॥
tataḥ śrēṣṭhī bhaṇati nr̥paṁ nāhaṁ vaidyō na mantratantrajñaḥ । dēvaḥ punarādēśaṁ dadātīmaṁ kathaṁ nu tatō rājā ॥23॥
bhaṇati tvayā nijatanaya auṣadhabhaiṣajyamantratantraiḥ । jīvitō rasan na ca vaidyaḥ kaścidāhr̥taḥ ||24||
ityādi kathayati naravarē śrēṣṭhī bhaṇati hasilā । kriyatāṁ mama prasādō rahasā tatastatkṣaṇādēva || 25 ॥
rājñā saṁjñayā lōkē'pasāritē sa kathayati । yathāvr̥ttaṁ vr̥ttāntaṁ tatō rājñā pr̥ṣṭa ēvam ॥ 26 ॥
kiyanmātraṁ dravyaṁ dātavyaṁ tasmā adyāpi kathaya । pañcāśatsahasaṇyacāpi tiṣṭhanti dātuṁ tasmai ॥ 27 ॥
ityādikathāṁ kathayitvā śrēṣṭhī vrajati rājājñayā । nijagēhē putrō'pi hi vivinā pālayati gr̥hidharmam ||28||
navaraṁ sō'dhikataraṁ nityaṁ dēśāvakāśikē ramatē । athānyadā sa bahirudyānē yāvad gacchati ॥ 29 ॥

supāsamāha-caritryasmi -
tō piccha rāyavāriyē naraṁ pavarasaṁḍhiprārūḍhaṁ । nāmēṇa caṁḍasīhaṁ cirapariciyamuciyavihiputraṁ ||30||
saṁbhāsiūṇa puccha gacchasi taṁ kattha, sō bhai mitta ! | rāyāēsēṇa ahaṁ gacchissaṁ daviḍanivapāsē ||
viggahanimittamaha saṁdhikāraṇā, tō bhagai siṭṭhisuō । tatthēgō nitramaṁtī anugōtti taē sa bhaṇiyavvō ।
maha vayaṇēṇaṁ ēvaṁ jaha sigdhaṁ paṭṭavēsu maha davvaṁ । taha paḍivayaṇaṁ pēsatu maha bhaṇiyassēha siggharaṁ ||33||
ēvaṁ ca maē kajjaṁ sijjhēi sayaṁ gaēṇa tappāsē । kiṁtu maha asthi niyamō jōyaṇapaṇagassa uvarimi ||
tavaṁ nēya maē chammāsā jāba, uvari mōkkalayaṁ । jōyaṇasayaṁ divaḍhaṁ cauddisi tā tumēva tahi ||35||
nivakaṇaṁ gacchasi miliō ēmēva kahavi taṁ ittha । sijjhissai iya kajjaṁ sāhinnāṇaṁpi tassa taē ||
ēvaṁ ēvaṁ rahē kahiyavaṁ tō tayaṁpi kēṇāvi | sāhijjataṁ nisurya tēṇavi kahiyaṁ naridassa ||37||
1
rannā āṇatō sacivō jaha visihiṇō puttaṁ । āṇāvasu baṁdhēuṁ jaṁ duṭṭhō sō mahāpāvō ||38||
mahavēriyasacivēṇaṁ saṁsaggiṁ kuṇai taha ya vavahāraṁ । tā suṁdarō na ēsō niggahiyavtrō maē tamhā || 39॥
tō saciva ārakkhiyamāṇavara rahampri tassa gahaṇatthaṁ । tēṇavi sō āṇīō baṁdhēuṁ rāyapāsamma ||40||
taṁ sōuṁ tō siṭṭīvi pattō nivassa pāsamma । sayaṇajaṇapēriēṇaṁ vinnattō tēṇa naranāhō ||41 ॥
kiṁ dēva ! imēṇa kathaṁ vijhēṇaṁ jēṇa cōrabaṁdhēhiṁ । baṁdhēḍaṁ āṇīō, tō rāyā bhaṇai tayabhinu ||42 ||
niggahiyavvō ēsō sārīriyaniggahēṇa tuha taṇaō । jō kuṇai pasaṁgaṁ maha rikahiṁ, bhaṇai tō siṭṭī ||43||
hōhī majjhanavāō sayaṇajaṇāō taō pasīūṇa । kuṇa daṁḍamikkavāraṁ giṇhēsu davvaṁ jamabhiruiyaṁ ॥ 44 ॥
1
tataḥ paśyati rājadauvārikaṁ naraṁ pravarōṣṭrīmārūḍham । nāmnā caṇḍasiṁhaṁ ciraparicitamucitavidhipūrvam ॥ 30 ॥
saṁbhāṣya pr̥cchati gacchasi tvaṁ kutra, sa bhaṇati mittra ! | rājādēśēnāhaṁ gamiṣyāmi draviḍanr̥papārśvē ॥ 31 ॥
vigrahanimittamatha saṁdhikāraṇāt, tatō bhaṇati śrēṣṭhitaḥ । tatraikō nr̥pamantrī amuka iti tvayā sa bhaṇitatryaḥ॥
mama vacanēnaivaṁ yathā śīghraṁ prasthāpaya mama dravyam । tathā prativacanaṁ prēṣaya mama bhaṇitasyēha śīghrataram ||33||
ētacca mayā kārya sidhyati svayaṁ gatēna tatpārthē । kintu mamāsti niyamō yōjanapañcakasyōpari || 34 ॥
gantavyaṁ naiva mayā ṣaṇmāsān yāvat upari mutkalam | yōjanaśataṁ dvitīyārdhaṁ caturdikṣu tasmāttvamēva tatra ॥ 35॥
nr̥pakāryēṇa gacchasi milita ēvamēva kathamapi tvamatra । sētsyatīti kārya sābhijñānamapi tasya tvayā ||36||
ēvamēvamiti rahasi kathayitavyaṁ tatastadapi kēnāpi । kathyamānaṁ śrutaṁ tēnāpi kathitaṁ narēndrāya ||37||
tatō rājñā''jñaptaḥ sacikō yathā vidhuśrēṣṭhinaḥ putram । ānāyaya baddhvā yad duṣṭaḥ sa mahāpāpaḥ || 38 ||
madvairisacivēna saṁsargaṁ karōti tathā ca vyavahāram । tasmānna sundara ēṣa nigrahītavyō mayā tasmāt ||39||
tataḥ sacitra ārakṣikamājñāpayati rahasi tasya grahaṇārtham । tēnāpi sa ānītō baddhvā rājapārśvē ||40||
tat śrutvā tataḥ śrēṣṭhī vidhu: prāptō nr̥pasya pārśvē । svajana janaprēritēna vijñaptastēna naranāthaḥ ॥ 41 ॥
kiṁ dēva ! anēna kr̥taṁ vindhyēna yēna caurabandhaiḥ । baddhvā''nītaḥ, tatō rājā bhaṇati tadabhimukham ||42||
nigrahītavya ēṣa śārīrikanigrahēṇa tava tanayaḥ । yaḥ karōti prasaṅgaṁ mama ripubhiḥ, bhaṇati tataḥ śrēṣṭhī ॥ 43 ॥

saṁkhakahā ।
581
tō mahayā kaṭṭaṇaṁ pannāsasahassadaṁḍaparimāṇaṁ । kāūṇaṁ sō mukō siṭṭivarōhēṇa garuṇa || 45 ||
nīō gimmi baṁdhēhiṁ pīḍiō āgaō ya dāhajarō tō siṭṭī paribhāvaṛa nūṇaṁ marihī imō jēṇa ||46 ॥
gahiō imēṇa lakkhō lakkhaṁ paribhāviūṇa tō bhaṇiō | dhammammi ujjamijjasu muṁca gihāīsu paḍivadhaṁ ॥
tō sō bhai siddhi bīē sikkhāvayammi aiyārō | āṇavaṇēṇaṁ vatthussa nimmiō lōhatthē ||48 ||
tassa phalaṁ aṇuhūyaṁ ihalōēvi hu maē ahantrēṇa । paralōē puṇa ajjavi aṇuhavaṇīmaṁ visēsēṇa ॥ 49 ॥
ahariyaciṁtāmaṇiṇō guṇaguruṇō kēvi tāya ! varaguruṇō । āhavasu maha samīvē jēṇa visōhēmi appāṇaṁ ॥
tō siṭṭhī sayamēva ya tāṇa samīvē vaēi tā jāva । paralōyaṁ saṁpattō sō puttō tēṇa bhāvēṇa ॥ 51 ॥
uvana sōhammē taō cuō sijjhihī ya taiyabhavē । tā bhō ! kalaṁkiyavvō lēsēṇavi nēya niyaniyamō ॥
॥ iti dvitīya śikṣāvrataprathamāticārē vindhyakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
bhaviṣyati mamāpavādaḥ svajanajanāt tataḥ prasadya । kuru daṇḍamēkavāraṁ gr̥hāṇa dravyaṁ yadabhirucitam ॥ 44 ॥
tatō mahatā kaṣṭēna pañcāśatsahasūdaṇḍaparimāṇam । kr̥tvā sa muktaḥ śrēṣṭhayuparōdhēna guruṇā ॥45॥
nītō gr̥hē bandhaiḥ pīḍita āgataśca dāhajvaraḥ । tataḥ śrēṣṭhī paribhāvayati nūnaṁ mariṣyatyayaṁ yēna ॥ 46 ॥
gr̥hītō'nēnaṁ lakṣō lakṣaṁ paribhāvya tatō bhaṇitaḥ । dharma udyaccha muñca gr̥hādiṣu pratibandham ॥47॥
tataḥ sa bhaṇati śrēṣṭhinaṁ dvitīyē śikṣāvratē'ticāraḥ । ānāyanēna vastunō nirmitō lōbhagrastēna ॥ 48 ॥
tasya phalamanubhūtamihalōkē'pi hi mayā'vanyēna । paralōkē punaradyāpyanubhavanīyaṁ viśēṣēṇa ॥ 49 ॥
adharitacintāmaṇīnguṇagurūnkānapi tāta ! varagurūn । āhvayasva mama samīpē yēna viśōdhayāmyātmānam |
tataḥ śrēṣṭhī svayamēva ca tēṣāṁ samīpē vrajati tāvadyāvat । paralōkaṁ saṁprāptaḥ sa putrastēna bhāvēna ॥ 51 ॥
upapannaḥ saudharmē tataścyutaḥ sētsyati ca tr̥tīyabhavē । tasmād bhōḥ ! kalaṅkayitavyō lēśēnāpi naiva nijaniyamaḥ ॥

kuṇa pāhēyaṁ paṇa tīē vihiyaṁ tahēva taṁ jhatti । gharavāvāravisēsē nirūviḍaṁ taṁ ca sumuhuttē ||12||
sō saṁbalāī gahiuṁ caliō bhuttūṇa paharadugasamaē । puraparisarammi pattō ciṁcāvaṇamajjhabhāgampi ||13||
niyamita digavakāśaḥ svayaṁ na gacchati prēṣayatyanyam । sa śrāddhō'vidagdhaḥ saḍḍha iva sa duḥkhaṁ cinōti ॥ 1 ॥

ityādi śrutvā vinayaṁ pratipadyatē sagr̥hidharmam । sūrīṇāṁ pādamūlē paścād gacchati nijagēhē ॥7॥
athānyadā ca śrēṣṭhī sthiradēvō dēvabhūmimanuprāptaḥ । saḍḍhō gr̥hasya svāmī saṁjātō'nyadā sa tu ॥ 8 ॥
vibhavabhraṁśōtkarṣita durjanalōkātparibhavaṁ sahatē । paribhāvayati manōmadhyē satyamēva kēnacitpaṭhitam ॥9॥
mānin ! pranaṣṭā yadi na tanūstatō dēśaṁ tyaja । mā durjanakarāṅgulibhirdaśyamānō bhrama ॥ 10॥
iti cintayitvā tēna bhaṇitā mahilā'haṁ gamiṣyāmi । arthōpārjana hētōḥ kasminnapi dēśāntarē tarasā ॥11॥
kuru pāthēyaṁ praguṇaṁ tayā vihitaṁ tathaiva tajjhaṭiti । gr̥havyāpāraviśēṣān nirūpyatāṁ ca sumuhūrttē ॥12॥
sambalāni gr̥hītvā calitō bhuktvā praharadvikasamayē । puraparisarē prāptaściñcāvanamadhyabhāgē ॥ 13 ॥

saḍhakahā ।
583
tō parisatō suttō saṁvalayaṁ saṁṭhavēvi ūsīsē । jā cihna citatō katthāhaṁ jāmi gayapunnō ? || 14 ||
navi atitha kōvi baṁdhū naya suyaṇō nēya mittaggō ya । sunnā savvāu disā viśvaviuttāṇa jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ॥
viṇu vihavihiṁ dāridiaha sunnau sabbu disicakku । dharaṇīyali suhisaṁkulivi bhaṇai na kutri piu takku ॥
iya citatas tarhi viyaṁbhiyaṁ jiṁbhiyāhiṁ muhakuharē । tammi paviddhaṁ sahasā tassa taō ciṁciṇīē phalaṁ ॥
tō sō tōsabasēṇaṁ sauṇōtti muṇēvi citaē tuṭṭō | kaha muhapasāraṇaṁ maha kaha ciṁcāē phalapavēsō ? |
tā nūṇaṁ maha hōhī kō avō akaṁḍaō cēva । gurulābhō jā ēvaṁ citai tā uttara disāō || 19||
āgacchataṁ picchara siyavasaṇadharaṁ palaṁbakaraṁ । kayakaṇayapāyāpāya paṁkayaṁ paṁkayadalacchaṁ ||20||
taṁda sō citai nūṇaṁ viṇayārihō imō purisō । 'viṇaō āhavai siri' iya muṇivayaṇaṁ sarēūṇa ||
an tō sahasā masaṇēhaṁ sāgayaṁti bhaṇamāṇō । ciravillahasvabhimuhaṁ sō jāi vēgēṇa ||22||
gaṁtuṁ taccaraṇē sō namiūṇa pamajjaē ya paḍaṇa । tappāṇipaṁkayaṁ niyakarampi kāuṁ samāṇēi ||23||
cicāvalacchāē sattharē tō nivēsiuṁ tassa । sōēi caraṇakamalaṁ naēṇa vissāmaṇaṁ kuṇai ||24||
tē purisēṇa puṭṭō kattha tumaṁ kō si kattha saṁcaliō ? । kēṇa va paōyaṇēṇaṁ sō sāhai tassa tō ēvaṁ ॥
ihanayara siṭṭhitaṇaō sāvayakulasaṁbhavō vihavahīṇō । jāō jaṇayammi maē siṭṭhipayāōvi tō bhaṭṭhō ॥ 26 ॥
sayaṇēhiṁ paribhūō atthōvajjaṇakaraṇa caliō haiṁ । puraparisarasaraṇaparissamēvi āvāhium̐ bāḍhaṁ ||27||
vissaṁtō ittha taō taṁ pattō diṭṭigōyarē majjha । sō bhai maē diṭṭhē dālidajalaṁjali dē ||28||
1
tataḥ pariśrāntaḥ suptaḥ śambalaṁ saṁsthāpyōcchīrṣē । yāvattiṣṭhati cintayan kvāhaṁ yāmi gatapuṇyaḥ 1 ॥ 14 ॥
naivāsti kō'pi bandhurna ca svajanō naiva mittravargaśca । śūnyāḥ sarvā diśō vibhavaviyuktānāṁ yad bhaṇitam ॥
vinā vibhavaidaridrasya śūnyaṁ sarva dikcakram । dharaṇītalē suhr̥tsaṁkulē'pi bhaṇati na kō'pi pica takram ॥ 16॥
iti cintayatastatra vijr̥mbhitaṁ jr̥mbhābhirmukhakuharē । tasminpraviṣṭaṁ sahasā tasya tataściñcinyāḥ phalam ॥17॥
tataḥ sa tōṣavaśēna śakuna iti jñātvā cintayati tuṣṭaḥ । kathaṁ mukhaprasāraṇaṁ mama kathaṁ ciñcāphalapravēśaḥ ॥ 18॥
tasmānnūnaṁ mama bhaviṣyati kō'pyapūrvō'kāṇḍata ēva । gurulābhō yāvadēvaṁ cintayati tāvaduttara diśaḥ ॥ 19 ॥
āgacchantaṁ paśyati sitavasanadharaṁ pralambakaram । kr̥takanakapādukāpādapaṅkajaṁ paṅkajadalākṣam ॥20॥
taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā sa cintayati nūnaṁ vinayārhō'yaṁ puruṣaḥ । ' vinaya āhūyatē śriyam iti munivacanaṁ smr̥tvā ॥21॥
abhyuttiṣṭhati tataḥ sahasā sasnēhaṁ svāgatamiti bhaṇan । ciradr̥ṣṭavallabhasyēvābhimukhaṁ sē yāti vēgēna ॥22॥
gatvā taccaraṇān sa natvā pramārṣṭi ca paṭēna । tatpāṇipaṅkajaṁ nijakarē kr̥tvā samānayati ॥ 23॥
ciñcābahalacchāyē srastarē tatō nivēśya tasya । śōcayati caraṇakamalaṁ nayēna viśrāmaṇāṁ karōti ॥ 24 ॥
tēna puruṣēṇa pr̥ṣṭaḥ kva tvaṁ kō'si kutra saṁcalitaḥ ? । kēna vā prayōjanēna sa kathayati tasya tata ēvam ॥25॥
iha nagara śrēṣṭhitanayaḥ śrāvaka kulasaṁbhavō vibhavahīnaḥ । jātō janakē mr̥tē śrēṣṭhapadādapi tatō bhraṣṭaḥ || 26॥
svajanaiḥ paribhūtō'rthōpārjanakr̥tē calitō'ham । puraparisarasaraṇapariśramē'pyābādhya bāḍham ||27||

supāsanāha-cariammi-
āgaccha jēṇa daṁsēmi tujjhaṁ thēvaṁtarē gurunihāṇaṁ । tō sō tēṇa samaṁ ciya saṁcaliō uttarāhuttaṁ ||29||
jatya paḍhamaṁ sa paṇaō tēṇaṁ tatthēva daṁsiyā tassa | caurō ya cūyarukkhā tāṇaṁ ca ahē daviṇakalā ||
kahiyā bhaṇiyaṁ ca imaṁ ahināṇaṁ kuṇa imāṇa sāhāsu । tō tēja niyayavatthaṁcalāu cīrīja karēūṇa ||
baddhā tāṇa thuḍēsuṁ tō puṇaravi tattha ciciṇitarussa | chāyāē ubaviṭṭhā tō taṁ pucchēi sō ēvaṁ ||32||
ki jayaramalaṁkariyē jammamahēṇaṁ tara mahāpurisa ! । kiṁ puṇaravi puramihiṁ pavittiyavvaṁ niyahi ? ||33||
tō kahai tassa siddhō uttaradisiramaṇibhālaphalatilayaṁ । kaṇayapuraṁ nāmēṇa tattha bhavō hai mahābhāga ! |
gaṁtavvaṁ puṇa ihiṁ sammēyagirimmi titthajattāē । kāyanvō tattha maē kālō kaliyāusēsēṇa ||35|
tā vaccha ! vacca sahiṁ pūrasu paṇayāṇa vaṁchiyasuhāī । gahiūṇa imaṁ davvaṁ rāyassa nivēiuṁ jamhā ||36||
aṇujāṇihī tuhēyaṁ nihiṁ nivō majjha maṁtasattīē । nō bhēyavvaṁ kassavi vilasasu davvaṁ jahicchāē ||37||
iya bhaṇiu sō valiō saḍḍhōvi gihaṁ gaō paōsammi । tō bhāriyāē puṭṭhō kimasauṇō kōvi saṁpattō ? ॥
sō bhai pahāṇatarī jāō sauṇō piē ! pabhāyammi । hōhī payaḍaphalatthō tā saṁpai paraṇayaṁ kuṇasu || 39 ॥
jiṇapūyaṇōvagaraṇaṁ tīivi vihiyaṁ tava simyaṁpi । kāūṇaṁ jiṇapūyaṁ sōvi hu suttō pabhāyami ॥ 40 ॥
kāū jiṇavaṁdaṇakicaṁ gahiu uvāyaṇaṁ kiṁpi । saṁpattī nivapāsē nivēiō nivaiṇō namiuṁ ॥ 41 ॥
savyō nihivr̥ttatō tēvi aṇujāṇiyaṁ nihāṇaṁ taṁ । tō rannānnāō pattō niyamaṁdirē sōvi ॥ 42 ॥
viśrāntō'tra tatastvaṁ prāptō dr̥ṣṭigōcarē mama । sa bhaṇati mayi dr̥ṣṭē dāridryajalāñjaliṁ dēhi ॥ 28 ॥
āgaccha yēna darśayāmi tava stōkāntarē gurunidhānam । tataḥ sa tēna samamēva saṁcalita uttarābhimukham ॥29॥
yatra prathamaṁ sa praṇatastēna tatraiva darśitāstasmai । catvāraśca cūtavr̥kṣāstēṣāṁ cādhō draviṇakalaśāḥ ॥ 30 ॥
kathitā bhaṇitaṁ cēdamabhijñānaṁ kurvēṣāṁ śākhāsu । tatastēna nijavastrāñcalātkhaṇḍāni kr̥tvā ॥ 31 ॥
baddhāni tēṣāṁ śākhāsu tataḥ punarapi tatra ciñcinītarōḥ । chāyāyāmupaviṣṭau tatastaṁ pr̥cchati sa ēvam ||32||
kiṁ nagaramalaṁkr̥taṁ janmamahēna tvayā mahāpuruṣa ! । kiṁ punarapi puramidānīṁ pavitrayitavyaṁ nijapadaiḥ ? ||33||
tataḥ kathayati tasya siddha uttaradigramaṇībhālaphalatilakam । kanakapuraṁ nāmnā tatra bhavō'haṁ mahābhāga ! ||34||
gantavyaṁ punaridānīṁ sammētagirau tīrthayātrāyai । kartavyastatra mayā kālaḥ kalitāyuḥ śēṣēṇa ॥ 35 ॥
vatsa ! vraja svagr̥haṁ pūraya maṇatānāṁ vāñchitasukhāni । gr̥hītvēdaṁ dravyaṁ rājñē nivēdya yasmāt ॥ 36 ॥
anujñāsyati tavaitaṁ nidhiṁ nr̥pō mama mantraśaktyā । nō bhētavyaṁ kasmādapi vilasa dravyaṁ yathēccham ||37||
iti bhaṇitvā sa calitaḥ saḍṭō'pi gr̥haṁ gataḥ pradōṣē । tatō bhāryayā pr̥ṣṭaḥ kimaśakunaḥ kō'pi saṁprāptaḥ ? ॥
sa bhaṇati pradhānatarō jātaḥ śakunaḥ priyē ! prabhātē । bhaviṣyati prakaṭaphalārthastasmātsaṁprati praguṇaṁ kuru || 39॥
jinapūjanōpakaraṇaṁ tayāpi vihitaṁ tathaiva śīghramapi । kr̥tvā jinapūjāṁ sō'pi hi suptaḥ prabhātē ||40||
kr̥tvā nivandanakr̥tyaṁ gr̥hītvōpāyanaṁ kimapi । saṁprāptō nr̥papārśvē nivēditō nr̥patayē natvā ॥ 41 ॥
sarvō nidhivr̥ttāntastēnāpyanujñātaṁ nidhānaṁ tat । tatō rājñānujñātaḥ prāptō nijamandirē sō'pi ॥ 42 ॥

kāū sāmariṁga vihīē gaṁtūna tattha ukkhaṇai । siddhakahiyaṁ nihāṇaṁ niyagēhē nēi tō lōō || 43॥
tradaare ēi gihē pāulāī parāī । iti vaddhāvaṇatthaṁ sayaṇajaṇō puna visēsēṇa ||44||
yataḥ:-
" saṁpadi sapadi ghaṭatē kutō'pi saṁpattisahabhuvō lōkāḥ । varṣābhūnivahā iva kālē kōlāhalaṁ kr̥tvā || "
tō sō tōsēṇa taō pāulalōēṇa parigaō pattō । cēiyaharammi tattō vihiṇā havaṇacaṇaṁ kuṇai || 45 ।।
vicca paraṁ davvaṁ puṇaravi pattō gimmi sayaṇajuō । bhuṁjēi saṁvibhāgaṁ kāūṇaṁ sāhuvaggassa ||46 ||
aha tēṇaṁ pāraddhō vahārō kahavi dūradēsēsu । gihidhammē savisēsaṁ samujjamaṁ kuṇai sō nicca ॥47॥
aha diviyaṁ kayāvi hu gahiyaṁ tēṇaṁ samāsaō ēvaṁ । duvihaṁ tivihēṇa iō jōyaṇapaṇavīsaō paraō ॥ 48 ॥
māsēgaṁ jāva maē gaṁtavvaṁ nēya jāyakajjēvi । puvviṁ disivbaē puṇa saḍḍhasayaṁ causuvidisāsu || 49 ||
āsi kayaṁ mōkalayaṁ, kattōvi hunisuṇiyaṁ imaṁ tēṇa । sirinayaraṁ pai kaḍayaṁ thāvaranayarāhivassa tahiṁ ॥ 50 ॥
tō niyalē lihiu pavaī niyāṇa vaṇiyaputtāṇa । nibbhiccabhicapāsē lihiyaṁ tēṇērisa tattha ॥ 51 ॥
jaha ihanagaranariṁdō savvavarṇapi ēi saṁvr̥ḍhō । sirinayaraṁ para tamhā paṇiyaṁ savvaipi ṭhāsu ॥ 52 ॥
kāū giriduggē ṭhāyavvaṁ kaidiṇē taō puṇavi । maha lēhē iha pattē vavahariyavvaṁ tahēva tarhi ॥ 53 ॥
aha lēhavāhaganarō lēhēṇa samaṁ ca cārapurisēhi । addhapahēcciya pattō 'kassa tumaṁ' pucchiē khuddhō ॥54॥
tō thāvaranaravaṇō samapiō tēhi lēhajuttō sō । lēhaṁ vāivi tattō kuviō sacivassa appē || 55 ॥
kr̥tvā sāmagrī vidhinā gatvā satrātkhanati । siddhakathitaṁ nidhānaṁ nijagēhaṁ nayati tatō lōkaḥ || 43॥
gr̥hītākṣapātravastra ēti gr̥hē gāyanāḥ pracurāḥ । āyanti vardhanārtha svajanajanaḥ punarviśēṣēṇa ॥44॥
tataḥ sa tōṣēṇa tēna gāyanalōkēna parigataḥ prāptaḥ । caityagr̥hē tatō vidhinā snapanārcanaṁ karōti ॥45॥
vyayatē pracuraṁ dravyaṁ punarapi prāptō gr̥hē svajanayutaḥ । bhuṅgē saṁvibhāgaṁ kutvā sādhuvargasya ॥ 46 ॥
atha. tēna prārabdhō vyavahāraḥ kathamapi dūradēśēṣu । gr̥hidharmē saviśēṣaṁ samudyamaṁ karōti sa nityam ॥47॥
atha digtrataṁ kadāpi hi gr̥hītaṁ tēna samāsata ēvam । dvividhaṁ trividhēnētō yōjanapañcaviṁśatitaḥ parataḥ ॥48॥
māsamēkaṁ yāvanmayā gantavyaṁ naiva jātakāryē'pi । pūrva digvatē punaḥ sārdhaśataṁ catasr̥ṣvapi dikṣu ॥ 49 ॥

tatō nijalēkhaṁ likhitvā prasthāpayati nijēbhyō vaṇikputrēbhyaḥ । nibhr̥tyabhr̥tyapārśvē likhitaṁ tēnēdr̥śaṁ tatra ॥ 51 ॥
yathēhanagaranarēndraḥ sarvabalēnāpyēti saṁvyūḍhaḥ । śrīnagaraṁ prati tasmātpaṇyaṁ sarvamapi sthāpaya ॥ 52 ॥
kr̥tvā giridurgē sthātavyaṁ katidināṁstataḥ punarapi । mama lēkha iha prāptē vyavaharttavyaṁ tathaiva tatra ॥ 53 ॥
atha lēkhavāhakanarō lēkhēna samaṁ ca cārapurupaiḥ । ardhapatha ēva prāptaḥ kasya tvaṁ pr̥ṣṭē kṣubdhaḥ ॥ 54 ॥

sōvitaṁ paribhāviya rāyāsēṇa sadayasamīvē । paṭṭavai aṁgarakkhē bhaṇai ya baṁdhivi tamāha ॥ 56 ॥
tērhi ada vihiyaṁ āṇīō naravarassa pāsammi । rannā tō sō bhaṇiō rē rē pāviṭṭa nikiṭṭa ! ॥57॥
paccakkhasattu hēriya ! maha vittiṁ taṁ samaggamavi tattha । jāṇāvasi lēhēṇaṁ maha purasiṭṭīvi taṁ hōuṁ ॥ 58 ॥
tā niggajōggō taṁ navaraṁ mukō si ēkavāraṁ tu | sāhammiutti kāuṁ nō ēvaṁ puṇavi kāvvaṁ ॥ 59 ॥
paḍhamakasāyavasēṇaṁ kayatthiō jaṁsi taṁpi khamiyanvaṁ । iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ mukkō ēttō sō niyagihē pattō ॥ 60 ॥
baṁdhēhi pīḍiō sō citai rē jīva ! jāṇa kajjammi । ailōhaggahaghatthō niyamadhuraṁ cūrasi hayāsa ! ||
puttakalattāīṇaṁ, tē dūraṭhiyā na dukkhasaṁpi । givhaṁti ahaṁ haddhī ēgō duhabhāyaṇaṁ jāō ||62 ||
guruniyamabhaṁga tarukusumasaṁniha jīva ! baṁdhaṇāīyē । aṇuhūyaṁ iha tumaē phalaṁ tu kumaīsu pāvihisi ॥ 63 ॥
iya ciṁtaṁtō pattō paralōyaṁ puvvavaddhaāuvasā | nāgakumārasurēsuṁ taō cuō bahuduhaṁ sahiuṁ ॥ 64||
sijjhissai dhuyakammō, tā bhō thēbaṁpi niyamamālinnaṁ । nō kāyantraṁ jamhā puṇōvi aidullahā vōhī ॥
॥ iti dvitīyaśikṣāvratē dvitīyāticāravipākē saḍḍhakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
sō'pi hi taṁ paribhāvya rājādēśēna saḍḍasamīpē । prasthāpayatyaṅgarakṣānbhaṇati ca baddhvā tamānayata ॥ 56 ॥
tairapi tathaiva vihitamānītō naravarasya pārśvē । rājñā tataḥ sa bhaṇitō rē rē pāpiṣṭha nikr̥ṣṭa ! ॥57॥
pratyakṣaśatruhērika ! mama vr̥ttiṁ tvaṁ samagrāmapi tatra । jñāpayasi lēkhēna mama puraśrēṣṭhyapi tvaṁ bhūtvā ॥ 58 ॥
tasmānnigrahayōgyastvaṁ kintu muktō'syēkavāraṁ tu । sādharmika iti kr̥tvā nō ēvaṁ punarapi kartavyam ||19||
prathamakaṣāyavaśēna kadarthitō yadasi tadapi kṣantavyam । iti bhaṇitvā mukta itaḥ sa nijagr̥hē prāptaḥ ॥ 60 ॥
bandhaiḥ pīḍitaḥ sa cintayati rē jīva ! yēṣāṁ kāryē । atilōbhagrahagrastō niyamadhuraṁ cūrṇayasi hatāśa ! ॥ 61 ॥
putrakalatrādīnāṁ, tē dūrasthitā na duḥkhāṁśamapi । gr̥hṇantyahaṁ hā dhigēkō duḥkhabhājanaṁ jātaḥ ॥62॥
guruniyamabhaṅgatarukusumasaṁnibhaṁ jīṁva ! bandhanādikam । anubhūtamiha tvayā phalaṁ tu kugatiṣu prāpsyasi ||63॥
iti cintayan prāptaḥ paralōkaṁ pūrvavaddhāyurvaśāt । nāgakumārasurēṣu tataścyutō bahuduḥkhaṁ sōḍā || 64 ॥ •
sētsyati dhutakarmā, tasmādbhōḥ stōkamapi niyamamālinyam | nō kartavyaṁ yasmātpunarapyatidurlabhō bōdhiḥ ॥

gahiyadē sāvagāsō sarvaṁ jō karai kāsamāīhi । maijalahivva sa dukkhaṁ pāvara ihaiṁpi agarūyaṁ ||1||
tathāhi ; -
iha bhara hē rahavattaṁ naraṁ bhūramaṇibhālatalatilayaṁ । samaraṁgaṇaladdhajasō rāyā riuvikkamō tattha ||2||
aimucchiō ya rajjē jāē jāē suē suṇēūṇa । sō tāṇaṁ chiṁdēī kannō । īṇi aṁgāī || 3 ||
kiṁbahunā taha kuvvara rajjamsa ajōggayā jahā huṁti । avirayasammadiṭṭhī maṁtī tassatthi maijalahī ||4||
mayaṇasirīnāmāē rannō bhajjāē bhāṇiō maṁtī । jaha pasiūṇaṁ rakkhasu maha garbha niyayabuddhīē ॥5॥
paḍivanna tabvayaṇaṁ sacivēṇaṁ sikkhavittu ēgaṁtē । dēvīsamagavbhabhavā niyadāsī pēsiyā tattha || 6 ||
kahakahavi maṁsaō samagaṁ pasavō viṇimmiō tēṇa । dēvīē ō jāō iyarīē suyā taō jhati ॥ 7॥
sacitrabhaṇiyāē mahalliyāē kāūṇa tāṇa parivittiṁ । sējjāvālē khiviḍaṁ dāsī sacivaggihē mukkā ||8 ॥
puttasamēyā, tattō mahalliyā nivaiṇō kahai ēvaṁ । dēvīē suyā jāyā sōuṁ taṁ mōṇamalliyā || 9 ||
harivikamōtti nāmaṁ ṭhaviyaṁ puttassa maṁtigēhammi । siyapakkhasasaharō iva vaḍḍhai sa kalāhiṁ kaliyataṇū ||

aha annayāya kēṇavi bhaṇiō vasuhāhivō tumaṁ ēttha । nāmēṇa cēva, rāyā maṁtī paramatthaō jamhā ॥ 12 ॥
sicchāi dēi gioes vilasai sicchāē karai phēḍai ya । sāmaṁtāijaṇaṁ taha pōsai niyakōsa mukkōi ||
