tō rāyā paricita sacca ēsō bhaṇēi jēṇa maē । visayapasattēṇa tayā na kayā ciṁtāvi rajjassa || 14 ||
gr̥hītadēśāvakāśaḥ śabdaṁ yaḥ karōti kāsādibhiḥ । matijaladhiriva sa duḥkhaṁ prāpnōtīhāpyatiguru ॥ 1 ॥
iha bharatē rathavr̥ttaṁ nagaraṁ bhūramaṇībhālatalatilakam । samarāṅgaṇalabdhayaśā rājā ripuvikramastatra ॥ 2 ॥
atimūcchitaśca rājyē jātājātānsutān śrutvā । sa tēṣāṁ chinatti karṇauṣṭhādīnyaṅgāni ||3||
kiṁbahunā tathā karōti rājyasyāyōgyā yathā bhavanti । aviratasamyagdr̥ṣṭimantrī tasyāsti matijaladhiḥ ॥ 4 ॥
madanaśrīnāmayā rājñō bhāryayā bhāṇitō mantrī । yathā prasadya rakṣa mama garbha nibuddhayāṁ ||5||
pratipannaṁ tadvacanaṁ sacivēna śikṣayitvaikāntē । dēvīsamagarbhabhavā nijadāsī prēṣitā tatra ॥ 6 ॥
kathakathamapi mantravaśataḥ samaṁ prasavō vinirmitastēna । dēvyāḥ sutō jāta itarasyāḥ sutā tatō jhaṭiti ॥7॥
sacivabhaṇitayā buddhyā kr̥tvā tayōḥ parivr̥ttim । śayyāpālē kṣiptvā dāsī sacivagr̥hē muktā ॥8॥
putrasamētā, tatō vr̥ddhā nr̥patayē kathayatyēvam । dēvyāḥ sutā jātā śrutvā tad maunamālīyatē ॥9॥
harivikrama iti nāma sthāpitaṁ putrasya mantrihē । sitapakṣaśaśadhara iva vardhatē sa kalābhiḥ kalitatanuḥ ॥ 10 ॥
atha kālakavalitē naravarē harivikramō nr̥paḥ sthāpitaḥ । saciva nihitabhāraḥ sō'pi hi vilasati svēcchayā ॥
athānyadā ca kēnāpi bhaṇitō vasudhādhipastvamatra । nāmnaiva, rājā mantrī paramārthatō yasmāt ॥12॥
svēcchayā dadāti gr̥hṇāti vilasati svēcchayā karōti sphēṭayati । sāmantādijanaṁ tathā pōṣayati nijakōśamutkr̥ṣṭam ॥
tatō rājā paricintayati satyamēṣa bhaṇati yēna mayā । viṣayaprasaktēna tadā na kr̥tā cintāpi rājyasya ॥ 14 ॥

supāsanāha-caritryasmi -
tā dāūṇaṁ kiṁcivi khudda ēsaṁ visēsaō tassa । tadakaraṇē tō daṁḍaṁ savvassēṇaṁ vihissāmi || 15॥
iya ciṁtiūṇa rannā bhaṇiō maṁtī kayannuyapurisaṁ । daṁsasu kayaṁ mē ayāṇuyaṁ yāśuyaṁ ca tahā ॥ 16 ॥
annaha nicchapuvvaṁ hōhī tuha maraṇamēva jai saraṇaṁ । tō maṁtī niyagēhē pattō aiāulō hiyaē ||17||
tassatthi gihē duhiyā sujasā nāmēṇa buddhibalakaliyā । puṭṭhō tīē sacivō rahammi ki āulō tāya ! |
lakkhijjasi ajja tumaṁ, sāhai sō tīi nivasamāiṭuṁ । sā bhaṇai ittiēṇavi samāulattaṁ na tuha juttaṁ ॥
ēyaṁ duhāēsa pūrissamahaṁ nivassa kiṁtu taē । parihariyanvō ēsō tavvayaṇaṁ tēṇa paḍivannaṁ ॥ 20 ॥
tattōsā gahiūṇaṁ suṇayasituṁ rayagadārayatamēyaṁ । saṁpattā nivapāsē samagaṁ sacivēga tō rannā || 21 ||
bhaṇiō maṁtī ki tē samāṇiyā puvvasaṁsiyā purisā ? । sō āha majjha duhiyāē āṇiyā dēva ! cihnaṁti ? ॥
tōtē sā puṭṭhā daṁsivi suṇayaṁ kahēi sē ēyaṁ । āhāra piṁḍiyādāṇamittaō mannaē sukayaṁ ||23||
caṁḍālassavi pārtha, tā pahu ! ēsō kayannuō nūṇaṁ । taṁ ciya kayagyasaṁghassa sēharō jēṇa sacivēṇa || 24||
āja māōvi tumaṁ buḍhi nīō payammisaṁṭhaviō । taṁ ciya haṇiuṁ vaṁchasi kaha na tuma hōsi jaha bhaṇiō ।।
ēsa rayaō sujāṇō jamhā rāīē muṇai vatthāṇi । jassa taṇayāṇi jāṇiuṁ, annāṇī majjha puṇa tāō ||
jō ittiryapi na muṇai avivēī kannadubbalō rāyā । taha tujjhavi sēvāē vihavaṁ vaṁchēi jaha bhaṇiyaṁ ||27||
"avivēkini yō bhūpē kuryād gr̥ddhiṁ samr̥ddhayē । gacchēd digantaraṁ manyē khamāruhya samr̥ddhayē ॥
ghaṭavat paripūrṇō'pi vidagdhō rāgavānapi । grahītuṁ śakyatē kēna pārthivaḥ karṇadurbalaḥ ? ॥”
iccāi nisuṇiūṇaṁ savilakkhō bhai naravaī maṁtiṁ । khamasu mahāyasa ! ivhi jaṁ avaraddhaṁ maē tujjha ||
1
tasmāddattvā kañcidapi kṣudrādēśa viśēṣatastasya । tadakaraṇē tatō daṇḍaṁ sarvasvēna vidhāsyāmi ॥ 15 ॥
iti cintayitvā rājñā bhaṇitō mantrī kr̥tajñapuruṣam । darśaya kr̥taghnaṁ mē'jñāyakaṁ jñāyakaṁ ca tathā ॥ 16 ॥
anyathā niścayapūrvaṁ bhaviṣyati tava maraṇamēva yadi śaraṇam । tatō mantrī nijagēhē prāptō'tyākulō hr̥dayē ॥
tasyāsti gr̥hē duhitā suyaśā nāmnā buddhibalakalitā । pr̥ṣṭastathā sacivō rahasi kimākulastāta ! ॥ 18 ॥
lakṣyasē'dya tvaṁ, kathayati sa tasyai nr̥pasamādiṣṭam । sā bhaṇatīyatāpi samākulatvaṁ na tava yuktam ॥19॥
ētaṁ duṣṭādēśaṁ pūrayiṣyāmyahaṁ nr̥pasya kintu tvayā । parihartavya ēṣa tadvacanaṁ tēna pratipannam ॥20॥
tataḥ sā gr̥hītvā śunakaśiśuṁ rajakadārakasamētam । saṁprāptā nr̥papāirvē samaṁ sacivēna tatō rājñā ॥ 21॥
bhaṇitō mantrī kiṁ tvayā samānītāḥ pūrvaśaṁsitāḥ puruṣāḥ ? | sa āha mama duhitrānītā dēva ! tiṣṭhanti ॥
tatastēna sā pr̥ṣṭā darśayitvā śunakaṁ kathayati tasyaitat । āhārapiṇḍikādānamātratō manyatē sukr̥tam ॥23॥
cāṇḍālasyāpi prāyaḥ, tasmātprabhō ! ēṣa kr̥tajñēō nūnam । tvamēva kr̥taghnasaṁghasya śēkharō yēna sacivēna ||24|
ā janmanō'pi tvaṁ vr̥ddhiṁ nītaḥ padē saṁsthāpitaḥ । tamēva hantuṁ vāñchasi kathaṁ na tvaṁ bhavasi yathā bhaṇitaḥ ? ||
ēṣa rajakaḥ sujñānō yasmādrātrau jānāti vastrāṇi । yasya saṁbandhīni yāni tu, ajñānī mama punastātaḥ ॥ 26 ॥
ya iyadapi na jānātyavivēkī karṇa durbalō rājā । tathā tavāpi sēvayā vibhavaṁ vāñchati yathā bhaṇitam ||27|

" pāṣāṇajālakaṭhinō'pi girirviśālaḥ saṁbhidyatē pratidinaṁ vahatā jalēna ।
karṇōpajāpapiśunaiḥ parighr̥ṣyamāṇaḥ kō vā na yāti vikr̥tiṁ dr̥ḍhasauhr̥dō ? ||
tubhēhivi khamiyavaṁ jaṁ kiṁci maē virūvamāyariyaṁ । niyamudaṁ paḍigāhasu vihavēṇa samaṁ maha gihāō ||
tō rannā bahāē dhariu sacivō imaṁ puṇō bhaṇiō । nō muddā muttavvā rajjaṁpi hu tujjha āyataṁ ॥ 30 ॥
tō uṭṭhēḍaṁ sacivō pāē saṁlaggiūṇa taṁ bhaṇai । jāvajjīvaṁ niyamō maha muddā naridēhi ॥ 31 ॥
tā maṁca mamaṁ sāmiya ! samaṇō hōhāmi tuha aṇunnāē । bhaṇai nivō na kahaṁpihu aṇujāṇistāmi taṁ jēṇa ॥
mama āyatō dēhō tuha taṇaō caiva majjha kajjammi । vivvēyavvō niyamā na annahā, bhaṇaṛa tō sacivō ॥ 33॥
ēvaṁ ciya pahu ! jaivi hu kharakammamahaṁ tahāvina karissaṁ । iha atthē nibbaṁdhō tubbhēhiṁvi nēya kāyavvō ।
tō taṁ nicchayasāraṁ vayaṇaṁ suṇiūṇa naravarō bhāi | pālasu sāvayadhammaṁ gihaḍiō caiva tō sacivō ॥ 35 ॥
saṁpattō niyagēhē duhiyāsahiō ahannayā sōvi । gīyatyagurusamīyē paḍivajjaiṇuvvayāīṇi || 36 ||
pālēi paidiṇaṁpi hu bīē sikkhāvaē visēsēṇa । saṁkhivaī disiniyamaṁ maṁtī aha annayā ēvaṁ ||37||
jaha niyagihāu vāhi gaṁtavvaṁ nēya ajja diṇamajjhē । kāraṇavasēṇa kēṇai, aha rannā tassa pāsammi ||
paṭṭaviō paḍihārō vaccatēṇāvi tēṇa taggēhē । diṭṭhō maṁtī ēgaṁtasaṁṭiō kāsasannā ||39||
ariṇō pahāṇapurisaṁ hakārivi kiṁpi maṁtayaṁtō ya । sō āgaṁtūṇa ihaṁ ii vr̥ttaṁtaṁ kahai rannō ॥40॥
tō kōhaggipalittō paḍihāraṁ bhaṇai gaccha maṁtigihē । vaṁdhēvi pacchabāhuṁ taṁ āṇasu majjha pāsamma ॥ 41 ॥
ityādi śrutvā savailakṣyō bhaṇati narapatirmantriṇam । kṣamasva mahāyaśaḥ ! idānīṁ yadaparāddhaṁ mayā tava ॥28॥
yuṣmābhirapi kṣantavyaṁ yatkiñcinmayā virūpamācaritam । nijamudrāṁ pratigrāhaya vibhavēna samaṁ mama gr̥hāt ॥ 29 ॥
tatō rājñā bāhau dhr̥tvā saciva idaṁ punarbhaṇitaḥ । nō mudrā mōkḍavyā rājyamapi hi tavāyattam ||30||
tata utthāya sacivaḥ pādē saṁlagya taṁ bhaṇati । yāvajjīvaṁ niyamō mama mudrāyā narēndra ! idānīm ||31||
tasmānmuñca māṁ svāmin ! śramaṇō bhaviṣyāmi tavānujñayā । bhaṇati nr̥pō na kathamapi hyanujñāsyē tvāṁ yēna ॥
mamāyattō dēhastava saṁbandhyēva mama kāryē । vyayitavyō niyamānnānyathā, bhaṇati tataḥ sacivaḥ ॥33॥
ēvamēva prabhō ! yadyapi hi kharakarmāhaṁ tathāpi na kariṣyē । ihārthē nirbandhō yuṣmābhirapi naiva kartavyaḥ ॥ 34 ॥
tatastanniścayasāraṁ vacanaṁ śrutvā naravarō bhaṇati । pālaya śrāvakadharmē gr̥hasthita ēva tataḥ sacivaḥ ||35||
saṁprāptō nijagēhē duhitr̥sahitō'thānyadā sō'pi । gītārthagurusamīpē pratipadyatē'ṇuvratādīni ॥ 36 ॥
pālayati pratidinamapi hi dvitīyē śikṣāvatē viśēṣēṇa । saṁkṣipati diniyamaṁ mantryathānyadēvam ||37||
yathā nijagr̥hādvahirgantavyaṁ naivādya dinamadhyē । kāraṇavaśēna kēnāpi, atha rājñā tasya pārśvē ॥ 38 ॥
prasthāpitaḥ pratihārō vrajatāpi tēna tadguhē । dr̥ṣṭō mantrayēkāntasaṁsthitaḥ kāsasaṁjñayā ॥ 39 ॥
arēḥ pradhānapuruṣaṁ hakkārayitvā kimapi mantrayaṁśca । sa āgatyēhēti vr̥ttāntaṁ kathayati rājñē ||40||

560
supāsanāha-cariasmi --
tēṇavi tahēva vihiyaṁ bhaṇiō rannā taō imaṁ maṁtī । ajjavi na muyasi khāraṁ jaṁ mannasi majjha sattujaṇaṁ ॥
taha khāmiōvi sammāṇiōvi taiyā maē sayaṁ caiva । tā kimahaṁ tuha jōggō jaṁ jāṇasi taṁ karijjāsu ॥
puṇa maha visayaṁ pāṇē na harāmi tujjha jēṇa sayaṁ । tē gacchihaṁti nūṇaṁ sāmiviruddhaṁ caraṁtassa ||44 ||
i sa narāvisa jagaṇīvi mayaṇasirināmā । tatthāgayā ruyaṁtī sōuṁ maṁtissa baṁdhāī || 45 ॥
pabhaṇai vaccha ! kiyēyaṁ maṁtissa kayatthaṇaṁ kuṇasi ēvaṁ | dujjaṇajaṇavayaṇēhiṁ paramuvayārissa sayakālaṁ ॥46॥
saṁpa puṇa savisēsaṁ dhammammi raō na maṁgulaṁ kuṇai । iyara jaṇassavi ēsō nūṇaṁ samasattamittapaṇō ॥47॥
kiñca ।
aviyārikaṇa kajjē suhamasuhaṁ vā kuṇati nahu garuyā । tā duchu kathaṁ tumaē jaṁ baddhō ēsa sahasēva ॥ 48 ॥
kiñca ।
sacivaduhiyāē taiyā kayagyasirasēharō tumaṁ caiva । kahiō taṁ ciya tumaē saccaviyaṁ iya kuṇatēṇa ॥49॥
iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ dēvī baṁdhē chidēvi tikkhachuriyāē । aṇuṇai maṁti sōvi hu bhaṇaī maha cēva iha dōsō ||50 ||
jēṇajja bhaē niyamō gahiō ēvaṁ na gēhamajjhāō । nīhariyavvaṁ tattō kāsisa karēū ॥51॥
āhūō dēvi ! maē sattunarō puvvaparicayavasēṇa । dēsāvagāsiyavaē aiyārō hōi iya vihiē ॥ 52 ॥
tarasa phalaṁ aṇuhūyaṁ maē sayaṁ caiva natthi dēvassa । thēvōvi hu iha dōsō iya suṇivi pasaṁtarōbharō ||13||
yā khamāī maṁti vayaṇēhiṁ viṇayasārēhiṁ । maṁtīvi jāi gēhē suhāsaṇēṇa nivāṇāē ||54||
tataḥ krōdhāgnipradīptaḥ pratihāraṁ bhaṇati gaccha mantrigr̥hē । baddhvā paścādvāhu tamānaya mama pārśvē ॥ 41 ॥
tēnāpi tathaiva vihitaṁ bhaṇitō rājñā tata idaṁ mantrī । adyāpi na muñcasi kṣāraṁ yanmanyasē mama śatrujanam ॥
tathā kṣamitō'pi sammānitō'pi tadā mayā svayamēva । tasmātkimahaṁ tava yōgyō yajjānāsi tatkuryāḥ ॥ 43 ॥
muñca punarmama viṣayaṁ prāṇānna harāmi tava yēna svayam । tē gamiṣyanti nūnaṁ svāmiviruddhaṁ carataḥ ।।44 ॥
iti prabhaṇatō narādhipasya jananyapi madanaśrīnāmā । tatrāgatā rudatī śrutvā mantriṇō bandhādi ||45 ||
prabhaṇati vatsa ! kimētanmantriṇaḥ kadarthanaṁ karōṣvēvam । durjanajanavacanaiḥ paramōpakāriṇaḥ sadākālam ||46||
saṁprati punaḥ saviśēṣaṁ dharmē ratō nāniṣṭaṁ karōti । itarajanasyāpyēṣa nūnaṁ samaśatru mittramanāḥ || 47॥
avicārya kārya śubhamaśubhaṁ vā kurvanti na khalu guravaḥ । tasmād duṣṭhu kr̥taṁ tvayā yadvaddha ēṣa sahasaiva ॥ 48 ॥
sacivaduhitrā tadā kr̥taghnaśiraḥ śēkharastvamēva । kathitastadēva tvayā satyāpitamiti kurvatā ॥ 49 ॥
iti bhaṇitvā dēvī bandhān chittvā tīkṣṇakṣurikayā । anunayati mantriṇaṁ sō'pi hi bhaṇati mamaivaha dōṣaḥ ||
yēnādya mayā niyamō gr̥hīta ēvaṁ na gēhamadhyāt । nissartavyaṁ tataḥ kāsitaśabdaṁ kr̥tvā ॥ 51 ॥
āhūtō dēvi ! mayā śatrunaraḥ pūrvaparicayavaśēna । dēśāvakā śikavatē'ticārō bhavatīti vihitē ॥ 52 ॥
tasya phalamanubhūtaṁ mayā svayamēva nāsti dēvasya । stōkō'pi khalviha dōṣa iti śrutvā praśāntarōpabharaḥ ||
rājāpi kṣamayati mantriṇaṁ vacanairvinayasārēḥ । mantryapi yāti gēhē sukhāsanēna nr̥pājñayā ॥54॥
।

sō kō mahaṁta jāō sē baṁdhapīḍiyaṁgassa । taiyadiṇammi vimukō pāṇēhiṁ jēṇa sō sahasā ||55॥
tattō sō sōhammē apiṭṭhiyasuravarō samppannō । tamhā cuō vidēhē sijjhissara taiyamami ॥ 56 ॥
॥ iti dvitīyaśikṣāvratē tr̥tīyāticāravipākē matijaladhimantrikathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
sa kō'pi mahājvarō jātastasya bandhapīḍitāṅgasya । tr̥tīyadinē vimuktaḥ prāṇairyēna sa sahasā ||15||
tataḥ sa saudharmē'lparddhikasuravaraḥ samutpannaḥ । tasmācyutō vidēhē sētsyati tr̥tīyajanmani ॥ 56 ॥

kajjavasēṇaṁ dūradviyassa daṁsēi jō u appāṇaṁ । gahiyadēsāvagāsō kaṇḍuvva lahēi sō dukkhaṁ ॥ 1 ॥
tathāhi;
-
puramatthi māṇakhēḍaṁ chakkhaṁḍadharāē dhariyagurusōhaṁ । paribhaviyasayalariucakkavikkamō vikkamācō ||2||
taṁ pālai savvakalāṇa pāragō tassa paṇaiṇī paumā । tāṇaṁ vikkamasēṇō taṇaō viṇayāiguṇabhavaṇaṁ ||3||
aha kaṇhamittasahiō gaō gaīdammi sō samāruhiuṁ । naṁdaṇavaṇābhirāmē ārāmē jaṇiyajaṇakāmē ||4||
tattha purisēṇa kēṇavi bhaṇiō jaha kumara ! bhāriyāē samaṁ । rayaṇīē kēliharaē suttō haṁ jāva ciṭṭhāmi ||
kaṁkēllipāyavāō uttariūṇa maūrapōṣaṇa | mahabhajjāgīvāō avahariyā rayaṇamālatti ||6||
majjha niyaṁtassa taō puṇaravi pattō sa tammi rukkhami । mukkō mavi vāṇō tassa taō sōvi maha laggō ||
sō puṇa ciṭṭha tatthavi taḍaviyasiṁhaḍamaṁḍiyakuḍaggō । navi tassa kiṁci pahavai na bhayaṁ kassāvi tassatthi ||
tā kāūṇa pasāyaṁ āgaṁtūṇaṁ khaṇaṁ palōēsu । taṁ pakkhiṁ tō kumarō pattō tatthēva taṁ niyai ||9||
pucchai ya vihiyamaṇō bhō bhō taṁ kīsa naccasi maūra !। sō bhaṇai kumara ! tōsēṇa sō puṇō suṇasu jaha jāō ||
ahamāsi rāyaputō rauḍō khuḍiyasīlalakārō । tō ēgā siṭṭisuyā saṁghaḍiyā majjha ruṭṭhā ॥11॥
taṁ hariumahaṁ caliō samagaṁ satthēṇa siṁdhudēsamma । satyē javēṇa jaṁtē sā maṁdagaī visālacchī || 12 ||
satthāṇumaggalaggā gacchaṁtī saha maē taō satthē । dūraṁtariē dōnivi parisaṁtāī pahasamēṇa || 13 ||
pacchā caiva ṭhiyāī maggaṁ mōttūṇa nivbhayattāō । rayaṇīē paḍhamapaharammi ramijaṁ suttāī, ittōya || 14 ||
kāryavaśēna dūrasthitāya darśayati yastvātmānam । gr̥hītadēśāvakāśaḥ kr̥ṣṇa iva labhatē sa duḥkham ॥1॥
puramasti mānakhēṭaṁ paṭkhaṇḍadharāyāṁ dhr̥taguruśōbham । paribhūtasakalaripucakravikramō vikramādityaḥ ||2||
tatpālayati sarvakalānāṁ pāragastasya praṇayinī padmā । tayōrvikramasēnastanayō vinayādiguṇabhavanam ॥3॥
atha kr̥ṣṇa mittrasahitō gatō gajēndrē sa samāruhya । nandanavanābhirāma ārāmē janitajanakāmē ||4||
tatra puruṣēṇa kēnāpi bhaṇitō yathā kumāra ! bhāryayā samam । rajanyāṁ kadalīgr̥hē suptō'haṁ yāvattiṣṭhāmi ||5|
kaṅkēllipādapāduttīrya mayūrapōtēna । madbhāryāgrīvātō'pahr̥tā ratnamālēti ॥ 6 ॥
māya paśyati tataḥ punarapi prāptaḥ sa tasmin vr̥kṣē । muktō mayāpi bāṇastasya tataḥ sō'pi mama lagnaḥ ||7||
sa punastiṣṭhati tatrāpi tataśikhaṇḍamaṇḍitakuṭāgraḥ । naiva tasya kiñcitprabhavati na bhayaṁ kasyāpi tasyāsti ॥
tasmātkr̥tvā prasādamāgatya kṣaṇaṁ pralōkasva । taṁ pakṣiṇaṁ tataḥ kumāraḥ prāptastatraiva taṁ paśyati ||9||
pr̥cchati ca vismitamanā bhō bhōstvaṁ kasmānnr̥tyasi mayūra ! । sa bhaṇati kumāra ! tōṣēṇa sa punaḥ śr̥ṇu yathā jātaḥ ॥
ahamāsaṁ rājaputrō rāṣṭrakūṭaḥ khaṇḍitaśīlālaṁkāraḥ । tata ēkā śrēṣṭhatā saṁghaṭitā mayā rūpāḍhyā ॥11॥
tāṁ hr̥tvā'haṁ calitaḥ samaṁ sārthēna sindhudēśē । sārthē javēna yāti sā mandagatirviśālākṣī ॥12॥
sārthānurmārgalagnā gacchantī saha mayā tataḥ sārthē । dūrāntaritē dvāvapi pariśrāntau pathiśramēṇa ॥ 13 ॥
paścādēva sthita mārga muktvā nirbhayatvāt । rajanyāṁ prathamapraharē ranvā suptau itaśca ॥ 14 ॥

563
rayaṇīē carimajāmammi kahavi ēmēva jaggiyammi maē । nō sā diṭṭhā niuṇaṁ savvattha gavēsiyāvi tahiṁ ||
tō citiyaṁ maē iya jai sā pacchāmuhā gayā valiuṁ । piyarāī sumarēuṁ tō tīē na suṁdaraṁ vihiyaṁ ॥ 16 ॥
mammi dusattā haṇihaṁti imaṁ vicitiūṇa maē । aruṇōdayavēlāē tappayati niyaṁtēṇa ॥ 17 ॥
aisigyapatidaṁsaṇā jāṇiyaṁ jahā haṇiyā । vagghēṇa nigviṇēṇa maha bhajjā tō gaō satyē || 18 ||
satyāhivassa kahi taṁ vr̥ttaṁtaṁ imaṁ ca sō bhaṇiō । jāba ahaṁ tassuddhiṁ lahēmi tā ittha ṭhāha ॥ 19 ॥
tēvitaṁ paḍivannaṁ dinnā ya sahāiṇō pavarasuhaḍā । tō tēhi saha gaēṇaṁ vagbō diṭṭō maē suttō ॥ 20 ॥
taha vālābāhujyaṁ varaṁgulīyaṁ sakaḍagakēūraṁ । uttattakaṇayasaṁka liyakaliyamaha tīē nuurajuyaṁ ||21||
rayaṇāvalī ya ēsā diṭṭhā tassēva saṁnihāṇammi । tō hakiō maē sō tittō tapisiyamasi ||22|
rērē liṭṭiya ! lōhasi ajjavi dharaṇīē nihaṇiuṁ vālaṁ । tuha piṭṭāō kaḍḍēmi nūṇa kaṁdōṭṭadalanayaṇi ||23||
tamasuyaputraṁ vayaṇaṁ suṇiḍaṁ vagbō samuṭṭiō jhatti | phōḍatō iva vaṁbhaṁḍamaṁḍavaṁ gajjiyaravēṇa ||24||
kaṁpāvitōya atucchapucchaacchōḍaṇāhiṁ bhūvīṭhaṁ । sajjiyakamō kamēṇaṁ kayaṁtakappō garuppō ||25||
paḍiō majvaraṁ tō maēvi tikkhayarakhayarakīlēṇa । vāmakaraggaṭhiēṇaṁ viddhā jīhā sauuḍā ||26||
dāhiṇakaraṭṭiyāē churiyāē āhaō ya sō uyarē । tō takkhaṇēṇa mukkī pāṇēhiṁ sō, iō ya maē ॥ 27॥
bālādēhāvayavē gahiūṇaṁ kaḍagakuṁḍalāīpi । khuradhariyavagyadēhō pattō satthāhivasamīvaṁ ॥ 28 ॥
bhaṇiō imaṁ maē sō rayaṇaurē rayaṇasaṁcaō siṭṭhī । tabbhajjā dēvasirī jaṇaṇī ēīē ramaṇīē ||29||
rajanyāṁ caramayāmē kathamapyēvamēva jāgr̥tēna mayā । nō sā dr̥ṣṭā nipuṇaṁ sarvatra gavēṣitāpi tatra ॥ 15 ॥
tataścintitaṁ mayēti yadi sā paścānmukhā gatā valitvā । pitarau smr̥tvā tatastayā na sundaraṁ vihitam ॥ 16॥
mārgē duṣṭasattvā haniyantīmāṁ vicintya mayā । aruṇōdayavēlāyāṁ tatpadapaṅkiṁ paśyatā ॥ 17॥
atiśīghravyāghrapadapaṅkidarśanājjñātaṁ yathā hatā । vyāghrēṇa nighr̥ṇēna mama bhāryā tatō gataḥ sārthē ॥18॥
sārthādhipāya kathayitvā taṁ vr̥ttāntamidaṁ ca sa bhaṇitaḥ । yāvadahaṁ tacchuddhiṁ labhē tāvadatra tiṣṭha ॥ 19 ॥
tēnāpi tat pratipannaṁ dattāśca sahāyāḥ pravarasubhaṭāḥ । tatastaiḥ saha gatēna vyāghrō dr̥ṣṭō mayā suptaḥ ॥20॥
tathā bālābāhuyugaṁ varāṅgulīyaṁ sakaṭaka kēyūram । uttaptakanakaśr̥ṅkhalākalitamatha tasyā nr̥purayugam ॥21॥
ratnāvalī caiṣā dr̥ṣṭā tasyaiva saṁnidhānē । tataḥ śabditō mayā sa tr̥ptastatpiśitamaśitvā ॥22॥
rērē lampaṭa ! lōṭhasyadyāpi dharaṇyāṁ nihatya bālām । tavōdarātkr̥ṣāmi nūnamutpaladalanayanām ॥23॥
tadaśrutapūrva vacanaṁ śrutvā vyāghraḥ samutthitō jhaṭiti । sphōṭayanniva brahmāṇḍamaṇḍapaṁ garjitaravēṇa ॥ 24 ॥
kampayaṁścātucchapucchācchōṭanābhirbhūpīṭham । sajjitakramaḥ kramēṇa kr̥tāntakalpō gurudarpaḥ ॥ 25॥
patitō mamōpari tatō mayāpi tīkṣṇatarakhādirakalina । vāmakarāgrasthitēna viddhā jihvā sauṣṭhapuṭā ||26||
dakṣiṇakarasthitayā kṣurikayā''hataśca sa udarē । tatastatkṣaṇēna muktaḥ prāṇaiḥ saḥ, itaśca mayā ॥27॥
bālādēhāvayavān gr̥hītvā kaṭakakuṇḍalādyapi । kṣuradhr̥tavyāghradēhaḥ prāptaḥ sārthādhipasamīpam ||28||

tīi imaṁ ābharaṇaṁ apijjasu nicchaṣaṇa gaṁtūṇa | sāhijjasu jahadihaṁ majjha pasāyaṁ vihēūṇa ||30||
ēēhi avayavēhiṁ samamēva ciyāē jaliyajalaṇāē । appāṇayahaṁ khiviḍaṁ piyāē maggēṇa gacchissaṁ ||31||
khamiyanvaṁ maha savvaṁ tumaē taha majjha sayaṇavaggassa । kahiyaccō buttatō ēsō maha khāmaṇāē samaṁ ||32||
satyāhivēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ lōyavyavahāradhammavajjhamiṇaṁ । jaṁ mahilāē saddhiṁ jalaṇapavasē samāyarasi ||33||
mahilā purisēṇa samaṁ marē iya tāva lōyavavahārō । bhaṇiyaṁ mavi nēhō pāyēṁ purisāṇa nō jamhā ||34||
chuhiyāṇa bhōyaṇamiva rāō ramaṇīsu hōi purisāṇa | nēhō puṇa viralāṇaṁ jō maraṇaṁtēvi nivvaḍai ||35||
tahāṇugayā vahāva bahusō viyaṁ piyē viṁti । iccāi palaviūṇaṁ raiyaciyāē lahu paṭṭi || 36 ||
saha mahilāvayavērhi mariūṇaṁ vaṁtarī ahaṁ jāō । kīlaṁtō iha pattō satyā hivaīvi sakalatō ||37||
tas ya kalattavacchatthalammi rayaṇāvalī niyā dinā । tadaṁsaṇēṇa nāṇōvaōgaō jāṇiyaṁ jhatti ॥ 38 ॥
puttaṁ savrvvapi huhariyā rayaṇāvalī maē kumara ! । kāūṇa mōrarūvaṁ tō harisō majjha saṁjāō ॥ 39 ॥
jai pattiyaha na majjhaṁ tā ittō kēvalīvi ciṭṭhēi | ujjāṇaavarabhāgē sahayāratarussa hami ||40||
taṁ pucchaha maha cariyaṁ tō kumarō kaṇhamitta parikaliō | sakalattapurisajutō gahiyamaūrō tahi pattō ||
dēvikēvala sō vō samuciyammi ṭhāṇammi । tō patthāvē kumarō pucchara taṁ kēvali ēvaṁ ॥ 42 ॥ |
bhayavaṁ ! ēsa sa maūrō putrabhavaṁ kērisō kahiṁ hutō । kiṁ vihiyaṁ suhamasuhaṁ sāhasu pasiūṇa maha inhiṁ ||
I
bhaṇita idaṁ mayā sa ratnapurē ratnasaṁcayaḥ śrēṣṭhī । tadbhāryā dēvaśrījananyētasyā ramaṇyāḥ ॥ 29 ॥
tasyā idamābharaṇamarpaya niścayēna gatvā । kathaya yathādr̥ṣṭaṁ mayi prasādaṁ vidhāya ||30||
1
ētairavayavaiḥ samamēva citāyāṁ jvalitajvalanāyām । ātmānamahaṁ kṣiptvā priyāyā mārgēṇa gamiṣyāmi ||21||
kṣamitavyaṁ mama sarvaṁ tvayā tathā mama svajanavargāya । kathayitavyō vr̥ttānta ēṣa mama kṣāmaṇayā samam ||32||
sārthādhipēna bhaṇitaṁ lōkavyavahāradharmavācamidam । yad mahilayā sārdhaṁ jvalanapravēśaṁ samācarasi ॥ 33 ॥
mahilā puruṣēṇa samaṁ mriyata iti tāvallōkavyavahāraḥ । bhaṇitaṁ mayāpi snēhaḥ prāyaḥ puruṣāṇāṁ nō yasmāt ||
kṣudhitānāṁ bhōjana iva rāgō ramaṇīṣu bhavati puruṣāṇām । snēhaḥ punarviralānāṁ yō maraṇāntē'pi nirvartatē ॥35॥
tr̥ṣṇānugatā bappīhā api bahuśaḥ priyaṁ priyaṁ bruvanti । ityādi pralapya racitacitāyāṁ laghu praviṣṭaḥ ||36||
saha mahilāvayavairmr̥tvā vyantarō'haṁ jātaḥ । krīḍanniha prāptaḥ sārthādhipatirapi sakalatraḥ ||27||
tasya ca kalatravakṣaḥsthalē ratnāvalī nijā dr̥ṣṭā । tadarśanēna jñānōpayōgatō jñātaṁ jhaṭiti ||38||
pūrvōktaṁ sarvamapi hi hr̥tā ratnāvalī mayā kumāra ! | kr̥tvā mayūrarūpaṁ tatō harṣō mama saṁjātaḥ ॥ 39 ॥
yadi pratīyā na māṁ tadēta: kēvalyapi tiṣṭhati । udyānāvarabhāgē sahakāratarōradhaḥ ॥ 40 ॥
taṁ pr̥cchata mama caritaṁ tataḥ kumāraḥ kr̥ṣṇamityaparikalitaḥ । sakalatrapuruṣayuktō gr̥hītamayūrastatra prāptaḥ ॥ 41 ॥
vanditvā kēvalinaṁ sa upaviṣṭaḥ samucitasthānē । tataḥ prastāvē kumāraḥ pr̥cchati taṁ kēvalinamēvam ॥42॥
bhagavan ! ēṣa sa mayūraḥ pūrvabhavē kīdr̥śaḥ kutrābhūt । kiṁ vihitaṁ śubhamaśubhaṁ kathaya prasadya mamēdānīm ||43||

kaṇhakahā ।
565
kēvaliṇā kahiyaṁ savvaṁpi tahēva jaha maūrēṇa । kumarapaḍivōhaṇatthaṁ ahiyayaraṁ ittiyapi jahā ||44 ॥
hamajjhavasaṁtīē tīē bālāē āgayā niddā । tō sā vagghēṇa hayā uppannā tiriyajāīē || 45 ||
kumarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ munipuṁgava ! raisuhamajjhavasapi । kiṁ iyaphalayaṁ jāyai, tō nāṇī kahaha tassa imaṁ ॥
hamajyā saṁtō tō aha maraṛa kahavi tō jīvō । aiduggaduggaīē gacchai guṇagāmajuttōvi ||47||
vāidēsaṇaṁ nisuṇiūṇa kumarō duvālasavirhapi । paḍivajjā gihidhammaṁ juttō mittēṇa kaṇhēṇa ||48 ||
gha foors sammataṁ rayaṇamāliṁga khivium̐ । kumarassa kaṁṭhadēsē namiya muṇi tō gayā ṭhāṇaṁ ॥ 49 ॥
yē karēi dhammaṁ sahamitō sayāvi uvauttō । dēsavagāsiē aha gahiō kaṇhēṇa iya niyamō ॥ 50 ॥
pōhālā bahiṁ maē tā na ajja gaṁtavvaṁ । jāva divasāvasāṇa, aha tattha samāgaō purisō ॥ 51 ॥
rassa saṁtiō kuṇai bahuvi ' kaha kaṇha' iya sadē । pōsahasāladuvārē pihiyammi uccaṭhāṇami ॥52॥
sō sai appāṇaṁ tassa vihiyamōṇōvi । tadaṁsaṇēṇa tēṇaṁ pōsahasālākavāḍāī || 53 ||
ḍiyāī, ughāḍiūṇa pattō ya kaṇhapāsamma | kumarabhaṇiyāī sāhai jā tātra kuōvi viharatō ।।
kaṇyāsa baṁdī sāhasiyahasiyavalabuddhī । dhariḍaṁ bahāē tayaṁ churiyaṁ daṁsēi bhaī ya ॥ 55 ॥
sukkhaō ahaṁ tō viyarasa kaṇayassa dasa sahassāī । kumarapurisēṇa vāhim̐ ṭhāūṇa kayā taō bubā ||
lēō paurō lōō kumarōṣi samāgaō ō tēṇa । thaṁbhēṇa samaṁ vaddhō kaṇhō gāḍhaṁ taō churiyaṁ ॥ 57 ॥
kaṭhiṇa thakō sō baṁdī, bhaṇai taṁ taō kumarō । muṁcasu maha mittamimaṁ jaṁ maggasi taṁ payacchassaṁ ।
: kēvalinā kathitaṁ sarvamapi tathaiva yathā mayūrēṇa । kumārapratibōdhanārthamadhikatara miyadapi yathā ॥ 44 ॥
sukhamadhyavasyantyāstasyā bālāyā āgatā nidrā । tataḥ sā vyāghrēṇa hatōsannā tiryagjātau ॥45॥
: kumārēṇa bhaṇitaṁ munipuṅgava ! ratisukhādhyavasānamapi । kimitiphalakaṁ jāyatē, tatō jñānī kathayati tasyēdam ||
sukhamadhyavasyan suptō yadi mriyatē kathamapi tatō jīvaḥ । atidurgadurgatau gacchati guṇagrāmayuktō'pi ॥ 47 ॥
ādidēśanāṁ śrutvā kumārō dvādaśavidhamapi । pratipadyatē gr̥hidharma yuktō mistrēṇa kr̥ṣṇēna ॥ 48 ॥
surō'pi gr̥hṇāti samyaktvaṁ ratnamālāṁ kṣiptvā । kumārasya kaṇṭhadēśē natvā muniṁ tatō gatāḥ sthānam ॥
raḥ karōti dharma kr̥ṣṇa mittraḥ sadāpyupayuktaḥ । dēśāvakāśikē'tha gr̥hītaḥ kr̥ṣṇēnēti niyamaḥ ॥10॥
paudhaśālāyā bahiyā tāvannādya gantavyam । yāvaddivasāvasānaṁ, atha tatra samāgataḥ puruṣaḥ ॥ 51 ॥
[rasya satkaḥ karōti bahuvidhān 'kr̥ṣṇa kr̥ṣṇa' iti śabdān । pauṣadhaśālādvārē pihita uccasthānē ॥52॥
tvāsa darśayata ātmānaṁ tasmai vihitamaunō'pi । taddarśanēna tēna pauṣadhaśālākapāṭāni ॥ 53 ॥
||ṭatāni, udghāṭya prāptaśca kr̥ṣṇapārśvē । kumārabhaṇitāni kathayati yāvattāvatkutō'pi viharan ॥54॥
: kr̥ṣṇasakāśē bandī sāhasika hasita balabuddhiḥ । dhr̥tvā bāhau tāṁ kṣurikāṁ darśayati bhaṇati ca ॥ 55 ॥
mukṣitā'haṁ tatō vitara kanakasya daśa sahasrāṇi । kumāra puruṣēṇa bahiḥ sthitvā kr̥tā tatō bumbā ॥ 56 ॥
utaḥ pracurō lōkaḥ kumārō'pi samāgatastēna । stambhēna samaṁ baddhaḥ kr̥ṣṇō gāḍhaṁ tataḥ kṣurikām ||17||

tō tēṇa bhīēṇaṁ pāsatyayadasa sahassadammāī | abhaēṇa samaṁ ciya maggiyāiṁ kumarēṇa dinnāī || 59||
tō baṁdī kumarakarē laggēuṁ niggaō purahasa bahiṁ । pacchā pacchāhuttaṁ kumaraṁ namiuṁ visajjēi ||60||
kanhōvi ruhirabhariō gāḍhaṁ baṁdhēhi pīḍiō saṁtō । tatthēva ṭhiō ēvaṁ paribhāvaṁtō bhavasarūvaṁ ॥ 61 ॥
" janma maraṇāya niyataṁ bandhurduḥ khāya dhanamanirvr̥tayē । tannāsti yanna vipadē tathāpi lōkō nirālōkaḥ ||
ghanāpāyaḥ kāyaḥ prakr̥ticapalā śrīrapi khalā, mahābhōgā rōgāḥ kuvalayadr̥śaḥ sarpasadr̥śaḥ ।
gr̥haìvēśaḥ klēśaḥ praṇayiṣu sukhaṁ sthairyavimukhaṁ, yamaḥ svairī vairī tadapi na hitaṁ karma vihitam ॥”
disivayakalaṁka taruṇō kusumamiṇa jaṁ ihēva iya dukkhaṁ । phalamaḍalaṁ paralōē kugaigayassēvamaha hōhī ||62 ||
iccā bhāvaṇāē diṇasēsaṁ gamiya niyagharē pattō । dāhajarēṇaṁ gahiō maō ya taiē di tattō ॥ 63 ॥
upannō jōisiō dēvō cai taō ya taiyammi । jammammi mōkkhasōkkhaṁ dhuyakammō pāvihī nūṇaṁ ॥ 64 ॥
vikkamasēṇakumārō kamēṇa caraṇaṁ sunimmalaṁ lahiuṁ । uppannavimalanāṇō siddhō nidhuṇiyakammamalō || 65||
॥ iti dvitīyaśikṣāvatāticāravipākē kr̥ṣṇakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
ākr̥pya sthitaḥ sa candī, bhaṇati taṁ tataḥ kumāraḥ । muñca mama mittramidaṁ yanmārgayasi tatprayaṁsyāmi ||18||
tatastēna bhītēna pārśvasthadaśasahasūdrammāṇi । abhayēna samamēva mārgitāni kumārēṇa dattāni ॥59॥
tatō bandī kumārakarē lagitvā nirgataḥ purād bahiḥ । paścātpaścānmukhaṁ kumāraṁ natvā visr̥jati ॥ 60 ॥
kr̥ṣṇō'pi rudhirabhr̥tō gāḍhaṁ bandhaiḥ pīḍitaḥ san । tatraiva sthita ēvaṁ paribhāvayan bhavasvarūpam ॥ 61 ॥
digbatakalaṅkatarōḥ kusumamidaṁ yadihaivēti duḥkham । phalamatulaṁ paralōkē kugatigatasyaiva mama bhaviṣyati ॥62॥
ityādibhāvanayā dinaśēṣaṁ gamayitvā nijagr̥hē prāptaḥ । dāhajvarēṇa gr̥hītō mr̥taśca tr̥tīyē dinē tataḥ ॥ 63 ॥
utpannō jyōtiṣikō dēvaścyutvā tataśca tr̥tīyē । janmani mōkṣasaukhyaṁ dhutakarmā prāpsyati nūnam ॥ 64 ॥
vikramasēnakumāraḥ kramēṇa caraṇaṁ sunirmalaṁ labdhvā । utpannavimalajñānaḥ siddhō nirdhūtakarmamalaḥ ॥ 65 ॥

sigāsa khiviūṇa parasta kakkarāīyē। jō appaṁ jāṇavai sa lahai sōmōntra dukhāī ॥ 1 ॥
tathāhi ;-
bhōgauraṁ asthi puraṁ gurubhōgitva bahuvinivāsaṁ । nimmalamaṇikaravasaraṁ durasaṇaparivajjiyaṁ kiṁtu ॥ 2 ॥
tatthāsi sōmanāmō siddhī sōmantra suyaṇakumuyāṇa । bhajjā agaṁgasēṇā agaṁgadhariṇivva tassāsi ||3||
tāṇaṁ ca parōpparapīinivbharaṁ viyōkkhadirayāṇaṁ । akaliyāṇa kālō bōlai dōguṁdagāva ||4||
aha annayā paḍhyā tavbhajjā tīē kannayā jāyā । samaē agaṁgasuṁdarī nāpi paṭṭiyaṁ tīsē ||5||
niruvamā nimmēra paramasuṁdēradaliyaraidappā | kahakahavi payatēṇaṁ vihiṇāvi viṇimiyā mantrē || 6 ||
kiṁtu adūvā sā didibhāvi kuṇa na hu kōi । naya kōdi varai baraī piyarēhiṁ dijjamānaṁpi ॥7॥
mayaṇānalapajjaliyā parapurisē paidipi patthatī । punnālitti bhaṇijjai tattō sā nayaralōēṇa ॥ 8 ॥
taṁ sōuṁ dūmijjai hasiyai sahipāhi lajjaē ahiyē । sōhaggamagirā sā pūyai hēravallaḍhāīyaṁ ॥ 9 ॥
sōhagaṁjaṇasōhaggaguliyatilayāiyaṁ ca virai । piyakāriyadhūvēhiṁ dhūvēī apaṇō dēhaṁ ॥ 10 ॥
taha kāmadēva jhāya javaī ya tipuravijjāī । tahavi hu ubviyaṇijjā jāyai sā purisavagassa ॥ 11 ॥
āinnāī pirāī tīē pucchati divvadēvanaṁ । nēmittiryapi daṁsaṁti taha ya bahumaṁtavāīṇa ||12||
kuladēvayāṇa pūyaṁ taha vivihōvāiyāī icchaṁti । dēvavhavaṇāiēhiṁ nhāyaṁti tahōsahīhiṁpi || 13 ||
ki bahuṇā,
gr̥hītadēśāvakāśaḥ kṣiptvā parasmai karkarādikam । ya ātmānaṁ jñāpayati sa labhatē sōma iva duḥkhāni ॥1॥
bhōgapuramasti puraṁ gurubhōgitanuriva bahuvr̥ (vi) ṣanivāsam । nirmalamaṇikaraprasaraṁ dvirasanaparivarjitaṁ kintu ॥
tatrāsītsōmanāmā śrēṣṭhī sōma iva svajana kumudānām । bhāryā'naṅgasēnā'naṅgagr̥hiṇīva tasyāsīt ॥3॥
tayōśca parasparaprītinirbharaṁ viṣaya saukhyaniratayōḥ । akalitaduḥkhayōḥ kālō gacchati daugundakayōriva || 4 ||
athānyadā prasūtā tadbhāryā tasyāḥ kanyakā jātā । samayē'naṅgasundarī nāmāpi pratiṣṭhitaṁ tasyāḥ ||5||
nirupamarūpā nirmaryādaparama saundarya dalitaratidarpā । kathaṁkathamapi prayatnēna vidhināpi vinirmitā manyē || 6 ||
kintvatidurbhagā sā dr̥ṣṭyabhyāsē'pi karōti nahi kaścit । na ca kō'pi vr̥ṇutē varākīṁ pitr̥bhyāṁ dīyamānāmapi ॥
madanānalaprajvalitā parapuruṣānpratidinamapi prārthayamānā । asatīti bhaṇyatē tataḥ sā nagaralōkēna ॥8॥
tat śrutvā dūyatē hastē sakhībhirlajjatē'dhikam । saubhāgyamārgayitrī sā pūjayati haraballabhādikam ॥9॥
saubhāgyāñjana saubhāgyaguḍikātilakādikaṁ ca viracayati । priyakāridhūpē dhūpayatyātmanō dēham ॥10॥
tathā kāmadēvamantraṁ dhyāyati japati ca tripurāvidyādi । tathāpi hyudvējanīyā jāyatē sā puruṣavargasya ॥ 11 ॥
ādīṇa pitarau tasyāḥ pr̥cchatō divyadaivajñam । naimittikamapi darśayatastathā ca bahumantravādibhyaḥ ॥ 12 ॥
kuladēvatānāṁ pūjāṁ tathā vividhōpayācitānīcchataḥ । dēvasnapanādibhiḥ snātastathaiauṣadhībhirapi ॥ 13॥

supāsanāha - cariśrasmi-
jaṁ kiṁpi kavi sāhai tajjaṇayāī kuṇaṁti taṁ savvaṁ । taṁtagayē maṁtagayaṁ paraṁ davvakkhayaṁ kāuṁ || 14 ||
tahavi hu diṭṭhī na ramai narāṇa navajuvvaṇāṇavi kayāvi । taddēhē bhamarāṇava sukusumiē kiyavarṇāmi ||
aha pattā tammi purē guruṇō caunāṇiṇō kayāvi taō । sō sōmacaṁda siṭṭhī duhiyāē saṁjuō gaṁtuṁ ॥
vaṁdai gurubhattīē payakamalaṁ tassa sūriṇō samaē । pucchara kiṁ maha duhiyaṁ pariṇēuṁ nēcchaē kōvi ? |
bhaṇai gurū puvvakaryaṁ kammaṁ ēīē saṁpayamunaṁ । siṭṭī bhai kahaṁ piva tō sūrī sāhaē ēvaṁ ||18|
puramatthi puiṭhāṇaṁ ghaṇajaō nāma tattha naranāhō । trimalō nāmēṇa vaṇī vissuō sai tabbhajjā |
dhaṇasirināmā savvaṁgasuṁdarī sīlasāliṇī kulayā । suviṇīyā ya sulajjā miu appasubhāsirī saralā ||
paṁcapayāra bhaē tīē samaṁ bhuṁjaē vimalasiṭṭī । taṇayābhāvō sallai duṇhaṁpi hu bhāi taha vimalō ||21||
kō nāma guṇamaraṭṭō sōhaggamaḍappharō ya kō tāsi । kā vā suhāsiyā kāmiṇīṇa jāsiṁ suō natthi ॥
tō dhaṇasirīē bhaṇiyaṁ piyayama ! pariṇēsu kaṁpi kulajāyaṁ । jāyaṁ tīē jaṛa kahavi jāyaē punnajōgēṇa ||
vimalēṇaṁ tō bhaṇiyaṁ puttrēṇavi amha tēṇa na hu kajjaṁ । tuha uyarasarē haṁsō kīliuṁ jō na avayarihī ||
tō
bhaṇai piyā piyayama ! mā mā jaṁpēsu ērisaṁ vayaṇaṁ । davvassa rakkhaṇaṭṭā kicca ciya ēyamaviyappaṁ ॥
tō tīē vayaṇa siriṣpahā nāma pavarakulakannā | pariṇīyā vimalēṇaṁ pālai taṁ sā niyayaṁtra ||26||
tō kama sā pattā jōvvaṇamaha annayā dhaṇasirīē । kiṁpi kuṇaṁtī kammaṁ nivāriyā sacchahiyayāē ||
kiṁbahunā,
yatkimapi kō'pi kathayati tajjananījanakau kurutastatsarvam । tantragataṁ mantragataṁ pracuraṁ dravyakṣayaṁ kr̥tvā ॥ 14 ॥
tathāpi hi dr̥ṣṭirna ramatē narāṇāṁ navayauvanānāmapi kadāpi । taddēhē bhramarāṇāmiva sukusumitē kiṁśukavanē ॥ 15॥
atha prāptāstasminpurē guravaścaturjñānāḥ kadāpi tataḥ । sa sōmacandra śrēṣṭhī duhitrā saṁyutō gatvā ॥ 16 ॥
vandatē gurubhaktyā padakamalaṁ tasya sūrēḥ samayē । pr̥cchati kiṁ mama duhitaraṁ pariṇētuṁ nēcchati kō'pi ? || 17 ||
bhaṇati guruḥ pūrvakr̥taṁ karmaitasyāḥ sāṁpratamudīrṇam । śrēṣṭhī bhaṇati kathamiva tataḥ sūriḥ kathayatyēvam ॥18॥
puramasti pr̥thivīsthānaṁ dhanañjayō nāma taṁtra naranāthaḥ । vimalō nāmnā vaṇig viśrutō vasati tadbhāryā ॥
dhanaśrīnāmā sarvāṅgasundarī śīlaśālinī kulajā । suvinītā ca sulajjā mr̥dvalpasubhāṣitrī saralā || 20॥
pañcaprakārabhōgāṁstayā samaṁ muṅktē vimalaśrēṣṭhī । tanayābhāvaḥ śalyati dvayōrapi hi bhaṇati tathā vimalaḥ ||21||
kō nāma guṇagarvaḥ saubhāgyagarvaśva kastāsām । kā vā sukhāsikā kāminīnāṁ yāsāṁ sutō nāsti ॥22॥
tatō dhanaśriyā bhaṇitaṁ priyatama ! pariṇaya kāmapi kulajātām । jātaṁ tasyāṁ yadi kathamapi jāyatē puṇyayōgēna ॥
vimalēna tatō bhaṇitaṁ putrēṇāpi mama tēna na hi kāryam । tavōdarasarasi haṁsaḥ krīḍituṁ yō nāvatarīṣyati ||24||
tatō bhaṇati priyā priyatama ! mā mā jalpēdr̥śaṁ vacanam । dravyasya rakṣaṇārthaṁ kr̥tyamēvaitadavikalpam ॥25॥
tatastasyā vacanēna śrīprabhā nāma pravarakulakanyā । pariṇītā vimalēna pālayati tāṁ sā nijasutāmiva ॥ 26 ॥
tataḥ kramaśaḥ sā prāptā yauvanamathānyadā dhanaśriyā । kimapi kurvatī karma nivāritā svacchahr̥dayayā ॥27॥

tō kuviyā sā jaṁpara taṁciya ēkkā viyāṇasē savvaṁ । annō na kōvi jāṇai kiṁcivi suviyakkhaṇā tamhā ||
savvaṁ kuṇasu sayaṁ ciya gihakammaṁ majjha puṇa samāēsaṁ । mā dēsu ayāṇuyāē kaiyāvi hu pavvadivasēvi ||
iya nicaṁpi paōsaṁ taduvari sā vaha, vimalasiṭṭīvi । vārai sirippahaṁ, sā tahavi na viramēi kuddhamaī |
pihuōyaraē tattō ghariyā vimalēṇa tahavi īsāē । bīhijjai jai vimalō saṁbhāsai dhaṇasiri kahavi ॥
pavtrāiyā ya ēgā ahannayā gēhamāgayā saṁtī । tīi phalaphulavatthāiēhiṁ sā raṁjiā vāḍhaṁ ||32||
tō tīē sā bhaṇiyā kajjaṁ sāhēsu majjha dussajjha । jaṁ kiṁci tujjha ruiyaṁ vacchē! aviyappaō jēṇa ॥
uccāraṇathaṁbhaṇamōhaṇāi savvaṁpi maha karagayaṁva । tō siripahā payaṁpai taṁ mōtu natthi bhuvaṇēvi ||34||
kōvi samatthō annō dīṇāṇaṁ vacchalō chaliyakālō । tā maha kāuṁ pasāyaṁ savattidukkha khayaṁ nēsu || 35 ॥
paccāiyāē bhaṇiyaṁ tuhicchiyaṁ vacchi ! nicchiyaṁ kāhaṁ । kiṁpuṇa viṇā sahāyaṁ na sijjhaē kiṁpitā davvaṁ ॥
dēsu tumaṁ tajjōgaṁ tīra davvaṁpi kiṁpi sē dinaṁ । kajjasiddhīē pūyaṁ tujjha karissāmi bhaṇiyā ya ||37||
tō tarigāu pavvāiyāvi punnāliyāē gēhammi । gaṁtūṇaṁ tīē samaṁ patthuyakajjammi jē kiccaṁ ॥ 38॥
taṁ maṁtara aha vimalē pahē vayaṁtammi sō jahā muṇai । punnāliyā tahacciya pucchai pavvāiyaṁ ēvaṁ ||39||
jaha kattha tumaṁ caliyā sā pabhaṇai dhaṇasirīē paḍhaviyā । gacchissaṁ dhaṇagēhē dūīkajjēṇa jēṇa dhaṇō ॥
kasaṁya bhaṁsā rōsēṇa gihammi ajja nō pattō । tā mā kuṇavakkhēvaṁ sigdhaṁ ciya tattha gacchissaṁ ॥
jāva na dhaṇasiribhattā samēi vimalō niyammi gēhammi । tāva ghaṇaghaṇasirīṇaṁ saṁjōyamahaṁ karistāmi ||
tataḥ kupitā sā jalpati tvamēvaikā vijānīṣē sarvam । anyō na kō'pi jānāti kiñcidapi suvicakṣaṇā tasmāt ॥
sarva kuru svayamēva gr̥hakarma mama punaḥ samādēśam । mā dēājñāyikāyāḥ kadāpi hi parvadivasē'pi ॥ 29 ॥
iti nityamapi pradvēṣaṁ tadupari sā vahati, vimalaśrēṣṭhyapi । vārayati śrīprabhāṁ sā tathāpi na viramati kruddhamatiḥ ॥
pr̥thagapavara kē tatō dhr̥tā
vimalēna tathāpīrṣyayā । bādhyatē yadi vimalaḥ saṁbhāṣatē dhanaśriyaṁ kathamapi ॥31॥
pravrājikā caikāthānyadā gēhamāgatā satī । tathā phalapuṣpavastrādikaiḥ sā rañjitā bāḍham ||32||
tatastayā sā bhaṇitā kārya kathaya mama duḥsādham । yatkiñcittava rucitaṁ vatsē ! avikalpatō yēna ||33||
uccāṭanastambhanamōhanādi sarvaṁ mama karagatamiva । tataḥ śrīprabhā prajalpati tvāṁ muktvā nāsti bhuvanē'pi ॥34॥
kō'pi samarthō'nyō dīnānāṁ vatsalaśchalitakālaḥ । tasmānmayi kr̥tvā prasādaṁ sapatnīduḥkhaṁ kṣayaṁ naya ॥35॥
pravrājikayā bhaṇitaṁ tavēpsitaṁ vatsē ! niściṁta kariṣyē । kintu vinā sahāyaṁ na sidhyati kimapi tasmād dravyam ॥
dēhi tvaṁ tadyōgyaṁ tayā dravyamapi kimapi tasyai dattam । kāryasiddhau pūjāṁ tava kariṣyāmi bhaṇitā ca ॥ 37॥
tatastadgr̥hāt pratrājikāpyasatyā gēhē । gatvā tathā samaṁ prastutakāryē yat kr̥tyam ||38|
tanmantrayatyatha vimalē pathi vrajati sa yathā jānāti । asatī tathaiva pr̥cchati pravrājikāmēvam ॥39॥
yathā kutra tvaṁ calitā sā prabhaṇati ghanaśriyā prasthāpitā । gamiṣyāmi dhanagēhē dūtīkāryēṇa yēna dhanaḥ ॥ 40 ॥
kr̥tasaṁkētabhraṁśād rōṣēṇa gr̥hē'dya nō prāptaḥ । tasmād mā kurvavakṣēpaṁ śīghramēva tatra gamiṣyāmi ॥41॥

।
simasahāvō mayaṇō simasahāvāu mahiliyāōvi । gururāgaṁdhapaṇāō krimakajjaṁ jaṁ na kuvvaṁti ? |

uttamakulōvajāyā mahilā pāyēṁ aṇuttamē ramai । kulasēlayāvi sariyā nūṇaṁ nīyayaramaṇusarai ||49॥
tājā kulē kalaṁka nō paḍai tāva pēiē ēyaṁ । pēsēmi dhaṇasiriṁ iya paribhāvatō siṁhaṁ pattō ॥ 50 ॥
patthāvē bhai piē ! maha vr̥ttaṁ kuṇasi, bhaṇai tō sāvi । kiṁ pāṇēsa ! mamaṁ paṛa ajja tuma ērisaṁ vayasi ? ।।

athavā |

muñcanti sānurāgaṁ kāṅkṣanti sadbhāva snēhaparihīṇam । guṇamapi jānanti dōṣaṁ kāmagrahamōhitā vāmāḥ || 47||
rūpaṁ kulaṁ kalā parākramaḥ saṁpadapi na pramāṇam । sō'nyaḥ kō'pi guṇō yataḥ prēma pravistr̥ṇōti ॥ 48 ॥

prastāvē bhaṇati priyē ! mamōktaṁ karōṣi bhaṇati tataḥ sāpi । kiṁ prāṇēśa ! māṁ pratyadya tvamīdr̥śaṁ vadasi ? ||11|

tataḥ sā'śrutapūrvaṁ vacanaṁ śrutvā tatkṣaṇa ēva । patitā gharaṇyāṁ ladhvanuṣiktā śatilajalēna ॥53॥

iyasō ta
sōmakahā |
hāvi tasalaṁghaṇīyavaṇō si । tō tuha āēsōciya iha atthē maha pamāṇati ।
tēti satyō gavēsiō iti । vāhaṇasahāyasarimā visajiyā bhaṇivisā ēvaṁ ॥
maha āṇāē punaravi āgaṁkavaṁ taē iha vahā ya । bhaṇiyā sahāipuriyā isīē piugharavārāō ||58 ||
lihitō taṁ suṇiūṇa tī bahurunnaṁ । taha citiyaṁ ca ēvaṁ maēvaraddhaṁ kimani mannē || 59 ॥
annaha kimēvamēsō jaṁpara kaiyāvi niṭhuraṁ vayaṇaṁ । kiṁtu na sarēmi kiṁcivi avarāhaṁ ā vivāhāō ||
iya vinaṁtī pattā satthēṇa samaṁ sajaṇayanayarammi । tattō sahāiṇōviya baliyā sā puṇa gayā gēhē ॥ 61 ॥
taṁ daddhuṁ jaṇayāī rahiyaṁ sahiyājaṇēhiṁ kasiṇamuhi । rōyaṁti sahasacciya harisavisāēhi gahiyāī ॥ 62 ॥
cititi hākimēlā ēgā viṣaṇummaṇā vigayatēyā । sasurakulāō pattā amha suyā iya akaṁḍēvi ? |
tō nēhabharāī taṁ pariraṁbhaṁti tāī aha sāvi । aśmaṁtubhariyahiyayā ahiyayaraṁ rōviḍaṁ laggā || 34 ॥
āsa siyā piūrhi puṭṭāē sāhiyaṁ jahāvittaṁ । taṁ sōūṇaṁ tāīvi ciṁtaṁti imaṁ sadukhāī || 65 ||
kiṁ sōpaī viratō kiṁvā ēsā kulāṇa maliṇayarī । kiṁvā divōgō unnamaha aṁtarāīyaṁ ? ||
aba sakkkīē imīē uvari uttāriō paī hōjjā । kiṁ vā ēīēvi hu saṁpai punnakkhaō jāō ? ||
icāra citiūṇaṁ duhiyā duhē jāṇaṇaṭṭāē । kuladēvayāē pūyā jaṇaēṇa viraiyā rāō || 68 ||
tappuraō paṇihāṇaṁ kārḍa suttō ya dharaṇivapi । tō paccakkhīhōuṁ pacchimajāmammi sō tīē ||69 ||

1
tatō maṇitamidaṁ tēnāsti priyē ! kāraṇamihādēśē । tasmātkuru tamēkavāraṁ tataḥ prabhaṇati dhanaśrīrēvam ॥ 15 ॥
yadyapi śakyamētattathāpi tvamalaṅghanīyavacanō'si । tatastavādēśa ēvēhārthē mama pramāṇamiti ॥ 56 ॥
iti śrutvā tadvacanaṁ tēnāpi sārthō gavēṣitō jhaṭiti | vāhana sahāyasadr̥śī visarjitā bhaṇitvā saivam ||17||
mamājñayā punarapyāgantavyaṁ tvayēha tathā ca । bhaṇitāḥ sahāyapuruṣā asyāḥ pitr̥gr̥hadvārāt ||17||
valitatryamabhuktaistatastat śrutvā tayā bahu ruditam । tathā cintitaṁ caitanmayāparāddhaṁ kimapi manyē ॥ 59 ॥
anyathā kimēvamēṣa jalati kadāpi niṣṭhuraṁ vacanam । kintu na smarāmi kañcidapyaparādhamā vivāhāt ॥60॥
iti cintayantī prāptā sārthēna samaṁ svajanakanagarē । tataḥ sahāyā api ca calitāḥ sā punargatā gēhē ॥ 61 ॥
dr̥ṣṭrā pitarau rahitāṁ sakhījanaiḥ kr̥ṣṇagukhīm । rudatīṁ sahasaiva harṣaviṣādābhyāṁ gr̥hītō ॥ 62 ॥
cintayatō hā kimēṣaikā vimanaunmanā vigatatējāḥ । śvaśurakulātprāptā'smatsutētyakāṇḍē'pi ॥ 63 ॥
tataḥ snēhanirbharau tāṁ parirabhātē tāvatha sāpi । atimantubhr̥tahr̥dayā'dhikataraṁ rōdituṁ lagnā ||64 ||
āśvāsitā pitr̥bhyāṁ pr̥ṣṭyā kathitaṁ yathāvr̥ttam । tat śrutvā tāvapi cintayata idaṁ saduḥkhau ||65 ||
kiṁ sa patirviraktaḥ kiṁ vaiṣā kulayōrmalinakarī । kiṁ vā daivaprayōga udīrṇamathāntarāyikam ॥ 66 ॥
athavā sapatnyā ahyā uparyuttāritaḥ patirbhavēt । kiṁ vaitasyā api hi saṁprati puṇyakṣayō jātaḥ 1 ॥ 67 ॥
।
ityādi cintayitvā duhitr̥duḥkhahētujñānārtham । kuladēvatāyāḥ pūjā janakēna viracitā rātrau ||68 ||
tatpurataḥ praṇidhānaṁ kr̥tvā sutaśca dharaṇīpaṭṭē । tataḥ pratyakṣībhūya paścimayāmē sa tayā ॥ 69 ॥

bhaṇiō siṭṭī jaṛa dhaṇasirīē thēōvi natthi iha dōsō । ēsā mahāsaī khalu navacaṁdakalavya vimalaguṇā ||
kiṁtu savakkī paricāriyāē pavvāiyāya kavaḍēna । aliyakalaṁka mimīē mammi suṇāviō vimalō ।। 71 ।
saṁjāyāsaṁkēṇaṁ kulalaṁchaṇabhīruṇāvi tēṇāvi । paṭṭaviyā iha ēsā tā mā khēyaṁ samuvvahasu || 72 ||
kaivapadiṇāṇa majjhē vimalō ēhī sayaṁ imaṁ naihī । iya kahiuṁ kuladēvī sahāṇaṁ paḍigayā, ittō ॥ 73 ॥
siṭṭīvi pahāē dhaṇasirīē sāhēi rayaṇivr̥ttataṁ । isīsinivyuyamaṇā tō sāvi hu gamai kavi diṇē ||
aha bhikkhāpariyāē samāgayaṁ ajjiyāṇa saṁghārḍa | piugēhē daṭṭūṇaṁ vaṁdai sā bhattibharakaliyā || 75 ||
paḍilāi ya bhattīē bhattapāṇāiṇā sabahumāṇaṁ । pucchara basahiṁ tāō tīē sāhaṁti amuttha ||76 ||
tō muttuttarakālē gaṁtuṁ vasahīē vaṁdara gaṇiṇi । sīlamaī nāmēṇaṁ sapariaṇaṁ tīē pāsamma ||77 ||
uvaviṭṭhā bhūvīḍhē pucchara dhambhaṁ parēṇa viṇaṇa । tīē kahiō sambhaṁ kasāyavisayāṇa ya vivāgō || 78 ॥
taha abhakkhāṇaphalaṁ iṁdiyasaṁvaraṇamāiyaṁ ca tahā । nimmalasammattaguṇā taha micchattassa dōsāvi ॥ 79 ॥
iya nisuṇiūṇa sahasā ullasiyaṁ jīvavīriyaṁ tīē । pattaṁ auvvakaraṇaṁ bhinnō kammaṭṭagaṁṭhīvi ॥80॥
paḍivō jidhammō gahiyāīṇuvvayāī savvāī | vaṁdiya tō ajjāō saṁpattā dhanasirī gēhē ॥ 81 ॥
appāṇaṁ sakayatthaṁ mannatī suddhadhammalābhēṇaṁ । vihuṇiyapiyavirahaduhā gayaṁpi kālaṁ na yāi ॥ 82 ॥
itaśca ।
aha annadi kavi hu sirippahā vimalabhāriyā sahasā । gahiyā mahājarēṇaṁ jhijjara niścapi dēhēṇa ||
bhaṇitaḥ śrēṣṭhī yathā dhanaśriyāḥ stōkō'pi nāstīha dōṣaḥ । ēṣā mahāsatī khalu navacandrakalēva vimalaguṇā ॥ 70 ॥
kintu sapatnīparicārikayā pravrājikayā kapaṭēna । alīkakalaṅkamasyā mārgē śrāvitō vimalaḥ ॥ 71 ॥
saṁjātāśaṅkēna kulalāñchanīruṇāpi tēnāpi । prasthāpitēhaiṣā tasmād mā khēdaṁ samudraha ॥ 72 ॥
katipayadinānāṁ madhyē vimala ēṣyati svayamimāṁ nēṣyati । iti kathayitvā kuladēvī svasthānaṁ pratigatā, itaḥ ॥
śrēṣṭhyapi prabhātē dhanaśriyai kathayati rajanivr̥ttāntam । īṣadaṣannirvr̥tamanāstataḥ sāpi hiṁgamayati katyapi dinān ॥
atha bhikṣāparyāyē samāgatamārthikayōryugmam । pitr̥gēhē dr̥ṣṭvā vadantē sā bhaktibharakalitā ॥75॥
pratilambhayati ca bhaktyā bhaktapānādinā sabahumānam । pr̥cchati vasatiṁ tē tasyāḥ kathayatō'mutra || 76 ॥
tatō bhuktōttarakālē gatvā vasatau vandatē gaṇinīm । śīlamatīṁ nāmnā saparijanāṁ tasyāḥ pārśvē ॥ 77 ॥
upaviṣṭā bhūpīṭhē pr̥cchati dharmē parēṇa vinayēna । tayā kathitaḥ samyak kaṣāyaviṣayāṇāṁ vipākaḥ ॥78॥
tathābhyākhyānaphalamindriyasaṁvaraṇādikaṁ ca tathā । nirmalasamyaktvaguṇāstathā mithyātvasya dōṣā api ॥79॥
iti śrutvā sahasōllasitaṁ jīvavīrya tasyāḥ । prāptamapūrvakaraṇaṁ bhinnaḥ karmāṣṭakagranthirapi ॥80॥
pratipannō jinadharmō gr̥hītānyaṇuvratāni sarvāṇi । vanditvā tata āryāḥ saṁprāptā dhanaśrī ॥81॥
ātmānaṁ svakr̥tārtha manyamānā śuddhadharmalābhēna । vidhutapriyavirahaduḥkhā gatamapi kālaṁ na jānāti ॥ 82॥
athānyadinē kathamapi hi śrīprabhā vimalabhāryā sahasā । gr̥hītā mahājvarēṇa kṣīyatē nityamapi dēhēna ||83॥

dhamadhama siraṁ dhaṇiyaṁ jāyai sūlaṁpi bhajjaē piṭṭhī | vāṇagaṁ gasiyaṁ khijjai vāṇīvi vayaṇami ||84||
pabalīhavēi sāsō gāḍhaṁ pīḍēi tīē maharōgō । āhūyā vimalēṇaṁ vijjā maṁtannuṇō tattō ॥ 85 ॥
paccakhāyā tēhivitō tīē vimalasamuhaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ । na hu jīvistāmi ahaṁ tō maṁ millēha bhūmīē ॥ 86 ॥
hakāra sayaṇajaṇaṁ khāmēmō jēṇa tēṇa taha kāuṁ । bhaṇiyā sā taṁ saṁpai nidaha kammāī asuhāī || 87||
tīē bhaṇiyaṁ piyayama ! kayāī bahuyāī pāvakammāī । kiṁpuṇa nigviṇakammaṁ maē mahaṁta kathaṁ ēkkaṁ ॥ 88 ॥
nivbhagga sēharāē mōhaggahagahiyagāḍhahiyayāē । avivēyataraliyāē rādhāē nihīṇā ॥89॥
itthiyaṇasulahaīsāgasiyāē tayā alīyamavi ālaṁ । pavvāiyāmuhēṇaṁ mahāsaīē dhaṇasirīē ॥ 90 ॥
uttamakulajāyāē uttamasattāē khatijuttāē । sasilēhāē iva nikkalaṁkamaṇavayaṇakāyāē ॥ 91 ॥
pīīvicchēyatthaṁ tujjha sayā tayaṇurattacittassa । ārōviyaṁ maē jaṁ taṁ ajjavi sallaē hiyaē || 92 ||
iya sōūṇaṁ vimalō pacchattāvēṇa citaē haddhī । maha kannaḍubbalattaṁ akajjakāritayaṁ taha ya ॥ 93 ॥
ahaha ! avivēyapasarō haddhī taha majjha bhāgadhijjāṇa । taha majjha nīikōsallayā ya khīṇacciya iyāṇi ॥
jēṇa aṇajjēṇa maē taiyā pavvāiyākayapabaṁdhaṁ । sōūṇaṁ sahasacciya paṭṭaviyā kulaharaṁ daiyā ||95 ||
tā ajjavi maha nūṇaṁ kiṁcivi punnassa vilasiyē asthi । jaṁ kahiō ēīē sabbhāvō maraṇakālēvi ॥96॥
iya citiūṇa sigdhaṁ dhaṇasiripēīharammi saṁcaliō । tīsē āṇayaṇatthaṁ vimalō pattō ya sipi ॥ 97||
kayaciyapaḍivattī sasurāīṇaṁ taō dhanasirīē । puṭṭhō rahampi kusala jaṁpara vimalō samannubharaṁ ॥ 98 ॥
ghamaghamati śirō gāḍhaṁ jāyatē śūlamapi bhajyatē pr̥ṣṭham । vātēnāṅgaṁ grastaṁ kṣīyatē vāṇyapi vadanē ॥84॥
prabalībhavati śvāsō gāḍhaṁ pīḍayati tāṁ mahārōgaḥ । āhūtā vimalēna vaidyā mantrajñāstataḥ ॥85॥
pratyākhyātā tairapi tatastayā vimalasaṁmukhaṁ bhaṇitam । na khalu jīviṣyāmyahaṁ tatō māṁ muñcata bhūmau ॥ 86 ॥
hakkārayata svajanajanaṁ kṣamayāmō yēna, tēna tathā kr̥tvā । bhaṇitā sā tvaṁ saṁprati ninda karmāṇyaśubhāni ॥ 87 ॥
tayā bhaṇitaṁ priyatama ! kr̥tāni bahūni pāpakarmāṇi । kintu nirghuṇakarma mayā mahat kr̥tamēkam ||88||
nirbhāgyaśēkharayā mōhagrahagr̥hatigāḍhahr̥dayayā । avivēkataralitayā rāgāndhayā nihīnayā ॥ 89 ॥
strījanasulabhērṣyāgrastayā tadā'līkamapyālam । pratrājikāmukhēna mahāsatyā dhanaśriyāḥ ॥90॥
uttamakulajātāyā uttamasattvāyāḥ kṣāntiyuktāyāḥ । śaśilēkhāyā iva niṣkalaṅkamanōvacanakāyāyāḥ ॥ 91 ॥
prītivicchēdārthaṁ tava sadā tadanuraktacittasya । ārōpitaṁ mayā yattadadyāpi śalyati hr̥dayē ॥ 92 ॥
iti śrutvā vimalaḥ paścāttāpēna cintayati hā dhik । mama karṇadurbalatvamakāryakāritvaṁ tathā ca ॥93॥
ahaha ! avivēkaprasarō hā viktathā mama bhāgadhēyāni । tathā mama nītikuśalatā ca kṣīṇaivēdānīm ॥94॥
yēnānāryēṇa mayā tadā pratrājikākr̥taprabandham । śrutvā sahasaiva prasthāpitā kulagr̥haṁ dayitā ॥ 95||
tasmādadyāpi mama nūnaṁ kiñcidapi puṇyasya vilasitamasti । yatkathita ētayā sadbhāvō maraṇakālē'pi ॥96॥
iti cintayitvā śīghraṁ dhanaśrī paitr̥kagr̥hē saṁcalitaḥ । tasyā ānayanārthaṁ vimalaḥ prāptaśca śīghramapi ॥97॥

supāsanāhacariyammi-
kimattakāriṇō majjha muddhē ! kusalēṇa pucciēṇāvi । sā bhāi sāmi ! ēvaṁ mā jaṁpasu natthi tuha dōsō ||
putanimittaṁ atyassa lōbhaō pāvapagaṇayaṁtīē । pariṇāviō maē taṁ jaṁ tassa viyaṁbhiyaṁ ēyaṁ ॥ 100 ॥
tō vayaṁ aparaṁ mannunivbharattāō । bāhullalōyaṇō sō tīsēmimuhaṁ bhai ēvaṁ ॥ 101 ॥
bhadaṁ sajjaṇacaṁdaṇatarūṇa savyaṁga saṁgacaṁgāṇa | ujjhatāṇavi jēsi gaṁdhō bhavaṇaṁ suhāvēi ॥ 102 ॥
avayārasayāṇivi pasaṁti tayaṁpi nēya uvayāraṁ । sucahiyyā sahiyayā va haṁdi supaṇā na nijjaṁ tē ।।
niyakulakusumiyaṁkē sacchē sacchi ! tahiṇāravya । aṇubhūyaṁ suhamasuhaṁ jaṁ taṁ maha kahasu kisiyēgi ! |
tō sā sāha savvaṁ gahivaralaṁbhamāīyaṁ tassa । sō bhaṇai majjhavi imaṁ dāvasu sugurūṇa pāsāu || 105 ॥
tō pāsa gaṇiṇīguruvimalasūripāsampi । nēvi samapi vimalaṁ vaṁdāvara tāṇa payaparamē ॥ 106॥
suṇai khaṇaṁ jiṇavaṇaṁ tattō vibhava dhaṇasirī sūriṁ । pahu ! viparasu maha paiṇō gimmiṁ tēhi taha vihiyē ।।
aha sō sapiō caliō pattō sapurē sirippahaṁ niyaī । jīvati niruyaṁga tō taṁ paṛa jaṁpaē ēvaṁ || 108॥
jaha tujjha vayaṁ savvaṁ pūrissaṁ piugihē ṭhiyāēvi । tō tattha tu vacca iya sōnaṁ ghaṇasirī bhagai ॥ 109 ॥
pāsu laggiūṇaṁ jaha maha bhaiṇī imā maha gidēvi । ciṭṭiēsai tā kijjaḍa tīē pasāō samāēvi |
ēvaṁ hōutti taō siripahaṁ bhagai dhaṇasirī ēvaṁ | gaṁtūṇa sāhē ! khamāvasu saṁpai taṁ ajjauttati ॥ 111 ॥
tī tava vihiyaṁ vimalavi bhaṇēi khamiyamēva maē । jaṁ khamai tujjha bhaiṇī kiṁtu puṇō iya na kāyavvaṁ ॥
kr̥tōcitapratipattiḥ śvaśurādīnāṁ tatō dhanaśriyā । pr̥ṣṭō rahasi kuśalaṁ jalpati vimala: samanyubharam ॥98॥
kimayuktakāriṇō mama mugdhē ! kuśalēna pr̥ṣṭēnāpi ? | sā bhaṇati svāmin ! ētanmā jalpa nāsti tava dōṣaḥ ॥
putranimittamarthasya lōbhataḥ pāpamagaṇayantyā । pariṇāyitō mayā tvaṁ yattasyā vijr̥mbhitamētat ॥ 100 ॥
tatastadvinayaṁ dr̥ṣṭvā'dhikataraṁ manyunirbharatvāt । bāṣpavallōcanaḥ sa tasyā abhimukhaṁ bhaṇatyēvam ॥ 101 ॥
bhadraṁ sajjanacandratarūṇāṁ sarvāṅgasaṅgaṅgānām । dahyamānānāmapi yēṣāṁ gandhō bhavanaṁ subhāvayati ॥ 102 ॥
apakāraśatānyapi vismaranti tanumapi naivōpakāram । śūnyahr̥dayāḥ mahr̥dayā vā hanta sujanā na jñāyantē ॥
nijakula kumudamr̥gāṅkē svacchē mr̥gaśāvākṣi ! taddinādārabhya। anubhūtaṁ sukhamasukhaṁ yattammāṁ kathaya kr̥śāṅgi ! ॥
tataḥ sā kathayati sarva gr̥hidharmōpalambhādikaṁ tasmai । sa bhaṇati madyamapīmaṁ dāpaya sugurūṇāṁ pārśvāt ॥ 105॥
tataḥ sā prabhātasamayē gaṇinīguruvimalasūripārśvē । nītvā samamapi vimalaṁ vandayati tēṣāṁ padapadmam ॥ 106 ॥
śr̥ṇōti kṣaṇaṁ jinavacanaṁ tatō vijñapayati dhanaśrīḥ sūrim । prabhō ! vitara mama patyē gr̥hidharma taistathā vihitam॥
atha sa sapriyaścalitaḥ prāptaḥ svapurē śrīprabhāṁ paśyati । jīvantīṁ nīrugaṅgīṁ tatastāṁ prati jalpatyēvam ॥ 108 ॥
yathā tava vyayaṁ sarvē pūrayiṣyāmi pitr̥gr̥hē sthitāyā api । tatastatra tvaṁ vrajēti śrutvā dhanaśrarbhiṇati ॥ 109 ॥
pādayōrlagitvā yathā mama bhaginīyaṁ mama gr̥hē'pi । sthāsyati tasmātkriyatāṁ tasyāḥ prasādō mamāpi ॥110॥
ēvaṁ bhavatviti tataḥ śrīprabhāṁ bhaṇati dhanaśrīrēvam । gatvā sakhi ! kṣamaya saṁprati tvamāryaputramiti ॥ 111 ॥
tayā tathaiva vihitaṁ vimalōṁ'pi bhaṇati kṣamitamēva mayā । yatkṣamatē tava bhaginī kintu punariti na kartavyam ॥

tō putravāṇaṁ bhōgē bhuṁjaṁti tāī tuṭṭhāī । aha annadiṇē bhaṇiō sahasā vimalō dhaṇasirīē ॥ 113 ॥
saṁsārō duhasārō khaṇaramaṇīō ya ramaṇīvaggōvi । taḍitaralaṁ tāruṇṇaṁ vibhaṁguraṁ jīvayavvapi ॥ 114 ॥
kiñca ।
daiyaṁ nēhahīṇaṁ sambhāvavivajjiōnna suhisaṁghō । sīlarahiyantra bhajjā kiriyavva sunāṇaguṇarahiyā ||
gaṁdharahiyaṁva kusumaṁ atyavihaṇassa bhōyachan । nayamukkōvva nariṁdō vayaṇaṁtra surayaṇaparicattaṁ ॥ 116 ॥

kiṁtu samapi ēvaṁ kāyavyaṁ suyaṇu ! tā vilaṁsu । thēvadiyahāī jā dēmi niyadhaṇaṁ sattakhittēsu ॥ 119 ॥
bahu manniyammi tīē niyadatraṁ dēvi tēsu ṭhāṇēsu । samagaṁ sirippahāē taha ghaṇasiribhāriyāēva ॥ 120 ॥
sumuhuttē gurumūlē vimalō giṇhai vihīaiṁ pavvajjaṁ । cariūṇa dukkaratavaṁ pajjētē aṇasaṇaṁ kāuṁ ॥ 121 ॥
sāīvi sōhammē uppannāī mahaṭṭiyasurēsu | tāṇa majjhāō cahauṁ sirippahā tujjha iha dhūyā ॥ 122 ॥
puvvadukampabasāō jāyā aiḍubbhagā iha bhavēvi । iya suṇiuṁ sā saṁjāyajāisaraṇā bhaṇai sūri ॥ 123 ॥
jaha kahiyaṁ nāha ! tara hē taṁ dētu majjhatā dikkhaṁ । ummūlēmi samūlaṁ kammataruṁ jēṇa sigyamahaṁ ॥। 124 ||
tō parāṇumayā tīē mūrīvi dēi pavvajjaṁ । siṭṭī ya sōmacaṁdō sāvayadhammaṁ pavajjēi || 125 ||
aiyārāṇa sarūvaṁ savvavayāpi kahai taṁ sūrī । taṁ nāuṁ namiūṇa ya vacai siṭṭī niyagimmi ॥ 126॥
1
tataḥ pūrvapravāhēṇa bhōgān bhuñjatē tē tuṣṭāḥ । athānyadinē bhaṇitaḥ sahasā vimalō dhanaśriyā ॥ 113 ॥
saṁsārō duḥkhasāraḥ kṣaṇaramaṇīyaśca ramaṇīvargō'pi । taḍittaralaṁ tāruṇyaṁ vibhaṅguraṁ jīvitavyamapi ॥ 114 ॥
dayita iva snēhahīnaḥ sadbhāvavivarjita iva suhr̥tsaṁvaḥ । śīlarahitēva bhāryā kriyēva sujñānaguṇarahitā ॥ 115 ॥
gandharahitamiva kusumamarthavihīnasya bhōgavāñchēva । nayamukta iva narēndrō vacanamiva suracanāparityaktam ॥116॥
yathā naiva śōbhatē tathā narajanma saddharmavarjitaṁ subhaga ! | tasmānmāṁ muñcēdānīṁ pravajyāṁ yēna gr̥hṇāmi ॥117॥
iti śrutvā vimalō jalpati rambhōru ! mayā na kadāpi । tavājñāyā bhaṅgaḥ kartavya iti mama pratijñā ॥ 118 ॥
kintu samamapyētatkartavyaṁ sutanu ! tasmādvilambasva । stōkadivasāni yāvaddadāmi nijavanaṁ saptakṣētryām ॥ 119॥
cahu
matē tayā nijadravyaṁ dattvā tēṣu sthānēṣu । samaṁ śrīprabhayā tathā dhanaśrībhāryayāpi ॥120॥
sumuhūrtē gurumūlē vimalō gr̥hṇāti vidhinā pravrajyām । caritvā duṣkaratapaḥ paryantē'naśanaṁ kr̥tvā ॥121॥
sarvē'pi sauva utpannā maharddhikasurēṣu । tēṣāṁ madhyāccyutvā śrīprabhā tavēha duhitā ॥ 122 ॥
pūrva duṣkarmavaśatō jātā'tidurbhagēhabhavē'pi । iti śrutvā sā saṁjātajātismaraṇā bhaṇati sūrim ॥ 123 ॥
yathā kathitaṁ nātha ! tvayā tathaiva taddēōhi mama tāvaddīkṣām | unmūlayāmi samūlaṁ karmataruṁ yēna śatrimaham ॥
tataḥ pitranumatāyai tasyai sūrirapi dadāti pravrajyām । śrēṣṭhī ca sōmacandraḥ śrāvakadharmaṁ prapadyatē ॥ 125 ॥
aticārāṇāṁ svarūpaṁ sarvavratānāmapi kathayati taṁ sūriḥ । tajjñātvā natvā ca vrajati śrēṣṭhī nijagr̥hē ॥ 126 ॥

supāsanāha-caritryammi-
pālai gihatthadhammaṁ jahōvaiṭuṁ ahannayā tēṇa । dēsāvagāsiyavayaṁ paḍivanna ērisa bihiṇā || 127 ||
jaha ajja ma bāhi pōsahasālāu tā na gaṁtavvaṁ । jāva diṇaṁ, tō hiṭṭō diṭṭhō bhittō pahē jaṁtō ॥ 128 ॥
niyajāṇāames kakaramikaṁ khivēṛa tastuvariṁ । sō uṇa tassa na laggō nivamēkaḍamatthaē paḍiō ||
tō sō ghurughurumāṇō pō sahasālāē garuyakōvēṇa । pattō sisiyāsē kharayara naharēhiṁ ullihai || 130 ||
tadēha, sō pukkarai garuyasadēhi taṁ nisāmēuṁ । paccāsannagihāṇaṁ samāgayā sāvayā bahuyā ॥ 131 ॥
diṁḍēhi tēhiṁ sō pagō hakiō gaō vāhi । tō pāriyasāmaiō mahayā kaḍē niyagēhaṁ ॥ 132 ||
pattō tattō himāṇusēhiṁ pakkhāliūṇa taddēhaṁ । ruhirāvilamavilaṁbaṁ vijjā hakkāriyā pavarā ॥ 133 ॥
takkahiyaōsahērdi uvalittaṁ bassa gatamittō ya । māhidajarō jāō paccakkhāō ya vijjēhiṁ ॥ 134॥
tāṇāpaḍikatō jōisiyasurēsa marivi uvavannō । tattō cuō samāṇō sijjhissai taiyajanmammi ||
bhittīgayacittāī nīrāsārēṇa nimmalāīpi । jaha mailijjēti tahā vayāī aiyārakaraṇēṇa || 136 ||
jaha savvasarīragayaṁ visaṁ niraṁbhitta kamāṇaṁti । taha pubbagahiyaniyamē savittharē niti saṁkhēvaṁ ॥ 137॥
tē dhannā kayannā lahukammā jē paikkhaṇaṁ bhavvā । icchāē cchēyaparā savvaca saṁkhiti sayā || 138 ॥
॥ iti pañcamāticārē sōmacandrakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
॥ tatsamāptau dvitīyaṁ śikṣāvataṁ samāptam ॥
pālayati gr̥hasthadharmaṁ yathōpadiṣṭamathānyadā tēna । dēśāvakāśikavataṁ pratipannamīdr̥śaṁ vidhinā ॥ 127 ॥
yathā'dya mayā bahiḥ pauṣadhaśālāyāstāvanna gantavyam । yāvaddinaṁ, tatō hr̥ṣṭaṁ dr̥ṣṭaṁ mittraṁ pathi yāt ॥ 128॥
nijajñāpanahētōḥ karkaramēkaṁ kṣipati tasyōpari । sa punastasya na lagnō nr̥pamarkaṭamastakē patitaḥ ॥ 129 ॥
tataḥ sa ghughurāyamāṇaḥ pauṣadhaśālāyāṁ gurukōpēṇa । prāptaḥ śrēṣṭhisakāśē kharataranakhairairullikhati ॥ 130 ॥
taddēhaṁ sa pūtkarōti guruśabdaistanniśamya । pratyāsannagr̥hēbhyaḥ samāgatāḥ śrāvakā bahavaḥ ॥ 131 ॥
dr̥ḍhadaṇḍaistaiḥ sa plavagō niṣiddhō gatō bahiḥ । tataḥ pāritasāmāyikō mahatā kaṣṭēna nijagēham ॥ 132॥
prāptastatō gr̥hamānuṣaiḥ prakṣālya taddēham । rudhirāvilamavilambaṁ vaidyā hakkāritāḥ pravarāḥ ॥ 133॥
tatkathitauṣavairupaliptaṁ tasya gātramitaśca । māhēndrajvarō jātaḥ pratyākhyātaśca vaidyaiḥ ॥ 134 ॥
tatsthānāpratikrāntō jyautiṣikasurēṣu mr̥tyōpapannaḥ । tataścyutaḥ san sētsyati tr̥tīyajanmani ॥135॥
bhittigatacitrāṇi nīrāsārēṇa nirmalānyapi । yathā malinīkriyantē tathā vratānyaticārakaraṇēna ॥ 136॥
yathā sarvaśarīragataṁ viṣaṁ nirudhya daṁśamānayanti । tathā pūrvagr̥hīta niyamānsavistarānnayanti saṁkṣēpam ॥ 137 ॥
tē dhanyāḥ kr̥tapuṇyā laghukarmāṇō yē pratikṣaṇaṁ bhavyāḥ । icchācchēdaparāḥ sarvavratāni saṁkṣipanti sadā ॥ 138 ॥

āhāradahasakāravabhavāvārapāsahī cauhā । dēsēṇa va savrvvaṇa va kāyavvā bhavvasattā ||1||
pōsahapōsiyasaddhammacāriṇō jē havaṁti daḍhacittā । tē dēvāṇavi pujjā havaṁti jaha malayakēunivō ॥2॥
tathāhi ;
puramatthi atthasāraṁ susalaṁkāra sōhiamuāraṁ । varakavikavvaṁva puraṁ siribhuvaṇaṁ bhuvaṇavivakhāyēṁ ||3||
tattha nivō nayanilaō malaō dālitāvataviyāṇaṁ । sirimalayakēunāmā, bhajjā tassatthi malayamaī ॥
buddhisamubhihāṇō maṁtī tassāvi buddhivalakaliō । nikkhittarajjabhārō tammi nivō lalai līlāē ||
aha annā nariṁdō asthāṇasabhāē ciṭṭaē jāva । tāba akahā gayaṇē duṁduhisadō samucchaliō || 6 ||
tō rāyā taṁ suṇiḍaṁ asthāṇaṭiō sakōuyaṁ jāva | gayaṇaṁgaṇaṁ palōyai tā picchai suragaṇaṁ iṁtaṁ || 7 ||
tampajjhē muṇivasaha pisaṁḍigōraṁ aṇaṁga samaruvaṁ । parivvaṁtaṁ bhattivbharēṇa surakhayaravidēṇa ||8||
tō rāyā saṁbhatō aśuddhivi vinnavē taṁ sāhuṁ । majjhaṇukaṁpaṁ kāuṁ khaṇaṁ samōyaraha pasiūṇa ||9||
tō sāhū tavvayaṇaṁ suṇiuṁ suṇiuṁ guṇaṁ ca tassa taō | avayariō taggēhē surakhayarasamaniō tattō ||
nihatthēṇa rāyā bhāsaṇamuvaṇamēṛa suṇivaraṇō। uvaviddhaṁ tattha muṇi vaṁdai vihiṇā saparivārō ॥11॥
saṁbhāsiūṇa nivaī pāraddhā dhammadēsaṇā muṇiṇā । paḍhamaṁ ciya jaidhammō dasappayārō imō kahiō || 12॥
khaṁtī ya madava ajjava muttī tava saṁjamē ya bōdhavvē । sacaṁ sōyaṁ ākiṁcaṇaṁ ca baṁbhaṁ ca jaidhammō ॥13॥
kāraṇaakāraṇēhi ya kuddhē duvvayaṇabhāsirē haṇirē । uvasaṁtamaṇēṇa parē jaiṇā khaṁtī karēyavvā || 14 ||
āhāradēhasatkārabrahmavyāpārapauṣadhacaturdhā । dēśēna vā sarvēṇa vā kartavyō bhavyasattvaiḥ ॥ 1 ॥

pauṣadhapōṣitasaddharmacāriṇō yē bhavanti dr̥ḍhacittāḥ । tē dēvānāmapi pūjyā bhavanti yathā malayakētunr̥paḥ ||2||
puramastyarthasāraṁ suśabdālaṁkāraśōbhitamudāram । varakavikāvyamiva puraṁ śrībhuvanaṁ muvanavikhyātam ||3||
tatra nr̥pō nayanilayō malayō dāridryatāpataptānām । śrīmalayakētunāmā, bhāryā tasyāsti malayamatī || 4 |
buddhisamudrābhidhānō mantrī tasyāpi buddhibalakalitaḥ । nikṣiptarājyabhārastasminnr̥pō lalati līlayā ॥5॥
athānyadā narēndra āsthānasabhāyāṁ tiṣṭhati yāvat । tāvadakasmād gaganē dundubhiśabdaḥ samucchalitaḥ ॥ 6 ॥
tatō rājā tat śrutvā''sthānasthitaḥ sakautukaṁ yāvat । gaganāṅgaṇaṁ pralōkatē tāvatpaśyati suragaṇamāyantam ||7||
tanmadhyē munivr̥ṣabhaṁ kanakagauramanaṅgasamarūpam । paristūyamānaṁ bhaktibharēṇa surakhacaravr̥ndēna ||8||
tatō rājā saṁbhrāntō'bhyutthāya vijñapayati taṁ sādhum । mayyanukampāṁ kr̥tvā kṣaṇaṁ samavasarata prasadya ॥ 9 ॥
tataḥ sādhustadvacanaṁ śrutvā jñātvā guṇaṁ ca tasya tataḥ । avatīrṇastadvēhē surakhacarasamanvitastataḥ ||10||
nijahastana rājā bhadrāsanamupanayati munipatayē । upaviṣṭaṁ tatra muniṁ vandatē vidhinā saparivāraḥ ॥ 11 ॥
saṁbhāṣya nr̥patiṁ prārabdhā dharmadēśanā muninā । prathamamēva yatidharmō daśaprakārō'yaṁ kathitaḥ ॥ 12 ॥
kṣāntiśca mārdavārjavē muktistapaḥ saṁyamaśca bōddhavyaḥ । satyaṁ śaucamā kiñcanyaṁ ca brahma ca yatidharmaḥ ॥13॥
kāraṇākāraṇābhyāṁ ca kruddhē durvacanabhāṣitari hantari । upaśāntamanasā parē yatinā kṣāntiḥ kartavyā ॥ 14 ॥

supāsanāha-cariṣyasmi-
māṇassa vidhāyakaraṁ iha bhannai maddavaṁ agavyattaṁ । viṣayassa mūlajōṇi taṁ jaṇāvaskāyavvaṁ ॥ 15 ॥
māyā kuḍalasahāvō tappaḍivakvaṁ ca ajjavaṁ nēyaṁ । rijubhāvō hi muṇidō visuddhadhammaṁ samujjiṇa ||
sayaṇacaṇavisaya ubagaraṇadēhamāīsu jō paricāō । sā muttī maṁtavvā apabiṁdhattaṇarurūpā ॥17॥
hōi tō uṇa duvihō bāhirama bhiṁtarō ya tatthavi ya । ēkkikō chabhēō bārasabhēō tavō miliō ||
tathāhi :-
aṇasaṇamūṇōyariyā vittīsaṁkhēvaṇaṁ rasañcāō । kāyakilēsō saṁlīṇayā ya bajjhō tavō hōi ॥ 19 ॥
pāyacchittaṁ viṇaō vēyāvacca tahēva sajjhāō । jhāṇaṁ ussaggōvi ya abhiṁtaraō tavō hōi || 20 ॥
paṁcāsavā viramaṇaṁ paṁcidiyaniggahō kasāyajaō | daṁḍattayassa viraī saṁjamō sattarasabhēō ||21||
avisaṁvāyagavayaṇaṁ kāyamaṇōvayaṇasuddhisaṁjutta । ēyaṁ cauppayāraṁ bhuṇiṇā saccē bhagavaṁ ||22||
davvabhāvabhēyaṁ sōyaṁ duvihaṁ jiṇēhiṁ pannattaṁ । davvamuvagaraṇamāī taggayasōyaṁ karēyabvaṁ ||23||
bhāvē sōyaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ kasāyadōsēhi vajjiyaṁ cittaṁ । paramatthasōyamēyaṁ panataṁ vīrāgēhi ||24||
kīra kāyayassavi massa pakkhālaṇaṁ suhēṇēva । aicikaṇamalalittaṁ duppakkhālē jaō cittaṁ ||25||
saṁtē asaṁtēsu ya vatsu mucchā pariggahō bhaṇiō । tattha nirīhattamaī ākicanaṁ ca nihiṁ ||26||
ōrāliyavēḍabbiyaitthīṇaṁ jō u tivihativihēṇa । paricāō navabhēyaṁ taṁ va vitiṁ jiṇavasahā ||27||
iya dasabhēyaṁ dhammaṁ sammaṁ suvisuddhakaraṇavāvārō । paripālatō vihiṇā sāhū kammakkhayaṁ kuṇai ||28||
mānasya vighātakaramiha bhaṇyatē mārdavamagarvatvam । vinayasya mūlayōnistadyatinā'vaśyakartavyam ॥15॥
māyā kuṭilasvabhāvastatpratipakṣaṁ cārjavaṁ jñēyam । r̥jubhāvō hi munīndrō viśuddhadharma samarjayati ॥ 16 ॥
svajanadhanaviṣayōpakaraṇadēhādiṣu yaḥ parityāgaḥ । sā muktirmantavyā'pratibandhatvasvarūpā ॥17॥
bhavati tapaḥ punardvavidhaṁ bāhyamābhyantaraṁ ca tatrāpi ca । ēkaikaṁ ṣaḍbhēdaṁ dvādaśabhēdaṁ tapō militam ॥ 18 ॥
anaśanamūnādaritā vr̥ttisaṁkṣēpaṇaṁ rasatyāgaḥ । kāyaklēśaḥ saṁlīnatā ca bāhyaṁ tapō bhavati ॥ 19 ॥
prāyaścittaṁ vinayōṁ vaiyāvr̥ttyaṁ tathaiva svādhyāyaḥ । dhyānamupasargō'pi cābhyantaraṁ tapō bhavati ||20|
pañcāśravāda viramaṇaṁ pañcēndriyanigrahaḥ kaṣāyajayaḥ । daṇḍatrayasya viratiḥ saṁyamaḥ saptadaśabhēdaḥ ॥ 21॥
avisaṁvādakavacanaṁ kāyamanōvacanaśuddhisaṁyuktam । ētaccatuṣprakāraṁ muninā satyaṁ bhaṇitavyam ||22||
dravyabhāvaprabhēdaṁ śaucaṁ dvividhaṁ jinaiḥ prajñaptam । dravyamupakaraṇādi tadvataśaucaṁ kartavyam ||23||
bhāva śaucaṁ bhaṇitaṁ kaṣāyadōṣairvarjitaṁ cittam । paramārthaśaucamētat prajñataṁ vītarāgaiḥ ||24||
kriyatē kāyagatasyāpi malasya prakṣālanaṁ sukhanaiva । aticikkaṇamalaliptaṁ duṣprakṣālaṁ yataścittam ॥29॥
satsvasatsu ca vastuṣu mūrcchā parigrahō bhaṇitaḥ । tatra nirīhatvamatirākiñcanyaṁ ca nirdiṣṭam ||26||
audārikavaikriyastrīṇāṁ yastu trividhatrividhēnaṁ । parityāgō navabhēdaṁ tad brahma bruvanti jinavr̥ṣabhāḥ ||27||
iti daśabhēdaṁ dharma samyak suviśuddhakaraṇavyāpāraḥ । paripālayan vidhinā sādhuḥ karmakṣayaṁ karōti ॥ 28 ॥

tō bhaṇiyaṁ naravaraṇā asamatyō hē muṇida ! muṇidhammē । tō sāhasa gimmiṁ sammaṁ yaha nāha ! pasiūṇa ||
tō muṇiṇā sē kahiō sammattāī duvālasavihōvi । dhammō sō paḍivō amacasahiēṇa tēṇāvi ||30||
sāhūvi tamaṇujāṇiva surakhayarasabhāē saṁgaō paraō। pagaēṇaṁ kajjēṇaṁ, rāyā jimmaraō ||31||
kālaṁ gamēi kaiyā rayaṇīē pōsahaṁ kuṇai vihiṇā । rāyā saṁtīvi naridabhuvaṇabhāgammi, tāṇaṁ ca ||32||
dhammaviyā parāṇaṁ bōlaṇaṁ jāmiṇīē jāmadugaṁ । nidāē aṇitīē rannā tō paryāṇiō maṁtī ||33||
kahasu apuvvaka mēṁ vimhayarasa saṁgayaṁti tayabhimuhaṁ । bhaṇai sacivōvi nisuṇasu avahiyacittō nariṁda ! tumaṁ ॥
asthi iha bharahavāsē vāsavanayaraṁva vivahasayakaliyaṁ । nāmēṇa gharātilayaṁ taṁ pālai bhuvanapālaniyō ||
amaraguruvisasahiō ahannayā jā nivō vayai bāhi । tō picchakammi gimmi migaṁ baṁdhubharaṇīṇaṁ ।।
ētaṁ kiṁpi taṁ ca daṇa । na imaṁ suṁdaramii kahivi amaraguruṇō nitrō jāi ||37||
jā tāva vivaṇimajjhē piccha macchaṁ hasaṁtayaṁ taliyaṁ । vikaṇaṇatthaṁ kēṇāvi āṇīyaṁ dhīvaranarēṇa ||38||
taṁ daṭhṭhē mahīvālō cita tiriōṣi vigayajīdōvi । acchariyaṁ jaṁ ēsō hasai taō pucchaē vijasaṁ ।।
amaraguruṁ kiṁ kāraṇamēsō iya hasai dahi amhē । niyapannāē nāum̐ sāhaha maha iti kiṁ bahuṇā ? ||
anna na ittha vāsō tuhatthi, viusōvi tō imaṁ bhaṇai । maha dēsu māsamēgaṁ avahīē, nivōvi taha kuṇai ॥
gaṁtuṁ tō sōcihna niyagihammi citāurō na bhuṁjēi । na ya suyaī rayaṇīē kahamēyaṁ mē muṇēyavvaṁ ||42 ||
iya ciṁti nisare frohai avasōiyaṁ tarhi sadaṁ । lahai imaṁ jaha uttara disā taṁ muṇihisi iti ॥

1
taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā mahīpālaścintayati tiryaṅṅapi vigatajīvō'pi । āścarya yadēṣa hasati tataḥ pr̥cchati vidvāṁsam ||39||
amaraguruṁ kiṁ kāraṇamēṣa iti hasati dr̥ṣṭrēhāsmān । nijaprajñayā jñātvā kathaya māṁ jhaṭiti kiṁ bahunā ? ॥40॥
anyathā nātra vāsastava syāt, vidvānapi tata idaṁ bhaṇati । mama dēhi māsamēkamavadhau nr̥pō'pi tathā karōti ॥
gatvā tataḥ sō'pi hi nijagr̥hē cintāturō na bhuṅktē । naca svapiti rajanyāṁ kathamētanmayā jñātavyam ॥42॥

610
supāsanāha- cāraāmma-
ya
tō sō draṇamēva saṁbadi patōi tarhi tattō । miliō maggē ēgō uttaradisi māhaṇō tahasa ||44||
amaraguruṇā sa puḍhō gaṁtav kattha māhaṇa ! kahēsu । sō bhaṇai amugagāmasmi jēṇāhaṁ tattha vatthavō ॥
tēvi puṭṭhō viusō sāhasa tumaēvi kattha gaṁtavvaṁ ? । pabhaṇai viusō tuhagāmasīmaparaōvi gaṁtavvaṁ ॥ 46 ॥
jaṛa ēvaṁ tō lahaṁ jāō satthā parōparaṁ amha । iya jaṁpatā pattā saritīrē tō ya viusēṇa || 47 ||
puvyamuttāriyāōṁ vāṇahāō pasu ṭhadiyāō । tāō caraṇārhitō duiēṇa karēṇa dhariyāō ||48 ||
tō iyarō ciṁtēī sōvi jaṇō jalaṁ vigāhitō ! uttārai gamaṇīō caraṇāhitō, kahamimēṇa || 49||
vivarīyaṁ āyariyaṁ ahavā kimimī majjha citāē ? | iya ciṁtatō viusēṇa saha purō jāi tā jāva ||
tāvavirahi dōhiṁ dō ḍivī pahammi bahudalō । sirajvarithariyachattō viusō uvavisa tassa talē ॥
duiō dūrē ghari chattivavisa tassa pāsammi । viusē dahuṁ citai vivarīyamahāsalō ēsō ॥ 52 ॥
chāyāē dharai chataṁ maggē saṁkōiūṇa taṁ vahai | ahavā viusō ēsō na buddhiviyalō paṭṭē ॥ 53 ॥
tattō paraō vaccataēṇa dahūṇa suphaliyē khittaṁ । bhaṇiyaṁ diēṇa ēvaṁ khittāhivaissa parakā ॥54॥
hōhiṁti, bhaṇai viusō jaī khaddhaṁ hōhihī na puvvipi । taṁ sōūṇaṁ iyarō cita vivarīyataramēyaṁ ॥ 55 ॥
puṇaravi puraō vacataēṇa daṇa uccadēvala । vippēṇaṁ salattaṁ aisōhaṇamāyayaṇamēyaṁ ॥ 56 ॥
tō bhaṇiya viusēṇaṁ sōhaṇamēyaṁ jai na aṇāyayaṇaṁ । hōhī, tōṇakkhēhiṁ vippō mōṇēṇa vaccaṁtō ॥57॥
iti cintayitvā niśi gr̥hṇātyavasvāpikāṁ tatra śabdam । labhata imaṁ yathōttaradiśi tvaṁ jñāsyasīdamiti ॥ 43 ॥
tataḥ sa tatkṣaṇamēva ca samuhya prasthitastatra prāptaḥ । militō mārga ēka uttaradiśi brāhmaṇastasya ॥44॥
amaraguruṇā sa pr̥ṣṭō gantavyaṁ kutra brāhmaṇa ! kathaya । sa bhaṇatyamukagrāmē yēnāhaṁ tatra vāstavyaḥ || 45 ॥
tēnāpi pr̥ṣṭō vidvān kathaya tvayāpi kutra gantavyam । prabhaṇati vidvāṁstvadgrāmasīmaparatō'pi gantavyam ॥ 46 ॥
yadyēvaṁ tatō ramyaṁ jātaḥ sārthaḥ parasparamāvayōḥ । iti jalpantau prāptau saritīrē tataśca viduṣā ॥ 47 ॥
pūrvamuttāritē upānahau pādayō: sthāpitē । tē caraṇābhyāṁ dvitīyēna karēṇa dhr̥tē ॥ 48 ॥
1
tata itaraścintayati sarvō'pi janō jalaṁ vigāhamānaḥ । uttārayati pādukē caraṇābhyāṁ kathamanēna ||19||
viparītamācaritamathavā kimanayā mama cintayā ? | iti cintayanviduṣā saha purō yāti tāvadyāvat ॥10॥
tāpataptābhyāṁ dvābhyāṁ dr̥ṣṭō viṭapī pathi bahuladalaḥ । śirauparighr̥tacchatrō vidvānupraviśati tasya talē ॥ 51 ॥
dvitīyō dūrē dhr̥tvā chatrikāmupaviśati tasya pārśvē । vidvāṁsaṁ dr̥ṣṭā cintayati viparītamahāsya ēṣaḥ ॥ 52 ॥
chāyāyāṁ dharati cchatraṁ mārgē saṁkōcya tadvahati । athavā vidvānēṣa na buddhivikalaḥ pravarttatē ॥ 53 ॥
tataḥ paratō trajatā dr̥ṣṭrā suphalitaṁ kṣētram । bhaṇitaṁ dvijēnaitatkṣētrādhipatēḥ pracurakaṇāḥ ॥54॥
bhaviṣyanti bhaṇati vidvān yadi muktaṁ bhaviṣyati na pūrvamapi । tatśrutvētaraścintayati viparatitaramētat ॥15॥
punarapi puratō vrajatā dr̥ṣṭōccadēvakulam । viprēṇa saṁlapitamatiśōbhanamāyatanamētat ॥56॥
tatō bhaṇitaṁ viduṣā śōbhanamētadyadi nānāyatanam | bhaviṣyati, tatō rōṣairviprō maunēna trajan ॥57॥

malaya kē ukahā ।
611
saṁpattō niyagāmē dhariō viusōvi tēṇa pāhuṇaō । tassavi ya gihaṁ puṇa bālapaṁḍiyā jōyaē duhiyā ||
bhaṇiyā sājaṇaṇaṁ jaha paḍivattī imassa kāyavvā । aigōravēṇa tīēvi kāraviō bhōyaṇāīyaṁ ॥ 59 ॥
muttuttarammi viusē suttē viṣēṇa pucchiyā duhiyā । jaha imiṇā gamaṇīō kiṁ sarimajjhē parihiyāō ? |
sabvōvi jaṇō pāyaṁ jalē visaṁtōna ēvamāyarai । tō bhaṇiyaṁ duhiyāē tāya ! murukkhō si taṁ jēṇa || 61||
sakarakaṁṭakīlayavēhō pāyāṇa havai jalamajjhē । tabhīēṇaṁ imiṇā pāēsu kayāu gamaṇīu || 62 ||
tachāyāē ṭhiēṇavi chattaṁ dhariyaṁ kahaṁ imēti । iya puṭṭhā sā jaṁpara viusōcciya ēsa tāya ! jaō ||63||
tarusēṭhiyapakkhīṇaṁ mā uvariṁ paḍa asuilēsōviṁ । iya buddhīē imiṇā sirammi dhariyaṁ niyaṁ chataṁ ||64 ||
tō khittavaiyaraṁpi hu sā puṭṭhā bhraṇai jai na tappahuṇā । aggimakhāīē imaṁ hōhī khaddhaṁ khutā bhavyaṁ ॥ 65 ॥
āpa puṭṭhā sā bhai tāya ! āyayaṇaṁ । jai cōrajāraṭhāṇaṁ na hu hōhī tō ya āyayaṇaṁ ।।
iccāi japamāṇī viusē nisuniyā diyassa suyā । tō citai maha kajjaṁ imīē sijjhirasai na aṁtī ||
sāvi hu tabbuddhīē suraṁjiyā bhaṇai tāya ! viusāō | maṁ pariṇāksu tā sō niyaduhiyaṁ bhaṇai kimajuttaṁ ? |
kiṁtuttamajāīō ēsō amhāṇa jai tumaṁ mahai । pariṇēḍaṁ tā laḍaṁ aha viusō paṭṭiō gāyē ॥ 69 ॥
tō tappakkhi maggē tahasaggaō diyasuyāē । uccāvari mukkā kaṇayamayaviṭiyā niyayā || 70 ||
sā diusēṇaṁ diṭṭhā gahiyā ya jalēṇa khāliḍaṁ tattō । taṁ giṇtō diṭṭhō viṣpasuyāē taō bhaṇiō ||
kiṁ asuī ōhitō ginhasi ēyaṁ taō bhai viusō | uccārāōvi kaṇayaṁ giṇhēyavvaṁ jaō bhaṇiyaṁ ॥
saṁprāptō nijagrāmē dhr̥tō vidvānapi tēna prāghūrṇakaḥ । tasyāpi ca gr̥haṁ punarvālapaṇḍitā dyōtayati duhitā || 18 ||
bhaṇitā sā janakēna yathā pratipattirasya kartavyā । atigauravēṇa tayāpi kāritō bhōjanādikam ||19|
muktāttarē viduṣi suptē viprēṇa pr̥ṣṭā duhitā । yathā'nēna pādukē kiṁ sarinmadhyē parihitē ? ||60 ||
sarvō'pi janaḥ prāyō jalē viśannaivamācarati । tatō bhaṇitaṁ duhitrā tāta ! mūrkhō'si tvaṁ yēna ॥ 61 ॥
śarkarākaṇṭakakīlakavēdhaḥ pādayōrbhavati jalamadhyē । tadbhītēnānēna pādayōḥ kr̥tē pādukē ॥ 62 ॥
1
tarucchāyāyāṁ sthitēnāpi cchatraṁ ghr̥taṁ kathamanēnēti । idaṁ pr̥ṣṭā sā jalpati vidvānēvaiṣa tāta ! yataḥ ॥ 63 ॥
tarusaṁsthitapakṣiṇāṁ mōpari patatvaśucilēśō'pi । iti buddhyā'nēna śirasi dhr̥taṁ nijaṁ chatram ॥ 64 ॥
tataḥ kṣētravyatikaramapi hi sā pr̥ṣṭā bhaṇati yadi na tatprabhuṇā । agrimakhādya idaṁ bhavēdbhuktaṁ khalu tadā bhavyam ॥ 65 ॥
āyatanavyatikaramapi hi pr̥ṣṭā sā bhaṇati tāta ! āyatanam | yadi caurajārasthānaṁ nahiṁ bhavēttataścāyatanam ॥
ityādi jalpantī viduṣā śrutā dvijasya sutā । tataścintayati mama kāryamanayā sētsyati na bhrāntiḥ ॥67॥
sāpi hi tabuddhayā surañjitā bhaṇati tāta ! viduṣā । māṁ pariṇāyaya tataḥ sa nijaduhitaraṁ bhaṇati kimayuktam ? ||
kintūttama jātika ēṣō'smāsu yadi tvāṁ kāṅkṣati । pariṇētuṁ tadā ramyamatha vidvānprasthitō grāmē ॥ 69 ॥
tatastatparīkṣāhētōrmārgē tasyāgratō dvijasutayā । uccārōpari muktā kanakamaya mudrikā nijā || 70 ||
sā viduṣā dr̥ṣṭā gr̥hītā ca jalēna kṣālitvā tataḥ । tāṁ gr̥hṇan dr̥ṣṭō viprasutayā tatō bhaṇitaḥ ॥ 71 ॥

612
supāsanāha cariammi--
“bālādapi hitaṁ grāhyamamēdhyādapi kāñcanam । nīcāpyuttamāṁ vidyāṁ strīratnaṁ duṣkulādapi ।।”
tō tīē sō bhaṇiō jai ēvaṁ tō balēsa pariṇēsu । maṁ hīṇavippaduhiyaṁ tō taṁ sō kuṇai taha caiva ॥ 73 ॥
kaivayadiṇāvasāṇē bhaṇiyā viusēṇa sā imaṁ vayaṇaṁ । niyapiyaraṁ bhaṇasu tumaṁ mōkalai jēṇa simyaṁpi ||74 ||
tī sōtā bhaṇiō kisaō suhaya! tēṇa sē kahiyē । nivaāṇāē sarūvaṁ sā paṇai ahaṁ bhalissāmi ||
macchyahāsayahēū nāōcciya jaṁ maē, taō viusō । nivbhayacittō caliō tīē samaṁ niyahiṁ pattō ॥
mātē tō rannā tassa gihē pēsiō niō purisō । āhavaṇatyaṁ sigyaṁ tattō viusassa bhajjāē || 77||
sō bhaṇiō jasō maggassa sayēṇa bāhiō bāḍhaṁ । ajjavi suttō cihna ahaṁ kahissāmi naravaiṇō ॥
āgaṁtuṁ jaṁ puṭṭō tajhyā viusō, taō imō bhai | gaṁtuṁ kahēmi ēyaṁ tuha vayaṇaṁ sāmiṇō tattō ॥ 79 ॥
nivaāēsaṁ puṇaravi tujjha kahissāmi tō gaō purisō । kahiyaṁ taṁ naravaiṇō tassavi aikōuyaṁ jāyaṁ ॥ 80 ॥
mahilāṇavi iya buddhī kahihī mayamacchahasiyahēḍaṁ jā । tā dadvavvā amhēhiṁ sādi, āhavasu taṁ simyaṁ ॥
tēvisā āhūyā saṁpattā naravaissa pāsammi । tō puṭṭhā sā rannā kō hēū macchahasaṇammi ? ॥ 82 ॥
tō isa samaya ! ēgaṁta dēsa majjha pasiūṇa | sāhēmi jēṇa macchassa hasiyahē ihēba lahuṁ ॥ 83 ॥
vihiyaṁ tahēva rannā tīē bhaṇiyaṁ nariṁda ! nisuṇēsu । karikhaṁdhagaēṇa taē putraṁ dinaṁ mihuṇabhēgaṁ ||8 4 ||
ētampi nividdhaṁ niyapāsāyassa mattavāraṇaē । tassa ya sahōyarassavi tuha jāyā ērisī saṁkā ॥ 85॥
ēyaṁ na suṁdaraṁ ciya jaṁ ētami maṁtara nivihaṁ । iya tuha cittaṁ nāuṁ vaṁtaradēvēṇa kēṇāvi || 86 ॥
kimaśucērgr̥hṇāsyētāṁ tatō bhaṇati vidvān | uccārādapi kanakaṁ grahītavyaṁ yatō bhaṇitam ॥72॥
tatastayā sa bhaṇitō yadyēvaṁ tatō valasva pariṇaya | māṁ hīnavipraduhitaraṁ tatastatsa karōti tathaiva ॥73॥
katipayadināvasānē bhaṇitā viduṣā sēdaṁ vacanam । nijapitaraṁ bhaṇa tvāṁ prēṣayati yēna śīghramapi ॥74॥
tataḥ sa tāvadbhaṇitaḥ kimutsukaḥ subhaga ! tēna tasyai kathitam । nr̥pājñāyāḥ svarūpaṁ sā praṇatyahaṁ bhaliṣyē ॥ 75 ॥
matsyahāsya hēturjñāta ēva yanmayā, tatō vidvān । nirbhayacittaścalitastayā samaṁ nijagr̥haṁ prāptaḥ ॥76॥
māsāntē tatō rājñā tasya gr̥hē prēṣitō nijaḥ puruṣaḥ । āhnānārtha śīghraṁ tatō viduṣō bhāryayā ॥ 77 ॥
sa bhaṇitō yathā vidvān mārgasya śramēṇa bādhitō bāḍham । adyāpi suptastiṣṭhatyahaṁ kathayiṣyāmi narapatayē ॥ 78॥
āgatya yatpr̥ṣṭastadā vidvān, tatō'yaṁ bhaṇati । gatvā kathayāmyētattava vacanaṁ svāminē tataḥ ॥ 79 ॥
nr̥pādēśaṁ punarapi tubhyaṁ kathayiṣyāmi tatō gataḥ puruṣaḥ । kathitaṁ tannarapatayē tasyāpyatikaiautukaṁ jātam ॥ 80 ॥
mahilānāmapīti buddhiḥ kathayiṣyati mr̥tamatsyahasitahētuṁ yā । tasmāddraṣṭavyā'smābhiḥ sāpyāhvayasva tāṁ śīghram ॥
tēnāpi sā''hūtā saṁprāptā narapatēḥ pārśvē । tataḥ pr̥ṣṭā sā rājñā kō hētumatsyahasanē ? ॥ 82 ॥
tatō jalpati sā svāmin ! ēkāntaṁ dēhi mama prasadya । kathayāmi yēna matsyasya hasitahētumihaiva laghu ॥ 83 ॥
vihitaṁ tathaiva rājñā tayā bhaṇitaṁ narēndra ! śr̥ṇu । kariskandhagatēna tvayā pūrva dr̥ṣṭaṁ mithunamēkam ॥84॥
ēkāntē niviṣṭaṁ nijaprāsādasya mattavāraṇē । tasya ca sahōdarasyāpi tava jātēdr̥śī śaṅkā || 85 ||

malaya kahā ।
613
mayamacchē avayariḍaṁ hasiyaṁ jaha picchai naravaī ēsō । para chiḍḍāī niyacchai na picchaē niyayachiḍḍāī ||
yataḥ,
"sarvaḥ parasya paśyati vālāgrādapi tanūni chidrāṇi । ātmakr̥tāni na paśyati himagiriśikharapramāṇāni ॥ "
tō bhaṇiyaṁ naravaraṇā maha kiṁ chiḍḍuṁ kahēsu, sā bhaṇai । abhaēṇa maha pasāyaṁ karēsu sāhēmi jēṇa tayaṁ ॥ 88 ॥
tēvi tahēva vihiyaṁ, tō pabhaṇai vālapaṁḍiyāvi phuḍaṁ । tuha sayalaṁpivarōhaṁ dēva ! vidvaṁ jaō tattha ||
kittimadāsīvēsā taruṇanarā kuccavirahiyā bahuyā । ēkkikkīē pāsē ciṭṭhaṁti vilāsadullaliyā ॥90॥
jai paccaō na vijjai maha vayaṇē dēva! tō ya ēgaṁtē । gattaṁ khaṇāviūṇaṁ dēvīō taha ya dāsīō ॥ 91 ॥
ēvaṁ bhaṇasu maē jaha diṭṭhāō sumiṇayammi rayaṇīē । dāsīhi juttāō savvāuvi niyayadēvīō ॥ 92 ॥
gattaṁ phaḍamāṇīō tā ēyaṁ saccayaṁ kuha ihi । rannāvi hu kabhaṇiyaṁ tahatti kārāviyaṁ sigghaṁ ॥ 93 ॥
tō śrīsadharēhi narēhiṁ phaḍiyā jhaḍatti sā gattā । tō bālapaṁḍiyāē bhaṇiyaṁ purisā imē dēva ! ||94 ॥
ēyāō ramaṇīō phaḍiu na taraṁti thaṇaniyaṁvabharā । tō thīvēsā purisā parikkhijaṁ jhātta niggahiyā ||
tō naravaṇā puṭṭhā kaha jāṇasi taṁ bhaṇēi buddhīē । kiṁpi kahai niyajaṇaṇī vaṁtariṇī sumariyā suhumaṁ ॥
tabbuddhiraṁjiō sō sammāṇēuṁ visajjaē taṁ tō । ciṁtai cōjjaṁ majjhavi bhajjāu kuṇaṁti jamakajjaṁ ॥ 97 ||
imiṇā vēraggēṇa amaraguruṁ ṭhāviūṇa maṁtipaē । taha niyaputtaṁ rajjē gihivi dikkha gaō mōkkhaṁ ॥ 98 ॥
itthaṁtarammi gayaṇē surajuyalēṇaṁ tu picchamāṇēṇa । pōsahasālāē nivō amaccabhaṇiyaṁ nisāmitō || 99 ॥
1
ētanna sundaramēva yadēkāntē mantrayati niviṣṭam । iti tava cittaṁ jñātvā vyantaradēvēna kēnāpi ॥ 86 ॥
mr̥tamatsyē'vatīrya hasitaṁ yathā paśyati narapatirēṣaḥ । paracchidrāṇi paśyati na paśyati nijacchidrāṇi ॥ 87 ॥
tatō bhaṇitaṁ narapatinā mama kiṁ chidraṁ kathaya, sābhaṇati । abhayēna mama prasādaṁ kuru kathayāmi yēna tat ॥88॥
tēnāpi tathaiva vihitaṁ, tataḥ prabhaṇati bālapaṇḍitāpi sphuṭam । tava sakalō'pyavarōdhō dēva ! vinaṣṭō yatastatra ॥
kr̥ttrimadāsīvēṣāstaruṇanarāḥ kūrcavirahitā bahavaḥ । ēkaikasyāḥ pārśvē tiṣṭhanti vilāsa durlalitāḥ ॥90॥
yadi pratyayō na vidyatē mama vacanē dēva ! tataścaikāntē । garta khānayitvā dēvīstathā ca dāsīḥ ॥ 91 ॥
ēvaṁ bhaṇa mayā yathā dr̥ṣṭāḥ svapnē rajanyām । dāsībhiryuktāḥ sarvā api nijadēvyaḥ ॥92॥
gartaṁ sphaṭantyatasmādētat satyaṁ kurutēdānīm । rājñāpi hi tadbhaṇitaṁ tathaiva kāritaṁ śīghram ॥93॥
tataḥ strīvēṣavarairnaraiḥ sphaṭitā jhaṭiti sā gartā । tatō bālapaṇḍitayā bhaṇitaṁ puruṣā imē dēva ! ॥94॥
ētā ramaṇyaḥ sphaṭituṁ na śaknuvanti stananitambabharāt । tataḥ strīvēṣāḥ puruṣāḥ parīkṣya jhaṭiti nigr̥hītāḥ ॥
tatō narapatinā pr̥ṣṭā kathaṁ jānāsi tvaṁ, bhaṇati buddhayā । kimapi kathayati nijajananī vyantarī smr̥tā sūkṣmam ॥
tadbuddhirañjitaḥ saṁ sammānya visr̥jati tāṁ tataḥ । cintayatyāścarya mamāpi bhāryāḥ kurvanti yadakāryam ॥97॥
anēna vairāgyēṇāmaraguruṁ sthāpayitvā mantripadē । tathā nijaputraṁ rājyē gr̥hītvā dīkṣāṁ gatō mōkṣam ॥98 ॥
atrāntarē gaganē surayugalēna tu paśyatā | pauṣavaśālāyāṁ nr̥pō'mātyabhaṇitaṁ niśamayan ॥99॥

diṭṭhō ta ya bhaṇiō iyarasurō sammadidvidēvēṇaṁ । jaha pōsahāō nivaī sakōvi na cāliḍaṁ sakō ।
tō guruaṇakkhabhaṇiō sō dēvō jāi rāyapāsamma । bhaṇai narāhiba ! tuṭṭhō tuha dhammaparikkacittēṇa ॥
tō maggasu kiṁci varaṁ jēṇa payacchēmi vaṁchiyaṁ savvaṁ । tō bhaṇai nivō suravara ! paōyaṇaṁ mē na kēṇāvi ॥
tō sō pāyasamayaṁ vivbiuṁ bhaṇai pārasu nariṁda ! | pōsahamēyaṁ jēṇaṁ nēmi tumaṁ mērusiharammi || 103 ||
sāsayajiṇapaḍimāē vaṁdaṇahēu taō ya naranāhō । sajjhāyakaraṇamāṇēṇa jāṇiuṁ aḍūḍharattaṁti ||104 ||
tō pōsahaṁpi pārai na uttaraṁ dēi kuṇai sajjhāyaṁ । tō sō dēvō kuviō dāruṇaviyaṇāu sē kuṇai ॥ 105 ॥
kannacchibhiī, sō sammaṁ sahai iya vibhāvitō । rē jīva ! sahasu sabasō viyaṇāu khaṇaṁtaraṁ jēṇa ||
narayammi tumē sahiyā paliōnamasāyarāṁī tāī taō । mā ubvijjasu inhi suravidiyāpi viyaṇāṇaṁ ॥
mā ēyammi paōsa paramuvayārimmi kuṇasu tumamihiṁ । cirakālavēiyavvaṁ kammaṁ acirēṇa jēṇēsō ॥ 108 ॥
vēyāvara viyaṇāhi pāṇatakarāhi tā tumaṁ jīva ! । ālōyasu duccariyaṁ siddhasamavakhaṁ samapi ॥ 109 ॥
khāmēsu savvasattē iya jā citai nivō surō tāva | nāṇēṇa niyai ēsō ki caliō pōsahāō navā ||
jāva na picchai caliyē tilatusamittaṁpi taṁ mahāsattaṁ । tō viyaṇāu saṁhariya khāmaē sō surō ēvaṁ ॥
khamasu mahāsa! ihi annāṇapamāyarāgadōsēhiṁ । vihiyā jaṁ viyaṇāō nikkāraṇavēriēṇa maē ॥ 112 ॥
aha sō nivēṇa bhaṇiō kō tuha dōsō surēsa ! puvvakayaṁ । amhāṇamasuhakammaṁ samuinnaṁ vēiyaṁ ca tahā ॥
tuhasā hijjavasēṇaṁ niyacittapasannayāṇubhāvēṇa । annaha bahuyabhavēsuvi jaha kahavi hu saṁkhavijja ahaṁ । । 1914 ||
dr̥ṣṭastataśca bhaṇita itarasuraḥ samyagdr̥ṣṭidēvēna । yathā pauṣadhānnr̥patiṁ śakrō'pi na cālayituṁ śaktaḥ ॥ 100 ॥
tatō gururāṣabhr̥taḥ sa dēvō yāti rājapārśvē । bhaṇīta narādhipa ! tuṣṭastava dharmaparaikacittēna ॥ 101 ॥
tatō mārgaya kañcidvāraṁ yēna prayacchāmi vāñchitaṁ sarvam । tatō bhaṇati nr̥paḥ suravara ! prayōjanaṁ mē na kēnāpi ॥
tataḥ sa prabhātasamayaṁ vikr̥tya bhaṇati pāraya narēndra ! | pauṣadhamētaṁ yēna nayāmi tvāṁ mēruśikharē ॥103॥
śāśvatajinapratimāyā vandanahētōstataśca naranāthaḥ । svādhyāyakaraṇamānēna jñātvā'rdharātramiti ॥104॥
nō pauṣadhamapi pārayati nōttaraṁ dadāti karōti svādhyāyam । tataḥ sa dēvaḥ kupitō dāruṇa vēdanāstasya karōti ॥
karṇākṣiprabhr̥tiṣu, sa samyak sahata iti vibhāvayan । rē jīva ! sahasva svavaśō vēdanāḥ kṣaṇāntaraṁ yēna ॥ 106 ॥
narakē tvayā sōḍhāḥ palyōpamasāgarāṇi tāni tataḥ । mōdvija idānīṁ suravihitābhyō'pi vēdanābhyaḥ ॥ 107 ॥
maitasminpradvēṣaṁ paramōpakāriṇi kuruṣva tvamidānīm । cirakālavēdayitavyaṁ karmācirēṇa yēnaiṣaḥ ॥ 108॥
vēdayati vēdanābhiḥ prāṇāntakarībhistasmāttvaṁ jīva ! | ālōcaya duścaritaṁ siddhasamakṣaṁ samagramapi ॥ 109 ॥
kṣamaya sarvasattvāniti yāvaccintayati nr̥paḥ surastāvat । jñānēna paśyatyēṣa kiṁ calitaḥ pauṣadhād navā ॥ 110 ॥
yāvanna paśyati calitaṁ tilatupamātramapi taṁ mahāsattvam । tatō vēdanāḥ saṁhr̥tya kṣamayati sasura ēvam ॥ 111॥
kṣamasva mahāyaśaḥ ! idānīmajñānapramādarāgadvēṣaiḥ । vihitā yad vēdanā niṣkāraṇavairiṇā mayā ॥ 112 ॥
atha sa nr̥pēṇa bhaṇitaḥ kastava dōṣaḥ surēśa ! pūrvakr̥tam । asmākamaśubhakarma samudīrṇaṁ vēditaṁ ca tathā ॥ 113 ॥

iccāī jaṁpamāṇāṇa tāṇa sūrō samuggaō jāva । tā bhaṇiyaṁ dēdēṇaṁ saccamiṇaṁ jaṁpiyaṁ kēhi ॥ 115 ॥
āvaisahassakasavaṭṭaēsa dhaṇiyaṁ kasijjamāṇassa । purisamsa suvannassa va māhappaṁ pāyarḍa hōi ॥ 116 ॥
sacivasahiēṇa tattō vihiṇā pāritu pōsahaṁ rannā । bhaṇiō amarō paḍivajja saṁpayaṁ daṁsaṇaṁ suddhaṁ ॥ 117 ॥
tēvi tahatti vihiyaṁ tuṭṭō dēvō paryaṁpaē ēvaṁ । givha imaṁ maṇikuṁḍalajuyalaṁ tō bhaṇai naranāhō ॥ 118 ॥
kiṁ kajjaṁ ēēṇaṁ tumha pasāēṇa maha gharē natthi । saṁkhāvi hu ēyāṇaṁ tō dēvō bhaṇai naranāhaṁ ॥ 119 ॥
hu
ēyassa pabhāvēṇaṁ pabhavaṁti na dēvadāṇavā khudā । dūrēṇaṁ puṇa maṇuyā navavērasamaccharamaṇāvi ॥ 120 ॥
iccāi bhaūṇaṁ sō dēvō dēvalōyamaṇupattō । rāyāvi hu āvassayavihipuvvaṁ pūiūṇa jiṇaṁ ॥ 121 ॥
taṁ maṇikuṁḍalajuyalaṁ parihēḍaṁ nivasaī ya atthāṇē । sāmaṁtamaṁtisahiō tō vimhaiō jaṇō bhai ॥ 122 ॥
suragirikaḍaṇipariṭṭiyacaṁdāiccāṇa sirimaṇuharati । savaṇēsu kuṁḍalāī pahuṇō sirimalayakēussa ||
iccāī jaṁpamāṇō jā lōō ciṭṭaē nivasayāsē । tā ahimarēṇa kēṇavi chalēṇa rannō kaō ghāō ॥
maṇikuṁḍalāṇubhāvā satthaṁ nō pahaviyaṁ nariṁdassa । tō sō ghāyagapuriyō gahiō saṁnihiyamuhaḍēhi || 125||
puṭṭhō abhayaṁ rannā kēṇa tumaṁ pēsiō mahavahatthaṁ ? । tēṇavi saccai kahiyaṁ savvaṁ rannāvi tō mukkō ।। 126||
tō maṁrti bhai nivō surasā hijjēṇa jīviyaṁ pattaṁ । akayadhammassa iharā maraṇaṁ samuvaṭṭiyaṁ hutaṁ ॥ 127 ॥
tāpuvvapurisamaggaṁ aṇusarimō saṁpayaṁpi kumarassa । arisīhassa vihēuṁ rajjabhisēyaṁ taō maṁtī ॥ 128 ॥
tvatsāhāyyavaśēna nijacittaprasannatānubhāvēna । anyathā bahubhavēṣvapi yathā kathamapi hi saṁkṣapayēyamaham ॥ 114 ॥
ityādi jalpatōstayōḥ sūraḥ samudgatō yāvat । tāvad bhaṇitaṁ dēvēna satyamidaṁ jalpitaṁ kaiḥ ॥ 115 ॥
āpatsahasrakapapaṭṭēṣu gāḍhaṁ kadhyamāṇasya । puruṣasya suvarṇasyēva māhātmyaṁ prakaṭaṁ bhavati ॥ 116 ॥
sacivasahitēna tatō vidhinā pārayitvā pauṣadhaṁ rājñā । bhaṇitō'maraḥ pratipadyasva sāṁprataṁ darśanaṁ śuddham ॥ 117 ॥
tēnāpi tathēti vihitaṁ tuṣṭō dēvaḥ prajalpatyēvam । gr̥hāṇēdaṁ maṇikuṇḍalayugalaṁ tatō bhaṇati naranāthaḥ ॥ 118 ॥
kiṁ kāryamētēna tava prasādēna mama gr̥hē nāsti । saṁkhyāpi tēṣāṁ tatō dēvō bhaṇati naranātham ॥ 119 ॥
ētasya prabhāvēṇa prabhavanti na dēvadānavāḥ kṣudrāḥ । dūrēṇa punarmanujā navavairasamatsaramanasō'pi ॥ 120 ॥
ityādi bhaṇitvā sa dēvō dēvalōkamanuprāptaḥ । rājāpi hyāvaśyakavidhipūrva pūjayitvā jinam ॥121॥
tanmaṇikuṇḍalayugalaṁ paridhāya nivasati cāsthānē । sāmantamantrisahitastatō vismayitō janō bhaṇati ॥ 122 ॥
suragirikaṭinīpratiṣṭhitacandrādityayōḥ śriyamanuharētē । śravaṇayōḥ kuṇḍalē prabhōḥ śrīmalayakētōḥ ॥ 123॥
ityādi jalpanyāvallō kastiṣṭhati nr̥pasakāśē । tāvadabhimarēṇa kēnāpi cchalēna rājñē kr̥tō vātaḥ ॥ 124 ॥
maṇikuṇḍalānubhāvācchatraṁ nō prabhūtaṁ narēndrē । tataḥ sa ghātakapuruṣō gr̥hītaḥ saṁnihitasubhaṭaiḥ ॥ 125 ॥
pr̥ṣṭō'bhayaṁ rājñā kēna tvaṁ prēṣitō madvadhārtham ? । tēnāpi satyaṁ kathitaṁ sarvaṁ rājñāpi tatō muktaḥ ॥ 126 ॥
tatō mantriṇaṁ bhaṇati nr̥paḥ surasāhāyyēna jīvitaṁ prāptam । akr̥tadharmasyētarathā maraṇaṁ samupasthitamabhaviṣyat ॥

।
chaliō mucchāē imō gaṇaputtāiyāṇa aiṇiyaṁ । kiṁ bahuṇā ēsōcciya sāhissai akkharē lihiuṁ ॥
niyacariyaṁ tumhāṇaṁ, tēṇavi taha caiva sāhiyaṁ savvaṁ । tō paḍhamasuēṇaṁ tē āhūyā baṁdhuṇō tattha ||26||
tāṇavi kahiyaṁ tēṇaṁ piuṇō cariyaṁ taō ya kēvaliṇā । kahiō duvihō dhammō jaigihibhēēṇa savvāṇa |
paḍhasamatthē ta bhaṇiō nāṇī kahēha amhāṇa | sāvayadhammaṁ savvaṁ tō nāṇī kahai taṁ tāṇa ॥28॥
tō tēvi ha savisēsaṁ namiḍaṁ pucchaṁti sūripāsammi । pahu ! pōsahasadatthaṁ kahēha, sūrīvi tō kahai || 29 ॥
iti jalpan śrēṣṭhī mr̥tvā tatraiva malayamadhyē । jātaḥ plavaṅgapōtastanmr̥takr̥tyāni kr̥tvā ॥15॥
putrā api hi vyavahāraṁ kurvantyēkāntasaṁsthitāḥ sarvē । atha tēṣāṁ malayamadhyē samavasr̥taḥ kēvalī kadā ॥ 16 ॥
śrībhuvanabhānunāmā sadēvamanujāsurāyāṁ parṣadi । dharmaṁ vyākurvastatpitr̥javina plavagēna ॥17॥
sahakāratarusthitēna dr̥ṣṭastataḥ sō'pi śr̥ṇōti vacanārmadam । bhō bhō bhavyā mūrcchā parihartavyā prayatnēna ॥ 18 ॥
gr̥hadhanaputrakalatrādikēṣu kṣaṇadr̥ṣṭanaṣṭarūpēṣu । yēna saiva hēturgurupāpabharasya jīvānām ॥19॥
mūrcchāparigatacitta ārtavaśārtaḥ karōti yadi kālam । tatastiryakṣu gacchati yathā vaiśramaṇa ihanivāsī ॥20॥
śākhāmr̥gō'pi śrutvā nijanāma jātajātismaraṇaḥ saḥ । prāptaḥ kēvalipārśvē karōti praṇāmaṁ tataḥ parpat ॥ 21 ॥
vismitahr̥dayā pr̥cchati ka ēṣa vānaraḥ, kathayati jñānī । sa ēṣa vaiśramaṇō ya ihavāsī mayā kathitaḥ ॥ 22 ॥
parṣanmadhyagatēna prathamasutēna nijasya janakasya । śrutvā caritaṁ pr̥ṣṭō jñānī kathaṁ vānara ēṣaḥ ॥ 23 ॥
saṁjātō mama pitā vaiśramaṇaḥ śramaṇabrāhmaṇādibhyaḥ । yō dāpayandānaṁ, tataḥ prabhaṇati kēvalyēvam ||24||
chalitō mūrcchayā'yaṁ gr̥haghanaputrādikānāmatigāḍham । kiṁ bahunaipa ēva kathayiṣyatyakṣarāṇi likhitvā ॥ 25 ॥
nijacaritaṁ yuṣmabhyaṁ tēnāpi tathaiva kathitaṁ sarvam । tataḥ prathamasutēna ta āhūtā bandhavastatra ॥ 26 ॥
tēbhyō'pi kathitaṁ tēna pituścaritaṁ tataśca kēvalinā । kathitō dvividhō dharmō yatigr̥hibhēdēna sarvēbhyaḥ ||27||
prathamāsamathaistatō bhaṇitō jñānī kathayatāsmākam । śrāvakadharma sarvaṁ tatō jñānī kathayati taṁ tēbhyaḥ ||28||
