pōnever rūḍhī ēttha pavvāṇuvāyaō bhaṇiō। aṭṭamibhiīṇi ya tāṇi ittha samaē pasiddhāṇa ||30||
uvavasaṇaṁ jaṁ ca puṇō tērsi sō pōsahōvavāsati । bhannai dhammēṇa naraṁ pōsai vā pōsahō tēṇaṁ ||31||
āhāradēhasakārasaṁbhavāvārabhēyaō sōvi । caubhēō nidiṭṭhō siddhatē puvvasūrīhi || 32॥
sō dēsasavvabhēyā pattēyaṁpi hu duhā tarhi dēsē । nivatthucāō savvāhārāṇa savvammi ||33||
bhannai sarīrasakkārapōsahō dēsasavvabhēēṇa | duvihō tattha ya dēsē nidiṭṭhāṇaṁ paricāō ||34||
nhāṇuvvaṭṭaṇavannagavilēvaṇappamuhavivivatthūṇa । savvē uṇa savvēsiṁ cāō vatthūṇa nidiṭṭō ||35||
aha bhapōsō sō ēēṇa kamēṇa bhannaē duvihō । dēsē diṇāivaṁbhaṁ savrvva savvaṁ ahōrataṁ ॥ 36 ॥
vāvārā puṇa raṁdhāghara liṁpaṇadalaṇakhaṁḍaṇāīyā । asubhā subhā ya duvihā tattha dēsamma asuhāṇa ||37||
niṭṭhiāṇaṁ cāō savvēṇaṁ savvā pariccāō । suhavāvārāṇumayā pōsahiyassavi apaḍisiddhā ||38||
savvēṇaṁ puṇa ēvaṁ givhaṁtēṇaṁ avaskāyavvaṁ । sāmaiyaṁ taha muṇisaṁnihimmi pāēṇa ṭhāyavvaṁ ॥ 39 ॥
taha aiyāravimukkaṁ pālēyavaṁ imaṁ payattēṇaṁ । tē aiyārā ēē pannatā pōsahē paṁca ||40||
tadyathā;-
appaḍiduppaḍilēhiyaapamajjiyadupamajjiyāṇa sayā । savvāṇa sijjaphalagāṇa gahaṇaō mōyaṇē vāvi ॥
taha muttuccārāīṇa karaṇaō thaṁḍilammi ēmēva । taha pōsahassa samma apālaṇēṇaṁ aīyārā ||42 ||
iya sōuṁ siṭṭiyā savvē giṇhaṁti sāvayavayāī । pavagō puṇa paḍivajjai sadaṁsaṇaṁ aṇasaṇaṁ vihiṇā ||
tatastē'pi hi saviśēṣaṁ natvā pr̥cchanti sūripārśvē । prabhō ! pauṣadhaśabdārthaṁ kathayata, sūrirapi tataḥ kathayati ॥
pauṣadhaśabdō rūḍhyā'tra parvānuvācakō bhaṇitaḥ । aṣṭamīprabhr̥tīni ca tānyatra samayē prasiddhāni ||30||
upavasanaṁ yacca punastēṣu sa pauṣadhōpavāsa iti । bhaṇyatē dharmēṇa naraṁ puṣṇāti vā pauṣadhastēna ॥ 31 ॥
āhāradēhasatkārabrahmavyāpārabhēdataḥ sō'pi । caturbhēdō nirdiṣṭaḥ siddhāntē pūrvasūribhiḥ ||32||
sa dēśasarvabhēdātpratyēkamapi hi dvidhā tatra dēśē । nirdiṣṭavastutyāgaḥ sarvāhārāṇāṁ sarvasmin ॥33॥
bhaṇyatē śarīrasatkārapauṣadhō dēśasarvabhēdēna । dvividhastatra ca dēśē nirdiṣṭānāṁ parityāgaḥ ||34||
snānōdvartanavarṇakavilēpanapramukhavividhavastūnām । sarvasminpunaḥ sarvēṣāṁ tyāgō vastūnāṁ nirdiṣṭaḥ ||35||
atha brahmapauṣadhaḥ sa ētēna kramēṇa bhaṇyatē dvividhaḥ । dēśē dinādibrahma sarvasminsarvamahōrātram ॥ 36 ॥
vyāpārāḥ punaḥ pacanagr̥ha lēpanadalanakhaṇḍanādikāḥ । aśubhāḥ śubhāśca dvividhāstatra dēśē'śubhānām ||37||
nirdiṣṭānāṁ tyāgaḥ sarvasminsarvathā parityāgaḥ । śubhavyāpārā anumatāḥ pauṣadhikasyāpyapratiṣiddhāḥ ॥ 38 ॥
sarvēṇa punarētaṁ gr̥hṇatā'vaśyakartavyam । sāmāyikaṁ tathā munisaṁnidhau prāyēṇa sthātavyam ||39||
tathāticāravimuktaṁ pālayitavyamidaṁ prayatnēna । tē'ticārā ētē prajñaptāḥ pauṣadhē pañca ॥ 40 ॥
1
apratilēkhita duṣprati lēkhitāpramārjitaduṣpramārjitānāṁ sadā । sarvēṣāṁ śayyāphalakānāṁ grahaṇatō mōcanē vāpi ॥ 41 ॥
tathā mūtrōccārādīnāṁ karaṇataḥ sthaṇḍila ēvamēva । tathā pauṣadhasya samyagapālanēnātīcārāḥ ॥42॥

supāsanāha-cariammi-
kēvalanāṇī nicca tappāsaṭhiō karēi aṇusa । puttāvi tassa uvariṁ rayaṁti puṣphōvayārāī ||44 ||
jaṁpaṁti ya tayabhimuhaṁ kō idavtrassa tujjha punnaṭṭā । jiṇabhavaṇaviṁbapōtthayapabhiītuṁ vivvaislāmō ||45||
aṇumannai sōvi hu sattaditē taō marēūṇa । aṭṭamakappammi surō saṁjāō aimahiḍḍhīō || 46 ||
sēsiyāvi hu savvē sāvayavammaṁ kuṇaṁti uvauttā । pañcatihīsu ya givhaṁti pōsahaṁ taha caunbhēyaṁ ॥ 47 ॥
iya vaccatē kālē annayā pōsahammi gahiyammi । niddāpamāyavasaō paḍhamasuō kahavi uttālō || 48 ॥
appaḍilēhiyasējjaṁ giṇhaṁtō caiva karayalē ḍasiō । guruvisaharēṇa tattō mukkō pāṇēhiṁ nāgēsu || 49 ||
uvavanna tattōcciya mahāvidēhammi laddhapavvajjō । parimukkakammakavaō mōkkhasuhaṁ pāvihī ajharā || 50||
pōsahaṭiōvi duiō dhaṇiyaṁ nirddhadhasō tahā alasō । duppaḍilēhiyasijjaṁ samāruhaṁtō ya caraṇammi ||
aha kaiyāvi hudaṭṭō ahimuttunbhaḍavichuēṇa taō । ainiviḍapīḍiō sō mariḍaṁ bhavaṇāhivō jāō ||
taiōvi pōsahaṭiō sarīracitāē vāhiō bāḍhaṁ । apamajjiyathaṁḍillē rayaṇīē nisīhasamayami || 53 ॥
pāsavaṇaṁ kuṇamāṇō daṭṭhō gujjhammi bhūmiphōḍīē । mariūṇaṁ tō sōvi hu jōisiyasurēsu vavannō ॥54॥
turiōvi pōsahadiō maṁdaggī uyaravigaṇāvihurō । asahō sahasāvi taō dupamajjiyathaṁḍilē jhusirē ||
uccāraṁ kuṇamāṇō apāṇadēsammi garuyaparaḍāē । daṭṭō pīḍāē maō tattō sō vaṁtarī jāō ॥ 56 ॥
taha gahiyapōsaṇavi vihiō paṁcamasuraṇa paṁcamaō । aiārō, tō sōvi hu chuhiō ciṁtaṁtaō ēvaṁ ||
I
iti śrutvā śrēṣṭhitāḥ sarvē gr̥hṇanti śrāvakavratāni । plavagaḥ punaḥ pratipadyatē sadarśanamanaśanaṁ vidhinā ॥
kēvalajñānī nityaṁ tatpārśvasthitaḥ karōtyanuśāstim । putrā api tasyōpari racayanti puṣpōpacārādi || 4 ||
jalpanti ca tadabhimukhaṁ kōṭiṁ dravyasya tava puṇyārtham । jinabhavanabimbapustakaprabhr̥tiṣu vyayiṣyāmahē ॥45॥
tadanumanyatē sō'pi hi saptadināntē tatō mr̥tvā । aṣṭamakalpē suraḥ saṁjātō'timaharddhikaḥ ॥ 46 ॥
śrōṣṭhatā api hi sarvē śrāvakadharma kurvantyupayuktāḥ । parvatithiṣu ca gr̥hṇanti pauṣadhaṁ tathā caturbhēdam ॥ 47 ॥
iti vrajati kālē'thānyaṛhā pauṣadhē gr̥hītē । nidrāpramādavaśataḥ prathamasutaḥ kathamapyuttālaḥ || 48 ||
apratilēkhitaśayyāṁ gr̥hṇannētra karatalē daṣṭaḥ । guruviṣadharēṇa tatō muktaḥ prāṇairnāgēṣu ||49 ॥
upapannastata ēva mahāvidēhē labdhapratrajyaḥ । parimuktakarmakavacō mōkṣasukhaṁ prāpsyatyacirāt ॥10॥
pauṣavasthitō'pi dvitīyō gāḍhaṁ niṣṭhurastathā'lasaḥ । duṣpratilēkhitaśayyāṁ samārōhaṁśca caraṇē ॥51॥
atha kadāpi hi daṣṭō'hamuktōdbhavr̥ścikēna tataḥ । atinibiḍapīḍitaḥ sa mr̥tvā bhavanādhipō jātaḥ ||12||
tr̥tīyō'pi pauṣadhasthitaḥ śarīracintayā bādhitō bāḍham । apramārjitasthaṇḍilē rajanyāṁ niśīthasamayē ||13||
prasūvaṇaṁ kurvandaṣṭō guhyē bhūmisphōṭayā । mr̥tvā tataḥ sō'pi hi jyōtiṣika surēṣūpapannaḥ ॥ 54 ॥
turyō'pi pauṣadhasthitō mandāgnirudaravēdanāvidhuraḥ । asahaḥ sahasāpi tatō duṣpramārjita sthaṇḍilē'dhyuṣitē ॥ 55॥
uccāraṁ kurvannapānadēśē gurusarpēṇa । daṣṭaḥ pīḍayā mr̥tastataḥ sa vyantarō jātaḥ || 56॥
tathā gr̥hītapauṣadhēnāpi vihitaḥ pañcamasutēna pañcamaḥ । aticāraḥ, tataḥ sō'pi hi kṣudhitaścintayannēvam ॥17॥

jaha bahurvajaṇa kanapēsalaṁ rasavaī karāvē । bhuṁjissāmi pahāē ēvamāī vicitatō || 58 ॥
navaghaṇanivaḍiyadussahavijjupahārāhaō marēūṇaṁ । nāgēsuṁ vavannō taiyabhavē pāvihī mōkkhaṁ ॥ 59 ॥
iya jāṇiūṇa bhavvā ! kalaṁkamukkaṁ sayā vayaṁ dharaha | annaha tubbhēhiṁ bhavē bhamiyavvaṁ bhūrikālaṁpi ||60 ||
suvisuddhavayāī mahaṣphalāī bhaṁgē ya kaḍuvivāgāīṁ । varamaggahaṇaṁ ciya tāṇa hōjja mā pacchaō bhaṁgō ॥ 61 ॥
varamagmimmi pavēsō varaṁ visudvēṇa kammuṇā maraṇaṁ । mā gahiyavvayamaṁsō mā jīyaṁ khaliyasīlassa ॥62॥
tathā,
gacchaṁtēṇa ṭhiēṇaṁ niccaṁ kiccāī taha kuṇatēṇa । maṇavaikāēsa sayā uvaōgō nēya mōttanvō ||63 ||
jaha jaha vayapariṇāmō vaḍḍhai jaha nēya huṁti aiyārā । jaha ya visuddhī jāyai viraīē taha vihēvvaṁ ॥ 64 ॥
dhannā hu sāhuṇōcci visidvvayapālaṇujjayamaī ya । avi tē cayaṁti jīyaṁ karaṁti pāvaṁ na īsiṁpi ॥
paricattataṇuvihasā visayavirattā vimukavāvārā । tavasaṁjamakayacittā garmati kālaṁ nirāsā ||66 ॥
iya cauraṁgasamagaṁ sammaṁ jō pōsahaṁ vigayadōsaṁ । pālēi pavalaghaṇakammakayavaraṁ sō lahuṁ ḍahai ||67 ||
dhannā gharavāvāraṁ duhavāraṁ paḍiharita kayapunnā । punnatihīsuvi kuvvaṁti pōsahaṁ dōsaha suddhaṁ ॥ 68 ॥
॥ iti pauṣadhavratāticāravipākē vaiśravaṇaputrāṇāṁ kathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
yathā bahuvyañjanapakvānnapēśalāṁ rasavartī kārayitvā । mōkṣyē prabhāta ēvamādi vicintayan ॥58॥
navaghananipatitadussahavidyutprahārāhatō mr̥tvā । nāgēṣūpapannastr̥tīyabhavē prāpsyati mōkṣam ॥59॥
iti jñātvā bhavyāḥ ! kalaṅkamuktaṁ sadā vrataṁ dharata । anyathā yuṣmābhirbhavē śramitavyaṁ bhūrikālamapi ॥60॥
suviśuddhavratāni mahāphalāni bhaṅgē ca kaṭuvipākāni । varamagrahaṇamēva tēṣāṁ bhavēnmā paścādbhaṅgaḥ ॥ 61 ॥
varamagnau pravēśō varaṁ viśuddhēna karmaṇā maraṇam । mā gr̥hītavratabhraṁśō mā jīvitaṁ skhalitaśīlasya ॥ 62 ॥
gacchatā sthitēna nityaṁ kr̥tyāni tathā kurvatā । manōvacaḥ kāyēṣu sadōpayōgō naiva mōktavyaḥ ॥63॥
yathā yathā vratapariṇāmō vardhatē yathā naiva bhavantyaticārāḥ । yathā ca viśuddhirjāyatē viratēstathā vidhātavyam ॥
dhanyāḥ khalu sādhava ēva viśiṣṭatratapālanōdyatamatayaśca । api tē tyajanti jīvitaṁ kurvanti pāpaṁ nēdapi ॥
parityaktatanuvibhūṣā viṣayaviraktā vimuktavyāpārāḥ । tapaḥsaṁyamakr̥tacittā gamayanti kālaṁ nirāśaṁsāḥ ॥ 66 ॥
iti caturaṅgasamagraṁ samyag yaḥ pauṣadhaṁ vigatadōṣam । pālayati prabaladhanakarmatr̥ṇōtkaraṁ sa laghu dahati ॥67॥
dhanyā gr̥havyāpāraṁ duḥkhavāraṁ parihr̥tya kr̥tapuṇyāḥ । puṇyatithiṣvapi kurvanti pauṣadhaṁ dōṣaṣaṁ śuddham ॥68॥

saddhāmuddhaṁ nāyāgayaṁ ca taha kappaṇijjamasaṇāī । dijjā gihī muṇīṇaṁ kālē pattāṇa pattāṇa ॥ 1 ॥
ullasiyavahalapulaō dāṇaṁ sāhūṇa dēi jō suddhaṁ । sō saṁtimaivva lahuṁ pāvai surasōkkhasaṁpatti ||2||
tathāhi ;-
suramajjaṇakayasōhaṁ suvannakamalālirāyahaṁsaṁ । māṇasasaraṁva supayaṁ nāmēṇa vilāsapuranayara || 3 ||
tatyatthi satyasatthōhakayasamō paṁḍiuvva, supayaṁḍō ! riutimiraharaṇasūrō sūrō nāmēṇa naranāhō ॥4॥
tasmatthi piyā bhajjā sajjā sayalēsu dhammakajjēsu । nāmēṇa vilāsavaī baitaṇucitēhi paibhattā ||5||
taha tattha asthi siṭṭī niru dhammiḍḍhī visiddhaāyā । savvaguṇāṇāhārō sāhārō nāma supasiddhō ||
tappaṇī sunayaṇā vimalā nāmēṇa sōmasamavayaṇā | tāṇaṁ ca suyā jāyā saṁtimaī nāma sīlavaī ||7||
rūvaṁ saīē sīlaṁ saīṇa suṁdarimaṁ ca amarīṇa । gahiūṇaṁ jā niuṇaṁ mannē vihiṇā viṇimmaviyā ||8||
mā saṁsārammi imā nivaḍau ainivbharaṁ mai pasattā । bālattēvi hu cattā paiṇā visayāna cāraṇa || 9 ||
aha annayā ya tīē diṭṭhō kusumāgarammi ujjāṇē । vahumuṇijaṇapariyariō uvasamasirisaṁgaō sugaō ||
sōhagganihī guṇarayaṇasāyarō vayaṇanijjiyachaṇidū । bahuvibuhavaṁdaṇijjō kalikālēṇaṁ akalaṇijjō ॥
vēllahalabāhujuyalō sārayasasisōmayāsamāinō | pīūsamuhayavayaṇō jiyamayaṇō kamaladalanayaṇō || 12 ||
siriabhayadēvasūrī apuvvasūrō sayāvi udaillō | saṁtāvaharō suthirō bahubuhasaṁgō asattāsō ॥ 13 ॥
taṁ vaṁdiūṇa tīē tassa samīvē nisāmiō dhammō । jaisāvayabhēēṇaṁ gahiō ya gihīṇa saddhammō ॥ 14 ॥
śraddhāśuddhaṁ nyāyāgataṁ ca tathā kalpanīyamaśanādi । dadyād gr̥hī munibhyaḥ kālē prāptēbhyaḥ pātrēbhyaḥ ॥ 1 ॥
ullasitabahalapulakō dānaṁ sādhubhyō dadāti yaḥ śuddham । sa śāntimatīva laghu prāpnōti surasaukhyasaṁpattim ॥
suramamāṇajana (suramajjana) kr̥taśōbhaṁ suvarṇakamalālirājahaṁsādayam ।
mānasasara iva suprajaṁ ( payaskaṁ ) nāmnā vilāsapuranagaram ||3||
tatrāsti śastaśa (śā) straughakr̥taśramaḥ paṇḍita iva, supracaṇḍaḥ । riputimiraharaṇasūraḥ śūrō nāmnā naranāthaḥ |
tasyāsti priyā bhāryā sajjā sakalēṣu dharmakāryēṣu । nāmnā vilāsavatī vacastanucittaiḥ patibhaktā ॥5॥
tathā tatrāsti śrēṣṭhī niścitaṁ dharmaddhirviśiṣṭācāraḥ । sarvaguṇānāmādhāraḥ sādhārō nāma suprasiddhaḥ ||6||
tatpraṇayinī sunayanā vimalā nāmnā sōmasamavadanā । tayōśca sutā jātā śāntimatī nāma śīlavatī ||7||
rūpaṁ ratyāḥ śīlaṁ śacīnāṁ saundarya cāmarīṇām । gr̥hītvā yā nipuṇaṁ manyē vidhinā vinirmitā ॥8॥
mā saṁsāra iyaṁ nipatatvatinirbharaṁ mayi prasaktā । bālatvē'pi hi tyaktā patyā viṣayāṇāṁ tyāgēna ॥9॥
aśānyadā ca tayā dr̥ṣṭaḥ kusumākara udyānē । bahumunijanaparikarita upaśamaśrīsaṁgataḥ sugataḥ ॥ 10 ॥
yanavirguṇaratnasāgarō vadananirjitakṣaṇēnduḥ । bahuvibudha vandanīyaḥ kalikālēnākalanīyaḥ ॥11॥
kōmalabāhuyugalaḥ śāradaśaśisōmatāsamākīrṇaḥ । pīyūṣasubhagavacanō jitamadanaḥ kamaladalanayanaḥ ॥ 12 ॥
śrī abhayadēvasūrirapūrvasūraḥ sadāpyudayī । saṁtāpaharaḥ susthirō bahubu saṅgō'sattrāsaḥ || 13||

atihī saṁvibhāgē kaō visēsēṇa taha ya iha niyamō । dāṇavayaparavasāē suhagurupāyāṇa sūlammi ||15||
jaha asaṇapāṇakhāimasāimabhēō caunviddāhārō । tā na maē bhōttavvō jāva na dinō jaijaṇassa ॥ 16 ॥
tō baṁdiūṇa sūriṁ siṁhaṁ gayā pālaē ya niyaniyamē । aha kaiyāvi vivāhē nimaṁtiyā niddhasuyaṇēṇa ॥17॥
tattha gayā sā gurugōravēṇa uvavēsiyā sayaṇamajjhē । bhōyaṇanimittamaha sā sāhūṇa payaṁ palōyaṁtī ॥18॥
jā ci tā pattō ēgō saṁghāḍagō muṇīṇa taō । tēhivi kiṁcivi dāum̐ visajjiō jhatti tō pacchā ||
saṁtimaīē paḍhamaṁ phalāī parivēsiuṁ samāraddhaṁ । tō tīē taṁ nisiddhaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ sāhūṇa jaṁ dinnaṁ ||20||
taṁ majjhavi parivēsaha virasaṁpi hu vaṁjaṇāirahiyaṁpi । sēsassa majjha niyamō tō tēhiṁ taṁpi parivi ॥ 21 ॥
sāhūṇa jaṁ na dinnaṁ na bhuṁjaē taṁ pahēvi gacchaṁtī । iya pabhaṇatē lōē bhōttūṇa gayā jaṇaya gēhē ||22||
iccāi jīē cariyaṁ nō sakkai buhagurūvi vannēuṁ । aha pattō ghaṇasapaō virahiṇijaṇadukkha saṁjaṇaō ||23||
tō satta dilāī ghaṇē ghaṇataravārāhi varisamāṇammi । nīraṭṭāvi na pattō kōvi muṇī tīē gēhammi ||24||
tō sāvi hu kuṇamāṇī uvavāsaṁ paidi chuhakkaṁtā | bhaṇiyā piūhiṁ vacchē ! pārasu aipīḍiyā taṁ si ||
sā bhai tāya ! bhuṁjēmi kahamahaṁ sugurusaṁnihāṇammi | atihivibhāgavayaṁ jaṁ paḍivannaṁ niyayavāyāē ||26||
tō savvahāvi thakkē mēhē sumuṇīṇa dinnadāṇammi । bhōttavvaṁ tāya ! maē iya sōūṇaṁ bhaṇai sōvi ||27||
iya mā karēsu vacchē ! niyamaṁ gaṁtūṇa sāhuvasahīē । varisaṁtēvi ahaṁ tē hakkārissāmi, sā bhai ॥ 28 ॥

taṁ vanditvā tayā tasya samīpē niśamitō dharmaḥ । yatiśrāvakabhēdēna gr̥hītaśca gr̥hiṇāṁ saddharmaḥ || 14 |
atithīnāṁ saṁvibhāgē kr̥tō viśēṣēṇa tathā cēti niyamaḥ । dānavrataparavaśayā śubhagurupādānāṁ mūlē || 15॥
yathā'śanapānakhādimasvādimabhēdaścaturvidhāhāraḥ । tāvanna mayā bhōktavyō yāvanna dattō yatijanāya || 16 ||
tatō vanditvā sūriṁ gr̥haṁ gatā pālayati ca nijaniyamān । atha kadāpi vivāhē nimantritā snigvasvajanēna ||
tatra gatā sā gurugauravēṇōpavēśitā svajanamadhyē । bhōjananimittamatha sā sādhūnāṁ padaṁ pralōkamānā ॥ 18 ॥
yāvattiṣṭhati tāvatprāptamēkaṁ yugmaṁ munyōstataḥ । tairapi kiñcidattvā visarjitaṁ jhaṭiti tataḥ paścāt ॥ 19॥
śāntimatyai prathamaṁ phalāni parivēṣituṁ samārabdham । tatastayā tanniṣiddhaṁ bhaṇitaṁ sādhubhyāṁ yaddattam ॥20॥
tamapi parivēṣa virasamapi hi vyañjanādirahitamapi । śēṣasya mama niyamastatastaistadapi pariviṣṭam ॥21॥
sādhubhyāṁ yanna dattaṁ na bhuṅktē tatpathyapi gacchantī । iti prabhaṇati lōkē muktvā gatā janakagēhē ॥22॥
ityādi yasyāścaritaṁ nō śaknōti budhagururapi varṇayitum । atha prāptō ghanasamayō virahistrījanaduḥkhasaṁ janakaḥ ॥
tataḥ sapta dināni ghanē ghanataradhārābhirvarṣati । nīrārthamapi na prāptaḥ kō'pi munistasyā gēhē ||24||
tataḥ sāpi hi kurvatyupavāsaṁ pratidina kṣudākrāntā । bhaṇitā pitr̥bhyāṁ vatsē ! pārayātipīḍitā tvamasi ||
sā bhaṇati tāta ! mujhē kathamahaṁ sugurusaṁnidhānē । atithivibhāgatrataṁ yatpratipannaṁ nijavācā ||26||
tataḥ sarvathāpi sthitē mēghē sumunibhyō dattadānē । bhōktavyaṁ tāta ! mayēti śrutvā bhaṇati sō'pi ॥ 27॥
iti mā kuru vatsē ! niyamaṁ gatvā sādhuvasatau । varṣatyapyahaṁ tān hakkārayiṣyāmi, sā bhaṇati ॥ 28 ॥

iccāi nirmāṇiūṇaṁ samuṭṭiyāē samaggaparisāē । atihīṇa saṁvibhāgē lacchīēbhiggahō gahiō ||26||
bhaṇiō kēvalanāṇī majjha gihē paidiṇaṁpi niyamuṇiṇō । paviyadā pahuṇā bhikkhāṇuraga kāuṁ ॥
i bhaṇi sā pattā niyagēhē pālaē ya vayamēyaṁ । puttaṁ samīhamāṇī na uṇō dhammāhilāsēṇa ||28||
aha puvvakammavasaō puttumpattī na sē samupyannā । siḍhiliyāṇapainnā tattō lōyāṇuvittīē ॥ 29 ॥
viyara kiṁciva dāṇaṁ viyaliyabhattī jaīṇa nicvaṁpi । aha annayā ya kammivi mahasavē rasavaraṁ paraṁ ||
niṣphāiūṇa tīē sayalajaṇō mēliō niyagihammi । bhōyaṇahēuṁ tattō iṁtē daṭṭūṇa muṇivasa hē ||31||
mugapiṁḍiyāē uvariṁ ṭhāva sālidāliyālīō । tāvari pakannaṁ tō pattā sāhuṇō tattha ||32||
anbhujaṁ vaṁdai paḍilābhatthaṁ ca uṭṭhaē tattō । gahiūṇaṁ sālikūraṁ tō sā bhaṇiyā muṇivarēhiṁ ||33||
nō kampai amhāṇaṁ saccittanihittayaṁ imaṁ jēṇa । tō laggā nidēu appāṇaṁ suṇai jaha lōō ||34||
hā hā ahaṁ ahanā jamimaṁ sāhūṇa nēya uvayariyaṁ । phāsūyamēsaṇiyaṁpi hu kuviyā tō bhaṇai niyacēḍiṁ ||
hā duhu tara vihiyaṁ bhagganirāsē ! imaṁ kuṇaṁtīē । pakannāivisiddhaṁ savvaṁ saccittanikkhivaṇā ||36||
tō amaṇunaṁ dāraṁ tēsi samuvaṭṭiyā maṇē tuṭṭā । bhagai ahō ! maha hatthā ēyaṁ dētīē na varhati ॥ 37 ॥
tō muṇibhattāē dēvayāē sikkhākaē karō tīē । sarkarōḍiō sabhattō bhivi pattammi avayariḍaṁ ||38||
dēvī jaṁpara duḍē māyāviṇi kūḍa kāriṇi aṇajjē ! । cārittarayaṇanihiṇōvi muṇivarē iya pacēsi ॥ 39 ॥
ityaticāraviśuddhaṁ yaḥ pālayatyatithi saṁvibhāgavatam । sa iha paralōkē'pi ca prāpnōti sumahākalyāṇam ॥
ityādi śrutvā samutthitāyāṁ samagraparṣadi । atithīnāṁ saṁvibhāgē lakṣmyā'bhigrahō gr̥hītaḥ ||26||
bhaṇitaḥ kēvalajñānī mama gr̥hē pratidinamapi nijamunayaḥ । prasthāpayitavyāḥ pramuṇā bhikṣārthamanugrahaṁ kr̥tvā ॥
iti bhaṇitvā sā prāptā nijagēhē pālayati ca vratamētat । putraṁ samīhamānā na punardharmābhilāṣēṇa ॥28॥
atha pūrvakarmavaśataḥ putrōtpattirna tasyāḥ samutpannā । śithilitadānapratijñā tatō lōkānuvr̥ttyā ||29||
vitarati kiñcidapi dānaṁ vigalitabhaktiryatibhyō nityamapi । athānyadā ca kasminnapi mahōtsavē rasavatīṁ pracurām ॥
niṣpādya tayā sakalajanō mēlitō nijagr̥hē । bhōjanahētōstata āyatō dr̥ṣṭvā munivr̥ṣabhān ||31||
mudgapiṇḍikāyā upari sthāpayati sā śālisūpasthālīḥ । tāsāmupari pakvānnaṁ tataḥ prāptāḥ sādhavastatra ॥
abhyutthāya vandatē pratilābhārtha cōttiṣṭhati tataḥ । gr̥hītvā śālikūraṁ tataḥ sā bhaṇitā munivaraiḥ ||33||
nō kalpatē'smākaṁ sacittanihitamidaṁ yēna । tatō lagnā ninditumātmānaṁ śr̥ṇōti yathā lōkaḥ ||34||
hāhā amanyā yadidaṁ sādhubhyō naivōpacaritam । prāsukamēṣaṇīyamapi hi kupitā tatō bhaṇati nijacēṭīm ॥
hā duṣṭhu tvayā vihitaṁ bhāgyanirāśē ! idaṁ kurvatyā । pakvānnādiviśiṣṭaṁ sarvaṁ sacittanikṣēpaṇāt ॥ 36 ॥
tatō'manōjñaṁ dātuṁ tēbhyaḥ samupasthitā manasi tuṣṭā । bhaṇatyahō ! mama hastāvētaddadatyā na vahataḥ ||37||
tatō munibhaktayā dēvatayā śikṣākr̥tē karastasyāḥ । sakarōṭika : sabhaktaḥ stambhayitvā pātrē'vatīrya ॥38॥
1kha, rōṭhiō ।

iya nidivi dēvīē bhaṇiyā lacchī halē ! na haṇiyā si । jīvadayacciya dhammō iya bhaṇivi asaṇaṁ pattā ॥
dhikkāriyā ya lacchī sayaṇēhiṁ taō ya thōvakālēṇa । utyaṁbhiyā ya tīē appaḍikaṁtā ya mariūṇa ||41 ॥
paṇapaniyāṇamajjhē vavannā sā taō bhavē bhamiṁuṁ । saṁpattabōhilāmā lahihī sā mōkkhasōkkhaṁpi ॥ 42 ॥
iya nāūṇaṁ bhavvā ! aiyāravivajjiyaṁ vayaṁ caraha । iharā ihalōēvi hu pāvissaha tikkhadukkhāī ||43||
॥ ityatithisaṁvibhāgē prathamāticāradr̥ṣṭāntaḥ ॥
dēvī jalpati duṣṭē māyāvini kūṭakāriṇi anāryē । cāritraratnanidhīnapi munivarāniti pravañcayasē || 39॥
iti ninditvā dēvyā bhaṇitā lakṣmīrhalē ! na hatāsi । jīvadayaiva dharma iti bhaṇitvādarśanaṁ prāptā ॥ 40 ॥
dhikkāritā ca sakṣmīḥ svajanaistataśca stōkakālēna । uttambhitā ca tayā'pratikrāntā ca mr̥tvā ॥ 41 ॥
praṇaparṇikānāṁ madhya upapannā sā tatō bhavē bhramitvā । saṁprāptabōdhilābhā lapsyatē sā mōkṣasaukhyamapi ॥ 43 ॥
iti jñātvā bhavyāḥ ! aticāravivarjitaṁ vrataṁ carata । itarathēhalōkē'pi hi prāpsyatha tīkṣṇaduḥkhāni ॥ 43 ॥

saccittē pihaī dēyaṁ jōtihivibhāgakayaniyamō । sō baṁdhai ghaṇakammaṁ jaha baddhaṁ vijayasiṭṭiṇīē || 1 ||

pavarakhamāharakaliyaṁ bahuvijjāhara surūvavēyahaṁ । jaṇavayasaya saṁkinnaṁ vitthinnaṁ bharahakhittaṁva ॥2॥
bhalipuramatthi puraṁ asthisamatyō supatthivō patthō । tatthāsi tahā sujasō sammadddviī nayara siṭṭhī || 3 ||
tassāsi piyā vijayā vijayapaḍāyavtra kāmabhavaṇassa | jiṇadhammammi pamattā saṁsattā kumayacārīsu ॥4॥
aha sujasō ujjāṇē pāusakālammi saṁṭhiyā guruṇō । samajaladhisūriṇō vimalanāṇiṇō baṁdaē gaṁtuṁ ||
suṇai ya jiṇidadhammaṁ padivasa sūridēsaṇāhihō । bhaṇai ya bhajjaṁ gaṁtuṁ namiḍaṁ mūrti susu dhammaṁ ॥ 6 ॥
sā bhai ahaṁ gacchāmi kiṁtu jai tē na diti maha niyamē । saccittaṇatayāṇaṁ tō siṭṭī bhai na kayāī ॥
tē diti valā niyamaṁ disaṁti dhammaṁ suṇēttu taṁ bhavvā । jē jē niyamē maggaṁti tāṇa tē dēti jahajōgaṁ ||
iya dhīraviu nīyā gurūṇa pāsammi siṭṭiṇā bhajjā । vaṁdē uvaiṭṭhā tāṇa purō dhammasavatthaṁ ॥9॥
sammattāisāvayavayāī kahiyāī tīē tō bhaṇiyaṁ । atihīṇa saṁvibhāgē maha niyama dēha pasiūṇa || 10॥
tō tīē purō guruṇā savittharaṁ sāhiūna aiyārē । dinō niyamō atihivvayammi taha kahiyamēyaṁ ca ।।
pōsahapāraṇayammi niyamā sāhūṇa jaṁ kira na dinaṁ । taṁ bhuṁjai na hu saḍḍhō tō suddhō pōsahō hōi ॥ 12 ॥
savvāraṁbhapattā gihiṇō sāhūṇa saṁvibhāgasmi । niccaṁ karēṁti juttaṁ kiṁ puṇa uvavāsapāraṇaē ? || 13 ||
jō niccaṁ ciya jaiṇō visuddhabhāvēṇa saṁvibhāgaṁti । bhattēṇa maṇunnēṇaṁ tē suhiṇō huṁti savvattha ||14||
sacittēna pidadhāti dēyaṁ yō'tithivibhāgakr̥taniyamaḥ । sa badhnāti ghanakarma yathā baddhaṁ vijayaśrēṣṭhinyā ॥1॥
pravarakṣamāgharakalitaṁ bahuvidyādhara surūpavaidagdhya ( tāḍhya ) m । janapadaśatasaṁkīrṇa vistīrṇa bharatakṣētramiva ॥2॥
bhaddilapuramasti puramarthisamarthaḥ supārthivaḥ pārthaḥ । tatrāsīttathā suyaśāḥ samyagdr̥ṣṭirnaraśrēṣṭhī ॥ 3 ॥
tasyāsītpriyā vijayā vijayapatākēva kāmabhavanasya | jinadharmē pramattā saṁsaktā kumata cāriṣu || 4 ||
atha suyaśā udyānē prāvr̥ṭkālē saṁsthitān । śamajaladhisūrīn vimalajñānān vandatē gatvā ॥ 5 ॥
śr̥ṇōti ca jinēndradharmaṁ pratidivasa sūridēśanāhr̥ṣṭaḥ । bhaṇati ca bhāryāṁ gatvā natvā sūriṁ śr̥ṇu dharmam ||6||
sā bhaṇatyahaṁ gacchāmi kintu yadi tē na dadati mama niyamān । sacittānantānāṁ tataḥ śrēṣṭhī bhaṇati na kadācit ||
tē dadati balānniyamaṁ diśanti dharmaṁ śrutvā taṁ bhavyāḥ । yānyānniyamānmārgayanti tēṣāṁ tāndadati yathāyōgyam ॥8॥
iti dhīrayitvā nītā gurūṇāṁ pāvēṁ śrēṣṭhinā bhāryā । vanditvōpaviṣṭā tēṣāṁ purō dharmaśravaṇārtham ॥9॥
samyaktvādiśrāvakatratāni kathitāni tayā tatō bhaṇitam । atithīnāṁ saṁvibhāgē mama niyamaṁ datta prasadya ॥
tatastasyāḥ purō guruṇā savistaraṁ kathayitvāticārān । dattō niyamō'tithivratē tathā kathitamētacca ॥ 11 ॥
pauṣadhapāraṇē niyamātsādhubhyō yakila na dattam । tad mujhē na hi śrāddhastataḥ śuddhaḥ pauṣadhō bhavēt ॥12॥
sarvārambhapravr̥ttā gr̥hiṇaḥ sādhūnāṁ saṁvibhāgē । nityaṁ kurvanti yatnaṁ kiṁ punarupavāsapāraṇē 1 ॥ 13 ॥
yō nityamēva yatīn viśuddhabhāvēna saṁvibhajantē । bhaktēna manōjñēna tē sukhinō bhavanti sarvatra ॥ 14 ॥

tē dhannā dhaṇavaiṇō jāṇa dhaṇaṁ nivamēva uvaōgaṁ । vaccai jiṇabhavaṇēsuṁ jaīsu sāhammiēsuṁ ca || 15 ||
jaṁ navi dhaṇaṁ dhaṇīṇaṁ uvaujjai dhammiēsa kajjēsu । kajjavasarisaṁ taṁ khalu bahuēṇavi kō guṇō tēṇa ? |
dhannā tē khalu purisā dāṇaṁ ditāṇa jāṇa sayakālaṁ । vōlīṇamājyaṁ suvihiyāṇa suvisuddha bhattīē ||17|
iya bhāvanāē sammaṁ pakkhālittā maṇōmalaṁ savvaṁ । ārāhaē visuddhaṁ sāvayadhammaṁ sayā sahō ||18||
iya niṇiūṇa saṁvēgaparavasā mā bhaṇēi muṇirāya । maha gēhē nicaṁpi hu pēsēva maṇīṇa jayaṁ ||19|
tō sūrī tayabhinu bhai jahā vahmāṇajōgēṇa । caraṇēṣu laggiūṇaṁ siṭṭī pabhaṇēi taṁ ēvaṁ ||20||
ēvaṁ patthara karivi garuyakārunaṁ । jamhā nannōvāō imīē bhavajalahitaraṇammi ||21||
Fair jaṁpa siddhī pattō samajjaō gēhē । paviyaṁ munipalaṁ siṭṭigi sūriṇā samaē ||22||
taṁ ī sāda vaṁda bhattīē siṭṭiṇā sahiyā । cavihaāhārēṇa paḍilāi suddhasaddhāē ||23||
ēvaṁ nircapi ō siṭī dāvā padavvaṁ । tō sā ciṁtā ēvaṁ bahuvvaō amhagēhammi ||24||
niyamō mavi hiō atihī niyamēva dāṇammi । tā taha karēmi jaha dōvi huti ēvaṁ vicitē ।
bahulabahulattaṇaō sāli pāī thāliyāṇuvariṁ । vijjauracibhiḍēhi kuṇai pihāṇāī savvattha ||26|
jaha sāhūṇana kappaṛa, aha sāhusamāgamammi taha caitra । paḍivatti kāū samuha dāṇamadāraṁ ||27||
sālimuhaṁ gahiraṁ muṇīhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ sacitapahiyamaṇaṁ । amhāṇaṁ nō kappaṛa tā yā giṇhēsu amkaē ।
tō sābhaṇē hī sāhūṇa akapiyaṁ imaṁ jāyē । kasmāriyā kīivi majjha apunē iya vihiyē ||29|
tē dhanyā dhanapatayō yēṣāṁ dhanaṁ nityamēvōpayōgam । vrajati jinabhavanēṣu yatiṣu sādharmikēṣu ca ॥ 15 ॥
yannaiva dhanaṁ dhanināmupayujyatē dhārmikēṣu kāryēṣu । tr̥ṇādyutka rasadr̥śaṁ tatkhalu bahunāpi kō guṇastēna ! ॥ 16 ॥
dhanyāstē khalu puruṣā dānaṁ dadatāṁ yēṣāṁ sadākālam । atikrāntamāyuḥ suvihitēbhyaḥ suviśuddhabhaktyā ॥ 17॥
iti bhāvanayā samyak prakṣālya manōmalaṁ sarvam । ārādhayati viśuddhaṁ śrāvakadharma sadā śrāddhaḥ || 18 ||
iti śrutvā
saṁvēgaparavaśā sā bhaṇati munirājam । mama gēhē nityamapi hi prēṣayitavyaṁ munyōryugam ॥ 19 ॥
tataḥ sūristadabhimukhaṁ bhaṇati yathā vartamānayōgēna । caraṇēṣu lagitvā śrēṣṭhī prabhaṇati tamēvam ॥20॥
ētāṁ pramādabahulāṁ nistārayata kr̥tvā gurukāruṇyam । yasmānnānyōpāyō'syā bhavajaladhitaraṇē ॥ 21 ॥
ityādi japitvā śrēṣṭhī prāptaḥ sabhāryō gēhē । prasthāpitaṁ muniyugalaṁ śrēṣṭhagr̥hē sūriṇā samayē ||22||
tadāyat sā dr̥ṣṭrā vandatē bhaktyā śrēṣṭhinā sahitā । caturvidhāhārēṇa pratilambhayati śuddhaśraddhayā ||23||
ēvaṁ nityamapi tataḥ śrēṣṭhī dāpayati pracuradravyam । tataḥ sā cintayatyēvaṁ bahuvyayō'smad ||24||
niyamō mayāpi gr̥hītō'tithīnāṁ nityamēva dānē । tasmāttathā karōmi yathā dvāvapi bhavata ēvaṁ vicintya ॥
māyābahuttrataḥ śālighr̥tādīnāṁ sthālīnāmupari । bījapūracirbhaṭaiḥ karōti pidhānāni sarvatra ॥ 26 ॥
yathā sādhūnāṁ na kalpatē, atha sādhusamāgamē tathaiva । pratipattiṁ kr̥tvā samuttiṣṭhati dānamanudātum ||27||
śālipramukhaṁ grahītuṁ munibhirgaṇitaṁ sacittāpahitamidam । asmākaṁ nō kalpatē tasmānmā gr̥hāṇāmatkr̥tē ॥ 28 ॥

hā hā ahaṁ abhaggā jāyā iccāi japamāṇī sā । annaṁpi hu viharāvasu iya bhaṇiyā sēdviṇā tattō ||
vallacaṇagāidavvaṁ dāūṇaṁ muṇivarē namasēuṁ । niyagēhāu visajjai aṇugammivi kaivapayāī ||31||

tataḥ sā bhaṇati hā viksādhūnāma kalpyamidaṁ jātam । karmacārikayā kayāpi mamāpuṇyairiti vihitam ||29||

tathā ghaṭṭayati sacittaṁ kadāpyāyatō munīśvarāna dr̥ṣṭvā । kadā karē karōti sanīrapātramapyēvamēva ॥32॥
jvalitajvalanasyōpari dharati vr̥takūrasthālyādikam । ityēvaṁ kurvatī sādhubhiḥ kramēṇa sā jñātā ||33||
bahukūṭakapaṭakalitaiṣā dātuṁ nēcchati kimapi । uparōdhēna śrēṣṭinastathāpi tē yānti bhikṣārtham ||34||
athānyadā mr̥tā sā vāsitavamanēna pīḍitā bāḍham । praṇaparṇikānāṁ madhya upapannā vyantarasurēṣu ||35||
tataścyutā ca bhramiṣyati katyapi bhavāṁstatō vidēhavarṣē । saṁprāptacaraṇaddhiḥ siddhimapi hi prāpsyati kramaśaḥ ॥

lacchīmaṁdiranāmaṁ nayaraṁ iha asthisutthiyajaṇōhaṁ । sappurisacariyacittāī jattha bhavaṇāī dīsaṁti || 2 ||

aha caunāṇī mūrī samōsaḍhō tattha bāhirūjjāṇē । ujjāṇapālayāṇaṁ pāsammi gaō tathā sōvi || 6॥
uggāhaṇiyā tēvi hu sūrīṇa pāyamūlammi । jiṇadhammaṁ nisuṇatā diṭṭhā tō sōvitaṁ sūri ||7||
vaṁdē uvaviṭṭhō nisuṇai dhammaṁ parēṇa viṇaṇa | dāṇatavasīlabhāvaṇamaiyaṁ maimōhanimmahaṇaṁ ||8||
tathāhi ;-
dāṇasīta bhāvaṇasaṁsi dhīrihiṁ dhammu caunvihu daṁsiu ।
uttarativihakaraṇa asamatyahaṁ dāṇadhammu paru ji jayai gittha ||9||
āraṁbhaniyattāṇaṁ akaritāṇaṁ akāravitāṇaṁ । dhammaṭṭhā dāyavvaṁ gihīhiṁ sāhūṇa jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 10॥
saṁta vajjhamaṇicaṁ jō ṭhāṇē dāṇapi nō daē । varāō tucchaō ēsō kaha sīlaṁ duddharaṁ gharē ? || 11 ||
jamhā dhannāṇaṁ ciya narāṇa dēyaṁ ca dāṇasattī ya । pattēṇa ya saha jōgō jāyai ciracinnapunnēhi ||12||
tathāhi: -
kālātikramadānaṁ dadapi hi tatphalaṁ na prāpnōti । yathā dēvacandra śrāddhaḥ śaṭhacittō dānakr̥taniyamaḥ ॥1॥
lakṣmīmandiranāma nagaramihāsti susthitajanaugham । satpuruṣacaritacitrāṇi yatra bhavanāni dr̥śyantē ॥ 2 ॥
tatra dr̥ptārimr̥ganāthadarpadalanē sarabhasaḥ śarabhaḥ । śaśikāntikīrtisurasariddhimācalō vajrasāranr̥paḥ ॥3॥
tathā dēvacandranāmā nivasati vaṇik prabhūtadhanakalitaḥ । tadbhāryā dēvaśrīḥ śrīriva harēḥ sadānugatā ॥ 4 ॥
atikr̥paṇaḥ prakr̥tyā na dadāti dānaṁ kadāpi kasyāpi ca । tathāpi hi dharmābhilāṣī na vilāsī yauvanasthō'pi ।
atha caturjñānaḥ sūriḥ samavasr̥tastatra bahirudyānē । udyānapālakānāṁ pārśva gatastadā sō'pi || 6 ||
udgrāhaṇikā hē tōstē'pi hi sūrīṇāṁ pādamūlē | jinadharmaṁ śr̥ṇvantō dr̥ṣṭāstataḥ sō'pi taṁ sūrim ||7||
vanditvōpaviṣṭaḥ śr̥ṇōti dharma parēṇa vinayēna । dānatapaḥ śīlabhāvanāmayaṁ matimōhanirmathanam ॥8॥
dānaśīlatapōbhāvanāśaṁsitō dhīrairdharmaścaturvidhō darśitaḥ ।
uttaratrividhakaraṇāsamarthānāṁ dānadharmaḥ parō jayati gr̥hasthānām ||9||
ārambhanivr̥ttēbhyō'kurvaddhayō'kārayadbhayaḥ । dharmārthaṁ dātavyaṁ gr̥hibhiḥ sādhubhyō yadbhaṇitam ॥10॥
sad bāhyamanityaṁ yaḥ sthānē dānamapi nō dadyāt । varākastuccha ēṣa kathaṁ śīlaṁ durdharaṁ gharēt ॥ 11 ॥
yasmāddhanyānāmēva narāṇāṁ dēyaṁ ca dānaśaktiśca । pātrēṇa ca saha yōgō jāyatē ciracīrṇapuṇyaiḥ ॥ 12 ॥

annē kavi pārvati kiṁpi punnērhi tēvi viṇattā । pāṇañcaravi viśvaṁti niyadhaṇaṁ nēya jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ || 14 ||

ajja sumattaṁ bhuttaṁ pāgavihī majjha ajja khalu saphalā । jaṁ gurubhōyaṇasēsaṁ bhuṁjissamahaṁti sō tayaṇu ||
aṇugamiūṇaṁ muṇiṇō bhuṁjai ya sayaṁ muṇīṇa uvvariyaṁ । muṇiṇōvi gurusavāsē savvē ēyaṁ nivēyaṁti ||
bhaṇiyā jō guruṇā yassa gihē sayāvi gaṁtavvaṁ । avasarai kiviṇasadō pāvai taha nijjaraṁ jēṇa ||

kē'pi nijajīvitamapi hi saṁdēhatulāyāṁ sthāpayitvā sadā । laṅghantē jalanidhiṁ nahi prāpnuvanti varāṭikāṁ tathāpi ॥
anyē kathamapi prāpnuvanti kimapi puṇyaistē'pi kr̥paṇatvāt । prāṇātyayē'pi vyayantē nijadhanaṁ naiva yadbhaṇitam ॥

ādarapravardhitā api hi sarvaprayatnēna rakṣitā nityam । kr̥paṇānāṁ dhanasamr̥ddhiḥ parakāryārthā kumārīva ॥ 16 ॥
athavā kēṣāmapi jāyatē dhanasaṁpattirapi dānaśaktirapi । tathāpi kēṣāmapi durlabhaḥ supātrasaṅgō bhavati yasmāt ॥
sarvārambhanivr̥ttaṁ nirmalacittaṁ pavitracāritram | niṣkāraṇakaruṇārasayuktaṁ pātraṁ jagati viralam ||18||

iti śrutvā dēvacandrēṇābhigrahō'tithisaṁvibhāgē । gr̥hītastata āhūtā bhikṣārtha nijagr̥hē munayaḥ ॥ 20 ॥
samayē tē'pi hi prāptā viśuddhasiddhāntasaṁgraha nimittam । gr̥hṇāntē tēna dattaṁ yathōcitaṁ bhaṇati sa ēvam ॥ 21 ॥
adya subhaktaṁ bhuktaṁ pākavidhirmamādya khalu saphalaḥ । yad gurubhōjana śēṣaṁ bhōkṣyē'hamiti sa tadanu ||22||
anugamya munīn muṅgē ca svayaṁ munīnāmudvr̥ttam । munayō'pi gurusakāśē sarva ētannivēdayanti ॥ 23 ॥
bhaṇitā yatinō guruṇaitasya gr̥hē sadāpi gantavyam । apasarati kr̥paṇaśabdaḥ prāpnōti tathā nirjarāṁ yēna ॥ 24॥
tataḥ pratidivasa munayō gacchanti gr̥hē tasya bhikṣārtham । prakr̥tyā tasya bhāryōdāracittā tataḥ pracuram ॥25॥

niyamajjaṁ kivaṇattā paḍilābhissāmi muṇivarē ahayaṁ । ityaṭṭē maha niyamō iva bhaṇi vīryādivasamma ||
sayamēva gavasa muṇiṇō āmaṁtiūṇa niyagēhē । āgēuṁ paḍilāi ghaēṇa pariyaddhamāṇēṇa ||28||
tō baṁdi visajja muṇiṇō annattha vihari pattā | sūrīṇa saṁnihāṇē tā puṭṭā sūriṇā muṇiṇō ||
kiṁ tassa gihē laddhaṁ tō muṇiṇā daṁsiyaṁ tayaṁ tuṣpaṁ । guruṇāvi ya tē bhaṇiyā tassa gihē nēya gaṁtavvaṁ ||
animaṁtiēhi, tattō taiyadiṇē āgaō nimaṁtē । muṇivarabhōyaṇakālē samaikkaṁtammi, tō guruṇā !!
bhaṇiyaṁ bhuttā muṇiṇō abhattaī na jēhi bhō ! vihiyē । sahasīlayāē khēyaṁ kuṇamāṇō purṇāvi sō bhaṇiō ॥

॥ ityatithisaṁvibhāgavatē tr̥tīyāticāraṣṭaṣṭāntaḥ ॥

nijabhārthī kr̥paṇatvātpratilambhayiṣyāmi munivarānaham । atrārthē mama niyama iti bhaṇitvā dvitīyadivasē ||

tatō vanditvā visr̥jati munayō'nyatra vihr̥tya prāptāḥ | sūrīṇāṁ saṁnidhānē tadā pr̥ṣṭāḥ sūriṇā munayaḥ ॥ 29 ॥

mā kuru bhadra ! khēdaṁ kāraṇatō'dya tava gēhē । na gatā munayastataḥ sa bhuktō gatvā gēhē ॥ 33 ॥

tasmād bhō tāticāraḥ kartavyō naiva buddhimadbhiḥ । aticārānkurvankramēṇa bhaṅgamapi sa karōti ||25||

niyadapi parakaṁ pattē gihamāgaēva jē viṁti । kayaatihidāṇaṇiyamā thērivva lahaṁti tē dukkha ॥ 1 ॥

asthi suvisālasālaggabhaggaravirahaturaṁgagaipasaraṁ । nāmēṇaṁ vissapuraṁ vissassavi vissuyaṁ nagaraṁ ||2||
jaṁ vā kulīṇavāsaṁ muṇīhiṁ parivajjiyaṁ haripuripi । hasai harahā sasasahara hasiyajiṇaharasihara sōhāhiṁ ||

duttāradūratīrē phuḍiē jāṇammi gajjamāṇassa । purisarasa jalahijjhē jaha phalayāsāyaṇaṁ saraṇaṁ ||9||

supāsanāha-cariammi-
jaha lōhāna suvanaṁ taṇāṇa dhanaṁ dhaṇāṇa rayaṇāṁī । rayaṇāṇa kāmarayaṇaṁ taha bhō dhammāṇa jiṇadhammō ||
jaha naṁdaṇaṁ vāṇaṁ dumāṇa kappadumō muṇīṇa jiṇō । purisāṇa cakkavaṭṭī tahēva dhammāṇa jiṇadhammō ॥ 16 ॥
nāyāṇaṁ nāgidō caṁdō nakkhattatāragāṇaṁ ca । asurāṇaṁ asuriṁdō tahēva dhammāṇa jiṇadhammō || 17 ||
dēva dēviṁdō jahava nariṁdō narāṇa maijjhammi । jaha migavaī migāṇaṁ taha bhō dhammāṇa jiṇadhammō ॥ 18 ॥
sō duvihō pannattā jaigihibhēēṇa paḍhamaō dasahā । bīō bārasabhēō kamēṇa sō dēi sivasōkja ||
hafa paḍhō gahiō bīō kēṇāvi tāṇa pāsammi । atihīṇa saṁvibhāgē niyamaṁ thērī pavajjē ॥20॥
aha sā gimmi pattā bhōyaṇasamayammi maggaē maggaṁ । sumuṇīṇaṁ jaṛa picchaṛa tō jacchai tēsimasaṇāī ||
aha annayā ya kammivi pattē para mūsavammi kēṇāvi । dinnō ya kalamasālī pāyasaghayasaṁjuō tīē ||22||
raddhā khīrī tattō samāgaō māsapāraṇayakālē । ēgō mahātavassī tīē gharē sāvi tō kiṁci ||23||
vallacaṇavādibhattaṁ viyarai māyāē bhaṇai muṇisamuhaṁ । jai parakīyā khīrī na havai tā tuha ahaṁ dēmi ||
kiṁ ēttiyapunnāī hōrhiti kayāi maha abhagāē । jaṁ muṇiṇō pāraṇaē paramannaṁ maha gihē hōhī || 25 ||
kiṁpuṇa cāulanīraṁ givha jahicchāē phāsuēsaṇīyaṁ । jai tuha paōyaṇaṁ tā ēyaṁ maha saṁtiyaṁ jamhā ||26||
muṇiṇāvi hu taṁ gahiyē pajjattīē gaō ya annattha । thērīēvi paramannaṁ pacchā bhutaṁ samapi ||27||
kaḍakaṭapamāṇaṁ bhuttārayaṇīē carimajāmammi | sammattēṇa samēyaṁ vamiyaṁ taṁ takkhaṇē caiva ||28||
tathā rāgamahāgirinadīpravāhapīḍana galasthitō jīvaḥ । prāpnōti kō'pi sapuṇyaḥ samyaktvataruvarālambam ॥ 14॥
yathā lōhānāṁ suvarṇa tr̥ṇānāṁ dhānyaṁ dhanānāṁ ratnāni । ratnānāṁ kāmaratna tathā bhō dharmāṇāṁ jinadharmaḥ ॥ 15 ॥
yathā nandanaṁ vanānāṁ drumāṇāṁ kalpadrumō munīnāṁ jinaḥ । puruṣāṇāṁ cakravartī tathaiva dharmāṇāṁ jinadharmaḥ ॥ 16 ॥
nāgānāṁ nāgēndracandrō nakṣatratārakāṇāṁ ca । asurāṇāmasurēndrastathaiva dharmāṇāṁ jinadharmaḥ || 17 ||
dēvānāṁ dēvēndrō yathā vā narēndrō narāṇāṁ madhyē । yathā mr̥gapatirmr̥gāṇāṁ tathaiva dharmāṇāṁ jinadharmaḥ ॥ 18 ॥
sadvividhaḥ prajñaptō yatigr̥hibhēdēna prathamō daśadhā । dvitīyō dvādaśabhēdaḥ kramēṇa sa dadāti śivasaukhyam ॥ 19 ॥
kēnāpi prathamō gr̥hītō dvitīyō kēnāpi tēṣāṁ pārśvē । atithīnāṁ saṁvibhāgē niyamaṁ sthavirā prapadyatē ॥ 20 ॥
atha sā gr̥hē prāptā bhōjanasamayē mārgayati mārgam । sumunīnāṁ yadi paśyati tatō yacchati tēbhyō'śanādi ॥ 21॥
athānyadā ca kasminnapi prāptē paramōtsavē kēnāpi । dattaśca kalamaśāliḥ pāyasaghr̥tasaṁyutastasyai ॥ 22 ॥
rādvā kṣairēyī tataḥ samāgatō māsapāraṇakālē । ēkō mahātapasvī tasyā gr̥hē sāpi tataḥ kiñcit ॥ 23 ॥
vallacaṇakādibhaktaṁ vitarati māyayā bhaṇati munisaṁmukham । yadi parakīyā sairēyī na bhavēttadā tē'haṁ dadyām ॥
kimētāvatpuṇyāni bhavēyuḥ kadācinmamābhāgyāyāḥ । yanmunēḥ pāraṇa kē paramānnaṁ mama gr̥hē bhavēt ? || 25 ॥
kintvōdananīraṁ gr̥hāṇa yadr̥cchayā prāsukaiṣaṇīyam । yadi tava prayōjanaṁ tadaitanmadīyaṁ yasmāt ॥ 26 ॥
munināpi hi tad gr̥hītaṁ paryāptyā gataścānyatra । sthavirayāpi paramānaṁ paścād bhuktaṁ samagramapi ||27||
1 ka. kha. varayaraō ।

ēsōvi dēva dāṇaṁ kimahaṁ asamatthaō imāōvi । iya buddhīē ditō lahēi naṁdōvva appaphalaṁ ||1||
tathāhi ;-
suragiridīharadaṁḍō vasumaicaḍḍō sōhanēhillō | jaṁbuddīvō dīvōvya asthi pajjalirataraṇisihō ||2||
tammi bharahaṁ sukhittaṁ tassa ya khaṁḍampi majjhimillampi । dāhiṇadisivahutilayaṁ sirinilayaṁ siripuraṁ asthi ।।
jammi jiṇabhavaṇakala hōyakalasakara niyarapasarapiṁjariyaṁ । gayaṇaṁgaṇaṁ virāya divi saṁjhanbharāyasamaṁ ॥4॥
saralā sadalā sahalā sauṇajaṇāsēviyā siṇiddhā ya । aṁtō vivajaṇā bāhi puṇa biḍaviṇō jattha ||5||
tammi nariṁdō naravidavaṁdiō divāyarōvva tēyassī । nihaṇiyaarivalatimirō riuvalamahaṇōtti nāmēṇa ||6॥
ēkkōtthi navari dōsō kittipiyā jassa vilasai jahicchaṁ । gayavīḍārigihē suvi jasēṇa nibaṁdhuṇā saddhiṁ ॥
taha salavaṇivariō nivasai tatthēva guṇagaṇagarihō । siddhī suṁdaranāmā taha naṁdō vasaī tatthēva ||8||
aha rannō mattakarī ālāṇaṁ bhaṁjiūṇa annadiṇē । agaṇatō paḍikārē cūraṁtō rahagharāī ya ||9||
caliō vāhi gaṁtuṁ taṁ sōūṇaṁ bhaḍēhiṁ pariyariō । saṁcaliō piṭṭīē turayārūḍhō nivōvita ||10||
pavaraphalāṇāhāraṁ sāhāraṁ picchiūṇa ujjāṇē । caliō bīsāmatthaṁ hatthī jā tassa chāyā ॥ 11 ॥
tā paramavakharalīṇō taṇuṇā jhīṇō maṇammi addīṇō । kāusragammi ṭhiō diṭṭhō sāhū, tayaṇu sōvi
saṁjāyajā isaraṇō paṇamai pakāī varamuṇiṇō । taṁ picchiūṇa rāyā raṁjiyahiyaō bhai ēvaṁ ||
acchariyaṁ acchariyaṁ jaṁ tiriōvi hu namasaē sāhuṁ । tō amhāṇavi ēsō nama̭saṇijjōtti iya bhaṇiuṁ ॥

ēṣō'pi dadāti dānaṁ kimahamasamarthō'smādapi । iti buddhayā dadallabhatē nanda ivālpaphalam ॥1॥
suragiridīrghadaṇḍō vasumatīpātraḥ saraōdhasnēhavān । jambūdvīpō dīpa ivāsti prajvalitr̥taraṇiśikhaḥ ॥ 2॥
tasminbharataṁ sukṣētraṁ tasya ca khaṇḍē madhyamē । dakṣiṇadigvadhūtilakaṁ śrīnilayaṁ śrīpuramasti || 3 ||
yasmiñjinabhavanakaladhautakalaśakaranikarapratarapiñjaritam । gaganāṅgaṇaṁ virājatē dinē'pi sandhyārāga samam ||4||
saralā sadalā saphalā saguṇa ( śakuna) janā sēvitāḥ snigdhāśca । antarvibhavādayajanā bahiṣpunarviṭapinō yatra ॥5॥
tasminnarēndrō naravr̥ndavanditō divākara iva tējasvī । nihatāribalatimirō ripubalamathana iti nāmnā || 6 ||
ēkō'sti kintu dōṣaḥ kīrttipriyā yasya vilasati yathēccham । gatavrīḍārigr̥hēṣvapi yaśasā nijabandhunā sārdham ॥
tatra sakalavaṇigvariṣṭhō nivasati tatraiva guṇagaṇagariṣṭhaḥ । śrēṣṭhī sundaranāmā tathā nandō vasati tatraiva ॥8॥
atha rājñō mattakaryālānaṁ bhaṅktvā'nyadinē । agaṇayanpratikārāṁścūrṇayan rathagr̥hādīṁśca ॥9॥
calitō bahirgantuṁ tat śrutvā bhaṭaiḥ parikaritaḥ । saṁcalitaḥ pr̥ṣṭhē turagārūḍhō nr̥pō'pi tataḥ ॥ 10 ॥
pravaraphalānāmādhāraṁ śākhinaṁ dr̥ṣṭrōdyānē । calitō viśrāmārthaṁ hastī yāvattasya cchāyāyām ॥11॥
tāvatparamākṣaralīnastanunā kṣīṇō manasyadīnaḥ । kāyōtsargē sthitō dr̥ṣṭaḥ sādhuḥ, tadanu sō'pi ||12||
saṁjātajātismaraṇaḥ praṇamati padapaṅkajāni varamunēḥ । tad dr̥ṣṭrā rājā rañjitahr̥dayō bhaṇatyēvam ॥ 13 ॥
āścaryamāścaryaṁ yattiryaṅapi hi namasyati sādhum । tatō'smākamapyēṣa namasyanīya itīdaṁ bhaṇitvā ॥ 14 ॥

turayāō uttarēuṁ baṁda rāyā sapariyaṇō sāhuṁ । ubūhi kariṁdaṁ unaviṭṭō suddhabhūmī || 15 ||
aha vasaṁtē kariṇō hallaphalaē muṇissa namaṇatthaṁ । saṁpattā suṁdaranaṁdasiṭṭiṇō dōvi jugavapi ॥ 16 ॥
jhāṇasamatī taō sāhū sāhēi tāṇa jidhammaṁ । samayammi nivō pucchai taṁ sāhuṁ rēiyakara kōsō ॥ 17॥
kō nivvēō jāō vayagahaṇē tujjha jōvvaṇabharēvi । bhaṇai muṇī saṁsārē sulahōcciyarāya ! nivvēō ॥

jaivi hu tujjhavi tasvaṇaō a jāēi kahavi vēragaṁ । iya kāraṇā kahijjai takkahaṇamasaṁgayaṁ iharā ॥
tadyathā; --
asthi puhaīpasiddhā ubavaṇavaṇa khaṁḍamaṁḍiudēsā । rayaṇaurī varanayarī tattha nivō rayaṇacūḍōti ॥21॥
rajjamaṇupālayētō amāvasāē nisāē sō rāyā । parihariyapāvakaccō visajjiyāsēsa avarōhō ||22||
vāsarayaṁ pavō suci jāva sijjamārūḍhō । dīvasihāē diṭṭhī tāva niviṭṭhā taō diṭṭō ||23||
ēgō tarapayaṁgō dīvasihaṁ pavisiuṁ ahilasaṁtō । karuṇāpaṇaiṇiparipēriēṇa tō citiyaṁ rannā ॥ 24 ॥
ahaha barāō ēsō aāṇavimōhiō paīcammi । paḍiūṇaṁ mā ujjhau tattō gahium̐ karayalēṇa ||25||
kuṁciyavivaraṇa bahiṁ pakkhittō āgaō puṇō puṇavi । vēlāvaṇagaṁ jāva ya tō ciṁtā naravaī ēvaṁ ||26||
jaha niṇijjai lōē kila purisō rakkhiō uvāēhiṁ । vāsasayāīvi jīvai karēmi tā kiṁpuvāyaṁ sē ।।

turagāduttīrya vandatē rājā saparijanaḥ sādhum । upabr̥ṁdha karīndramupaviṣṭaḥ śuddhabhūmau ॥ 15॥

athōpaśāntē kariṇa ākulatvē munērnamanārtham । saṁprāptau sundaranandaśrēṣṭhinau dvāvapi yugapadapi ॥ 16 ॥
dhyānasamāptau tataḥ sādhuḥ kathayati tayōrjinadharmam । samayē nr̥paḥ pr̥cchati taṁ sādhuṁ racitakarakōśaḥ ॥ 17 ॥

tavāpi kintu manyē'dyāpi karma nivārakamasti । cāritrāvaraṇaṁ tasmāt śrūyatāmasmadvratahētum ||19||
yadi hi tavāpi tacchravaṇataśca jāyatē kathamapi vairāgyam । iti kāraṇātkathyatē tatkathanamasaṁgatamitarathā ॥
asti pr̥thivīprasiddhōpavanavanapaṇḍamaṇḍitēōddēśā । ratnapurī varanagarī tatra nr̥pō ratnacūḍa iti ॥21॥
rājyamanupālayannamāvāsyāyā niśi sa rājā । parihr̥tapāpakr̥tyō visr̥ṣṭāśēṣāvarōdhaḥ ||22||
vāsagr̥haṁ praviṣṭaḥ sukhacēṣṭō yāvacchayyāmārūḍhaḥ । dīpaśikhāyāṁ dr̥ṣṭistāvanniviṣṭā tatō dr̥ṣṭaḥ ||23||
ēkastaralapataṅgō dīpaśikhāṁ pravēṣṭumabhilaṣan । karuṇāpraṇayinīpariprēritēna tataścintitaṁ rājñā ॥ 24 ॥

kuñcitavivarēṇa bahiṣprakṣipta āgataḥ punaḥ punarapi । vēlāpañcakaṁ yāvacca tataścintayati narapatirēvam ॥26॥
yathā śrūyatē lōkē kila puruṣō rakṣita upāyaiḥ । vaśatānyapi jīvati karōmi tasmātkamapyupāyamasya ॥27॥

supāsanāha - cariśrami
maraṇaparittāṇamavassamatthi, jai jīvihī na puṇa ēsō । tā maccaparittāṇaṁ natthi hu bhuvaṇammi kastavi ya ।
iya citiūṇa rannā palōiyāī samaggapāsāī । tō dihō ya samuggō ēgō ughāḍiyadavārō ||30||
tō salahō gahiūṇaṁ pakkhittō tattha ḍhakkiuṁ dāraṁ । niyapāsē taṁ kāuṁ suttō rāyā samāhīē ॥ 31 ॥
farar fagaō cita kiṁ tassa maha uvāraṇa | jāyaṁ, tō ya samu ugghāḍivi picchaē jāva ||
tāva na piccha salahaṁ rayaṇujjōēṇa niru gavidvēpi । ēkaṁ gharakōiliyaṁ tattha nilukaṁ palōēi ||33||
tō ciṁtēṛa nariṁdō nūṇaṁ ēsō imāē giliutti । hī saṁsārasahāō sabvō khaṇadinōti ||34||
kila rakkhābuddhīē ēsa samuggē mayā parikkhittō। ētthāvē imīē gasiō naya mōkkhō asthi vihiyassa ॥
jittiyamittaṁ kammaṁ vihiyaṁ jīvēṇa puvvajammammi । tattiyamittaṁ ciya dēi sō phalaṁ natthi saṁdēhō ॥ 36 ॥
vijjā kuṇati kiriyaṁ sahajōēhiṁ maṁtabalajuttā | naya cāryati barāyā puvvakayaṁ kammamavaṇēḍaṁ ||37||
pañcakkhaṁ jēṇa imō maē payēgō samuggaē khittō । giliō gilōiyāē kō kira maccūē rakkhijjā ? ||
tō natthi ittha saraṇaṁ jayammi sacarācarammi jīvāṇa । puvyavihiyaṁ niyaṁ ciya kammaṁ sumahamuvaṇē ||
tā kīsa ēsa lōō na muyai gharavāsapamuhavāvāraṁ । ghaṇarāgadōsamr̥ḍhō siḍhilō saddhamma kiriyāē ? ||40||
ēvaṁ narāeiast sahasā vēraggamaggacaḍiyassa । jāyaṁ jāīsaraṇaṁ kammakkhayauvasamavasē ॥41॥
tō tēṇaṁ vinnāō punvabhavō supariyaṁ ca jaṁ paḍhiyaṁ । gayacārittāvaraṇō jhatti virattō bhavaduhassa ||42 ||
mr̥tyumukhādēnaṁ yadi kathamapi hi rakṣituṁ śakṣyāmi । tadā jñāsyāmyavaśyaṁ vaidyauṣadhamantratantrēḥ ॥28॥
maraṇaparitrāṇamavaśyamasti, yadi jīviṣyati na punarēṣaḥ । tadā mr̥tyuparitrāṇaṁ nāsti hi bhuvanē kasyāpi ca ॥
iti cintayitvā rājñā pralōkitāni samagrapārśvāni । tatō dr̥ṣṭaśca samudra ēka udghāṭitadvāraḥ ॥ 30 ॥
tataḥ śalabhō gr̥hītvā prakṣiptastatrācchādya dvāram । nijapārśvē taṁ kr̥tvā suptō rājā samādhinā ॥ 31 ॥
nidrākṣayē vibuddhaścintayati kiṁ tasya mamōpāyēna । jātaṁ, tataśca samudramudghāṭya paśyati yāvat ||32||
tāvanna paśyati śalabhaṁ ratnōdyōtēna niścitaṁ gavēpitamapi । ēkāṁ gr̥hōlikāṁ tatra nilīnāṁ pralōkatē ॥ 33॥
tataścintayati narēndrō nūnamēṣō'nayā gīrṇa iti । hī saṁsārasvabhāvaḥ sarvaḥ kṣaṇadr̥ṣṭanaṣṭa iti ||34||
kila rakṣā buddhacaiva samudrē mayā parikṣitaḥ । atrāpyanayā grastō naca mōkṣō'sti vihitasya ||35||
yāvanmātraṁ karma vihitaṁ jīvēna pūrvajanmani । tāvanmātramēva dadāti sa phalaṁ nāsti saṁdēhaḥ || 36 ||
'vaidyāḥ kurvanti kriyāmaiāṣadhayōgairmantrabalayuktāḥ । na ca śaknuvanti varākāḥ pūrvakr̥taṁ karmāpanētum ||37||
pratyakṣa yēnāyaṁ mayā pataṅgaḥ samudrē kṣiptaḥ । gīrṇō gr̥hōlikayā kaḥ kila mr̥tyōṁ rakṣēt ? ||38||
tatō nāstyatraṁ śaraṇaṁ jagati sacarācarē jīvānām । pūrvavihitaṁ nijamēva karma sukhamasukhamupanayati ॥ 39 ॥
tataḥ kasmādēga lōkō na muñcati gr̥havāsapramukhatryāpāram । vanarāgadvēṣamūḍhaḥ śithilaḥ saddharmakriyāyām ॥ 40 ॥
ēvaṁ narādhipatēḥ sahasā vairāgyamārgacārṭatasya । jātaṁ jātismaraṇaṁ karmakṣayōpaśamavaśēna ॥41॥

paṁcamuṭṭhilaō samaṇō parihariyasayalasāvajjō । varasēyaṁvaradhārī jāō sarayammi jalaubva ||43||
saṁnihi dēvayā tammi samayasmi tassa naravaiṇō । muṇimaggadaṁsaṇaṭṭā samappiyaṁ tassimaṁ liṁga ||44 ||
dhavalaṁ vimalaṁ kōmalasamhalaṁ samayabhaṇiyaparimāṇaṁ । bahupāvaraōharaṇaṁ syaharaṇaṁ bhavyamaṇaharaṇaṁ || 45||
muhapōttiyā ō bīyā pattāīyāī satta annāī । iya navavahisaṇāhō jāō pattēyabuddhō sō || 46 ॥
paccūsa nāūṇaṁ umghāḍiyagihakavāḍasaṁpuḍaō | sīhakisōrōvva guhāō niggaō, taṁ ca taha daṭṭhē ॥
sijjāvālī bhaṇai ammō ! dhāvēha ēsa tumha pahū। sēyavayavēsadhārī ēgāgī gaccha gihāō ||48 ||
taṁ suṇiūṇaṁ sahasā pahāviō pakkhalaṁtagaipasarō । sayalaṁtēuralōō vimukapukāra karuṇasarō ॥ 49 ॥
taha saṁbhamavasakhalamāṇacalaṇaraṇajhaṇiranēurarakhōhō । vāravilāsiṇilōō viluliyagurukuṁtalakalāvō ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ ca tāhi ēvaṁ hā daya ! dayāsamudda ! jayatāmi ! । kiṁ avakayamamhēhiṁ jaṁ cattā ēkahalāē ? ||
taha savilāsavilāsiṇinahāvalīvalaṇavadiō nicaṁ । sō cihurabharō bhamarōlisāmalō luṁciō kēṇa ? ||
kappūrapūracaṁdaṇamayaṇāhisamuāēkalaliyasmi । vāsahara mmivi tuṁbī kattha taē pāviyā ēsā ? ॥ 53 ॥
daviyaridāraṇasahaṁ sahai karē tumha sajalakaravālaṁ । unnāmayadasiyāṇa ēvaṁ puṇa pichaḍamajōgaṁ ||24||
ēvaṁ pipalavamāṇō aṁḍarapauramētimāijaṇō । siṁhāvalōiē ṇatri palōiō nēya maṇayaṁpi ॥ 55 ॥
sōhaṁ nariṁda ! samaṇō kahiyē jassērisa maē cariyaṁ । tō bhaṇai niyō taṁ ciya sakayatyō punnabhāgī ya ॥
tatastēna vijñātaḥ pūrvabhavaḥ smr̥taṁ ca yatpaṭhitam । gatacāritrāvaraṇō jhaṭiti viraktō bhavaduḥ khāt ॥ 42 ॥
kr̥tapañcamuṣṭilōcaḥ śramaṇaḥ parihr̥tasakalasāvadyaḥ । varaśvētāmbaradhārī jātaḥ śaradi jalada iva ॥ 43॥
saṁnihitadēvatayā tasminsamayē tasya narapatēḥ । munimārgadarśanārthaṁ samarpita tasmā idaṁ liṅgam ॥ 44 ॥
dhavalaṁ vimalaṁ kōmalasapakṣmalaṁ samaya bhaṇitaparimāṇam । bahupāparajōharaṇaṁ rajōharaṇaṁ bhavya manōharaṇam ||45 ॥
mukhavatrikā tu dvitīyā pātrādikāni saptānyāni । iti navōpavisanāthō jātaḥ pratyēkabuddhaḥ saḥ || 46 ॥
pratyūṣaṁ jñātvōdghāṭitagr̥hakapāṭapuṭataḥ । siṁhakiśōra iva guhātō nirgataḥ, taṁ ca tathā dr̥ṣṭvā ॥47॥
śayyāpālī prabhaṇatyamba ! dhāvataiṣa yuṣmatprabhuḥ । śvētapaṭavēṣavāryēkākī gacchati gr̥hāt ॥48॥
tat śrutvā sahasā pradhāvitaḥ prakhaladgatiprasaraḥ । sakalāntaḥ puralōkō vimuktapūtkārakaruṇasvaraḥ ॥ 49 ॥
tathā saṁbhramavaśaskhalacaraṇaraṇaraṇitr̥nūpuraravaughaḥ । vāravilāsinīlōkō vilulitagurukuntalakalāpaḥ ॥ 90 ॥
bhaṇitaṁ ca tābhirēvaṁ hā dayita! dayāsamudra ! jagatsvāmin! | kimapakr̥tamasmābhiryattyaktā ēkahēlayā ! ॥ 51 ॥
tathā savilāsavilāsinīnakhāvalīvalanavardhitō nityam । sa cikurabharō bhramarālīśyāmalō luñcitaḥ kēna ? ॥
karpūrapūracandanamr̥ganābhisamudvaikalalitē । vāsagr̥hē'pi tumbī kutra tvayā prāptaiṣā ? ॥53॥
tāridāra sahō rājatē karē tava sajalakaravālaḥ । ūrjāmayadaśānāmētatpunaḥ picchamayōgyam ||54 ॥
ēvamapi pralapannantaḥpurapracuramantryādijanaḥ । siṁhāvalōkitēnāpi pralōkitō naiva manāgapi ||15||
sō'haṁ narēndra ! śramaṇaḥ kathitaṁ yasyēdr̥śaṁ mayā caritam । tatō bhaṇati nr̥pastvamēva kr̥tārthaḥ puṇyabhāgī ca ॥56॥

ittiyamittaṇavi tujjha jasa jāō maṇammi nivvēō । nivvēyakāraṇāī ēvi bahuyāī dihāī ॥57॥
taha hu ahira sāmiya! vōmi pāvaṭhāṇēṣu । tā kāūna pasāyaṁ kahēsu maha samuciyaṁ dhammaṁ ॥
tō muṇiṇā sē kahiō dhammō duvihōvi, tēṇa gihidhammō । paḍivannō taha suṁdaranaṁdēhiṁ atihivayamēgaṁ ॥
aha kariṇō vr̥ttaṁ pucchara rāyā muṇī bhaṇai sammaṁ । jāṇē na kiṁtu ēsō bhaddagabhāvēṇa maha paṇaō ||
tō sahayāraṭhiēṇaṁ jakkhēṇaṁ sāhiyaṁ jahā ēsō । saṁjāyajāisaraṇō sāhuṁ dadrūṇa paḍibuddhō || 61 ||
puvvabhavē jaṁ ēsō gitthabhāvē guṇissa chattadharō । āsi, taō pahuvirahē mariūṇa karī samupapannō ||
vijhagiripāyamūlē gahiō gayaēhiṁ tuha pāsē । vivikaṇiō āuṁ iya sōūṇaṁ sasaṁvēgaṁ ॥ 63 ॥
muṇiṇāvi karī bhaṇiō sammattaṁ giṇha dēsavirahaṁ ca । tēṇavi tahatti vihiyē rāyāvi namasiuṁ sāhuṁ ||
pattō gimmi kariṇā saha suṁdaranaṁdasidviṇōvi tahā । niyaniyamihēsu pattā kuṇati dhammaṁ jahāgahiyaṁ ।।
aha annayā ya muṇiṇō guṇiṇō guṇacaṁdariṇō samiṇō । ujjāṇaragadē sē samōsaḍhā suddhabhūmī9 ॥ 66 ॥
tatthamaha tē suṁdaranaṁdā narēsarēṇa samaṁ । saṁvattā ujjāṇē vaidivi bhattīē upaviṭṭhā || 67 ||
nisuti suddhadhammaṁ, ahannayā suṁdarī payattēṇa । vaṁdivi tē āmaṁta niyagihē nēi samapi ॥ 68 ॥
jiviṁdatthaṁ pattō sūrī sapariyarō tattha | vaṁdēuṁ jiṇapaḍimaṁ ubavō kahara jidhammaṁ ॥ 69 ॥
tō suṁdarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ namiūṇaṁ vatthapattabhattāṇaṁ । gahaṇāṇuragahamahaṁ taṁ karēsu muṇināha ! tō sūrī || 7 ||
tayabhimuhaṁ bhai imaṁ suddhaṁ vatthaṁ havēi taṁ caiva । jaṁ dōsavippakkaṁ suṇēhi dōsā imē tē ya ॥ 71 ॥

iyanmātrēṇāpi tava yasya jātō manāsa nirvēdaḥ । nirvēdakāraṇāni mayāpi bahūni dr̥ṣṭāni ||17||
tathāpi hyadhikataramahaṁ svāmin! vartē pāpasthānēṣu । tasmātkr̥tvā prasādaṁ kathaya mama samucitaṁ dharmam ॥58॥
tatō muninā tasmai kathitō dharmō dvividhō'pi tēna gr̥hidharmaḥ । pratipannastathā sundaranandābhyāmatithivratamēkam ॥
atha kariṇō vr̥ttāntaṁ pr̥cchati rājā munirmaṇati samyak । jānē na kintvēṣa bhadrakabhāvēna māṁ praṇataḥ ॥ 60 ॥
tataḥ sahakārasthitēna yakṣēṇa kathitaṁ yathaipaḥ । saṁjātajātismaraṇaḥ sādhuṁ dr̥ṣṭrā pratibuddhaḥ ॥ 61 ॥
pūrvabhavē yadēṣa gr̥hasthabhāvē munēśchatravaraḥ । āsīt, tataḥ prabhuvirahē mr̥tvā karī samutpannaḥ ॥ 62 ॥
vindhyagiripādamūlē gr̥hītō gajabandhakaistavapārśvē । vikrīta ānīyēti śrutvā sasaṁvēgam || 63 ||
munināpi karī bhaṇitaḥ samyaktvaṁ gr̥hāṇa dēśaviratiṁ ca । tēnāpi tathēti vihitaṁ rājāpi namasthitvā sādhum ||
prāptō gr̥hē kariṇā saha sundaranandaśrēṣṭhināvapi tathā । nijanijagr̥hayōḥ prāptau kurutō dharmaṁ yathāgr̥hītam ॥ 65 ॥
athānyadā ca munayō guṇinō guṇacandrasūrayaḥ śaminaḥ । udyānaikadēśē samavasr̥tāḥ śuddhabhūmau ॥66॥
tadvandanārthamatha tau sundaranandau narēśvarēṇa samam । saṁprāptāyānē vanditvā bhaktyōpaviṣṭau ॥ 67 ॥
śr̥ṇutaḥ śuddhadharmam, athānyadā sundaraḥ prayatnēna । vanditvā tānāmantrayati nijagr̥hē nayati samamapi ॥ 68 ॥
jinapratimāvandanārthaṁ prāptaḥ sūriḥ saparikarastatra । vanditvā jinapratimāmupaviṣṭaḥ kathayati jinadharmam ॥ 69 ॥
tataḥ sundarēṇa bhaṇitaṁ natvā vastrapātrabhaktānām । grahaṇānugrahamatha tvaṁ kuru muninātha ! tataḥ sūriḥ ॥ 70||

tadabhimukhaṁ bhaṇatīdaṁ śuddhaṁ vastraṁ bhavati tadēva । yad dōṣavipramuktaṁ śr̥ṇu dōṣā imē tē ca ॥ 71 ॥

taṇhāurēṇa rannā bhaṇiō mittō jahā gavēsēha । katthavi jalaṁ suvimalaṁ tō mittō taṁ gavēsēuṁ ॥ 15 ॥
jā jāi vamaggaṁ matō pāṇiyaṁ tā suṇēi । sajalajalavāhagalagajjigahiravāṇi maṇūsassa || 16 ||
tō tayaṇusāraō jāi jāva tā picchaē muṇi ēgaṁ । suhathaṁḍilōvi harinaulāihi pariyariyaṁ ||17||
sajjhāyataṁ mahurajjhaṇīē tō namivi bhaṇai tayabhimuhaṁ । bhayavaṁ ! kāruṇiya ! kahēsu majjha iha kiṁpi jalaṭhāṇaṁ ||

saṁjāyajāisaraṇā rannō nāmassa savaṇaō yāvi । ēgā hariṇī diṭṭīē sanniḍaṁ nēi taṁ samagaṁ ||20||

pattō hariṇīē samaṁ rannō pāsamma pāiō nīraṁ । rāyā pucchara mittaṁ kā aisā kahasu maha hariṇī 1 ||22||

iya sōūṇaṁ hariṇīē saha nivō jāi muṇisayāsammi | vaṁdēi bhattijuttō muṇīvitaṁ dhammalābhēṇa ||24||
āṇaṁdēḍaṁ disaī sē jiṇadhammaṁ dubhēyamavi sōvi । nimuṇēi payattēṇaṁ hariṇīmittarhi saṁjuttō ॥ 25 ॥
tō patthāvē pucchara rāyā taṁ suṇivaraṁ migīvi imā । kaha majjha paṇayabhāvaṁ daṁsai pasiūṇa sāhē ||26||
avahinnāṇēṇa taō nāūṇaṁ muṇivarō kahai savvaṁ । puṇtrabhavaṁ hariṇīē nivassa puṇa tabbhava cēva ॥27॥
tadyathā;-
āsi imā tu ghariṇī saraṇī ghaṇanēha salilabharabhariyā । tuhamaṇamaṇōramārāmakāmakaṁ kēllisā hissa ||28||
tr̥ṣṇāturēṇa rājñā bhaṇitaṁ mittraṁ yathā gavēṣayata । kutrāpi jalaṁ suvimalaṁ tatō mittraṁ tad gavēṣayitum ||15||
yāvadyāti stōkamārga mārgayan pānīyaṁ tāvat śr̥ṇōti । sajalajalavāhagala garjigabhīravāṇī manuṣyasya ॥ 16 ॥
tatastadanusāratō yāti yāvattāvatpaśyati sunimēkam । śubhasthaṇḍilōpaviṣṭaṁ harinakulādibhiḥ parikaritam ॥
svādhyāyantaṁ madhuradhvaninā tatō natvā bhaṇati tadabhimukham । bhagavankāruṇika ! kathaya mamēha kimapi jalasthānam ॥
turagāpahr̥tamahāsēnanarapatiryēna tiṣṭhati klāntaḥ । tr̥ṣṇayā vananikuñjē, yāvad dadāti nōttaraṁ sādhuḥ ॥19॥
saṁjātajātismaraṇā rājñō nāmnaḥ śravaṇataścāpi । ēkā hariṇī dr̥ṣṭā saṁjñāya nayati taṁ samam ॥ 20 ॥
satpr̥ṣṭhē lagnaḥ sō'pi gatō yāvatpalvalē tatra । padminīpatrasusaṁsthitapuṭaṁ bhr̥tvā nīrasya ॥21॥
prāptō hariṇyā samaṁ rājñaḥ pārśvē pāyitō nīram । rājā pr̥cchati mitraṁ kaiṣā kathaya māṁ hariṇī ||22||
sa bhaṇati munisakāśē dr̥ṣṭaiṣā mamāpyētayā । darśitamētatsalilaṁ karuṇārasarasikahr̥dayayā ||23||
iti śrutvā hariyā saha nr̥pō yāti munisakāśē | vandatē bhaktiyuktō munirapi taṁ dharmalābhēna ||24||
ānandya diśati tasmai jinadharmaṁ dvibhēdamapi sō'pi । śr̥ṇōti prayatnēna hariṇāmitvābhyāṁ saṁyuktaḥ ॥ 25 ॥
tataḥ prastāvē pr̥cchati rājā taṁ munivaraṁ mr̥gyapīyam । kathaṁ mama praṇayabhāvaṁ darśayati prasadya kathaya ॥ 26॥
avadhijñānēna tatō jñātvā munivaraḥ kathayati sarvam । pūrvabhavaṁ hariṇyā nr̥pasya punastadbhavamēva ||27||
āsīdiyaṁ tava gr̥hiṇī saraṇirdhanasnēha salilabharabhr̥tā । tvanmanōmanōramārāmakāma kaṅkēlliśākhinaḥ ॥28॥

malayacaṁda kahā ।
1
647
baṁdhumanāmē ahannā tī vāsabhavaṇammi | nēhaparikkhā hēḍaṁ vilāsiṇī āṇiyā tumaē ॥ 29 ॥
tīē samaṁ khaṇamēgaṁ gamiūṇa visajjiyā taō ēsā । uvavaṇamajjhammi gayā citēumimaṁ samādattā ॥ 30 ॥
piyasaṁgakāraṇāī savvāīvi huṁti ēttha dukkha । ī । sō jīē na saṁjāō sā mahilā sutthiyā nicaṁ ॥
dhannāu tāu mannē kumārasamaṇīō samiyapāvāō । jāsimavamāṇamūlē visayasuhē nō maī jāyā ||32||
kiṁ pimmaṁ kō va piō kō viraō kērisī visayataṇhā । ēyamaputraṁ jāsi ṇamō ṇamō tāṇa samaṇīṇaṁ ।।
tāsiṁ suddhaṁ jīyaṁ jāhaṁ tavatāviē taṇukuḍīrē । dāhabhayā iva na kayaṁ mayaṇēṇa payaṁ maṇāpi ||34||
sacciya dhannā sā punnabhāyaṇaṁ jīē natthi piyasaṁgō | vaṇavasirāṇavi niccaṁ āvai nidāsuhaṁ tāṇa ||35||
jāṇa na jāō hiyaē puhaī bhamaṁtāṇa vallahō kōi । suhiyāṇa savvakālaṁ namō namō tāṇa ramaṇīṇa ॥
kiñca ।
pavaṇapa hillira jalanihitaraṁgaraṁgaṁtavēviraṁgassa । aṇuharai navari sasiṇō pēmmaṁ taralattaṇaguṇēṇa ||37||
dūraṭṭhiyaṁ parōkkhaṁ suhamasuhaṁ gōyaraṁ gahāṇaṁ ca । jāṇati jē viyaḍḍhā pēmmagaīē jaḍā tēvi || 38 ।।
tathāhi ;-
taṁ niviḍaviyaḍanēhaṁ vihaḍatēṇaṁ jhaḍatti rē divva ! । kiṁ pātra ! pātriyaṁ tē amayarasē khēvium̐ garalaṁ ? ॥39॥
iyatikkhadukkhamyagavaṇāī muhuṁ muhuṁ payaṁpaṁtī । hiyayaṁ phuḍiūṇa mayā īsāē vinaḍiyā varaī ॥ 40 ॥
ajjhāṇavaṇaṁ jāyā hariṇī ihēva ēīē । tuhanāmāyannaṇaō jāīsaraṇaṁ samupapannaṁ ॥41॥
iya sōuṁ bhaṇai jivō jaha kahiyē nāha ! taha imaṁ savvaṁ । kiṁtu imaṁ maha pāvaṁ jaha phiṭṭa kuṇasu tamuvāyaṁ ॥
bandhumatīnāmnāḍyānyadā tasthā vāsabhavanē । snēhaparīkṣā hē tōrvilā sinyānītā tvayā ॥ 29 ॥
tayā samaṁ kṣaṇamēkaṁ gamayitvā visr̥ṣṭā tata ēṣā । upavanamadhyē gatā cintayitumidaṁ samārabdhā ॥ 30॥
priyasaṅgakāraṇāni sarvāṇyapi bhavantyatra duḥkhāni । sa yasyā na saṁjātaḥ sā mahilā susthitā nityam ॥31॥
dhanyāstā manyē kumāraśramaṇī : śamitapāpāḥ । yāsāmapamānamūlē viṣayasukhē nō matirjātā ||32||
kiṁ prēma kō vā priyaḥ kō virahaḥ kīdr̥śī viṣayatr̥ṣṇā । ētadapūrvaṁ yāsāṁ namō namastābhyaḥ śramaṇībhyaḥ ॥ 33 ॥
tāsāṁ labdhaṁ jīvitaṁ yāsāṁ tapastāpitē tanukuṭīrē । dāhabhayādiva na kr̥taṁ madanēna padaṁ manāgapi ॥ 34॥
saiva dhanyā sā puṇyabhājanaṁ yasyā nāsti priyasaṅgaḥ । vanavāsinīnāmapi nityamāyāti nidrāsukhaṁ tāsām ॥
yāsāṁ na jātō hr̥dayē pr̥thivīṁ bhramantīnāṁ vallabhaḥ kaścit । sukhitābhyaḥ sarvakālaṁ namō namastābhyō ramaṇībhyaḥ ॥
pavanāndōlitajalanidhitaraṅgaraṅgadvēpitraṅgam । anuharatē kēvalaṁ śaśinaṁ prēma taralatvaguṇēna ||37||
dūrasthitaṁ parōkṣaṁ śubhamaśubhaṁ gōcaraṁ grahāṇāṁ ca । jānanti yē vidagdhāḥ prēmagatau jaḍāstē'pi ॥38॥
taṁ nibiḍavitatasnēhaṁ vighaṭayamānēna jhaṭiti rē daiva ! । kiṁ pāpa ! prāptaṁ tvayā'mr̥tarasē kṣiptvā garalam ? || 39॥
iti tīkṣṇaduḥkhasūcakavacanāni muhurmuhuḥ prajalpantī । hr̥dayaṁ sphōṭitvā mr̥tēṣyayā vinaṭitā varākī ||40||
ārtadhyānavaśēna jātā hariṇīvaitasyāḥ । tvannāmākarṇanatō jātismaraṇaṁ samutpannam ॥41॥

bhaṇaṛa muṇīdi uvāō jiṇadhammō caiva sōya puṇa vihō । jaisāyaṇa paḍhō isā khamāīō ||43||
bārasahā duiō puṇasammalāī jiṣēhi nidhiṭṭō । ēgavi taha samma jīvāpayatyahaṇaṁ ॥ 44 ॥
aha davvabhāvabhēvā nicchayavahāra ya taṁ duhiṁ | agamanisaga pōpaṭapariṇāmaō tihiṁ ॥ 45||
aha itthaṁ vā tivida khaiyaṁ khāōvattamiyaṁ ca upasamiyaṁ । avā kāragarōgībābāda sē tihiṁ ॥
sasāṇēṇa cahā arrest | samāī dalhā panavāē jaō yaṇiyaṁ ॥47॥
nissarayararuī āṇaruī sutī । abhigamavityā ruī kiriyāsatē ||48 ||
iya sammattaṁ kahiyē savitrē sāhuṇā naravarasya | saṁlēhāvasānō kaḍiō pacchāya girimpō ॥49॥
tō savasē sāhū pujhē ranā jahā kahaha majjha । saṁlēhaṇāvaṁ tō sāhū sē kahai ēvaṁ ||20||
ukkōsā saṁlēhā vārasa varisāī tattha cauvaritā । chaṭṭāiyō kiyā pāras panivigaī ||51||

ēkkāra risāichakkē viṁta bhuṁjē । parimiyavinē duiva kē anusā ||23||

1
iti śrutvā bhaṇati nr̥pō yathā kathitaṁ nātha ! tathēdaṁ sarvam । kintvayaṁ mama pāyathā aśyati kurutamupāyam ॥
bhaṇati munirapyupāyō jinadharma ēva sa ca punadvividhaḥ । yatiśrāvakamēdēna prathamō daśadhā kṣamādikaḥ ||43||
dvādaśadhā dvitīyaḥ punaḥ samyaktvādijinainirdiṣṭaḥ | ēkavidhaṁ tathā samyaktvaṁ jīvādipadārthaśraddhānam ॥ 44 ॥
atha dravyabhāvabhēdānniścayavyavahārataśca tad dvividham । abhigamanisargarūpaṁ pudgalapariṇāmatastrividham ॥45॥
athētthaṁ vā trividhaṁ kṣāyika kṣāyōpaśamika caupaśamikam । athavā kārakarōcakadīpakabhēdāttattrividham ॥ 46 ॥
sāsvādanēna caturdhā vēdakaprakṣēpatastu pañcavidham । naisargādi daśadhā prajñāpanāyāṁ yatō gaṇitam ||17||
nisargōpadēśarucirājñāruciḥ sūtrabījarucī ēva | abhigamavistārarucī kriyāsaṁkṣēpavarmarucayaḥ ||18||
iti samyaktvaṁ kathitaṁ savistaraṁ sādhunā naravarāya | saṁlēkhanāvasānaḥ kathitaḥ paścāca gr̥hidharmaḥ ॥49॥
tataḥ saviśēṣaṁ sādhuḥ pr̥ṣṭō rājñā yathā kathayata mama । saṁlēkhanāsvarūpaṁ tataḥ sādhustasmai kathayatyēvam ||10||
utkr̥ṣṭā saṁlēkhanā dvādaśa varṣāṇi tatra caturvarṣīm । paṭhāditapaḥ kr̥tvā pārayētparipūrṇavikr̥tibhiḥ ॥51॥
dvitīyacatuṣkē'pi tapastathaiva kēvala na kē vikr̥tim । varṣadvikamēkāntarācāmpāraṇaṁ kuryāt ॥52॥
ēkādaśavarṣādiṣaṭkē madhyamatapastatō bhuñjīta । parimitācāmlaṁ dvitīyaṣaṭkē'ṣṭamāditapaḥ ॥ 53 ॥
ācāmlapāraṇaṁ karōti yathēcchaṁ tataśca dvādaśam | ācāmlēna varṣē kintu paryantacaturmāsyām ||14||
ēkāntaritaṁ kuryāttailēnāṅkuśaṅkatē tu mā vadanam । pavanēna mīlayēdityutkr̥ṣṭā khalu saṁlēkhanā ॥55॥
ṣāṇmāsikī jaghanyā punaḥ saṁlēkhanā bhavatyubhayatra । pratyēkaṁ prajñaptāḥ pañcāticārā imē tē ca ॥ 56 ॥

kiñcaḥ--
jaṁ ajja suhaṁ bhaviṇō saṁbharaṇīyaṁ tayaṁ bhavē kallē । maggati niruvasaggaṁ apavaggasuhaṁ buhā tēṇa ||73 ||
sāmanēṇaṁ sammattamāīō śuṭṭiō maē dhammō | saṁpai aṇasaṇavihiṇā dēhamahaṁ caimicchāmi ||74 ||

aparaṁ ca ।
suciraṁ cinnā bhōgā jāyā lacchīvi tuha pasāēṇa | bahulāliyaṁpi dēhaṁ kayāvi ēmēva mōttavvaṁ || 76 ||
ēvaṁ japaṁtāṇaṁ tāṇaṁ gayaṇēṇa āgaō sāhū । sō cāraṇamuṇicaṁdō jassa sayāsamma gihidhammō ||77 ||
pattōpuvviṁ tattō taṁ dahuṁ bhaṇai naravarō ēvaṁ । ahaha aṇabhā buṭṭī saṁjāyā ajja puṇṇēhiṁ ॥ 78 ॥
vaṁda ya bhattiputraṁ nēi taō malayacaṁdapāsammi । sōvi viṇaraṇa namiḍaṁ saṁthuivayaṇaṁ bhaṇai ēvaṁ ॥ 79 ॥
nikkāraṇakaruṇārasa taraṁgiṇīgurugiriṁda ! muṇināha ! | paḍivannamahāvayabhāradharaṇadhōrēya ! tuha namimō ||
mahapuvvasukayapēriēhiṁ tumbhēhiṁ kayamihāgamaṇaṁ । kuṇaha pasāyaṁ saṁpaṛa aṇasaṇadāṇēṇa maha nāha ! || 81 ॥
bhaṇai muṇī tuha samayaṁ nāūṇa samāgaō iha api । tā aṇasaṇaṁ pavajjasu tēṇa pavannaṁ tayaṁ vihiṇā ||
paṇa aiyāravisuddhaṁ paripālēūṇa taṁ samāhīē । sō malayacaṁdasaḍḍhō uvavannō vaṁbhalōyammi ||83 ||
rāyāvi kuṇai sōyaṁ maraṇē mittassa dhammabaṁdhussa । tō muṇiṇā sō bhaṇiō mā naravara ! kuṇasu taṁ khēyaṁ ॥
tava dēhaṁ nissandēhamēva praguṇaṁ kārayiṣyāmi । tatō bhaṇati malayacandrō narapatērabhimukhamēvam ॥71॥
yathā durlabhaṁ manujatvaṁ jinēndravacanādikāṁ ca sāmagrīm । labdhvā puruṣēṇa sadā yatitavyaṁ śivasukhanimittam ॥
yadadya sukhaṁ bhavinaḥ smaraṇīyaṁ tad bhavētkalyē । mārganti nirupasargamapavargasukhaṁ budhāstēna ॥73॥
sāmānyēna samyaktvādikō'nuṣṭhitō mayā dharmaḥ । saṁpratyanaśanavidhinā dēhamahaṁ tyaktumicchāmi ॥74॥
yadgalati pratikṣaṇamēva balavīryaṁ matiḥ śrutiścāyuśca । añjaligatamiva salilaṁ rōgābādhayā mama nātha ! || 75 ||
suciraṁ cīrṇā bhōgā jātā lakṣmīrapi tava prasādēna । bahulālitō'pi dēhaḥ kadāpyēvamēva mōktavyaḥ ॥ 76 ॥
ēvaṁ jalpatōstayōrgaganēnāgataḥ sādhuḥ । sa cāraṇamunicandrō yasya sakāśē gr̥hidharmaḥ ||77 ||
prāptaḥ pūrvaṁ tatastaṁ dr̥ṣṭyā bhaṇati naravara ēvam । ahahānabhrā vr̥ṣṭiḥ saṁjātā'dya puṇyaiḥ ॥ 78 ॥
vandatē ca bhaktipūrvaṁ nayati tatō malayacandrapārśvē । sō'pi vinayēna natvā saṁstutivacanaṁ bhaṇatyēvam ॥79॥
niṣkāraṇakaruṇārasataraṅgiṇīgurugirīndra ! muninātha ! । pratipannamahāvratabhāragharaṇadhaurēya ! tubhyaṁ namāmaḥ ॥80॥
matpūrvasukr̥ta pariprēritairyuṣmābhiḥ kr̥tamihāgamanam । kuruta prasādaṁ saṁpratyanaśanadānēna mama nātha ! ॥ 81 ॥
bhaṇati munistava samayaṁ jñātvā samāgata ihāhamapi । tasmādanaśanaṁ prapadyasva tēna prapannaṁ tadvidhinā ॥ 82 ॥
pañcāticāraviśuddhaṁ paripālya tatsamādhinā । sa malayacandraśrāddha upapannō brahmalōkē ॥ 83 ॥
rājāpi karōti śōkaṁ maraṇē mitrasya dharmavandhōḥ । tatō muninā sa bhaṇitō yā naravara kuru tvaṁ khēdam ||

jēṇa jarāvaṇahatthō vāhisaya vinnasāyagō sahasā | māṇusamigē vahatō vihivāhō vāriumasakō ||85||
kiñca ।
ganbhappabhiimānīisalilacchēē saraṁva susaṁtaṁ । aṇusamayaṁ maramāṇē jīyaṁti jaṇō kahaṁ bhai ! ।। 86 ।।
tathā ।
saṁpatthiyāṇa paralōyamēgasatthēṇa satthiyārṇava । jai tattha kōi puraō vaccai kiṁ tassa sōēṇa ? || 87 ||
jaha vā luṇāi sassāī kāsavō pariṇayāī chittammi । taha bhūyāī kayaṁ tō vatthumahāvō imō tamhā ॥ 88 ॥
aparaṁ ca ।
jara tāva machaḍō sacchaṁdō suravarēsu viyarēi । accatamabhāvōvi ya jattha jarārōgavāhīṇaṁ ॥ 89 ॥
tā iha vāhijarārōgasōgaghatthammi maṇuyalōyammi | maccussa sō pamāō jaṁ jiyai narō nimēsaṁpi ॥ 90 ॥
tāmā adhīrajaṇasēviyassa sōyassa dēsu avagāsaṁ । na hu maccadāḍhalīḍhaṁ iṁdōvi pahū niyatē ॥ 91 ॥
iccāidēsaṇāra sōyaṁ uttāriūṇa naravaiṇō । paḍibōhivi bhavvajaṇa sāhū viharēi annattha ॥ 92 ॥
rāyāvi kuṇai dhammaṁ suiraṁ aha syaṇicarimajāmampi | pāsa kayāvi suttō mahatthamēyaṁ mahāsumiṇa ॥ 93 ॥
jaha ēgō kō vitarū guruvisaharavēḍhiō tahā jinnō । sāhācaukkakaliō mūlē bahusāvayāinē ||14||
ubbhaḍapavaṇapakaṁpaṇakaḍukaḍayaḍasaddamāvatīē | tassa ya sāhāē ahaṁ ēgāē kahavi laggumhi || 95 ||
hiṭṭhā dūrapasāriyadādāvikarālaāṇaṇō duṭṭhō | paṁcāṇaṇō viyaṁbha mēṁ nivaḍataṁ samīhitō ॥ 96 ॥
ittō ya kapi kōvi āgaō tattha sarahasō sarahō । taṁ daṇaṁ katthavi nahō paṁcāṇaṇō duṭṭhō ॥ 97 ॥
yēna jarādhanurhastō vyādhiśatavitīrṇa sāyakaḥ sahasā । mānuṣamr̥gān man vidhivyādhō vārayitumaśakyaḥ ॥
garbhaprabhr̥tyāvīcisalilacchēdē sara iva śuṣyat । anusamayaṁ mriyamāṇē jīvitamiti janaḥ kathaṁ bhaṇati ॥ 86 ॥
saṁprasthitānāṁ paralōkamēkasārthēna sārthitānāmiva । yadi tatra kaścitpuratō vrajati kiṁ tasya śōkēna ! ||7||
yathā vā lunāti sasyāni karṣakaḥ pariṇatāni kṣētrē । tathā bhūtāni kr̥tāntaḥ vastusvabhāvō'yaṁ tasmāt ॥88॥
yadi tāvanmr̥tyusubhaṭaḥ svacchandaḥ suravarēṣu vicarati । atyantamabhāvō'pi ca yatra jarārōgavyādhīnām ||89 ॥
tadēha vyāvijarārōgaśōkagrastē manujalōkē । mr̥tyōḥ sa pramādō yajjīvati narō nimēṣamapi ॥ 90 ॥
tasmānmā'dhīrajana sēvitasya śōkasya dēhyavakāśam । na hi mr̥tyudaṁṣṭrālīḍhamindrō'pi prabhurnivartayitum ॥ 91 ॥
ityādidēśanayā śōkamuttārya narapatēḥ । pratibōdhya bhavyajanaṁ sādhuviharatyanyatra ॥ 92 ॥
rājāpi karōti dharma suciramatha rajanicaramayā mē । paśyati kadāpi suptō mahārthamētaṁ mahāsvapnam ॥ 93 ॥
yathaikaḥ kō'pi tarurguruviṣadharavēṣṭitastathā jīrṇaḥ । śākhācatuṣkakalitō mūlē bahuśvāpadākīrṇaḥ ॥ 94 ॥
udbhaṭapavanaprakampanakaṭukaṭakaṭaśabdamāvahantyām । tasya ca śākhāyāmahamēkasyāṁ kathamapi lamō'smi ॥ 95 ॥
aghō dūraprasāritadaṁṣṭrā vikarālānanō duṣṭaḥ । pañcānanō vijr̥mbhatē māṁ nipatantaṁ samahimānaḥ ॥ 96 ॥

supāsanāhacariyami-
hu
tattaviṇa purī palōēḍa jāna paḍibuddhō । tāva na kiṁpi hu pāsa tō ciṁtā sumiṇamēyaṁti ॥98॥
tattō kapakāyacī pāyasamaē namitta jiganāhaṁ । atyāgē ubō mahasēṇanarāhiyō tattha ||19||
bāhara suviṇāramatyajāgara suniyasayalasatyatthē । tēvi hr̥taṁ uciṇaminivasati ||100 ॥
tāṇaṁ ca purō sāha puc sumiyaṁ naridavi । tēvi bhaṇa ēvaṁ jaō bhaṇiyē ॥
ārōhaṇaṁ tarūṇaṁ supasatyaṁ sa tu turayāgaṁ । daī hē hidvā viṇissa sahasā ||10||
sī puṇē sahī kōhi na munijjai dēva ! jēṇa sīhīti । vittāsi sudūraṁ suṇigamē tō visamaṁ ।।
samr̥ṇihī ēyaṁ tu suvabarō kōvi । tō rāyā pariyāvara kimatyasarī ihaṁ kō vi ॥ 104 ॥
ityaṁrambhi karakaliyayamālāpahihiyayā ya । ujjāṇavāliyā navivi naravaī va ēvaṁ ||105॥
iha dēva ! jāḍō samaya sūrī | bahusīsaṁparicāṇī siṁ ॥106 ॥
taṁ sōūna tī dāūṇē pāritōṣi dā । gaccha jāṇē supivika isamēṁ rāyā ॥107॥
pityācē sumimaṁ jahāhiṁ । tasvāraṁ nā sāha sūrīvita phalaṁ ॥ 108॥
jaha khakhī saṁsārī sātā puṇē gaicakkaṭhāṇīyā । vilariyā viṣayā bahusābapani sēvā।। 109॥
pavaṇō va puñcakammaṁ sāhāē jīē kahavi taṁ laggō । sāibā tīē u mēṁ sīḍō।। 110 ।।
sōcna tu samīhē māṇusa gaīē | itthaṁtarasmi jaṁ puṇa samāgaō tattha sarōvi । 111||
॥
itaśca kathamapi hi kō'nyāgatastatra sarabhasaḥ śarabhaḥ । taṁ dr̥ṣṭrā kutrāpi naḥ pañcānanō duṣṭaḥ ॥97॥
tatō vismayitamanāḥ puraḥ pralōkatē yāvatpratibuddhaḥ । tāvanna kimapi hi paśyati tataścintayati svapnamētāmiti ॥
tataḥ kr̥takartavyaḥ prabhātasamayē natvā jinanātham । āsthāna upaviṣṭō mahāsēnanarādhipastatra ॥99॥
vyāharati svapnaparamārthajñāyakājñātasakalaśāstrārthān । tē'pi hi mantraṁ bhaṇitvōcitasthānē nivasanti ॥ 100 ॥
tēṣāṁ ca puraḥ kathayati pūrvōktaṁ svapnaṁ narēndrō'pi । tē'pi hi bhaganti viṣaḥ svapnō'yaṁ yatō bhaṇitam ॥
ārōhaṇaṁ tarūṇāṁ supraśastaṁ darśanaṁ tu turagāṇām । duṣṭaṁ tathaivāvō vivr̥tavadanasya siṁhasya ||102 ॥
1
1
sa punaḥ śarabhaḥ kō'pi hi na jñāyatē dēva ! yēna siṁhō'pi । vitrāsitaḥ sudūraṁ svapna ēṣa tatō viṣamaḥ ||
aviṣayō'smanmatīnāṁ jñāsyatyētaṁ tu śrutadharaḥ kō'pi । tatō rājā paribhāvayati kimasti sūririha kō'pi ॥
atrāntarē karakalitakumudamālā prahr̥ṣṭahr̥dayā ca । udyānapālikā natvā narapatiṁ vijñapayatyēvam ॥ 105 ॥
iha dēva tavōdyānē samavasr̥taḥ samayasāgaraḥ sūriḥ । bahuśiṣyasaṁparivr̥taścaturjñānō labdhisaṁpannaḥ ॥106॥
tat śrutvā tasyai dattvā pāritōṣikaṁ dānam । gacchati tatrōdyānē svapnavidbhiḥ samaṁ rājā ॥ 107॥
।
natvā sūriṁ kathayati prastāvē svapnaṁ yathādr̥ṣṭam । tasyōpakāraṁ jñātvā kathayati surirapi tasya phalam ||108 ||
yathā vr̥kṣaḥ saṁsāraḥ śākhāḥ punargaticatuṣkasthānīyāḥ । viṣadharasadr̥śā viṣayā bahudhāpadasaṁnibhā rōgāḥ ॥ 109 ॥
pavanaśca pūrvakarma śākhāyāṁ yasyāṁ kathamapi tvaṁ lagnaḥ । sā punarmanujagatirēvāvastasyāstu yatsiṁhaḥ ॥ 110 ॥
sa mr̥tyurnipatantaṁ tvāṁ samīhatē mānuṣagatēḥ । atrāntarē yatpunaḥ samāgatastatra śarabhō'pi ॥ 111 ॥

sō puṇa kōvi hu sūrī maccuṁ ninnāsiūṇa tujjha taō | avvābāhē ṭhāṇē vissaī sumiṇaphalamēyaṁ ॥ 112 ॥
tō mahasēō rāyā sūri vinnavai sumiṇaphalamēyaṁ । ajjaṁ ciya jaha saccaṁ jāyai taha nāha ! kuṇasu lahuṁ ||
sūrīvi bhaṇai naravara ! mā paḍibaṁdhaṁ karēsi tō sōvi । niyaputtaṁ ṭhaviūṇaṁ rajjē giṇi sayaṁ dikkha ||
tatō yaduvihasikkha kēvalanāṇaṁ ca pāviūṇa lahuṁ । sivamaya lamaruyaṭhāṇaṁ mahasēṇamuṇī samaṇupattō ॥ 115 ॥
iya āsaṁsaṁ parivajjiūṇa jō kuṇai aṇasaṇaṁ vihiṇā । jai tabbhavē na sijjhai pāyaṁ tō taiyajammammi ||
dhannā sunippakaṁpā kayaaṇukaṁpā paṇaṭṭhasaṁkappā | jhāyaṁtā paramappaṁ aṇasaṇamaraṇaṁ pavajjaṁti ||17||
॥ iti saṁlēkhanāyāṁ malayacandrakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
sa punaḥ kō'pi hi sūrirmr̥tyuṁ nirṇāśya tava tataḥ । avyābādhē sthānē sthāpayiṣyati svapnaphalamētat ॥ 112 ॥
tatō mahāsēnō rājā sūriṁ vijñapayati svapnaphalamētat । adyaiva yathā satyaṁ jāyatē tathā nātha ! kuru laghu ॥
sūrirapi bhaṇati naravara ! mā pratibandhaṁ kārṣīstataḥ sō'pi । nijaputraṁ sthāpayitvā rājyē gr̥hṇāti svayaṁ dīkṣām ॥
tataśca dvivivaśikṣāṁ kēvalajñānaṁ ca prāpya laghu । śivamacalamaruksthānaṁ mahāsēnamuniḥ samanuprāptaḥ ॥ 115 ॥
ityāśaṁsāṁ parivarjya yaḥ karōtyanaśanaṁ vidhinā । yadi tadbhavē na sidhyati prāyastatastr̥tīyajanmani ॥ 116 ॥
dhanyāḥ suniṣprakampāḥ kr̥tānukampāḥ pranaṣṭasaṁkalpāḥ । dhyāyantaḥ paramātmānamanaśanamaraṇaṁ prapadyantē || 117॥

iya sammattasamēō sāvayadhammō duvālasavihōvi | saṁlēhaṇāvalāṇō saiyārō taha sahiṁtō ॥ 1 ॥
kahiō bhō tuha naravara ! sammaṁ paḍivajjiūṇa tā ēyaṁ । niraīyāraṁ pālasu nicalacittō paidipi ॥ 2 ॥
iya sōūṁ paṇa dāṇavīriō jiṇaṁ paṇamiūṇa । ārōvasu pasiūṇaṁ sāvayadhammaṁ maha imaṁti || 3 ||
tattō bhayavaṁ vihiṇā ārōvēūṇa taṁ nariṁdassa । sirinaṁdivarddhaṇapurā vihariumannattha nikkhatō ||4||
sattuṁjayagiripuragāmanayara pamuhēsu bahuyaṭhāṇēsu । samavasariya diktō bhavvē gihisā huē ||5||
paṇanavagaṇaharēhi sēvijjatōya muṇitilakkhēhiṁ । calakkhēhi ajāṇa tīsasahassāhiēhiṁ ca ||6||
sattāvannasahassā hiyadugalakkhēhiṁ sāvagāṇa tahā । tēṇavaisahasaca ulakkha saṁkhasaḍaḍhīhi tō ||7||
caudasapuvīṇa juō dōhiṁ sahassēhiṁ tīsa ahiēhiṁ । aṇugammaṁtō ya tahā kē liē kāra sahasēhiṁ ॥8॥
tinnisayāhiyagnnarasasahassa vē ucciladdhijuttēhiṁ । aṭṭasahassēhiṁ sacausaēhiṁ vāīhiṁ thuvaṁtō ||9||
ōhināṇīhiṁsayā sēvitō ya navasahassēhiṁ । maṇapajjadanāṇīṇaṁ sasadasayana va sahassēhi ||10||
gāmāgaranagarāi viharaṁtō vibuhavihiyapasiṇāṇaṁ । vivittarāī ditō paḍivōhaṁtō ya bhavvajaṇaṁ ॥ 11 ॥
varanāṇataraṇikiraṇēhiṁ tamabharaṁ bhaviṣayagēhāō । dūraṁ ninnāsitō pattō sammēyasēlampi ||12||
tatthavi yaksamayaṁ āsanna jāṇiūṇa nāṇēṇa । cihna supāsanāhō māsa ēvaṁ kayāṇasaṇō || 13 ||
bhavvāṇa hiyakaraṇē samujjaō bhavasi samacittō । jīviyamaraṇanirīhō jhāyaṁtō aki jhāṇaṁ || 14 |
1
iti samyaktvasamētaḥ śrāvakadharmō dvādaśavidhōṣi । saṁlēkhanāvasānaḥ sāticārastathā dr̥ṣṭāntaḥ ॥ 1 ॥
kathitō bhōstava naravara ! samyakpratipadya tasmādētam । niraticāraṁ pālaya niścalacittaḥ pratidinamapi || 2 ||
iti śrutvā prabhaṇati dānavīryō jinaṁ praṇamya । ārōpaya prasadya śrāvakadharmaṁ mamēmamiti ॥3॥
tatō bhagavān vidhinā''rōpya taṁ narēndrasya । śrīnandivardhanapurād vihartumanyatra niṣkrāntaḥ ||4||
śatruñjayagiripuragrāmanagarapramukhēṣu bahusthānēṣu । samavasr̥tya dīkṣamāṇō bhavyāngr̥hisādhubhēdēna ||5||
pañcanavatigaṇa sēvyamānaśca munitrilakṣaiḥ । caturlakṣyāryāṇāṁ triṁśatsahasyyadhikayā ca ॥ 6 ॥
satapañcāśatsahasyadhikadvilakṣyā śrāvakāṇāṁ tathā । trinavatisahasacaturlakṣasaṁkhyaśrāddhībhiḥ stūyamānaḥ ||7||
caturdaśapūrviṇāṁ yutō dvābhyāṁ sahasrābhyāṁ triṁśadadhikābhyām । anugamyamānaśca tathā kēvalyēkādaśasahasyā ||8||
triśatyadhikapañcadaśasaha sabai kriyalabdhiyuktaiḥ । aṣṭasahasnyā sacatuḥśatīkayā vādināṁ stūyamānaḥ ||9||
avadhijñānināṁ sadā sēvyamānaśca navasahasyā | manaḥ paryavajñānināṁ sasārdhaśatanavasahasyā ॥10॥
grāmākaranagarādiṣu viharan vibudhavihitapraśnānām । vividhōttarāṇi dadatpratibōdhayaṁśca bhavyajanam ॥ 11 ॥
varajñānataraṇikiraṇaistamōbharaṁ bhavyahr̥dayagēhāt । dūraṁ nirṇāśayanprāptaḥ sammētaśailē ॥12॥
tatrāpi ca mōkṣasamayamāsannaṁ jñātvā jñānēna । tiṣṭhati supārśvanāthō māsamēkaṁ kr̥tānaśanaḥ ॥13॥
bhavyānāṁ hitakaraṇē samudyatō bhavaśivayōḥ samacittaḥ । jīvitamaraṇanirīhō dhyāyannakriyaṁ vyānam || 14 ||

nivyāpatthāvāṁ |
655
ēgaṁ ca puvyalakkhaṁ caiuraṁgūṇaṁ carittapajjāyaṁ । paripāliūṇa paliyaṁkaāsaṇē saṁṭhiō bhayavaṁ ||15||
itthaṁtarampi nivbuigamaṇamaṇa jāṇiūṇa jiṇanāhaṁ । savvē suramuriṁdā samāgayā jinavarasamīvaṁ ॥ 16 ॥
kāū puṣpagaraṁ gaṁdhōdayavuṭṭivyaṁ tattō । siraraiyaaṁjalipuḍā namiūṇaṁ ṇiumārā ||17||
jaya jiṇasattama sattama ! vimukanīsēsakammanimmōya ! । bhavarakkhasavina ḍijjatajaṁtusaṁ tāṇasattāṇa ॥ 18 ॥
muttisirisaṁgamūkhya ! jiṇida ! tuhapāyapaumanasaṇēṇa । uvasama madhō gaṁdhasiṁdhurō takkhaṇēṇēva ||19||
aitikkhagāḍhadāḍhākarālamuhakadarō nivaddhakamō । na kamai mayanāhō jinavariṁda ! tuhanāmasaraṇēṇaṁ ||20||
naciravivibaṁdhē pariṣapirarahiyavirahiyagaīdē । jō sarai tumaṁ samaraṁgaṇammi taṁ jayasirī varai ||21||
lahalahiradīhajīhō aruṇacchicchōhapāḍaliyagayaṇō । tuha jhāṇēṇa na pahavai ahī citaḍaviyacaḍaphaṇō ||22||
dēva va vijjuduḍuriyakaṇṇadhārēvi | saṁjattiōvi vaccai tuha saraṇēṇaṁ jalahitīraṁ ||23||
1
iya ihalōē jāyara jaṇāna tuhanāmasaraṇamittēṇa । paralōē puṇa mōkkhō asaṁkhadukkhāṇa khayakārī ||24||
ēvaṁ bahuyōrhi sammēyagiriṭṭiyaṁ supāsajiṇaṁ । jā saṁthurṇati gurubhattinibbharā sayalasuranāhā ||25||
tā savvasaṁvarakara sēlēsi jayagurū samārūhiuṁ । samagaṁ vēyaṇiāukanāmaguttāiṁ khaviūṇa ||26||
saṭṭā chapāī dukarāī kīraṁti । bhujijjēti ya suddhaṁ tucchaarasāī asaṇāī ||27||
avamanijjai gāḍhāṇurattaramaṇīyaṇassa paḍibaṁdhō । muccai navanēhā baṁdhurō baṁdhavajaṇōvi ॥ 28 ॥
ēkaṁ ca pūrvalakṣaṁ caturaṅggyōnē cāritraparyāyam । paripālya palyaṅkāsanē saṁsthitō bhagavān ॥ 15 ॥
atrāntarē nirvr̥tigamanamanasaṁ jñātvā jinanātham । sarvē surāsurēndrāḥ samāgatā jinavarasamīpam ॥ 16 ॥
kr̥tvā puṣpaprakaraṁ gandhōdakavr̥ṣṭipūrvakaṁ tataḥ । śirōracitāñjalipuṭā natvā stōtumārabdhāḥ ॥ 17॥
jaya jinasattama saptama vinuktaniḥśēṣakarmanirmōka । bhavarākṣasavinaṭyamāna jantusantānasattrāṇa ! ||18||
muktistrīsaṅgamōtsuka jinēndra ! tvatpādapadmanamanēna । upaśāmyati madāndhō gandhasindhurastatkṣaṇēnaiva ॥ 19 ॥
atitīkṣṇagādr̥daṁṣṭrākarālamukhakandarō nibaddhakamaḥ । na krāmati mr̥ganātha jinavarēndra ! tvannāmasmaraṇēna || 20॥
nartitr̥vividhakabandhē parisarpitr̥rathikavirahitagajēndrē | yaḥ smarati tvāṁ samarāṅgaṇē taṁ jayaśrīvr̥ṇutē ||21||
lahaladditr̥dīrghajihvō'ruṇa kṣikṣōmapāṭalitagaganaḥ । tava dhyānēna na prabhavatyahirvitatacaṇḍaphaṇaḥ ॥22॥
vipulē durdinē vidyutkanduka trastakarṇadhārōpi । sāṁyātrikō'pi vrajati tava śaraṇēna jaladhitīram ||23||
itīha lōkē jāyatē janānāṁ tvannāmasmaraṇamātrēṇa । paralōkē punarmōkṣō'saṁkhya duḥkhānāṁ kṣayakārī ||24||
ēvaṁ bahumtōtraiḥ sammētagiristhitaṁ supārśvajinam । yāvatsaṁstuvanti gurubhaktinirbharāḥ sakalasuranāthāḥ ||25||
tāvatsarvasaṁvarakarī śailēśī jagadguruḥ samāruhya । samaṁ vēdanīyāyunāmagōtrāṇi kṣapayitvā ॥ 26 ॥
।
yadarthaṁ ṣaṣṭhāṣṭapramukhāṇi duṣkarāṇi kriyantē । mujyantē ca śuddhāmbhastucchārasānyaśanāni ||27||
avamanyatē gāḍhānuraktaramaṇījanasya pratibandhaḥ । mucyatē navasnēhabandhabandhurō bāndhavajanō'pi ॥28॥
1. jasaṁ ।

supāsanāha cariammi-
sēvijjaṁtī vīrāsaṇāī ṭhāṇāī taha aṇudipi । dijjaṁti kāussaggā sīyāya dusahakālēvi ॥ 29 ॥
tuḍiyabhavaviyaḍapāsō uttattasuvannavannasaṁkāsō । ahariyadiṇayarabhāsō sirivāsō jiṇavarasupāsō ||30||
phagguṇaka siṇāē sattamī mōkkhammi tammi saṁpattō | paṁcahi sāhusaēhiṁ sahiō caiūṇa niyarbudi ||31||
aha jayaguruguruvirahu bhavaṁtavāhappavāhanayaṇapuḍā | savvēvi suravariṁdā namiūṇaṁ bhaṇiumārā ||32||
saṁpai tumammi parinivyuyammi jayanāha ! tihuyaṇapaīvē । bhāraha khittaṁ guru prōha timirabhara nimbharaṁ jāyaṁ ॥ 33 ॥
bhattibharanivbharunbhijjamāṇaghaṇapulayapūriyasarīrā । āgaṁtūṇaṁ jayaguru ! inhiṁ kaṁ saṁthuṇissāmā ? ||34||
kassa va pūyaṁ raiūṇa saṁpayē nivbuyā bhavissāmō ? । savilāsalāsalīlaṁ kassava puraō karissāmā ? ||
tumamaṁtarēṇa siraraiyarayaṇamayama uḍamaṁḍalī ihiṁ । bhattitrasēṇaṁ sāmiya ! cuṁvissai kassa payavīḍhaṁ 1 ||36||
iya saṁthōūṇa puṇō puṇōvi namiūṇa vigayaāṇaṁdā । jiganāhassa sarīraṁ adūrasamma nisiyaṁti ||
tō suravaṇēṇaṁ vēsamaṇī kuṇai kaṇayarayaṇamayaṁ । varanivvāṇasmiviyaṁ ūsiyadhayacivacicaiyaṁ ||38||
tattō ya khīrasāyarajalēṇa vhaviūṇa jiṇatrarasarīraṁ । niyasiyavimaladukūlaṁ rayaṇamayāharaṇaruharaṁgaṁ ||39||
ruyamāṇē saccēvi hu khivaṁti siviyāē sasurasuravaiṇō । gaṁtūṇa avaradāhiṇadisāē suddhapi bhūbhāgē ||
gōsīsa caṁdragurudārūhi rayati tattha ciyajuyalaṁ । ēgāē khivaṁti jiṇaṁ avaraē sēsasāhugaṇaṁ ॥ 41 ॥
tattō duṁduhipamuhēsu gahīratū rēsu vajjamāṇēsu । savvattō khayarēsuṁ kusumakaraṁ muyaṁtēsu ॥ 42 ॥
sēvyantē vīrāsanāni sthānāni tathānudinamapi । dīyantē kāyōtsargāḥ śītātapadussaha kālē'pi ॥29॥
tuḍitabhavavikaṭapāśa uttaptasuvarṇavarṇasaṁkāśaḥ । adharitadinakarabhāsaḥ śrīvāsō jinavarasupārśvaḥ ॥30॥
phālgunakr̥ṣṇāyāṁ saptamyāṁ mōkṣē tasmin saṁprāptaḥ । pañcabhiḥ sādhuśataiḥ sahitastyaktvā nijaśarīram ||31||
atha jagadguruguruvirahōdbhavāṣpapravāhanayanapuṭāḥ । sarvē'pi suravarēndrā natvā bhaṇitumārabdhāḥ ||32||
saṁprati tvayi parinirvr̥tē jagannātha ! tribhuvanapradīpē | bhāratakṣētraṁ gurumōhatimirabharanirbharaṁ jātam ||33||
bhaktibharanirbharōdbhidyamānaghana pulakapūritaśarīrāḥ । āgatya jagadgurō ! idānīṁ kē saṁstōṣyāmaḥ ? ||34||
kasya vā pūjāṁ racayitvā sāṁprataṁ nirvr̥tā bhaviṣyāmaḥ । savilāsalāsyalīlāṁ kasya vā purataḥ kariṣyāmaḥ ? ॥
tvāmantarēṇa śirōracitaratnamayamukuṭamaṇḍalīdānīm । bhaktivaśēna svāmin ! cumbiyati kasya padapīṭham ||
itantutya punaḥ punarapi natvā vigatānandāḥ | jinanāthasya śarīramadūradēśē niṣīdanti ॥ 37 ॥
tataḥ surapativacanēna vaiśramaṇaḥ karōti kanakaratnamayīm । varanirvāṇaśibikāmucchritadhvajacihnamaṇḍitām॥38॥
tataśca kṣārasāgarajalēna snapayitvā jinavaraśarīram । nivasitavimaladukūlaṁ ratnamayābharaṇarucirāṅgam ||39 ॥
rudati sarvasminnapi hi kṣipanti śivikā sasurasurarpatayaḥ । gatvā'paradakṣiṇadiśaḥ śuddhē bhūbhāgē ||40||
gōśīcandanāgurudārubhī racayanti tatra citāyugalam । ēkasyāṁ kṣipanti jinamaparasyāṁ śēṣasādhugaṇam ॥41॥
tatō dundubhipramukhēṣu gabhīratūryēṣu vādyamānēṣu । sarvataḥ khacarēṣu kusumōtkaraṁ muñcatsu ॥42॥

nañcatīya surasuṁdarīsu saṁghammi sōyavidurasmi । dēvidēsu ya jayajayaravanibbharabhariyabhuvaṇē ||43||
aggikumārā niyaāṇaṇāra jalaṇaṁ ciyāē muṁcati । vāukumārā vāyaṁ kāūṇaṁ taṁ palīvati ||44 ||
avarē ya suravarā puṇa khivaṁta gaṁdha ḍhadhūyamuṭṭhīō । ēvaṁ kamēṇa masāiēsa daḍḍhēsu samayam ||45 ||
aisisirasurahiparimalakhīrōyasamudavāridhārāhi । thaṇiyakumārā aha nivvavaṁti ciyagaṁ jiṇidassa ||
uvarimadāhiṇasakahaṁ sakō giṇhēi hiṭṭimaṁ camarō । vāmaṁ pahuṇō uvarimamīsāṇō hiṭṭimaṁ tu balī ॥47॥
daṁtīṇa u sēsā surāriṁdā surā ya savvēvi । giṇhati maṁgalatthaṁ bhattibharunbhinnarōmaṁcā ||48 ||
dēvīō kusumāī sthāī nariṁdanārinaranivahā । savvōvi jaṇō givha ahamahamiyā puṇō rakkhaṁ ॥ 49 ॥
aha jattēṇaṁ nivvattiyammi takkālamuciyakiccammi | jayaguruguruvirahānalajālō lijhalakiyaṁ hiyayaṁ ॥ 50 ॥
nivvāviḍaṁ ca naṁdīsarammi vaccēti sasurasuranāhā । tatthadvāhiyamahima kāūṇaṁ paramabhattīē ॥ 51 ॥
baccēti dēvalōē bhattīē pūiuṇa jattēṇa । jiṇavarasakahāu khivaṁti rayaṇamaṇimaiyasuṁgammi || 52 ||
paṇaphaṇimaṇibhāsō dukkhadaṁdōlināsō, vihiyabhavapavāsō rāyarōsapaṇāsō ।
jaṇaṇiyasuhāsō saggamōkkhappayāsō disau jiṇasupāsō maṁgalaṁ vō sayā sō ॥ 53 ॥
lakkhaṇachēdaviṇaṁ jahi maē viraiyaṁ samayamukaṁ । micchāmi dukkaḍaṁ taṁ sōhēyavvaṁ ca suyaṇēhiṁ ॥ 54 ॥
॥ iti śrī supārśvanāthacaritaṁ samāptam ॥
nr̥tyantīṣu ca surasundarīṣu saṁdhē śōkavidhurē । dēvēndrēṣu ca jayajayaravanirbharabhr̥tabhuvanēṣu ॥ 43 ॥
agnikumārā nijānanājjvalanaṁ citāyāṁ muñcanti । vāyukumārā vātaṁ kr̥tvā taṁ pradīpayanti || 14 ||
aparē ca suravarāḥ punaḥ kṣipanti gandhāḍhyadhūpamuṣṭīḥ । ēvaṁ kramēṇa māṁsādikēṣu dagdhēṣu samayē ||15||
atiśiśirasurabhiparimalakṣīrōdasamudravāridhārābhiḥ । stanitakumārā atha nirvāpayanti citāṁ jinēndrasya ॥46॥
uparita dakṣiṇadaṁṣṭrāṁ śakrō gr̥hṇātyadhastanīṁ camaraḥ । vāmāṁ prabhōruparitanīmīśānō'dhastanīṁ tu baliḥ ॥ 47 ॥
dantāsthīni tu śēṣāḥ surāsurēndrāḥ surāśca sarvē'pi । gr̥hṇanti maṅgalārthaṁ bhaktibharōdbhinnarōmāñcāḥ ॥48॥
dēvyaḥ kusumāni vastrāṇi narēndranārīnaranivahāḥ । sarvōpi janō gr̥hṇātyahamahamikayā punā rakṣām ||49||
atha yatnēna nirvartitē tatkāla mucitakr̥tyē । jagadguruguruvirahānalajvālālīdagbhaṁ hr̥dayam ||50 ॥
nirvāpayituṁ ca nandīśvarē vrajanti sasurasuranāthāḥ । tatrāṣṭāhikāmahimānaṁ kr̥tvā paramabhaktyā ॥51॥
vrajanti dēvalōkē bhaktyā pūjayitvā yatnēna । jinavaradaṁṣṭrāḥ kṣipanti ratnamaṇimayasamudrē ॥ 52 ॥
pañcaphaṇimaṇibhāsō du:khadvandvālīnāśō vihitabhavapravāsō rāgaśēṣapraṇāśaḥ ।
janita jana sukhāśa: svargamōkṣaprakāśō diśatu jinasupārśvō maṅgalaṁ vaḥ sadā saḥ ॥53॥
lakṣaṇacchandōvihīnaṁ yadiha mayā viracitaṁ samayamuktam । mithyā mē duṣkr̥taṁ tacchōdhayitavyaṁ ca sujanaiḥ ॥54॥

praśastiḥ ।
iha asthi sayalamahivalayabhavaṇabhūsāē saraladhayadaṁḍō। kittipaḍāyāka liō siriharisaurō pavaragacchō ||
tammi jayasiṁhasūrī tuhiṇagiriduvva sayalasivanilaō । jamhā viṇiggayā surasarivya muṇisaṁtaī dhruvaṇē ॥2॥
tattō ya dayākamaliṇikaṁtō micchattatimirabharaharaṇō । sayalasiyaṁvara tilaō sūrī iha abhayasūriti ||3||
tassa susīsō siyajasajuhādhava liyasiyaṁvarābhōgō | paravāicakavihaḍapamahappō mayaṁkun ||4||
sirihēmacaṁdrasūrī jayasiṁhanarāhivaṁ pabōhēḍaṁ । rahajattāisu kajjēsu jēṇa taṁ kipi viṣphuriyaṁ ॥5॥
jassa mahajalahiniggaya vicittasatthāmayaṁ mahāmuṇiṇō । āsāiūṇa ajjavi lahaṁti ajarāmaraṁ ṭhāṇaṁ ||6||
tassaviya tini sīmā paḍhamō sirivijayasiṁhasūriti । ētavāyasaṁsaggaraṁgasāraṁgabhaṁgaharī ||7||
duiō amuvijjāsamuddasaṁpunnapunnimāiṁdō । jiṇapatrayaṇakumuyaviyāsagō ya siricaṁdrasūriti ॥ 8 ॥
pālatē sirilāḍadēsamuddē na kēvala jēṇa । jiṇapaśyaṇastra vihiyā pabhāvanā samaṇamupi || 9 ||
jasma ya munisuvyacariyaraṁgasālāē bilasiyā vāṇī । chaṁdāṇuyālaṁkāra sāliṇī lēkhanahuvva ॥ 10 ॥
taiō ya vivahajaṇamaṇa amaṁda āṇaṁdadāṇadullaliō । sirivicaṁdrasūrī, ahannayā sōvi viharatō ॥11॥
dhukyammi pattō puṁḍariyamuēṇa āsaḍēṇa tarhi । siripaumacaṁda ujjhāyapamuhasaṁgha bhaṇēūṇa ||12||
mannāviyā taō tē suvāsajiṇacariyakaraṇavisayampi । tēhivi taō niuttō sissalavō hēmasūrissa ॥ 13 ॥
gayalakkhaṇachaṁdēvi lēkhamaṇagaṇiṇā pavāsiya ēyaṁ । sirisattamajiṇacariyaṁ harau duī sayalasaṁghassa || 14 ||
1
ihāstisakalamahivalayabhavanabhūṣāyai saraladhvajadaṇḍaḥ । kīrttipatākākalitaḥ śrīharṣapuraḥ pravaragacchaḥ || 1 ||
tasmiñjaya siṁha sūristuhinagirīndra iva sakalaśivanilayaḥ । yasmādvinirgatā surasaridiva munisaṁtatirbhuvanē ॥2॥
tataśca dayākamalinīkāntō mithyātvatimirabharaharaṇaḥ । sakalasitāmbara tilakaḥ sūririhābhayasūririti ॥ 3॥
tasya suśiṣyaḥ sitayaśōjyōtsnādhavalita sitāmbarābhōgaḥ । paravādicakraviṭaghanaprakaṭamāhātmyō mr̥gāṅka iva || 4 ||
śrī hēmacandrasūrirjaya siṁha narādhipaṁ prabōdhya । rathayātrādiṣu kāryēṣu yēna tatkimapi visphuritam ||5||
yasya mukhajalādhēnirgatavicitraśāstrāmr̥taṁ mahāmunayaḥ । āsvādyāpi labhantē'jarāmaraṁ sthānam ॥6॥
tasyāpi ca trayaḥ śiṣyāḥ prathamaḥ śrīvijaya siṁhasūriiita । ēkāntavādasaṁsargaraṅgabhaṅgahariḥ ||7||
dvitīyō'mudravidyā samudra saṁpūrṇa pūrṇimācandraḥ । jinapravacana kumuda vikāsakaśca śrīcandrasūririti ॥ 8 ॥
pālayatā śrīlāṭadēśamudrāṁ na kēvalaṁ yēna । jinapravacanasya vihitā prabhāvanā śramaṇa mudrāmapi ॥9॥
yasya ca munisuvratacaritaraṅgaśālāyāṁ vilasitā vāṇī । chandō'nugatālaṁkāra śālinī lakavadhūriva ॥ 10 ॥
tr̥tīyaśca vibudhajanamanō'mandānandadāna durlalitaḥ । śrīvibudhacandrasūriḥ, athānyadā sō'pi viharan ॥ 11 ॥
dhandhukkē prāptaḥ puṇḍarīkasutēnā''saḍēna tatra । śrīpadmacandrōpādhyāya pramukhasaṁdhaṁ bhaṇitvā ॥ 12 ॥
mānitāstatastē supārśvajinacaritakaraṇaviṣayē । tairapi tatō niyuktaḥ śiṣyalavō hēmasūrēḥ ॥ 13 ॥

jaina- vividha sāhitya-śāstramālā mēṁ bapī huī pustakōṁ kī sūcī ।
(1)
( 1 ) surasundarī-cariaṁ ( karttā dhanēśvarasūri ) yaha 4000 gāthā pramāṇa prākr̥tabhāṣā kā
vaḍā hī manōhara suṁdara mahākāvya hai। baṛī vistr̥ta prastāvanā sarala saṁskr̥ta mēṁ dī gaī hai
jisasē granthakāra tathā aura 2 śrācārya saṁbandhī' anēka jñātavya itivr̥ttakā jñāna hōtā hai।
mūlya sādhāraṇa saṁskaraṇa ru. 2-0-0, rājasaṁskaraṇa ru. 3-0-0
2) haribhadrasūri-caritram - yaha 1444 granthakē praṇētā suprasiddha vidvān jainācārya hari-
bhī sulalita gadya mēṁ likhā huā saṁpūrṇa jīvana caritra hai। jō ki anēka granthōṁ
kā avalōkana kara baṛē hī pariśrama sē likhā gayā hai। mūlya ru. 0-4-0 mātra ।
( 3 ) saptasaṁdhāna-mahākāvyam- ( karttā mahōpādhyāya śrīmēghavijayajī gaṇi ) isamēṁ
r̥ṣabhanātha, śāntinātha, nēminātha, pārśvanātha, mahāvīrasvāmī, śrīkr̥ṣṇa aura rāmacandra yē
sātōṁ mahāpuruṣōṁ kē jīvana caritra varṇita haiṁ। āścarya kī bāta tō yaha hai ki isakē pratyēka
ślōkasē sātōṁkā jīvana caritra kā vr̥ttānta nikalatā hai। baṛā hī āścaryōtpādaka grantha
hai। aisā ēka bhī kāvya saṁskr̥ta sāhitya mēṁ nahīṁ hai । kaṭhina sthalōṁ mēṁ ṭippaṇa bhī
diyā gayā hai। mūlya mātra ru. 0-8-0 ।
(4-6-12) supāsanāha-cariaṁ ( karttā śrīlakṣmaṇagaṇi) prākr̥ta bhāṣā kā yaha ēka manō-
hara va bōdhaprada mahākāvya hai । sthala sthala mēṁ anēka manōrañjakathāōṁsē bharapūra hai। aisā
manōrama va subr̥hat prākr̥ta kāvya abhī taka anyatra kahīṁ nahī chupā । tīna bhāga mēṁ saṁpūrṇa
hai । pratyēka bhāgakā patrākākārakā mūlya 2-6-0, pustakākāra kā 2-0-0 ।

( 7 ) śāntinātha-caritram-- (kartā mahōpādhyāya śrīmēghavijayajī gaṇi) saṁskr̥ta sāhitya
mēṁ "naiṣadhīya caritra" ēka baṛā hī suramya rōcaka mahākāvya hai। jisakī kīrti sarvatra
phailī huī hai। yaha kāvya usī kāvya kī pādapūrtirūpa sē likhā gayā hai । śāntinātha
bhagavāna kā caritra varṇita hai। baṛā hī manōhara kāvya hai । mūlya 1-0-0 ।
(8) jaina lēkha saṁgraha (prathama bhāga ) saṁgrāhaka bābū pūraṇacandajī nāhara ēma. ē., bī.
ēla., vakīla-hāī kōrṭa, kalakattā । isamēṁ prācīna jaina mūrttiyōṁ tathā śilāōṁ para khudē
huē 1000 lēkhōṁ kā saṁgraha hai। isasē itihāsa sambandhī bahuta sī bātēṁ jānī jā sakatī
haiṁ। baṛē pariśrama sē tayyāra kiyā gayā hai। mūlya 5-0-0
।
(6) rayagāsēhara-kahā-karttā śrī jinaharṣa gaṇi। saṁskr̥ta chāyā sē yukta । mūlya ru. 0-8-0
(10) vivēkamaṁjarī । saṭīka prathama bhāga (sṭôka mēṁ nahīṁ hai ) ।
(11) prākr̥tasūktaratnamālā - isa grantha mēṁ bhinna bhinna viṣaya kē anēka prācīna prākr̥ta
subhāṣitōṁ kā saṁgraha kiyā gayā hai । saṁskr̥ta chāyā bhī dī gaī hai । aura sātha hī mēṁ
aṁgrējī bhāṣāntara bhī diyā gayā hai। mūlya 0-8-0
(12) kummāputtacariaṁ - yaha prākr̥tapadyavaddha grantha hai । isamēṁ kūrmāputra kā caritra varṇana
kiyā gayā hai। saṁskr̥ta chāyā yukta । mūlya 0-4-0 ।
